Title:Genesis

<b>KAPAMPANGAN BIBLE</b>

<b>Genesis</b>

Genesis <lbl>1:1</lbl>  King kamumulan lelangan na ning Dios ing banua at ing labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>1:2</lbl>	At ing labuad ala yang anyu at alang laman; at ing dalumdum atiu babo na ning kalalaman: at ing Espiritu ning Dios gagalo ya babo na ning lupa na ning danum.	

Genesis <lbl>1:3</lbl>	At sinabi na ning Dios, Mika ating sala: at mika ating sala.

Genesis <lbl>1:4</lbl>	At ikit na ning Dios ing sala, king iti mayap: at ing Dios kewani na ing sala king dalumdum.	

Genesis <lbl>1:5</lbl>	At ing pemalaguiu na ning Dios king sala Aldo, at ing kadalumduman inaus nang Bengi. At mika ating bengi at mika ating abak, ing metung a aldo.	

Genesis <lbl>1:6</lbl>	At ing Dios sinabi na, Mika ating kalaganapan king libutad ning danum, at iti kewani na ing danum king danum.

Genesis <lbl>1:7</lbl>	At ing Dios guewa na ing kalaganapan, at kewani na ing danum a atiu lalam na ning kalaganapan king danum a atiu babo na ning kalaganapan: at makanian ing milyari.	

Genesis <lbl>1:8</lbl>	At ing pemalaguiu na ning Dios king kalaganapan Banua. At mika ating bengi at mika ating abak, ing kaduang aldo.	

Genesis <lbl>1:9</lbl>	At ing Dios sinabi na, Mipamisan ing danum a atiu lalam na ning banua king metung a karinan, at lunto ing gabun a malangi: at makanian ing milyari.	

Genesis <lbl>1:10</lbl> 	At ing pemalaguiu na ning Dios king malangi Labuad; at ing kapamisanan ning danum inaus nong Dayatmalat: at ikit na ning Dios king iti mayap.

Genesis <lbl>1:11</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na, Mitubuanan ing gabun king dikut, tanaman a mikakabini, at dutung a mamunga a babie bunga agpang king keang pangadutung, a darala na ing keang bini, babo ning labuad: at makanian ing milyari. 	

Genesis <lbl>1:12</lbl> 	At tinubu king labuad ing dikut, tanaman a mikaka-bini agpang king karelang pangatanaman, at dutung a mamunga, darala na ing keang bini, agpang king karelang pangadutung: at ikit na ning Dios king iti mayap. 	

Genesis <lbl>1:13</lbl> 	At mika ating bengi at mika ating abak, ing katlung aldo. 

Genesis <lbl>1:14</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na, Mika ating sulu king kalaganapan ning banua bang mikawani ing aldo king bengi; at maguing tanda la, at dake-dake ning panaun, at karing aldo at banua: 	

Genesis <lbl>1:15</lbl> 	At maguing sulu la king kalaganapan na ning banua barang pasalan ing babo ning labuad: at makanian ing milyari. 

Genesis <lbl>1:16</lbl> 	At ing Dios guewa no ding aduang mangaragul a sulu; ing sulung peka-maragul panibalan na ing aldo, at ing peka-malating sulu panibalan na ing bengi: guewa nala naman ding batuin. 	

Genesis <lbl>1:17</lbl> 	At ing Dios binili no king kalaganapan ning banua, ban sunlag king babo ning labuad, 

Genesis <lbl>1:18</lbl> 	At bang manibala king aldo at king bengi, at bang mikawani ing sala king dalumdum: at ing Dios ikit na king iti mayap.

Genesis <lbl>1:19</lbl> 	At mika ating bengi at mika ating abak, ing kapat a aldo. 

Genesis <lbl>1:20</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na, Mika atin ing danum karing dakal a gagalo a melalang a maki bie, at ayup a susulapo babo na ning labuad king makabuklat nang kalaganapan ning banua. 	

Genesis <lbl>1:21<lbl> 	At ing Dios lelangan nala ding mangaragul a animal king dayatmalat, at ing balang mabie gagalo a melalang, a kayabe ra ding animal a malati king danum, agpang king karelang pangaasan, at ing balang ayup a baguiusan agpang king keang pangaayup at ing Dios ikit na king iti mayap. 

Genesis <lbl>1:22</lbl> 	At ing Dios binendicionan nala, sinabi na, Pasipamunga kayu, at magpakarakal, at katmuan yu ing danum karing dayatmalat, at ding ayup magpakarakal la king labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>1:23</lbl> 	At mika ating bengi at mika ating abak, ing kalimang aldo. 	

Genesis <lbl>1:24</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na, Mika atin ing labuad karing melalang a mabie agpang king karelang anyu, animales, at bague a gagapang, at ganid king labuad agpang king karelang panga-ganid: at makanian ing milyari. 

Genesis <lbl>1:25</lbl> 	At ing Dios guewa no ding ganid king labuad agpang king karelang panga-ganid, at ding animal agpang king karelang panga-animal, at ing balang bague gagapang babo na ning labuad agpang king keang anyu: at ing Dios ikit na king iti mayap. 

Genesis <lbl>1:26</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na, Lalangan taya ing tau king kekatang kalarawan, agpang king kekatang wangis: at pabustan lang sumakup karing asan king dayatmalat, at karing ayup king banua, at karing animales, at king mabilug a labuad, at king balang bague a gagapang king babo na ning labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>1:27</lbl> 	At ing Dios lelangan ne ing tau a kalarawan na, king larawan na ning Dios lelangan naya; lalaki at babai lelangan nala. 

Genesis <lbl>1:28</lbl> 	At ing Dios pepanuanan nala: at ing Dios sinabi na karela, Pasipamunga kayu, at magpakarakal, at laganapan yu ing labuad, at kekayu yang supilan; at sakupan yula ding asan king dayatmalat, at ding ayup karing banua, at ing balang bague a maki bie gagalo babo ning labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>1:29</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na, Oini, aku binie ke kekayu ing balang tanaman a mamini, a atiu babo nang lupa ning mabilug a labuad, at ing balang dutung, a king bunga ning dutung mikakabini; a kekayu maguing pamangan ye: 

Genesis <lbl>1:30</lbl> 	At king balang animal king labuad, at king balang ayup karing banua, at king balang bague gagapang king babo na ning labuad, a maki bie, ing anggang tanaman a saguiwa binie kung pamangan: at makanian ing milyari.

Genesis <lbl>1:31</lbl> 	At ing Dios ikit na ing anggang lelangan na, at oini, iti binang mayap. At mika ating bengi at mika ating abak, ing kanam a aldo. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:1</lbl>    	At meari la ding banua at labuad, at ing anggang ejercitu ra. 

Genesis <lbl>2:2</lbl> 	At inari na ning Dios king kapitung aldo ing dapat a depatan na; at pepainawa ya king aldo kapitu king anggang dapat a depatan na. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:3</lbl> 	At pepanuanan ne ning Dios ing kapitung aldo, at pengilinan ne; uling kaniti karin ya pepainawa king anggang dapat a depatan na king anggang lelangan na ning Dios. 

Genesis <lbl>2:4</lbl> 	Iti ing pangapalyari ra ding banua at ning labuad inyang melalang la, kanitang aldo a ing GUINUNG Dios lelangan na ing labuad at ing banua. 

Genesis <lbl>2:5</lbl> 	At ala pang tanaman king marangle a sinibut pa; uling e na pa pepauranan ning GUINUNG Dios king babo na ning labuad at alang taung magobra king gabun; 

Genesis <lbl>2:6</lbl> 	Dapot minukiat ibat king labuad ing ulap, diligan na ing anggang lupa na ning labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>2:7</lbl> 	At belangkas ne ping GUINUNG Dios ing tau a ibat king alikabuk ning gabun, at pengisnawanan ne king arung king pangisnawa ning bie; at ing tau meguing kaladua yang mabie. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:8</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios binili ne ing metung a mula king Eden, nangan king aslagan; at binili ne karin ing taung keang belangkas. 

Genesis <lbl>2:9</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios pepatubuan ne ing balang dutung a makawili king panlalawe, at mayap kanan; anti naman ing dutung ning bie king libutad ning mula, at ing dutung ning beluan king mayap at king marawak. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:10</lbl>	 At manibatan ya king Eden ing metung a ilug bang dilig king mula; at manibat karin mikawakawani ya, at meguing apat a sanga. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:11</lbl> 	Ing laguiu na ning mumuna Pison: iti ya ing makapatulug king mabilug nang gabun ning Havilah, nung nukarin ating guintu; 

Genesis <lbl>2:12</lbl> 	At ing guintu na ning gabun a ita mayap: atin mu namang karin bdelio at batung onix. 

Genesis <lbl>2:13</lbl> 	At ing laguiu na ning kaduang ilug Gihon: iti makapatulug ya naman king mabilug nang gabun ning Cush. 

Genesis <lbl>2:14</lbl> 	Ing laguiu na ning katlung ilug Hidekel: iti ya ing mamagus king arapan ning Asiria. At ing kapat a ilug ya ing Eufrates. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:15</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios kinua ne ing tau, at binili ne king mula na ning Eden baneng paimalanan iti at ingatan. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:16</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios inutus na king tau, sinabi na, King balang dutung king mula timawa kang mangan: 

Genesis <lbl>2:17</lbl> 	Dapot king dutung na ning beluan king mayap at marawak, e ka mamangan kea: uling king aldo a mangan ka kea mate kang alang pangakabla. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:18<lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios sinabi na, E mayap king ing tau magsasarili ya; ilalang keng kasaup na a dikil kea. 

Genesis <lbl>2:19</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios lelangan ne king gabun ing balang animal king marangle, at ing balang ayup karing banua; at dela no king tau bang akit na nung nanung yaus na kareti: at ing nanumang pemalaguiu na ning tau king balang pemalaguiu na ning tau king balang mabie melalang, ita ya ing laguiu na. 

Genesis <lbl>2:20</lbl> 	At minie yang laguiu ing tau karing anggang animal, at karing ayup karing banua, at king balang ganid king marangle; dapot e ya makakit a kausap na dikil king tau. 	

Genesis <lbl>2:21</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios bildug na ing malalam a tudtud king tau, at metudtud ya; kanita kinanua yang metung karing keang taguiang, at binili na ing laman king lugal na: 	

Genesis <lbl>2:22</lbl> 	At ing taguiang, a kingua na ning GUINUNG Dios king lalaki, guewa neng metung a babai, at dela ne king lalaki. 

Genesis <lbl>2:23</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning lalaki, Iti ya ngeni ing butul ding butul ku, at laman ning laman ku: iti mipalaguiuwan yang Babai, uling meakua ya king lalaki. 

Genesis <lbl>2:24</lbl> 	King uli na niti lakuan ne ning lalaki i tata na at i indu na, at makiabe ya king asawa na: at maguing metung lang laman. 

Genesis <lbl>2:2</lbl>	At parapara lang lubas, ing lalaki at ing asawa na, at e la mipapalkarine. 

Genesis <lbl>3:1</lbl>   	Ngeni ing ubingan sutil ya a maiguit karing anggang animales king marangle a lelangan na nang GUINUNG Dios. At sinabi na king babai, Wa, sinabi na wari ning Dios kekayu, E ko mamangan king nanumang dutung king mula? 	

Genesis <lbl>3:2</lbl> 	At ing babai mekibat ya king ubingan, Karing bunga ra ding dutung king mula mangan kami: 	

Genesis <lbl>3:3</lbl> 	Dapot king bunga na ning dutung a atiu king libutad ning mula, sinabi na ning Dios, E ko mamangan kaniti, ni e ye tatagkilan, magkang mate kayu. 

Genesis <lbl>3:4</lbl> 	At ing ubingan sinabi na king babai, King katutuan e ko mate: 

Genesis <lbl>3:5</lbl> 	Uling balu na ning Dios a king aldo a mangan ko kaniti, kanita mibuklat la ding kekong mata, at maguing anti kong Dios, abalu yu ing mayap at ing marawak. 

Genesis <lbl>3:6</lbl> 	At inyang ikit na ning babai king ing dutung mayap yang kanan, at king makawili ya karing mata, at king dutung yang makapagnasa ban a pakiabutan ing kabiasnan, kinanua ya karing bunga na, at pengan ne; at dininan naya naman ing keang asawa, at mengan ya namang anti ya. 

Genesis <lbl>3:7</lbl> 	At mibuklat lang parapra ding karelang mata, at abalu ra king lubas la; at tinai la king bulung higuera, at guewa rang tapitapi ra.

Genesis <lbl>3:8</lbl> 	At dimdam da ing siwala na nang GUINUNG Dios a lalakad king mula king karimlan na ning aldo: at sinalikut ya ing lalaki at ing asawa na king arapan nang GUINUNG Dios king busal da ding dutung ning mula. 	

Genesis <lbl>3:9</lbl> 	At inaus neng Guinung Dios ing lalaki, at sinabi na kea, Nuka karin? 

Genesis <lbl>3:10</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Dimdam ku ing siwala mu king mula, at mitakutan ku, uling lubas ku; at sinalikut ku. 

Genesis <lbl>3:11</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Ninung sinabi keka a lubas ka? Mengan ka king dutung a inutus ku kekang e me kakanan? 	

Genesis <lbl>3:12</lbl> 	At ing lalaki mekibat ya, Ing babaing binie mung kayabe ku, dininan naku king dutung, at aku mengan ku.

Genesis <lbl>3:13</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios sinabi na king babai, Nanu ing depatan mu? At sinabi na ning babai, Ing ubingan piraya naku, at mengan ku. 

Genesis <lbl>3:14</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios sinabi na king ubingan, Anti ning depatan mu iti, misumpa ka karing anggang animales, at karing anggang ganid king marangle; ing salu mu ya ing ilakad mu, at alikabuk ing kanan mu king anggang aldo na ning kekang bie: 

Genesis <lbl>3:15</lbl> 	At pipagkamuan dakayu ika at ing babai, at ing bini mu ampon ing bini na: iti ya ing dumunut king buntuk mu, at ika dunutan me sakung. 	

Genesis <lbl>3:16</lbl> 	King babai sinabi na, Parakalan kung bina ing kekang kasakitan, at ing kekang pamangagli; king kasakitan ipanganak mo ding kekang anak; at ing nasa mu maguing king asawa mu, at ya pamajalan naka. 	

Genesis <lbl>3:17</lbl> 	At kang Adam sinabi na, Anti na ning pemintuan mu ing siwala na ning asawa mu, at mengan ka king dutung, a inutus ku keka, sinabi ku, E me kakanan: Makasumpa ing gabun king uli mu; king kapagalan mu mangan ka king anggang aldo na ning kekang bie; 	

Genesis <lbl>3:18</lbl> 	Suksuk at alibubu ing isibut nang maguing keka; at mangan ka karing tanaman king marangle; 

Genesis <lbl>3:19</lbl> 	King uli ning pawas na ning kanuan mu mangan kang tinape, angga king mibalik ka king gabun; uling kea karin meakua: uling alikabuk ka, at king alikabuk ka mibalik. 

Genesis <lbl>3:20</lbl>	At inaus ne ning lalaki ing laguiu ning keang asawa Eva; uling ya ing indu ra ding anggang mabie. 	

Genesis <lbl>3:21</lbl> 	At i GUINUNG Dios guewa ne i Adam at ing asawa na tunikang balat, at pepaimalanan nala. 	

Genesis <lbl>3:22</lbl> 	At sinabi nang GUINUNG Dios, Oini, ing tau meguing metung yang anti itamu, balu na ing mayap at ing marawak; ngeni pin, magkang iyatyat ne ing gamat na, at guntal ya king dutung na ning bie, at mangan ya, at mie yang alang angga—

Genesis <lbl>3:23</lbl> 	Uli na nita pepalakuan neng GUINUNG Dios king mula na ning Eden, bayang galo king gabun nung nuya ibat meakua. 

Genesis <lbl>3:24</lbl> 	Nung inya tinabi ne pin lual ing tau; at binili ne king aslagan na ning mula ning Eden ing Querubin, at metung a talibung a mitatau a lilibut king misusumangid, baneng ingatan ing dalan ning dutung na ning bie. 

Genesis <lbl>4:1</lbl>    	At akilala ne ning lalaki i Evang asawa na; at kinagli ya, at penganak ne i Cain, at sinabi na, Mika anak kung lalaki king saup nang GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>4:2</lbl> 	At pepasibayu penganak ne i Abel a kapatad na. At meguing pastul yang tupa i Abel, dapot i Cain meguing talagalo ya king gabun. 

Genesis <lbl>4:3</lbl> 	At milyari kabang lalakad ing panaun, i Cain migdala ya king bunga na ning gabun metung a ain kang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:4</lbl> 	At i Abel, migdala ya naman karing pangane karing keang kawan at karing pekamataba kareti. At lingusan neng GUINU i Abel at ing ain na: 	

Genesis <lbl>4:5</lbl> 	Dapot e ne lingusan i Cain at ing keang ain. At i Cain mikapali yang bina, at melulam ya ing keang lupa. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:6</lbl> 	At i GUINU sinabi na kang Cain, Baket mikapali ka? At baket melulam ing kekang lupa? 	

Genesis <lbl>4:7</lbl> 	Nung ika darapat ka sang mayap, e wari iti matangap? At nung e ka darapat mayap, ing kasalanan mibili king pasbul; at keka ing maguing nasa na; dapot ika ing sumakup kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:8</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Cain king kapatad nang i Abel. At milyari, inyang atilu karing king marangle, king i Cain tinalakad yang laban king kapatad nang i Abel, at pete ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:9</lbl> 	At i GUINU sinabi na kang Cain, Nuya karin i Abel a kapatad mu? At ya mekibat ya, E ke balu; aku waring talaingat king kapatad ko? 	

Genesis <lbl>4:10</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na kea, Nanung depatan mu? Ing siwala na ning daya na ning kapatad mu daralung kanaku manibat king gabun. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:11</lbl> 	At ngeni makasumpa ka king gabun, a biklat ne ing keang asbuk banang tanggapan ing daya ning kekang kapatad a ibat king kekang gamat; 	

Genesis <lbl>4:12</lbl> 	Ngening galo ka king gabun, e na na ibie keka manibat ngeni ing keang sikanan; maguing magpalayaslayas ka at maglibutlibut king labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>4:13</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Cain kang GIUNU, Tutung mipakaragul ing kakung kaparusan a maiguit king aguiu kung pibatan. 

Genesis <lbl>4:14</lbl> 	Oini, ika tinabi muku ngeni king lupa na ning gabun; at king kekang arapan misalikut ku; at maguing palayaslayas ku at maglibutlibut king labuad; at malyari, king ing ninumang manakit kaku, patayan naku. 

Genesis <lbl>4:15</lbl> 	At pekibatan neng GUINU, Uli na niti ing ninumang makamate kang Cain, miparusan yang makatapitung ukdu. At i GUINU dininan neng tanda i Cain, magkang ing ninumang makakit kea patayan ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:16</lbl> 	At meko ya i Cain king arapan nang GUINU, at menuknangan ya king labuad ning Nod, king aslagan na ning Eden. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:17</lbl> 	At kilala neng Cain ing keang asawa; at kinagli ya, at penganak ne i Enoc; at mitalakad yang metung a ciudad, at inaus na ing laguiu na ning ciudad, agpang king laguiu na ning keang anak, a i Enoc. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:18</lbl> 	At kang Enoc mibait ya i Irad; at i Irad ayanak ne i Mehujael; at i Mehujael ayanak ne i Methusael, at i Methusael ayanak ne i Lamech. 

Genesis <lbl>4:19</lbl> 	At i Lamech kinanua yang adua nang asawa: ing laguiu na ning metung Ada, at ing laguiu na ning kadua Zilla. 

Genesis <lbl>4:20</lbl> 	At i Ada penganak ne i Jabal: ya ing ibpa ra ding manuknangan karing kubu at ating animal. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:21</lbl> 	At ing laguiu na ning keang kapatad Jubal: ya ang ibpa ra ding anggang talatigtig alpa at pitu. 

Genesis <lbl>4:22</lbl> 	At i Zilla, penganak na neman e Tubal-Cain, ing pande king pamangutud karing balang kasangkapan a tangsu at bakal: at ing kapatad nang babaing Tubal-Cain ya pin i Naama. 

Genesis <lbl>4:23</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Lamech karing keang asawa: Ada at i Zilla, pakiramdaman yu ing siwala ku; Ikong asawa nang Lamech, tingiran yu ing sasabian ku: Uling mekamate kung metung a lalaki uling sinugat naku, at metung a baintau uling peluka naku: 	

Genesis <lbl>4:24</lbl> 	Nung makapipitung ukdung miablasan ya i Cain, katutuan i Lamech makatapitung pulung makatapitung ukdu. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:25</lbl> 	At kilala neng pisabayung Adam ing keang asawa; at menganak yang metung a lalaki, at ing inaus na king laguiu na Set: Uling, ya sinabi na, Ing Dios dininan nakung aliwang bini a kalili nang Abel; uling pete neng Cain. 	

Genesis <lbl>4:26</lbl> 	At i Set mika anak ne mang metung a lalaki; at ing inaus na king laguiu na Enos. Manibat kanita pigmulan da na ding tau a minaus king laguiu nang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>5:1</lbl>   	Iti ing libru ding dai nang Adam. King aldo a lelangan ne ning Dios ing tau, melalang ya king kalarawan na ning Dios; 	

Genesis <lbl>5:2</lbl> 	Lalaki at babai lang lelangan na, at pepanuanan nala, at ing inaus naking laguiu ra Adam, kanitang aldo a lelangan nala. 

Genesis <lbl>5:3</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Adam dinalan atlungpulung banua, a menganak yang metung a lalaki a kawangis na, makalupa ya king keang larawan; at ing inaus na king keang laguiu Set: 

Genesis <lbl>5:4</lbl> 	At ding meguing aldo ng Adam kaibat neng penganak i Set walu lang dalan a banua: at menganak yang lalaki at babai. 	

Genesis <lbl>5:5</lbl> 	At ding anggang aldo a meguing bie nang Adam siam a dalan atlungpulung banua: at mete ya. 

Genesis <lbl>5:6</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Set dinalan at limang banua, at ayanak ne i Enos: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:7</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Set kaibat neng ayanak i Enos, walung dalan at pitung banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai. 

Genesis <lbl>5:8</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Set siam lang dalan at labingaduang banua: at mete ya. 

Genesis <lbl>5:9</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Enos siamapulung banua, at ayanak ne i Cainan: 

Genesis <lbl>5:10</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Enos kaibat neng ayanak i Cainan, walung dalan at labinglimang banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:11</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Enos siam lang dalan at limang banua: at mete ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>5:12</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Cainan pitungpulung banua, at ayanak ne i Mahalalel: 

Genesis <lbl>5:13</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Cainan kaibat neng ayanak i Mahalalel, walung dalan at apatapulung banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 

Genesis <lbl>5:14</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Cainan siam a dalan at apulung banua: at mete ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>5:15</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Mahalalel, anamapulu at limang banua, at ayanak ne i Jared: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:16</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Mahalalel kaibat neng ayanak i Jared, walung dalan at atlungpulung banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:17</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Mahalalel, walung dalan siamapulu at limang banua: at mete ya. 

Genesis <lbl>5:18</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Jared dinalan anamapulu at aduang banua, at ayanak ne i Enoc: 	


Genesis <lbl>5:19</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Jared kaibat neng ayanak i Enoc walung dalan a banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 

Genesis <lbl>5:20</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Jared siam lang dalan anamapulu at aduang banua: at mete ya. 

Genesis <lbl>5:21</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Enoc anamapulu at limang banua, at ayanak ne i Matusalem: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:22</lbl> 	At linakad ya i Enoc a kayabe na ning Dios, kaibat neng ayanak i Matusalem atlung dalan a banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 

Genesis <lbl>5:23</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Enoc atlu lang dalan anamapulu at limang banua: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:24</lbl> 	Linakad ya pin Enoc a kayabe ning Dios: at e ya meakit; uling kingua ne ning Dios.

Genesis <lbl>5:26</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Matusalem kaibat neng ayanak i Lamech pitung dalan walungpulu at aduang banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 

Genesis <lbl>5:27</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Matusalem siam lang dalan anamapulu at siam a banua: at mete ya. 

Genesis <lbl>5:28</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Lamech dinalan walungpulu at aduang banua, at menganak yang metung a lalaki: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:29</lbl> 	At ing inaus na king keang laguiu Noe, sinabi na, Iti patulan nakatamu king kekatang dapat at king dapat da ding kekatang gamat, a dinatang king uli na ning gabun a simpa nang GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>5:30</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Lamech kaibat neng ayanak i Noe limang dalan siamapulu at limang banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai: 	

Genesis <lbl>5:31</lbl> 	At ding anggang meguing aldo nang Lamech pitung dalan pitungpulu at pitung banua: at mete ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>5:32</lbl> 	At i Noe atin yang limang dalan a banua tua: ayanak ne i Sem, i Cam, at i Jafet. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:1</lbl>   	At milyari, inyang migmula nong merakal ding tau babo na ning lupa na ning gabun, at menganak lang babai, 

Genesis <lbl>6:2</lbl> 	At ikit da ding anak na ning Dios king ding anak dang babai ding tau mangalagu la; pesikua lang karelang asawa karing anggang pinili ra. 

Genesis <lbl>6:3</lbl> 	At i GUINU sinabi na, Ing kakung Espiritu e maki laban king tau kapilan man, uling ya man laman ya: dapot ding maguing aldo na dinalan at aduangpulung banua. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:4</lbl> 	Atilu king gabun ding gigante kanitang panaun a ita, at anti naman kaibat na niti, inyang datang la ding anak nang lalaki ning Dios karing anak dang babai ding tau, at ila menganak la karela: deti ila namang meguing masikanan manibat king mumunang panaun, a ila ding lalaking bantug. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:5</lbl> 	At ikit nang GUINU king ing kasalanan ning tau dakal king labuad, at king ing mabilug nang pamiisip king keang pusu pawang mung marawak. 

Genesis <lbl>6:6</lbl> 	At sinisi ya i GUINU king alalang ne ing tau keti king labuad, at melungkut ya king keang pusu. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:7</lbl> 	At i GUINU sinabi na, Lipulan ke ing tau a kakung lelangan king lupa na ning gabun; ing tau, at ing animal, at ding bague a gagapang, at ding ayup karing banua; uling sisisian ku ing pamanlalang ku karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:8</lbl> 	Dapot i Noe menakit yang kalam karing mata nang GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>6:9</lbl> 	Deti ilang dai nang Noe. I Noe lalaki yang banal, at sakdal king kapanaunan na: linakad ya i Noe a kayabe na ning Dios. 

Genesis <lbl>6:10</lbl> 	At i Noe mika anak yang atlung lalaki, i Sem, i Cam, at i Jafet. 

Genesis <lbl>6:11</lbl> 	At merawak ing labuad king arapan na ning Dios, at ing labuad kinatmu king pamisasalangsangan. 

Genesis <lbl>6:12</lbl> 	At ikit na ning Dios ing labuad, at, oini, merawak; uling peparawak na ning anggang laman ing karelang pamanlakad king babo na ning labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>6:13</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na kang Noe, Ing kawakasan na ning anggang laman dinatang king arapan ku; uling ing labuad mitmu king pamisasalangsangan king pamamilatan da; at oini, aku lipulan kula a kayabe ning labuad.

Genesis <lbl>6:14</lbl> 	Gawa kang metung a daung king dutung a cipres; gawan mo ding silid king daung, at salaksakan meng galagala kilub at lual. 

Genesis <lbl>6:15</lbl> 	At makanian yang gawan mu iti: atlu yang dalan a siku king kaba ing daung, limangpulung siku king liwalas, at atlung pulung siku king katas. 

Genesis <lbl>6:16</lbl> 	Gawa kang metung a awang king daung, at angganan meng metung a siku nangan babo; at ibili me ing pasbul ning daung king katalindikingan; gawan meng atlu balag, lalam, kadua, at katlu. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:17</lbl> 	At aku, oini, iparala ku ing metung a albug ning danum king babo ning labuad, bang lipulan ing anggang laman, a maki pangisnawa ning bie, king lalam ning banua; ding anggang atiu king labuad mate la. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:18</lbl> 	Dapot italakad ku ing tipan ku keka; at lungub ka king daung, ika, at ding anak mung lalaki, at ing asawa mu, at ding asawa ra ding anak mung kayabe mu. 

Genesis <lbl>6:19</lbl> 	At ding anggang mabibie, karing sablang laman, adua karing balang anyu misake ka king daung, balang mie kayabe mu; lalaki la at babai la sa. 

Genesis <lbl>6:20</lbl> 	Karing ayup agpang king karelang panga-ayup, at karing animal agpang king karelang panga-animal, at king balang gagapang a bague king gabun agpang king keang anyu, adua king balang metung a anyu ilub mu lang kayabe mu, balang maingat mie. 

Genesis <lbl>6:21</lbl> 	At magdala ka king anggang pamangan a kakanan, at tipunan mung tungkul keka; at maguing pamangan mu, at karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>6:22</lbl> 	Makanian ing depatan nang Noe; agpang king anggang inutus ning Dios kea, makanian ing depatan na. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:1</lbl>   	At i GUINU sinabi na kang Noe, Sake ka at ing mabilug mung bale king daung; uling keka menakit kung matulid king arapan ku king daing iti. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:2</lbl> 	King balang animal a malinis kuma ka tiapitu-pitu, lalaki at ing keang babai; at karing animal a e malinis, adua, ing lalaki at ing keang babai: 

Genesis <lbl>7:3</lbl> 	Karing ayup banua, tiapitu-pitu, lalaki at babai, bang ingatan lang bining mabie babo na ning lupa na ning mabilug a labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:4</lbl> 	Uling pangalabas na ning pitung aldo, aku pauranan ku babo na ning labuad apatapulung aldo at apatapulung bengi; at lipulan ke ing balang maki bie a depatan ku king babo nang lupa ning gabun. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:5</lbl> 	At depatan nang Noe agpang king anggang inutus na keang GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>7:6</lbl> 	At i Noe atin neng anam a dalan a banua tua kanitang ing albug ning danum dinatang king babo na ning labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:7</lbl> 	At sinake ya i Noe, at ding anak na, at ing asawa na, at ding asawa ra ding anak na, kayabe no king daung, uli ning danum ning albug. 

Genesis <lbl>7:8</lbl> 	Karing animal a malinis, at karing animal a e malinis, at karing ayup, at king balang bague gagapang babo na ning gabun. 

Genesis <lbl>7:9</lbl> 	Tidua-tidua minta la kang Noe king daung, lalaki at babai, anti mo ing inutus na ning Dios kang Noe. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:10</lbl> 	At milyari kaibat ning pitung aldo, king ing danum ning albug atiu king babo ning labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:11</lbl> 	King kanam nang dalan a banua ning bie nang Noe, king kaduang bulan, king kalabing pitung aldo ning bulan, king aldo mu ring ita mengasira la ding anggang bukal ning maragul a kalalaman, at ding awang na ning banua mengabusni la. 

Genesis <lbl>7:12</lbl> 	At ing uran atiu babo na ning labuad apatapulung aldo at apatapulung bengi. 

Genesis <lbl>7:13</lbl> 	At kanita mu ring aldo a ita sinake ya i Noe, at i Sem, at i Cam, at i Jafet, ding anak nang Noe, at ing asawa nang Noe, at ding atlu rang asawa ding anak na kayabe rala, king daung; 

Genesis <lbl>7:14</lbl> 	Ila, at ing balang animal a ganid agpang king keang panga-animal at ing balang animal a mamu agpang king keang panga-animal at ing balang bague a gagapang babo na ning labuad agpang king keang anyu, at ing balang ayup agpang king keang anyu, ing balang ayup ning balang anyu. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:15</lbl> 	At minta la kang Noe king daung, tidua-tidua karing anggang laman a mika ating pangisnawa ning bie. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:16</lbl> 	At detang linub karin, linub la lalaki at babai karing anggang laman, anti mo ing inutus na kea ning Dios: at i GUINU kilung ne. 

Genesis <lbl>7:17</lbl> 	At ing albug apatapulung aldo king babo na ning labuad; at ing danum dinagul, at guinato ya ing daung, at mitas ya babo ning labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>7:18</lbl> 	At minyaul ing danum, at meragul a bina king babo na ning labuad; at linayag ya ing daung babo na ning lupa na ning danum. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:19</lbl> 	At ing danum minyaul a bina king babo na ning labuad; at ding anggang bunduk a mangatas a atiu king lalam ning banua limbug la. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:20</lbl> 	Labinglimang siku king katas ing iniguit na ning danum; at limbug la ding bunduk. 

Genesis <lbl>7:21</lbl> 	At mete la ding anggang laman a gagalo king babo ning labuad, ding ayup, at ding animal, at ding ganid, at ing balang bague a gagapang babo na ning labuad, at ing balang tau: 

Genesis <lbl>7:22</lbl> 	Ding anggang ating pangisnawa ning espiritu ning bie karing karelang arung, ding anggang atiu king gabun a mamala, mete la. 	

Genesis <lbl>7:23</lbl> 	At melipul la ding anggang maki bie a mabibie king babo nang lupa ning gabun, ding tau at ding animal, at ding gagapang, at ding ayup banua; at melipul la king labuad: at mitagan yang dili na i Noe, at ding abe na king daung. 

Genesis <lbl>7:24</lbl> 	At minyaul ing danum king babo ning labuad dinalan limangpulung aldo. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:1</lbl>   	At ing Dios anganaka ne i Noe, at ding anggang ganid at ding anggang animal a kayabe na king daung: at pepatiup ya ing Dios metung a angin king babo ning labuad, at ing danum kinati; 	

Genesis 8:2 	Mikabat la ding bukal king kalalaman at ding awang na ning banua, at ing uran king banua tinuknang; 	

Genesis <lbl>8:3</lbl> 	At minurung ing danum king babo ning labuad a alang likat: at kinati ing danum kaibat na ning dinalan limangpulung aldo. 

Genesis <lbl>8:4</lbl> 	At sinadsad ya ing daung king kapitung bulan, kalabing pitung aldo ning bulan, king babo ra ding bunduk na ning Ararat. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:5</lbl> 	At ing danum misundu king pamangati angga king kapulung bulan: king kapulung bulan, king mumuna nang aldo ning bulan, meakit la ding taluktuk ding bunduk. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:6</lbl> 	At milyari king kaibat ning apatapulung aldo, biklat neng Noe ing awang na ning daung a guewa na: 	

Genesis <lbl>8:7</lbl> 	At tiburan ne ing awak, at mine ya keta at karin, angga king ing danum melangi king babo ning labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:8</lbl> 	At inutusan ne ing patipati, bang lawan na nung ing danum kinati na king babo nang lupa ning gabun; 

Genesis <lbl>8:9</lbl> 	Dapot e ya menakit ing patipati nung nuno idalpak ing talampakan ding keang bitis, at mibalik ya kea king daung; uling ing danum atiu king babo nang lupa ning mabilug a labuad: at ya inatyat ne ing gamat na, at telanan ne, at linub ne kea king daung. 

Genesis <lbl>8:10</lbl> 	At menaya ya pang aliwang pitung aldo, at inutusan neng pasibayu ing patipati lual ning daung; 	

Genesis <lbl>8:11</lbl> 	At ing patipati mibalik ya kea king gatpanapun; at, oini, magdala yang metung a bulung a olivang pinti king keang tuktuk: inya atalastas nang Noe king ing danum kinati na king babo ning labuad.

Genesis <lbl>8:12</lbl> 	At menaya ya pang aliwang pitung aldo, at tiburan ne ing patipati; at iti e ne mibalik pang pepasibayu kea.

Genesis <lbl>8:13</lbl> 	At milyari king anam a dalan at metung a banua, king mumunang bulan, king mumunang aldo ning bulan, ing danum melangi king babo ning labuad: at leko neng Noe ing takap na ning daung, at mitio ya, at, oini, king ing lupa na ning gabun malangi. 

Genesis <lbl>8:14</lbl> 	At king kaduang bulan, king kaduangpulu at pitung aldo ning bulan, malangi ing labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:15</lbl> 	At ing Dios miniabi ya kang Noe, sinabi na, 

Genesis <lbl>8:16</lbl> 	Lual ka king daung, ika, at ing asawa mu, at ding anak mung lalaki, at ding asawa ra ding anak mu a kayabe mu. 

Genesis <lbl>8:17</lbl> 	Ilual me ing balang bague a maki bie kayabe mu karing anggang laman, ding ayup, at ding animal, at ing balang bague a gagapang king babo ning labuad balang pasipamaliping dakal king labuad, at pasipamunga at magpakarakal king babo ning labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:18</lbl> 	At linual ya i Noe, at ding keang anak a lalaki, at ing asawa na, at ding asawa ra ding keang anak a kayabe na: 

Genesis <lbl>8:19</lbl> 	Ing balang animal, ing balang bague a gagapang, ing balang ayup, ing nanumang gagalo king babo ning labuad, agpang king karelang anyu, linual la king daung. 

Genesis <lbl>8:20</lbl> 	At mitalakad ya i Noe metung a altar tungkul kang GUINU, at kinua ne ing balang animal a malinis, at ing balang ayup a malinis, at midaun yang ain a durukulan king babo ning altar. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:21</lbl> 	At aban nang GUINU ing malambut a bau; at sinabi nang GUINU king keang pusu, E ku na pasibayung isumpa ing gabun king uli na ning tau, uling ing nasa na ning pusu na ning tau marawak manibat king keang kayanakan; e ku ne pasibayung lipulan ing balang mabibie, anti mo ing depatan ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>8:22</lbl> 	Kabang ing labuad manatili, ing pamanasik at ing pamamalut, at ing dimla at pali, at kaleldo at kauran, at aldo at bengi e la patugut. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:1</lbl>   	At pepanuanan ne ning Dios i Noe ampon ding keang anak a lalaki, at sinabi na karela, Pasipanganak kayu, at magpakarakal kayu, at katmuan yu ing labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>9:2</lbl> 	At ing takut kekayu, at ing sindak kekayu mike karing anggang ganid king labuad, at king balang ayup karing banua; at ding sablang bague gagapang king gabun, at karing anggang asan king dayatmalat, miyayabie la king kekong gamat. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:3</lbl> 	Ing balang gagalo a mabibie maguing pamangan yula; anti mo ing pamamie ku karing anggang saguiwang gule kekayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:4</lbl> 	Dapot king laman a maki bie, king keang daya, e ko mamangan. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:5</lbl> 	At tune ing kekong daya, at ing daya na ning kekong bie, liliwan ku; at king gamat na ning balang ganid isingil ku: at king gamat ning tau, king gamat na ning balang kapatad ning tau, isingil ku ing bie na ning tau. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:6</lbl> 	Ing ninumang mibubu king daya na ning tau, king pamamilatan na ning tau mibubu ing keang daya: uling king larawan na ning Dios melalang ya ing tau. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:7</lbl> 	At ikayu, pasipanganak kayu, at magpakarakal kayu; dakal kong labis-labis king labuad, at ikayu magpakarakal ko kea. 

Genesis <lbl>9:8</lbl> 	At ing dios miniabi ya kang Noe, at karing keang anak a kayabe na, sinabi na, 	

Genesis <lbl>9:9</lbl> 	At aku, oini, itatalakad ku ing kanakung tipan kekayu, at karing kekong dai a tutuki kekayu; 	

Genesis <lbl>9:10</lbl> 	At king balang melalang a maki bie a kayabe yu, ding ayup, ding animal, at ing balang ganid king labuad a kayabe yu; karing anggang kinuldas king daung, pati king balang animal king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:11</lbl> 	At italakad ku ing kakung tipan kekayu; ni e ku na lipulan kapilanman ing anggang laman king danum na ning albug; ni e na mika albug bang sumira king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:12</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning Dios, Iti ing tanda ning tipan a depatan ku kaku at kekayu at king balang melalang a maki bie a kayabe yu, dikil karing keganaganang dai: 	

Genesis <lbl>9:13</lbl> 	Ing kakung pananari ibili ke king lulam, at iti ya ing maguing tanda na ning pamikasundu, kaku at king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:14</lbl> 	At malyari, king nung pakuldas kung metung a lulam king babo na ning labuad, king akit de ing pinanari king lulam, 

Genesis <lbl>9:15</lbl> 	At ganakan ku ing kakung tipan, a atiu kanaku at kekayu at king balang melalang a maki bie karing anggang laman; at ing danum e na maguing albug bang lumipul karing sablang laman. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:16</lbl> 	At magbili ya ing pinanari king lulam: at lawan ke, bakung ganakan ing alang anggang tipan ning Dios at king balang melalang a maki bie karing anggang laman a atiu babo ning labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:17</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na kang Noe, Iti ya ing tanda na ning tipan a telakad ku kanaku at karing anggang laman a atiu babo ning labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:18</lbl> 	At ding anak nang lalaking Noe, a kinuldas king daung, ila i Sem, at i Cam, at i Jafet: at i Cam ya ing ibpa nang Canaan. 

Genesis <lbl>9:19</lbl> 	Ding atlung deti anak nong Noe: at karela kinatmu ing mabilug a labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>9:20</lbl> 	At migmula ya i Noe a guinalo king gabun, at mibili yang metung a uvasan: 	

Genesis <lbl>9:21</lbl> 	At minimum ya king alak, at melasing ya; at ya melubas ya libutad na ning keang kubu. 

Genesis <lbl>9:22</lbl> 	At i Cam, a ibpa nang Canaan, ikit na ing kalubasan nang ibpa na, it sinabi na karing adua nang tad a atiu lual. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:23</lbl> 	At i Sem at i Jafet kinanua lang imalan, at binili ra karelang pago, at linakad lang paurung, at tikpan daing kalubasan na ning karelang ibpa; at ing lupa ra makabalikid king gulut, at e ra ikit ing kalubasan ning karelang ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:24</lbl> 	At miguising ya i Noe king lasing na king alak, at abalu na ing depatan na kea ning anak nang bungsu. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:25</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Misumpa ya i Canaan; maguing ipus de ding ipus da ding keang kapatad. 

Genesis <lbl>9:26</lbl> 	At ya sinabi, Nuan ya i GUINU, ing Dios nang Sem; at i Canaan maguing ipus ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>9:27</lbl> 	Ing Dios paragulan ne i Jafet, at pabustan yang manuknangan karing kubu nang Sem; at maguing ipus ne i Canaan. 

Genesis <lbl>9:28</lbl> 	At i Noe mebie ya kaibat ning albug atlung dalan at limangpulung banua. 

Genesis <lbl>9:29</lbl> 	At ding anggang aldo nang Noe siam adalan at limangpulung banua: at mete ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>10:1</lbl> 	Ngeni deti ila ding dai ra ding anak nang Noe, a mipalaguiuwan, Sem, Cam at i Jafet: at kareti mengabait la ding anak kaibat ning albug. 

Genesis <lbl>10:2</lbl> 	Ding anak nang Jafet: i Gomer, at i Magog, at i Madai, at i Javan, at i Tubal, at i Mesec, at i Tiras. 

Genesis <lbl>10:3</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Gomer: i Askenaz, at i Rifat, at i Togarma. 

Genesis <lbl>10:4</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Javan: i Elisa, at i Tarsis, at i Kitim, at i Dodanim. 

Genesis <lbl>10:5</lbl> 	Kareti mipirake la ding pulu ra ding bansa king karelang labuad, balang metung tungkul king keang amanu, agpang king karelang dai, karing karelang bansa. 

Genesis <lbl>10:6</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Cam: i Cus, at i Mizraim, at i Put, at i Canaan. 

Genesis <lbl>10:7</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Cus: i Seba, at i Havila, at i Sabta, at i Raama, at i Sebteca; at ding anak nang Raama: Saba, at i Dedan. 

Genesis <lbl>10:8</lbl> 	At i Cus ayanak ne i Nimrod: iti meguing mayupaya king labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>10:9</lbl> 	Iti meguing mayupaya yang mamangasu king arapan nang GUINU: inya mesabi, Anti ya mo i Nimrod, mayupaya yang mamangasu king arapan nang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>10:10</lbl> 	At ing meguing pigmulan na ning keang kayarian ya ing Babel, at ing Erec, at ing Acad, at ing Calne, king gabun na ning Sinar. 	

Genesis <lbl>10:11</lbl> 	Manibatan king gabun a ita mine ya Asiria, at telakad ne ing Nineve, at Rehoboth-Ir, at ing Cale,

Genesis <lbl>10:18</lbl> 	At ing Arvadeo, at ing Zemareo, at ing Hamateo: at kaibat mikalat la ding anggang sapni ra ding Cananeo. 	

Genesis </lbl>10:19</lbl> 	At ing meguing angganan da ding Cananeo manibatan Zidon, a nung isanu ing mame Gerar, angga king Gaza; nung mame king Sodoma at Gomorra at Adma at Zeboim, angga king Lasa. 

Genesis <lbl>10:20</lbl> 	Deti ila ding anak nang Cam, agpang karing karelang sapni, agpang karing karelang amanu, karing karelang labuad, karing karelang bansa.

Genesis <lbl>10:25</lbl> 	At kang Eber mibait la ding aduang lalaki: ing laguiu na ning metung Peleg; uling karing keang cayaldawan ing yatu mipirake; at ing laguiu na ning kapatad nang lalaki Joktan.

Genesis <lbl>10:31</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang Sem, agpang karing karelang sapni, agpang karing karelang amanu, karing karelang labuad, agpang karing karelang bansa.

Genesis <lbl>11:1</lbl> 	At ing mabilug a labuad metung mu ing amanu na at metung mu rin ing salita na. 	

Genesis <lbl>11:2</lbl> 	At milyari, king karelang pamaglakbe king aslagan, mekakit lang kapatagan king gabun na ning Sinar; at menuknangan la karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>11:3</lbl> 	At misabisabi la, Tara, gawa tamung lariu at itiba talang mayap. At guewa rong batu ding lariu, at ing pila guewa rang asung. 	

Genesis <lbl>11:4</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Tara, mitalakad tang kekatamung ciudad, at metung a torre, at ing keang taluktuk miras ya angga banua, at gawa tamung metung tang laguiu; magkang mikalat tamu king babo nang lupa ning mabilug a labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>11:5</lbl> 	At tinipa ya i GUINU baneng lawan ing ciudad at ing torre, a telakad da ding anak da ding tau.

Genesis <lbl>11:6</lbl> 	At i GUINU sinabi na, Oini, ing balayan metung mu, at deti ngan atin lang metung a amanu; at oiti ing pigmulan dang depat: at ngeni ninuman alang makasansala karela, king inakala rang daptan. 

Genesis <lbl>11:7</lbl> 	Tana, tipa tamu, at guluan tamu ing karelang amanu, bang e la makapitalastasan king karelang salita. 

Genesis <lbl>11:8</lbl> 	Makanian nong silbag GUINU manibat karin king babo nang lupa ning mabilug a labuad: at karelang likuan ing pamitalakad king ciudad. 

Genesis <lbl>11:9</lbl> 	Inya ing laguiung inaus da Babel; uling karin na guiluan GUINU ing amanu ning mabilug a labuad: at ibat karin silbag nong GUINU king babo nang lupa ning mabilug a labuad.

Genesis <lbl>11:15</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Selah kaibat neng ayanak i Heber apat a dalan at atlungpulung banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai.

Genesis <lbl>11:17</lbl>	At mebie ya i Heber kaibat neng ayanak i Peleg, apat a dalan at atlungpulung banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai. 

Genesis <lbl>11:18</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Peleg atlungpulung banua, at ayanak ne i Reu: 

Genesis <lbl>11:19</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Peleg kaibat neng ayanak i Reu, aduang dalan at siam a banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai.

Genesis <lbl>11:21</lbl> 	At mebie ya i Reu kaibat neng ayanak i Serug aduang dalan at pitung banua, at menganak yang lalaki at babai.

 i Abram, i Nahor at i Haran. 	And Terah lived seventy years, and begat Abram, Nahor, and Haran.
Genesis <lbl>11:27</lbl> 	Deti ilang dai nang Tare. I Tare ayanak ne i Abram, i Nahor, at i Haran; at i Haran ayanak ne i Lot. 	

Genesis <lbl>11:28</lbl> 	At mete ya i Haran king arapan na ning keang ibpa a i Tare king gabun a tibuan na king Ur da ding Caldeo.

Genesis <lbl>11:32</lbl> 	At ding meguing aldo nang Tare aduang dalan at limang banua: at mete ya i Tare karin Haran.

Genesis <lbl>12:1</lbl> 	Ngeni sinabi nang GUINU kang Abram, Mako ka king kekang labuad, at karing kekang kamaganak, at king bale na ning kekang ibpa, ume ka king gabun a ituru ku keka: 

Genesis <lbl>12:2</lbl> 	At gawan dakang metung a maragul a bansa, at ika panuanan daka, at paragulan ku ing kekang laguiu; at maguing metung kang kanuanan: 	

Genesis <lbl>12:3</lbl> 	At panuanan kula ding panuan keka, at ing misumpa keka isumpa ke; at mipanuanan la king uli mu ding anggang sapni king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:4</lbl> 	Inya mine ya i Abram, nung makananung sinabi na keang GUINU; at tinuki ya kea i Lot: at i Abram pitu neng pulu at limang banua tua kanitang meko ya Haran. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:5</lbl> 	At tiki neng Abram i Sarai a asawa na, at i Lot a anak na ning keang kapatad, at ing anggang pibandian a karelang atipun, at ding kaladuang karelang ikua karin Haran; at meko la balang ume king gabun na ning Canaan; at dinatang la king labuad ning Canaan. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:6</lbl> 	At linabas ya i Abram king gabun a ita angga king karinan ning Sichem, angga king dutung a encina ning More. At kanita ing Cananeo atiu king labuad a ita. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:7</lbl> 	At i GUINU pepakit ya kang Abram, at sinabi na, Karing kekang dai ibie ku ing gabun a iti: at mitalakad ya karin metung a altar kang GUINU a pepakit kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:8</lbl> 	At ibat karin linipat ya king bunduk a atiu king aslagan ning Betel, at karin ne telakad ing keang kubu, atiu king albugan ing Betel, at ing Hai atiu king aslagan: at karin mitalakad yang altar kang GUINU, at inaus ne ing laguiu nang GUINU, 	

Genesis <lbl>12:9</lbl> 	At i Abram miglakbe ya, melaus ya nangan pa king mauli. 

Genesis <lbl>12:10</lbl> 	At mika danup king labuad: at kinuldas ya i Abram mine ya Egipto, bayang manuknangan karin, uling maragul ing danup king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:11</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang malapit neng lungub Egipto, sinabi na kang Sarai a asawa na, Oini ngeni, akikilala ku king ika malagu kang babaing lawan: 	

Genesis <lbl>12:12</lbl> 	At malyari, king nung akit daka ding Egipcios, sabian da, Iti kea yang asawa: at patayan daku, at ika iligitas da ing bie mu. 

Genesis <lbl>12:13</lbl> 	Ngeni pin, pagamuamu ku keka, sabian mu, king kapatad daka; bang mipakayap ku king uli mu, at mie ya ing kaladua ku king uli mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:14</lbl> 	At milyari, king, inyang lungub ya i Abram karin Egipto, ding Egipcios ikit da king ing babai bina yang malagu. 

Genesis <lbl>12:15</lbl> 	At ikit de ding principes nang Faraon, at karela yang pinuri kang Faraon: at dela re ing babai king bale nang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:16</lbl> 	At pepakitanan neng lub a mayap i Abram king uli na: at atin yang tupa, at vaca, at asnong lalaki, at ipus a lalaki, at ipus a babai, at asna, at camello. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:17</lbl> 	At i GUINU perusan ne i Faraon at ing keang bale king maragul a batbat, king uli nang Sarai a asawa nang Abram. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:18 </lbl>	At i Faraon inaus ne i Abram, at sinabi na, Nanu iting depatan mu kanaku? Baket e mu sasabian king asawa me?

Genesis <lbl>12:19 </lbl>	Baket sinabi mu, Kapatad ke, nung inya kinua ke bakeng maguing asawa? Ngeni pin oyan ing asawa mo, kuanan me, at ume ka king kekang dalan. 	

Genesis <lbl>12:20</lbl> 	At i Faraon minie yang utus karing tau tungkul kea: at dela re king dalan, at ing keang asawa, at pati na ing sablang atiu kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:1</lbl> 	At sinampa ya i Abram king mauli menibatan Egipto, ya, at ing keang asawa, at pati na ing sablang atiu kea, at abe ne i Lot. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:2</lbl> 	At i Abram bina yang mabandi karing animal, king pilak, at king guintu. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:3</lbl> 	At melaus ya king keang lakad i Abram manibatan king mauli angga king Betel, angga king karinan a nung nu ya karin king minuna ing keang kubu, king pilatan na ning Betel at ning Hai, 	

Genesis <lbl>13:4</lbl> 	King karinan ning altar, a keang guewa king minuna: at i Abram inaus ne karin ing laguiu nang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:5</lbl> 	At makanian mu naman i Lot, a mine kayabe nang Abram, atin ya namang kawan a tupa, at kawan a vaca, at kubu. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:6</lbl> 	At ila e no aguiu ning gabun, a manuknangan lang miabe: uling binang dakal ing karelang pibandian, at e la malyaring manuknangan miabe. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:7</lbl> 	At mirinan lang pamisalangsangan ding pastul nang Abram at ding pastul nang Lot: at ing Cananeo at ing Pereceo menuknangan la kanita king labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>13:8</lbl> 	At i Abram sinabi na kang Lot, Ipakisabi ku keka, bang ekata miririnan pamisalangsangan, ika at aku, at ding pastul mu at ding pastul ku; uling mikapatad kata. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:9</lbl> 	E wari ing mabilug a labuad atiu king arapan mo? Aku pagamuamu ku keka, king kawani ka kaku: nung ika ume ka king kaili, aku ume ku king wanan, o nung ika ume ka king wanan, aku ume ku king kaili. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:10</lbl> 	At tinas no ding mata nang Lot, at abatiawan na ing mabilug nang Kapatagan ning Jordan, a pawang mayap paranuman king misusumangid, kanitang bayu na sinirang GUINU ing Sodoma at Gomorra, anti mo ing mulaan nang GUINU, anti mo ing gabun na ning Egipto a lulub Zoar. 

Genesis <lbl>13:11</lbl> 	Nung inya i Lot pinili na ing mabilug nang Kapatagan ning Jordan; at mine ya i Lot king aslagan: at mikawani lang adua. 

Genesis <lbl>13:12</lbl> 	I Abram menuknangan ya king gabun na ning Canaan, at i Lot menuknangan ya karing ciudad ning Kapatagan, at linipat ne ing keang kubu angga king Sodoma. 

Genesis <lbl>13:13</lbl> 	Ngeni ding tau Sodoma mangarawak la at makasalanan lang bina salang kang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:14</lbl> 	At i GUINU sinabi na kang Abram, kaibat nang kinawaning Lot kea, Itas mo ngeni ding kekang mata, at matio ka manibat keting kekang kabilian, nangan king paralaya at nangan king mauli at nangan king aslagan at nangan king albugan: 

Genesis <lbl>13:15</lbl> 	Uling ing mabilug a labuad a ababatiawan mu, ibie ku keka, at karing dai mu angga na king kapilan man. 

Genesis <lbl>13:16</lbl> 	At daptan ku king ing kekang bini maguing anti mo ing alikabuk king labuad: bang nung ninuman malyari nang abilang ing alikabuk ning labuad, malyari nala namang abilang ding kekang bini. 

Genesis <lbl>13:17</lbl> 	Talakad ka, lakaran mu ing gabun king kekaban na at king keang liwalas; uling iti ibie ku keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>13:18</lbl> 	At i Abram linipat ne pin ing keang kubu, at mine ya at menuknangan siping ding dutung a encina ning Mamre, a atilu king Hebron, at karin mitalakad yang altar kang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:1</lbl> 	At milyari king karing kayaldawan nang Amrafel a ari king Sinar, kang Ariok a ari king Elasar, kang Kedorlaomer a ari king Elam, at kang Tidal a ari ra ding Goiim, 

Genesis <lbl>14:2</lbl> 	A deti mekipamuk la laban kang Bera a ari king Sodoma, at laban, kang Birsa, a ari king Gomorra, kang Sinab a ari king Adma, at kang Semeber, a ari king Seboim, at king ari king Bela, (a iti i Zoar). 

Genesis <lbl>14:3</lbl> 	Deting sabla mitipun la king libis ning Sidim (a iti ing malat a dayat malat.) 

Genesis <lbl>14:4</lbl> 	Labingaduang banua ing pamaniuyu ra kang Kedorlaomer, at king kalabing atlung banua pesipanalangsang la. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:5</lbl> 	At king kalabingapat a banua dinatang ya i Kedorlaomer at ding aring kayabe na, at sigatan nala ding Refaim king Astarot-Karnaim, at ding Zucita king Ham, at ding Emita king Save-kiriataim. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:6</lbl> 	At ding Horeos king bunduk ning Seir, angga king El-Paran, a atiu king lele na ning ilang. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:7</lbl> 	At mibalik la, at dinatang la king Enmispat (a iti ing Cades,) at sigatan da ing mabilug dang labuad ding Amelecitas, at anti naman ding Amoreos, a manuknangan king Hasason-tamar. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:8 </lbl>	A linual ya ing ari king Sodoma, at ing ari king Gomorra, at ing ari king Adma, at ing ari king Zeboim, at ing ari king Bela, (a ya ing Zoar); at ila migayak lang pamakipamuk laban karela king libis ning Sidim; 	

Genesis <lbl>14:9</lbl> 	Laban kang Kedorlaomer a ari king Elam, at kang Tidal a ari ra ding Goiin, at kang Amrafel a ari king Sinar, at kang Ariok a ari king Elasar; apat a ari laban karing lima. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:10</lbl> 	Ngeni ing libis ning Sidim mitmu yang talagang burak; at pesitakas la ding ari king Sodoma at Gomorra, at mengabaldug la karin, at ding mitagan pesitakas la king kabundukan. 

Genesis <lbl>14:11</lbl> 	At kinua ra ing anggang pibandian ning Sodoma at Gomorra, at ing anggang pagkabie ra, at pesilako la. 

Genesis <lbl>14:12</lbl> 	At dela re i Lot, a anak na ning kapatad nang Abram, a manuknangan king Sodoma, at ing keang pibandian at meko la. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:13</lbl> 	Ngeni dinatang ya ing metung a mitakas, at belita ne kang Abram ing Hebreo: a ngeni manuknangan king siping ding encina ning Mamre, ing Amorreo, a kapatad nang Escol, at kapatad nang Aner; at deti kakampi nong Abram. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:14</lbl> 	At inyang dimdam nang Abram king ing keang kapatad mebijag ya, tiki na la ding sinane nang lalaki, a mibait king keang pibalebale, atlu langdalan at labingwalu, at tegal dala angga king Dan. 

Genesis <lbl>14:15</lbl> 	At mitapuk-tapuk la king bengi, ya at ding keang ipus, at sigatan dala, at tikian dala angga king Hoba, a atiu king kaili na ning Damasco. 

Genesis <lbl>14:16</lbl> 	At inuli na ing anggang pibandian, anti naman i Lot a kapatad na, at ing keang pibandian, anti naman ding babai at ing balayan. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:17</lbl> 	At linual ya ing ari Sodoma at segananne, kanitang mibabalik ne a ibat neng pete i Kedorlaomer at ding arian a kayabe na, king libis ning Save (a ya ing libis ning ari). 

Genesis <lbl>14:18</lbl> 	At i Melquisedec a ari Salem milual yang tinape at alak: at ya sacerdote ne ning Kakataskatasan a Dios. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:19</lbl> 	At pepanuanan ne, at sinabi na, Mipanuanan ya i Abram ning Kakataskatasan a Dios, a maki bandi king banua at labuad: 

Genesis <lbl>14:20</lbl> 	At nuan ya ing Kakataskatasan a Dios, a binie no king kekang gamat ding kekang ka salang. At dininan ne king kapulung dake ning keganagana. 

Genesis <lbl>14:21</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning ari king Sodoma kang Abram, Ibie mo kaku ding tau, at kuanan mung maguing keka ing pibandian. 	

Genesis <lbl>14:22</lbl> 	At mekibat ya i Abram king ari king Sodoma, Tinas ke ing kakung gamat kang GUINU, Dios a Kakataskatasan, a maki bandi king banua at labuad, 	

Genesis <lbl>14:23 </lbl>	King e ku kuma metung a kasinuldan ni metung mang panali ning tapakan ni king nanumang atiu keka, magkang sabian mu, Pepabandian ke i Abram: 

Genesis <lbl>14:24</lbl> 	Subali mu king pengan da ding kayanakan, at ing dake ra ding lalaking akayabe ku, i Aner, i Escol, at i Mamre; paburen lang pasikua king karelang dake. 	

Genesis <lbl>15:1</lbl> 	Kaibat da ding bague a deti dinatang ing amanu nang GUINU kang Abram king malikmata, sinabi na, E ka tatakut, Abram: aku ing kekang kalasag, at ing kekang ablas a binang maragul. 	

Genesis <lbl>15:2</lbl> 	At mekibat ya i Abram, Oh Guinung GUINU, nanung ibie mu kaku, akakit mung mabibie kung alang anak, at ing magmana king kakung bale, ining tau Damasco a i Eliezer? 

Genesis <lbl>15:3</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abram, Oini, e muku dininan bini: at, oini, metung yang penganak king kakung bale ing talapagmana ku. 

Genesis <lbl>15:4</lbl> 	At, kanita, ing amanu nang GUINU dinatang kea, a sinabi na, Iting tau e me maguing talapagmana; dapot ing lual king sarili mung atian ya ing maguing talapagmana mu. 

Genesis <lbl>15:5</lbl> 	At dela ne king kaliwalasan, at sinabi na, Lumawe ka ngeni banua, at bilangan mula ding batuin, nung abilang mula: at sinabi na kea, Makanian la naman ding maguing bini mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>15:6</lbl> 	At meniwala ya kang GUINU; at iti binilang nang katuliran kea. 

Genesis <lbl>15:7</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Aku i GUINU a kinanua keka king Ur a labuad da ding Caldeos, bang ibie ku keka ing labuad a iti a manan mu. 

Genesis <lbl>15:8</lbl> 	At ya mekibat ya, Oh Guinung GUINU makananu kung akilala king iti manan ku?

Genesis <lbl>15:13</lbl> 	At sinabi na kang Abram, Tune a pakatalastasan mu king ing kekang bini manaliwa yang balayan king labuad a e karela, at sumuyu la karing atiu karin: at pasakitan dong apat a dalan a banua:

Genesis <lbl>16:1</lbl> 	Ngeni i Sarai, a asawa nang Abram, e menganak kea: at ya atin yang metung a ipus a babai, a tau Egipto, a milaguiung Agar.

Genesis <lbl>16:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na ping Sarai kang Abram, Oini ngeni, i GUINU guewa na king baug ku; Pagamuamu ku keka, king lungub ka, king ipus kung babai; mekad mika anak ku king uli na. At pekiramdaman nang Abram ing siwala nang Sarai. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:3</lbl> 	At i Sarai, a asawa nang Abram, kinua ne i Agar a ipus nang babai, a tau Egipto, kaibat ning apulung banua a pamanuknangan nang Abram king gabun na ning Canaan, at binie ne kang Abram a asawa na baneng maguing asawa. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:4</lbl> 	At ya siniping ya kang Agar, at kinagli ya: at kanitang ikit na king kinagli ya, pepaalan neng ulaga ing keang guinung babai karing keang panimanman. 

Genesis <lbl>16:5</lbl> 	At i Sarai sinabi na kang Abram, Ing kakung pangaumis mitumpak keka: aku binie ke ing ipus kung babai king kandungan mu, at inyang akit nang kinagli ya, guewa nakung alang kabaldugan karing keang mata: i GUINU ya ing matul kanaku at keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:6</lbl> 	Dapot mekibat ya i Abram kang Sarai, Oyan, ing ipus mung babai atiu king gamat mu; daptan mu kea ing mayap king panimanman mu. At inumis neng Sarai, at tinakas ya king keang arapan. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:7</lbl> 	At ikit ne ning angel nang GUINU king siping ning metung a bukal ning danum king ilang, king siping ning bukal a atiu king dalan a mame king Shur. 

Genesis <lbl>16:8</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Agar, a ipus nang Sarai, nu ka ibat? at nu ka ume? At ya sinabi na, Tinakas ku king arapan nang Sarai a panginuan ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:9</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning angel nang GUINU, Mibalik ka king guinu mung babai, at isuku mu ing sarili mu lalam ding keang gamat. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:10</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning angel nang GUINU, Parakalan kong bina ding kekang bini, a e la mabilang king uli na ning keraklan da. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:11</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning angel nang GUINU, Oini, kinagli ka, at manganak kang metung a lalaki; at ing yaus mu king keang laguiu Ismael, uling pekiramdaman nang GUINU ing kekang pamagkasakit. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:12</lbl> 	At ya maguing asno yang bunduk king libutad da ding tau: ing keang gamat maguing salang ne ning balang tau, at ding gamat da ding tau salang la kea; at manuknangan yang salang king arapan da ding anggang kapatad na. 	

Genesis <lbl>16:13</lbl> 	At inaus ne ing laguiu nang GUINU a maniabi kea, Ika ing Dios a makakit: uling sinabi na, Linawe kea naman wari keti itang makakit kanako?

Genesis <lbl>17:1</lbl> 	At kanitang i Abram atin neng siamapulu at siam a banua tua, pepakit ya kang Abram i GUINU at sinabi na kea, Aku ing Dios a Mayupaya king Sabla: lumakad ka king arapan ku, at magpakasakdal ka. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:2</lbl> 	At gawan ku ing pangaku kaku at keka, parakalan dakang bina. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:3</lbl> 	At i Abram migsakab ya: at ing Dios miniabi ya kea, ngana.

Genesis <lbl>17:4</lbl> 	Tungkul kanaku, oini, ing kanakung tipan keka, at maguing ibpa raka ding dakal a bansa. 

Genesis <lbl>17:5</lbl> 	Ni e na mayaus Abram ing laguiu mu, nung e ing maguing laguiu mu Abraham; uling guewa rakang ibpa ra ding dakal a bansa. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:6</lbl> 	At parakalan dakang bina, at papanibatan ko keka ding anggang bansa at manibatan la keka ding ari. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:7</lbl> 	At italakad ku ing kakung tipan keka at karing kekang bini pangamate mu king mabilug dang dai a pangakung alang kapupusan, a aku maguing Dios muku, at ning kekang bini pangamate mu. 

Genesis <lbl>17:8</lbl> 	At ibie ku keka, at king kekang bini pangamate mu, ing gabun a tuknangan mu, ing mabilug nang gabun ning Canaan, a banding alang kapupusan; at aku ing maguing Dios da. 

Genesis <lbl>17:9</lbl> 	At sinabi ning Dios kang Abraham, At dikil keka, tuparan mu ing tipan ku, ika, at ding bini mu pangamate mu king karelang dai. 

Genesis <lbl>17:10</lbl> 	Iti ing kakung tipan, a tuparan yu, kaku at kekayu at king kekang bini pangamate mu: tulian ya ing balang lalaki kekayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:11</lbl> 	At patuli ko pin king laman ning kekang kasangkapan: at iti ya ing maguing tanda na ning tipan ku at kekayu. 

Genesis <lbl>17:12</lbl> 	At ing atin nang walung aldo matuli ya kekayu, ing balang lalaki king kekong dai, ing mibait king bale, o ing mesali king salapi ning ninumang tau king aliwang labuad a e king kekang bini.

Genesis <lbl>17:13</lbl> 	Karampatan yang matuli, ing mibait king kekang bale, at ing seli mu king kekang salapi: at ing kakung tipan, magbili king kekong laman, a pekatipan a alang angga. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:14</lbl> 	At ing lalaki a e tuli a e metuli ing laman ning keang kasangkapan, ing kaladua ita mikawani ya king keang balayan; lebagan na ing tipan ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:15</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning Dios kang Abraham, Dikil kang Sarai a asawa mu, e me ausan Sarai nung e Sara ing maguing laguiu na. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:16</lbl> 	At panuanan ke, at maiguit kaniti dinan dakang anak kea: wa, panuanan ke, at maguing indu re ding bansa; ding ari ding balayan manibatan la kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:17</lbl> 	Kanita i Abraham migsakab ya, at meili ya, at sinabi na king keang pusu, King taung dinalan nang banua mikaanak ya pa? at i Sara, siam neng pulung banua, manganak ya pa kaya? 	

Genesis <lbl>17:18</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abraham king Dios, Oh mananu na sang i Ismael mie ya king arapan mu! 

Genesis <lbl>17:19</lbl> 	At miniabi ya ing Dios, Tune, a katutuan i Sara a asawa mu manganak yang metung a lalaki; at ing yaus mu king laguiu na Isaac: at italakad ku ing kakung tipan a alang kapupusan kea karing bini na pangamate na. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:20</lbl> 	At tungkul kang Ismael, pekiramdaman daka: Oini, pepanunan ke, at papamungan ke, at parakalan keng binang dakal; mikaanak yang labing aduang principes, at gawan keng maragul a bansa. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:21</lbl> 	Dapot patibayan ku ing kakung tipan kang Isaac, a ipanganak nang Sara keka king panaun a iti ning banuang tutuki. 

Genesis <lbl>17:22</lbl> 	At pangayari nang mekisabi kea, minukiat ya ing Dios ibat kang Abraham. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:23</lbl> 	At i Abraham tiki ne i Ismael a anak na, at ding anggang mibait king keang bale, at ding anggang seli na karing keang salapi, ing balang lalaki karing lalaking abe na bale Abraham, at metuli ing laman ding kasangkapan da king aldo mu ring ita, anti ing sinabi na ning Dios kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>17:24</lbl> 	At i Abraham siam neng pulu at siam a banua tua, inyang matuli ing laman na ning keang kasangkapan.

Genesis <lbl>17:26</lbl> 	King aldo mu ring ita metuli ya i Abraham, at i Ismael a anak na. 

Genesis <lbl>17:27</lbl> 	At ding anggang lalaking kayabe na bale, ding mibait king keang bale, at ding mesali king salapi karing aliwang balayan, metuli lang kayabe na.

Genesis <lbl>18:3</lbl>	At sinabi na, Guinu ku, nung ngeni menakit kung kalam karing kekong mata, pagamuamu ku kekayu, king e ye lalabasan, ing kekong talasuyu:

Genesis <lbl>18:6</lbl>	At i Abraham mine yang mirarapal king kubu kang Sara, at sinabi na, Kuma kang agad atlung takal a mapinu ning arina, iyamas mu, at gawan mung mamun.

Genesis <lbl>18:20</lbl>	At i GUINU sinabi na, Anti ning ing kulisak na ning Sodoma at Gomorra binang sisikan, at uling ing kasalanan da binang mabayat;	

Genesis <lbl>18:21</lbl>	Kuldas ku ngeni, at lawan ku nung depatan dang lubus agpang king kulisak na, a miraras angga kanaku; at nung ali, kanakung abalu.

Genesis <lbl>18:22	</lbl>At meko la karin ding lalaki, at tinuru la Sodoma: dapot i Abraham makatalakad ya pa king arapan nang GUINU.	

Genesis <lbl>18:23	</lbl>At linapit ya i Abraham, at sinabi na, Lipulan mula naman ding banal a kayabe ra ding mangarawak?

Genesis <lbl>18:24</lbl>	Nung sakali ating limangpulung banal king kilub ning ciudad: gunawan mu wari at e mu pakawanan ing karinan alangalang karing limangpulung banal a atiu kilub na nite?	Peradventure

Genesis <lbl>18:25	</lbl>Marayu keka a daptan mu ing makanian, king ding banal patayan mulang kayabe ra ding mangarawak, king ding banal mianti la karing marawak; ita kapilan man e mu daptan: e wari ing Ukum ning mabilug a labuad ing katuliran ya ing daptan na?	

Genesis <lbl>18:26</lbl>	At i GUINU sinabi na, Nung makakit ku king Sodoma limangpulung banal king kilub ning ciudad, patawaran ku ing mabilug a karinan alangalang karela.	

Genesis <lbl>18:27</lbl>	At mekibat ya i Abraham at sinabi na, Oini ngeni, mengangas kung miniabi king kakung Guinu, king bistat alikabuk ku mu at abu:	

Genesis <lbl>18:28	</lbl>Nung sakali magkulang lang lima karing limangpulung banal: gunawan mu kaya ing mabilug a ciudad dikil karing limang kulang? At sinabi na, E ku gunawan, nung manakit kung apatapulu at lima.	Peradventure 

Genesis <lbl>18:29	</lbl>At ya pepasibayu yang miniabi kea, at ngana, Nung sakali ating mayakit a apatapulu. At sinabi na, E ku daptan alangalang karing apatapulu.

Genesis <lbl>18:30</lbl>	At sinabi na, Oh e ya sa mimua ing Guinu, at maniabi ku: nung sakali ating mayakit karin atlungpulu. At sinabi na, E ku daptan, nung manakit kung atlungpulu karin.	

Genesis <lbl>18:31</lbl>	At sinabi na, Oini ngeni, aku mengangas kung miniabi king Guinu: nung sakali karin ating aduangpulu. At sinabi na, e ku gunawan alangalang karing aduangpulu.	

Genesis <lbl>18:32</lbl>	At sinabi na, Oh e ya sa mimua ing Guinu, at maniabi na ku mung misan: nung sakali karin ating mayakit a apulu. At sinabi na, E ku gunawan alangalang karing apulu.
