  Genesis <lbl>19:1</lbl> 	At dinatang la pin ding aduang angeles king Sodoma king gatpanapun; at i Lot makalukluk ya king pasbul na ning Sodoma: at ikit nong Lot, at tinalakad ya a sinalubung karela; at ing lupa na diku ne king labuad; 

Genesis <lbl>19:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Oreni ngeni, ding kakung guinu, magbalik kayu, ipagamuamu ku kekayu, king lungub ko king bale na ning kekong talasuyu, at maglayunan kaniting kabukas, at manuas kong bitis, at pangamaranun mibangun kayu, at ibalaus yu ing kekong lakad. At ila sinabi ra, Ali; dapot king dalan ke manatili ngening benging iti. 

Genesis <lbl>19:3</lbl> 	At ya pinilit nong bina; at tinuki lang linub kea, at linub la king keang bale; at pigtawan nala, at linutu yang tinape alang levadura, at mengan la. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:4 </lbl>	Dapot bayu la pesipagkera, kilungan de ing bale, ding lalaki king ciudad, a lalaki king Sodoma, ing mabilug a balayan manibat king miayaliwang nayun, manibat karing kayanakan angga karing matua; 

Genesis <lbl>19:5</lbl> 	At inaus de i Lot, at sinabi ra kea, Nu la karin ding lalaki a dinatang keti keka ngening benging iti? ilual mo kekami, bami lang abalu. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:6</lbl> 	At i Lot liwalan nala king pasbul, at kebat ne ing pasbul king gugulatan na. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:7</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Pagamuamu ku kekayu, kapatad ku, king e yu daraptan ing anti kaniang marawak. 	
Genesis <lbl>19:8</lbl> 	Oini ngeni, aku atin kung aduang anak a babai a e ro kilala ding lalaki; paburen yuku, pagamuamu ku kekayu a ilual ko kekayu, at daptan yu karela ing mayap karing kekong panimanman: bukud mu karing lalaking deni a ala kong daraptan nanuman, anti ning atilu lalam nang lilung ning kakung bubungan. 

Genesis <lbl>19:9</lbl> 	At ila sinabi ra, Lisia ka kean. At sinabi ra, iti mine ya keti bang manaliwang balen, at bisa yang maguing ukum: ngeni daptanan dakang lalu pang marawak, maiguit karela. At bigla reng tinulak ing lalaki, i Lot, at pesilapit la bang siran de ing pasbul. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:10</lbl> 	Dapot ding lalaki inatyat do ding gamat da, at linub de i Lot king bale a kayabe ra, at kebat de ing pasbul. 

Genesis <lbl>19:11</lbl> 	At ding taung atiu king pasbul ning bale manibat king malati angga king maragul, binulag dala, nanupata mepagal lang manintun king pasbul. 	

Genesis 19:12 	At sinabi ra ding lalaki kang Lot, Atin ka pa nanuman kete? manuyang a lalaki at ding anak mung lalaki at anak mung babai, at ing ninumang atiu keka king ciudad, ilako mo king karinan a iti: 

Genesis <lbl>19:13</lbl> 	Uling gunawan mi ing karinan a iti, uling ing karelang kulisak minukiat king arapan nang GUINU; at i GUINU peparala nakami baming gunawan. 

Genesis <lbl>19:14</lbl> 	At i Lot linual ya, at sinabi na karing keang manuyang, a mengasawa karing keang anak a babai, at sinabi na, Talakad, lual ko king karinan a iti; uling i GUINU gunawan na ing ciudad a iti. Dapot inukul da ding keang manuyang anti yang mamiru. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:15</lbl> 	At inyang mabubuklat na ing abak, pemalaguanan de i Lot ding angeles, sinabi ra, Talakad ka, kuanan me ing asawa mu, at ding adua mung anak a babai a atiu keti, magkang pati ika matampus king dewakan ning ciudad. 

Genesis <lbl>19:16</lbl> 	Dapot magluatluat ya; at ding lalaki telanan de gamat, at ing gamat na ning keang asawa, at ding gamat da ding adua nang anak a babai, king pakalulu nang GUINU kea: at dela re, at binili re king lual na ning ciudad. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:17</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang adala na no lual, sinabi na, Itakas mu ing kekang bie; e ka babalikid king gugulutan mu, ni e ka tutuknang kaniting mabilug a kapatagan, tumukas ka angga king bunduk, a magkang matampus ka. 

Genesis <lbl>19:18</lbl> 	At i Lot sinabi na karela, Oh, e makanian, kanakung guinu:

Genesis <lbl>19:19</lbl> 	Oini ngeni, menakit yang kalam karing kekang mata ing kekong talasuyu, at peparagul mu ing kekang pakalulu, a pepatangal mu kanaku king pamagligtas mu king kakung bie; at aku e ku mitakas king bunduk, magkang dasnan naku ning marawak, at mate ku: 	

Genesis <lbl>19:20</lbl> 	Oini ngeni, ing ciudad a iti malapit ya bang karin ku tumakas, at malati ya. Oh itulut mung tumakas ku karin (e wari ita malati ya?) at mie ya ing kakung kaladua. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:21</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Lawan mu, tinggap daka naman tungkul kaniting bague, king e ku gunawan ing ciudad a sinabi mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:22</lbl> 	Magmalagua ka, tumakas ka karin; uling ala kung nanumang arapat anggang e ka miras karin. Uli na niti ing meaus king laguiu na ning ciudad a ita Zoar. 

Genesis <lbl>19:23</lbl> 	Ing aldo makaslag ne babo ning labuad kanitang i Lot miras ya king Zoar. 

Genesis <lbl>19:24</lbl> 	Kanita i GUINU pepauranan nang asupri at api ing Sodoma at Gomorra a menibatan kang GUINU ibat banua; 	

Genesis <lbl>19:25</lbl> 	At guinuno no detang ciudad, at ing mabilug a Kapatagan, at ding anggang manuknangan karing ciudad, at ing nanumang tinubu babo ning gabun. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:26 </lbl>	Dapot ing asawa na melikid ya king gugulatan na, at meguing asias yang asin. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:27</lbl> 	At mibangun yang maranun i Abraham panga-abak king karinan a ketalakaran na king arapan nang GUINU: 

Genesis <lbl>19:28</lbl> 	At linawe ya nangan king Sodoma at Gomorra, at king mabilug nang gabun ning kapatagan, at oini, at, oyan, ing asuk ning gabun minukiat anti mo ing asuk na ning metung a ornu. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:29</lbl> 	At milyari, king kanitang guinuno no ning Dios ding ciudad na ning kapatagan, aganaka ne ning Dios i Abraham, at tinubud ne i Lot ibat king libutad ning maguguno, kanitang gunawan no ding ciudad a penuknanganan nang Lot. 

Genesis <lbl>19:30</lbl> 	At i Lot minukiat ya ibat king Zoar, at tinuknang ya king bunduk, at ding adua nang anak a babai kayabe nala; anti ning tinakut yang manuknangan king Zoar: a tinuknang ya king metung a lukib, ya at ding adua nang anak a babai. 

Genesis <lbl>19:31</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning pangane king wali, Ing kekatang ibpa matua ya, at alang lalaki king labuad a lungub kekata agpang king ugali ning mabilug a labuad: 

Genesis <lbl>19:32</lbl> 	Ume ka keni, painuman teng alak ing kekatang ibpa, at sumiping katang kayabe na, bang aingat ta ing palipi ning kekatang ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:33</lbl> 	At pepainum deng alak i ibpa ra kanitang benging ita: at linub ya ing pangane, at siniping yang abe nang tata na; at e na balu ning ibpa inyang sumiping ya, ni aguiang inyang mibangun ya. 

Genesis <lbl>19:34</lbl> 	At milyari pangakabukasan, king sinabi na ning pangane king wali, Oini, aku siniping ku nabengi a kayabe nang ibpa ku: painuman taya namang alak ngening benging iti; at lungub ka, at sumiping kang abe na, batang aingat ing bini na ning kekatang ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:35</lbl> 	At pepainum daya namang alak i ibpa ra king benging ita: at tinalakad ya ing wali at siniping yang kayabe na; at e na balu iniang ya siniping ya, aguiang inyang mibangun ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:36</lbl> 	Makanian lang mika anak ding adua nang anak a babaing Lot king uli nang ibpa ra. 

Genesis <lbl>19:37</lbl> 	At ing pangane menganak yang metung a lalaki, at ing pemalaguiu na kea Moab: a iti ya ing ibpa ra ding Moabitas angga king aldo ngeni. 	

Genesis <lbl>19:38</lbl> 	At ing wali, menganak ya namang metung a lalaki, at ing pemalaguiu na kea Ben-ammi: a iti ya ing ibpa ra ding anak nang Ammon angga king aldo ngeni. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:1</lbl> 	At menibatan karin miglakbe ya i Abraham a nangan king gabun ning Mauli, at menuknangan ya king pilatan na ning Cades at Shur; at ya menaliwang balen king Gerar. 

Genesis <lbl>20:2</lbl> 	At miniabi ya i Abraham tungkul kang Sara a asawa na, Ya kaku yang kapatad: at i Abimelek a ari king Gerar mitubud ya, at kinua ne i Sara. 

Genesis <lbl>20:3</lbl> 	Dapot ing Dios mine ya kang Abimelek king panaguimpan king bengi, at sinabi na kea, Oini, ika kabud ka metung a taung mete, king uli na ning babaing kekang kinua; uling ya asawa ne ning metung a lalaki. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:4</lbl> 	Ngeni i Abimelek e ya linapit kea: at sinabi na, Guinu, patayan mu wari pati ing metung a banal a bansa? 

Genesis <lbl>20:5</lbl> 	E wari ya naman ing sinabi kanaku, Kapatad ke? at ya, aguiang ing sarili na sinabi na, Kapatad ke: king katapatan ning pusu ku at king kayalan dang malit ding gamat ku depatan ku iti. 

Genesis <lbl>20:6</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning Dios king panaguimpan, Wa, atatalastas ku a king katapatan na ning kekang pusu depatan mu iti, at kinawat daka naman king pamikasalang laban kanaku: inya pin e ku pepaintulut a tagkilan me. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:7</lbl> 	Ngeni pin, isubli me ing asawa na ning lalaki; uling manula ya, at ika panalangin naka, at mie ka: at nung e me isubli, bitasan mung alang sala mate ka, ika, at pati ing sablang atiu keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:8</lbl> 	At i Abimelek mibangun yang maranun pangaabak, at inaus no ngan ding keang ipus, at sinabi na ing anggang bague iti king daramdaman da: at ding tau mitakutan lang bina.

Genesis <lbl>20:9</lbl> 	Kanita inaus neng Abimelek i Abraham, at sinabi na kea, Nanu ing depatan mu kekami? at makananu kung mikasala keka, a dela mu kanaku at king kakung kayarian ing binang maragul a kasalanan? depatan mu kanaku ing dapat a e sukat marapat. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:10</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abimelek kang Abraham, Nanung akakit mu, king depatan mu iting bague? 

Genesis <lbl>20:11</lbl> 	At i Abraham mekibat ya, Uling iniisip ku, Tune a alang takut king Dios ing karinan a iti; at patayan daku king uli na ning asawa ku. 

Genesis <lbl>20:12</lbl> 	At ing katutuan naman kapatad ke, anak neng ibpa ku, dapot e ne anak indu ku; at meguing asawa ke: 	

Genesis <lbl>20:13</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang pepalakuan naku ning Dios king bale nang ibpa ku, sinabi ku kea. Iti ya ing pilubluban mung mayap a apakit mu kaku: king balang karinan a kekatang dasnan, sabian mu tungkul kanaku, Kapatad ke. 

Genesis <lbl>20:14</lbl> 	At i Abimelek kinanua yang tupa at baka, at ipus a lalaki at ipus a babai, at binie no kang Abraham, at sibli ne i Sarang asawa na. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:15</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abimelek, Oini, ing kakung gabun atiu king arapan mu: manuknangan ka nung nukarin ing mamayapan mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>20:16</lbl> 	At kang Sara sinabi na, Oini, dininan keng libu kapising pilak ing kapatad mu: lawan mu, iti takap ya keka king mata ra ding anggang kayabe mu; at king arapan ding sabla ika mika puri ka. 	
Genesis <lbl>20:17</lbl> 	At i Abraham menalangin ya king Dios: at pepakayap ne ning Dios i Abimelek, at ing keang asawa, at ding ipus nang babai; at ila menganak la. 	
Genesis <lbl>20:18 </lbl>	Uling kebat nong GUINU ding anggang palanakan da ding king bale nang Abimelek, king uli nang Sara, a asawa nang Abraham. 	

 Genesis <lbl>21:1</lbl> 	At dinalo ya i GUINU kang Sara anti mo ing sinabi na, at depatan nang GUINU kang Sara anti mo ing keang sinabi. 

Genesis <lbl>21:2</lbl> 	At kinagli ya i Sara, at menganak ya kang Abraham metung a anak a lalaki king keang ketuan, king panaun a sinabi na kea ning Dios. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:3</lbl> 	At Isaac ing inaus nang Abraham king laguiu na ning keang anak a penganak kea, a beit nang Sara. 

Genesis <lbl>21:4</lbl> 	At tilian neng Abraham i Isaac a anak na inyang walu neng aldo tua, anti mo ing inutus na kea ning Dios. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:5</lbl> 	At i Abraham dinalan neng banua tua, kanitang penganak ne kea i Isaac a anak na. 

Genesis <lbl>21:6</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Sara, ing Dios pepakailian naku: ninu mang makaramdam maili yang kayabe ku. 

Genesis <lbl>21:7</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Ninung maniabi kang Abraham, king i Sara pasusu yang anak? uling menganak ku keang metung a lalaki king keang ketuan. 

Genesis <lbl>21:8</lbl> 	At dinagul ya ing anak, at miawat ya king susu: at i Abraham migtau yang maragul king aldo a miawat ya king susu i Isaac. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:9</lbl> 	At ikit neng Sara ing anak nang Agar a tau Egipto a penganak na kang Abraham, a misusunu kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:10</lbl> 	Inya sinabi na kang Abraham, Palakuan me ing ipus a iti at ing keang anak: uling e ya magmana ing anak na ning ipus a iti a kayabe na ning anak ku, aguiang kayabe nang Isaac. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:11</lbl> 	At ing bague iti meguing mabayat a bina king panlalawe nang Abraham king uli na ning anak na. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:12</lbl> 	At ing Dios sinabi na kang Abraham, E mu pagmabayatan king kekang panlalawe ing tungkul king anak, at ing tungkul king kekang ipus a babai: king anggang sabian na kekang Sara, pakiramdaman mu ing siwala na; uling kang Isaac karin mayaus ing kekang bini. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:13</lbl> 	At anti naman king anak na ning ipus a babai gawa kung metung a bansa, uling bini me. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:14</lbl> 	At i Abraham mibangun yang maranun pangaabak, at kinanua yang tinape at metung a boting danum, at binie na kang Agar, pepapusan na king keang pago, at binie ne kea ing anak, at pepalakuan ne: at meko ya, at luyunluyun ya king ilang na ning Beer-seba. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:15</lbl> 	At mimin ing danum king boti, at inugse ne ing anak king lalam ning metung a mababang tanaman. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:16</lbl> 	At meko ya, at migluklukan ya king tulid na, a ing dayu na anti mo ing metung a bugnus king pana: uling sinabi na, E mu paintulut a akit ku ing kamatayan ning anak. 

Genesis <lbl>21:17</lbl> 	At dimdam na ning Dios ing siwala na ning anak; at ing angel na ning Dios inaus ne i Agar menibat banua, at sinabi na kea, Ninanu ka, Agar? E ka tatakut; uling ing Dios dimdam na ing siwala na ning anak king keang pangabili. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:18</lbl> 	Talakad ka, ibuat me ing anak, at sakluluan me karing gamat mu; uling ya gawan keng metung a maragul a bansa. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:19</lbl> 	At ing Dios biklat no ding mata na, at mekakit yang metung a talaga ning danum; at mine ya, at kitmuan ne ing boti king danum, at pepainum ne ing anak. 

Genesis <lbl>21:20</lbl> 	At ing Dios minantabe ya king anak, at dinagul ya; at menuknangan ya king ilang at meguing, kabang ya daragul ya, metung a mamana. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:21</lbl> 	At menuknangan ya king ilang na ning Paran: at i indu na kinua neng asawa na ibat king labuad na ning Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>21:22</lbl> 	At milyari kanita mu ring panaun ita, a miniabi ya kang Abraham i Abimelek, at i Fikol a pekapun na ning keang ejercito, ngana, Ing Dios atiu keka king nanumang daraptan mu: 	

Genesis <lbl>21:23</lbl> 	Ngeni pin isumpa mu kaku keti alangalang king Dios a e ka magtaksil kanaku, aguiang king kakung anak, aguiang karing anak da ding kakung anak: nung e agpang king mayubung pilubluban a depatan ku keka, makanian ing daptan mu kanaku, at king labuad a panaliwan mung balayan. 

Genesis<lbl> 21:24</lbl> 	At mekibat ya i Abraham, Susumpa ku.

Genesis <lbl>22:1</lbl> 	At milyari kaibat na ning bague a iti, pigsubukan ne ning Dios i Abraham, at sinabi na kea, Abraham; at ya sinabi na, Ati ku keni. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Kuanan me ngeni ing anak mu, ing bugtung mung anak, a Isaac, a pakamalan mu, at ume ka king gabun na ning Moria; at idaun me karin anting ain a durulukan babo ning metung karing bunduk a sabian ku keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:3</lbl> 	At i Abraham mibangun yang maranun pangaabak, at dininan neng sia ing keang asno, at mituki yang adua karing keang kayanakan a lalaki at i Isaac a keang anak; at kinutud yang dutung dikil king ain a durulukan, at tinalakad ya, at mine ya king karinan a sinabi na kea ning Dios. 

Genesis <lbl>22:4</lbl> 	King katlung aldo tinas nong Abraham ding mata na, at ikit na ing karinan king marayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:5</lbl> 	At i Abraham sinabi na karing keang kayanakan a lalaki, Manaya ko keti pati na ing asno, at aku at ing anak ume ke karin; at samba kami, at balikan dakayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:6</lbl> 	At kinua neng Abraham ing dutung king ain a durulukan, at pepapusan ne kang Isaac a anak na; at ya dela na king keang gamat ing api at ing sundang; at linakad lang miabe ding adua. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:7</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Isaac kang Abraham a ibpa na, at ngana, Ibpa ku: at ya sinabi na, Ati ku keni, anak ku. At ya sinabi na, Oini, ing api at ing dutung: dapot nuya karin ing biserung tupa dikil king ain a durulukan? 

Genesis <lbl>22:8</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abraham, Ing Dios isadia ne ing biserung tupa dikil king ain a durulukan, anak ku: inya ila melaus lang adua. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:9</lbl> 	At miras la king karinan a sinabi na kea ning Dios; at i Abraham telakad ne karin ing altar, at selese na ing dutung, at guinapus ne i Isaac a keang anak, at binili ne king babo ning altar, babo na ning dutung. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:10</lbl> 	At inatyat neng Abraham ing gamat na, at kinua ne ing sundang baneng paten ing anak na.

Genesis <lbl>22:13</lbl> 	At tinas nong Abraham ding mata na, at linawe ya, at, oini, ing metung a tupang lalaki king keang gugulatan makasilu la king laput ding keang sagu: at mine ya i Abraham at kinua ne ing tupang lalaki, at dinaun neng ain a durulukan a kalili na ning keang anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>22:14</lbl> 	At ing inaus nang Abraham king laguiu na ning karinan a ita GUINU-JIREH: anti mo ing kasebian angga king aldo ngeni, King bunduk nang GUINU misadia ya.

Genesis <lbl>22:18</lbl> 	At king kekang bini mipanuanan la ding anggang bansa keti king labuad; uling pemintuan mu ing siwala ku.

Genesis <lbl>23:7</lbl> 	At i Abraham tinalakad ya, at dinuku ya king balayan ning labuad, karing anak nang Het. 	

Genesis <lbl>23:8</lbl> 	At miniabi ya karela, ngana, Nung atin kong pilubluban a ikutkut ke ing mete ku bang mipanpan king panimanman ku, pakiramdaman yuku, at mamilatan ko kanaku kang Efron, a anak nang Zoar, 	

Genesis <lbl>23:9</lbl> 	Baneng ibie kanaku ing lukib na ning Macpela, a pibandian na, a atiu king angganan na ning keang marangle; king ganap a alaga ibie ne kanaku bang maguing pibandian a pikutkutan king libutad yu. 

Genesis <lbl>23:10</lbl> 	Ngeni i Efron makalukluk yang kayabe ra ding anak nang Het: at mekibat ya i Efron a Heteo kang Abraham king kapulungan da ding anak nang Het, karing anggang linub king pasbul na ning keang ciudad, sinabi na, 	

Genesis <lbl>23:11</lbl> 	Ali, guinu ku, pakiramdaman muku: ibabie ke keka ing marangle, at ing lukib a atiu karin, ibabie kea naman keka: king arapan da ding anak na ning kanakung balayan ibabie ku keka: ikutkut me ing kekang mete. 

Genesis <lbl>23:12</lbl> 	At i Abraham dinuku ya king arapan na ning balayan king labuad a ita.

Genesis <lbl>23:13</lbl> 	At miniabi ya kang Efron king kapulungan na ning balayan niting labuad, ngana, Dapot ipagamuamu ku keka, nung bisa ka, pakiramdaman muku: aku ibie ku ing alaga ning marangle; tanggapan mo kanaku, at ikutkut ke karin ing kakung mete. 	

Genesis <lbl>23:14</lbl> 	At mekibat ya i Efron kang Abraham, ngana kea, 	

Genesis <lbl>23:15</lbl> 	Guinu ku, pakiramdaman muku: ing alaga na ning kapirasung gabun apat a dalan a siclong pilak, nuno anti reti kaku at keka? ikutkut me pin ing kekang mete. 	

Genesis <lbl>23:16</lbl> 	At pekiramdaman neng Abraham i Efron; at tinimbang nong Abraham kang Efron ding salaping sinabi na king arapan da ding anak nang Het, apat a dalan a siclong pilak, piugalian dang salapi ding mangalakal. 	

Genesis <lbl>23:17</lbl> 	Inya ing marangle nang Efron, a atiu king Macpela, a atiu king tulid ning Mamre, ing marangle, at ing lukib a atiu karin, at ding sablang dutung a atiu king marangle, ding atiu king mabilug nang angganan king makapatulug, tinibe na 

Genesis <lbl>23:18</lbl> 	Kang Abraham ing pangabandi king arapan da ding anak nang Het, king arapan da ding anggang linub king pasbul ning keang ciudad. 	

Genesis <lbl>23:19</lbl> 	At kaibat na niti, kitkut neng Abraham i Sarang asawa na king lukib na ning marangle ning Macpela king tulid ning Mamre (ya ing Ebron), king gabun na ning Canaan. 	

Genesis <lbl>23:20</lbl> 	At ing marangle at ing lukib a atiu karin, tinibe ra kang Abraham ding anak nang Het, pibandian a kutkutan na. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:1</lbl> 	At i Abraham matua ne, at lipas ne king panaun: at pepanuanan neng GUINU i Abraham king sablang bague. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:2</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abraham king keang ipus, ing peka-matua king keang bale, a manibala king sablang kayatinan na, Ibili me, pagamuamu ku keka, ing kekang gamat king lalam na ning kakung puad. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:3</lbl> 	At pasumpan daka king uli nang GUINU, ing Dios ning banua at ing Dios ning labuad, a e me kakuang asawa ing kakung anak karing anak da ding Cananeos, a kayabe kung makapanuknangan keti: 	

Genesis <lbl>24:4</lbl> 	Dapot ume ka king kakung balen, at karing kakung kamaganakan, at ikua meng asawa ing anak kung Isaac. 

Genesis <lbl>24:5</lbl> 	At ing ipus mekibat ya kea, Nung sakali ing babai e ya mabisang tuki kanaku king labuad a iti: ibalik ke ping pasibayu ing anak mu king gabun a ibatan mo? 	

Genesis <lbl>24:6</lbl> 	At i Abraham sinabi na kea, Ingatan mung e ya mibalik ing anak ku karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:7</lbl> 	I GUINU, ing Dios ning banua, a kinanua kaku king bale na ning kakung ibpa, at king gabun a kakung tibuan, a miniabi kaku, a sinumpa kaku, ngana, King kekang dai ibie ku ing gabun a iti; ya itubud ne ing keang angel a mumuna keka, at ikua meng asawa na karin ing anak ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:8</lbl> 	At nung ing babai e ya bisang tuki keka, kanita mitimawa ka kaniting sumpa ku; bukud mu king ing anak ku e me pabalikan karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:9</lbl> 	At ing ipus binili ne ing gamat na king lalam nang puad Abraham a guinu na, at sinumpa ya kea tungkul king bague a iti. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:10</lbl> 	At ing ipus kinanua yang apulung camello, karing camello na ning keang guinu, at meko ya, daralan na ing peka-mayap king pibandian na ning keang guinu: at tinalakad ya, at mine ya king Mesapotamia, king ciudad nang Nacor. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:11</lbl> 	At pepasiklauran nala ding camello king lual ning ciudad siping ning talaga ning danum king gatpanapun, king oras a lulual lang sasaklung danum ding babai. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:12</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Oh GUINU, a Dios na ning guinu kung i Abraham, ipagamuamu ku keka, a paralan mukung mayap a kapalaran king aldo iti, at pakit kang ganaka king guinu kung i Abraham.

Genesis <lbl>24:13</lbl> 	Oini, ati ku makatalakad king siping ning bukal ning danum; at ding anak dang babai ding tau king ciudad a iti lulual lang sasaklung danum: 

Genesis <lbl>24:14</lbl> 	At mapalyari sa, king ing dalaga a nung kenu ku sabian, Ikuldas me ing banga mu, pagamuamu ku keka, bakung minum; at ya sabian na sa, Minum ka, at painuman kula naman ding kekang camello: iti na sa ya ing mitalaga king kekang talasuyung i Isaac; at king uli na niti akilala ku king depatan mu ing ganaka mu king kanakung guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:15</lbl> 	At milyari, bayu mepupus ing keang pamangamanu, king, oini, dinatang ya i Rebeca a mibait kang Betuel a anak nang Milca, a asawa nang Nacor, a kapatad nang Abraham, pupusanan ne ing keang banga king keang pago. 

Genesis <lbl>24:16</lbl> 	At ing dalaga bina yang malagung lalawan, metung yang dalagang alang bakas, ni alang lalaking mekakilala pa kea: a ya dinulung ya king bukal, at kitmuan ne ing keang banga at sinaka ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:17</lbl> 	At ing ipus milai yang sinagana kea, at sinabi na, Pagamuamu ku keka, painuman mukung ditak king danum na ning banga mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:18</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Minum ka, guinu ku: at mirapal ya, at kildas ne ing banga na king keang gamat, at pepainuman ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:19</lbl> 	At inyang kaibat na neng pepainum, sinabi na, Isaklu kula naman ding kekang camello, angga king mayari la ngang minum. 

Genesis <lbl>24:20</lbl> 	At migmalagawa ya, at bilus ne ing keang banga king pipainuman, at milaing pasibayu king talaga bang saklu, at sinaklu ya dikil karing anggang camello na. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:21</lbl> 	At ing tau linawe neng maratna, at ala yang bulad, banang abalu nung i GUINU pepagwaguian na ing keang lakad o ali na. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:22</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang meari nong mininum ding camello, king ing lalaki kinanua yang metung a singsing a guintu a timbang kapitnang siclo, at aduang pulcera a isulud karing keang gamat a timbang apulung siclong guintu, 

Genesis <lbl>24:23</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Kaninu ka anak? Pagamuamu ku keka, sabian mu kanaku. Atin keng silid king bale nang ibpa mu a apaglayunanan? 

Genesis <lbl>24:24</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na kea, Anak nakung Betuel a anak nang Milca, a iti ayanak ne kang Nacor. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:25</lbl> 	At sinabi na pa kea, Makanian mu naman atin keng are at dakal a pamangan, at karinan a paglayunanan. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:26</lbl> 	At ing lalaki diku ne ing buntuk na, at sinamba ya kang GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>24:27</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Purian ya i GUINU, ing Dios na ning kakung guinung i Abraham, a e na kewani ing keang pakalulu at ing keang pamagtapat king kakung guinu: anti mo aku, pitnubayan nakung GUINU king dalan angga king bale ra ding kapatad na ning guinu ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:28</lbl> 	At ing dalaga milai ya, at pepabalu na karing katubale nang indu na agpang kareting amanu.

Genesis <lbl>24:29</lbl> 	At Rebeca atin yang metung a kapatad a lalaki, a milaguiung Laban: at i Laban milai ya lual a mine king lalaki, king bukal. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:30</lbl> 	At milyari, pamanakit na king singsing, at karing pulcera a atiu karing gamat na ning keang kapatad, at pamanamdam na king amanu nang Rebeca a kapatad na, a sinabing, Makanian nang selita kanaku ning lalaki; king mine ya king lalaki; at, oini, makatalakad ya king siping da ding camello, king lele ning bukal. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:31</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Ume ka keni, pepanuanan nang GUINU; baket makatalakad ka kean lual? uling aku sidia ke ing bale, at ing pagkarinan da ding camello. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:32</lbl> 	At ing lalaki mine ya king bale, at kelag no ding camello; at dininan nong are at pamangan ding camello, at danum a penuas na karing keang bitis, at karing bitis da ding taung kayabe na.

Genesis <lbl>24:33</lbl> 	At inapag da king arapan na ing pamangan: dapot ya sinabi na, E ku mangan, anggang e ku asabi ing tubud kanaku. At ya sinabi na, Sabian mu.

Genesis <lbl>24:34</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Aku ipus nakung Abraham. 

Genesis <lbl>24:35</lbl> 	At i GUINU pepanuanan neng bina ing guinu ku; at ya peparagul ne: at dininan neng kawan a tupa at kawan a baka, at pilak at guintu, at ipus a lalaki at ipus a babai, at camello at asno. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:36</lbl> 	At i Sara a asawa ning guinu ku menganak ya king keang ketuan metung a lalaki king kanakung guinu: a ya ing dininan na king anggang pibandian na. 

Genesis <lbl>24:37</lbl> 	At pepasumpan naku ning kanakung guinu, sinabi na, E me kakuang asawa ing anak ku karing anak dang babai ding Cananeos, king gabun a panuknanganan ku: 	

Genesis <lbl>24:38</lbl> 	Dapot ume ka king bale nang ibpa ku, at kakung kamaganakan, at ikua meng asawa na ing anak ku. 

Genesis <lbl>24:39</lbl> 	At aku sinabi ku king kakung guinu, Nung sakali ing babai e ya mabisang tuki kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:40</lbl> 	At sinabi na kanaku, i GUINU, a king keang arapan lalakad ku, itubud ne keka ing keang angel, at ipala na ing kekang lakad; at ikua meng asawa na ing anak ku karing kakung kamaganakan, at king bale nang ibpa ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:41</lbl> 	Kanita mitimawa ka king kanakung sumpa, pangaras mu karing kakung kamaganakan; at nung e re ibie keka mitimawa ka king kanakung sumpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:42</lbl> 	At dinatang ku pin ngening aldo a iti king bukal, at sinabi ku, Oh GUINU a Dios na ning kanakung guinung i Abraham, nung siplala mu ngeni ing kanakung lakad a lalakad ku: 

Genesis <lbl>24:43</lbl> 	Oini, ati ku makatalakad king siping ning bukal ning danum; at mapalayari na sa king ing dalagang lual saklung danum, a kanakung sabianan, Ipagamuamu ku keka, dinan mu kung ditak a danum king kekang banga; 

Genesis <lbl>24:44</lbl> 	At sabian na kanaku, Minum ka, at isaklu ku la naman ding kekang camello: iti na sa ing babai a italaga nang GUINU king anak na ning kanakung guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:45</lbl> 	At bayu ku ayaring sinabi king kakung pusu, oini, i Rebeca lulual yang pupusanan ne ing keang banga; at kinuldas ya king bukal, at sinaklu ya: at sinabi ku kea, Pagamuamu ku keka painuman muku. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:46</lbl> 	At migmalagua ya, at kildas ne ing banga na king keang pago, at sinabi na, Minum ka, at ding camello mu painuman kula naman: inya minum ku, at pepainuman nala naman ding camello. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:47</lbl> 	At kitnan ke, at sinabi ku, Kaninu ka anak? At ya sinabi na, Anak nakung Betuel, a anak nang Nacor, a penganak na kang Milca: at binili ke ing metung a singsing king keang arung at ding pulcera karing keang gamat. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:48</lbl> 	At diku ke ing bunduk ku, at sinamba ku kang GUINU, at pinuri ke i GUINU, ing Dios na ning kakung guinung i Abraham, a minantabe kanaku king dalan a matulid bakeng kuanan ing anak nang babai ning kapatad na ning guinu ku a maguing asawa na ning keang anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:49</lbl> 	At ngeni nung ikayu dapat kong ganaka at katapatan king kanakung guinu, sabian yu kanaku: at kung ali, sabian yu kanaku; banakung magpildis king wanan, o king kaili. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:50</lbl> 	Kanita i Laban at i Betuel mekibat la at sinabi ra, Kang GUINU menibat iti: ikami e ke makasabi keka king marawak o king mayap. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:51</lbl> 	Oini, i Rebeca atiu king arapan mu, kuanan me, at mako ka, at maguing asawa ne ning anak na ning guinu mu. 

Genesis <lbl>24:52</lbl> 	At milyari, king, inyang damdaman na ning ipus nang Abraham ing karelang amanu, migsakab ya king labuad king arapan nang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:53</lbl> 	At ing ipus migdala yang iyas a pilak at iyas a guintu, at imalan, at binie na kang Rebeca: makanian mu naman dininan neng maulagang bague ing kapatad nang lalaki at i indu na. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:54</lbl> 	At mengan la at mininum, ya at ding lalaking kayabe na, at menatili lang kebukas; at pesibangun la pangaabak, at keang sinabi, Tuburan yuku king kakung guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:55</lbl> 	At miniabi ya ing kapatad na at i indu na, Paburen mung manuknangan ya pamu ing dalaga kekami maapulung aldo; at kaibat ume ya karin. 

Genesis <lbl>24:56</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na karela, E yuku babalam, anti ning i GUINU pinala na ing lakad ku; itubud yu na ku banakung ume king kakung guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:57</lbl> 	At ila sinabi ra, Ausan miya ing dalaga, at kutnan miya. 	

Genesis 24:58 	At inaus de i Rebeca, at sinabi ra kea, Tuki ka king lalaking ine? At ya mekibat ya, tuki ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:59</lbl> 	At pepaburean da neng tinuki i Rebeca a kapatad da, at ing babaing meningat kea, at ing ipus nang Abraham, at ding keang tau. 

Genesis <lbl>24:60</lbl> 	At pepanuanan de i Rebeca, at sinabi ra kea, Kapatad mi, maguing indu raka ding libulibu, at akamtan na ning kekang bini ing pasbul da ding keang salang. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:61</lbl> 	At i Rebeca tinalakad ya, at ding keang dalaga, at sinake la karing camello, at tinuki la king lalaki: at ing ipus dela ne i Rebeca, at meko la. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:62</lbl> 	At i Isaac menibatan ya king dalan a Beer-lahai-roi; uling tutuknang ya king gabun king Mauli. 

Genesis <lbl>24:63</lbl> 	At i Isaac linual ya king marangle bang manalangin king oras na ning gatpanapun: at inatna no ding mata na, at ikit na, at, oini, ating camellong daratang. 

Genesis <lbl>24:64</lbl> 	At i Rebeca inatna na no man ding mata na, at inyang ikit ne i Isaac, inuldas ya king camello. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:65</lbl> 	At sinabi na king ipus, Ninu iting lalaking lalakad king marangle a sasagana kekatamu? At ing ipus sinabi na, Iti ing guinu ku: at kinua ne ing keang talikbung, at migtalikbung ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:66</lbl> 	At ing ipus selese na kang Isaac ing keganaganang bague a depatan na. 	

Genesis <lbl>24:67</lbl> 	At dela neng Isaac king kubu nang indu na a i Sara, at kinua ne i Rebeca, at meguing asawa ne; at liguran ne: at mipatulan ya i Isaac pangamate nang indu na. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:1</lbl> 	At i Abraham mekiasawa yang aliwa, at ing laguiu na Ketura. 

Genesis <lbl>25:2</lbl> 	At penganak ne kea i Zimram, at i Joksan, at i Medan, at i Midian, at i Isbak, at i Suah. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:3</lbl> 	At i Joksan ayanak ne i Seba, at i Dedan. At ding anak nang Dedan ila ri Asurim, at Letusim, at Leumin. 

Genesis <lbl>25:4</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Midiam; i Efa, at i Efer, at i Hanoc, at i Abida, at i Eldaa. At deti ila ding anak nang Ketura. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:5</lbl> 	At i Abraham binie na ngan ing anggang kayatinan na kang Isaac. 

Genesis <lbl>25:6</lbl> 	Dapot karing anak na karing babai nang Abraham, dininan nong pagkalub Abraham; at mabie ya pa, pepalakuan na no kang Isaac a anak na, nangan king aslagan, king karinan king aslagan. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:7</lbl> 	At deti ilang meguing aldo na ning keang kabiayan king bie nang Abraham, dinalan pitungpulu at limang banua. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:8</lbl> 	At mepatad ing inawa nang Abraham, at mete ya king ganap a tua, metung a matuang lalaki, at mitmu karing banua, at miagum ya king keang balayan. 

Genesis <lbl>25:9</lbl> 	At kitkut de di Isaac ilang Ismael a anak na king lukib na ning Macpela, king marangle nang Efron a anak nang Zoar a Heteo, a atiu king tulid ning Mamre; 	

Genesis <lbl>25:10</lbl> 	Ing marangle a seli nang Abraham karing anak nang Het: karin ya mikutkut i Abraham, at i Sarang keang asawa. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:11</lbl> 	At milyari kaibat ning pangamate nang Abraham, a pepanuanan ne ning Dios i Isaac a anak na: at menuknangan ya i Isaac king siping ning Beer-lahai-roi. 

Genesis <lbl>25:12</lbl> 	Ngeni deti ila ding dai nang Ismael, a anak nang Abraham, a penganak nang Agar a tau Egipto, a ipus nang Sara: 	

Genesis <lbl>25:13</lbl> 	At deti pin ding laguiu ra ding anak nang Ismael, agpang king karelang laguiu, agpang king karelang dai: ing pangane nang Ismael, i Nabayot; at i Kedar, at i Adbeel, at i Mibsam, 

Genesis <lbl>25:14</lbl> 	At i Misma, at i Duma, at i Massa, 

Genesis <lbl>25:15</lbl> 	I Hadad, at i Tema, i Jetur, i Nafis, at i Kedema: 

Genesis <lbl>25:16</lbl> 	Deti ila ding anak nang Ismael, at deti ding laguiu ra, agpang karing karelang nayun at agpang karing karelang pipagsantungan; labingaduang principes agpang karing karelang bansa. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:17</lbl> 	At deti ilang meguing banua na ning bie nang Ismael, dinalan at atlungpulu at pitung banua: at mepatad ing inawa na at mete ya, at miagum ya king keang balayan. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:18</lbl> 	At menuknangan la manibatan king Havila angga king Shur a atiu king tulid ning Egipto, nung mame ka nangan Asiria: manuknangan ya king tulid da ding keang kapatad. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:19</lbl> 	At deti ila ding dai nang Isaac, a anak nang Abraham: i Abraham ayanak ne i Isaac: 	

Genesis <lbl>25:20</lbl> 	At i Isaac apat neng pulung banua inyang kinua ne i Rebeca, a anak nang Betuel a tau Siria king Padan-aram, a kapatad nang babaing Laban a tau king Siria, ban maguing asawa na.

Genesis <lbl>25:21</lbl> 	At menalangin ya i Isaac kang GUINU tungkul king keang asawa, uling baug ya: at pekiramdaman neng GUINU, at kinagli ya i Rebecang asawa na. 

Genesis <lbl>25:22</lbl> 	At mipapate la ding anak a atiu kilub na; at sinabi na, Nung makanian, baket mabibie ku pa? At mine ya ban ikutang na kang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:23</lbl> 	At sinabi nang GUINU kea, Adua lang bansa ding atiu king kekang atian, At adua lang balayan ding pikawanian a manibatan king kekang kilub: At ing metung a balayan maguing labis ya sikanan king metung a balayan; At ing matua sumuyu ya king wali. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:24</lbl> 	At inyang matupad ing aldo na ning keang pamanganak, oreni, kambal la ding king keang atian. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:25</lbl> 	At ing minuna mibait yang malutu, ing mabilug nang katawan anti yang imalan a maki bulbul; at ing inaus da king keang laguiu Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:26</lbl> 	At kaibat na nita linual ya ing kapatad na, at ing keang gamat makakaulya king sakung nang Esau; at pemalaguiwan neng Jacob: at i Isaac anam neng pulung banua inyang mibait la deti. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:27</lbl> 	At dinagul la ding anak lalaki: at i Esau meguing biasa ya king pamangasu, lalaki yang manuknangan king marangle; at i Jacob lalaki yang tajimik, a manuknangan karing kubu. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:28</lbl> 	Ngeni kaluguran neng Isaac i Esau, uling mamangan ya karing keang pengasuan: at i Rebeca kaluguran ne i Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:29</lbl> 	At miglutu ya i Jacob metung a kalutu: at dinatang ya i Esau a ibat king marangle, at mapagal ya: 	

Genesis <lbl>25:30</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Esau kang Jacob, Pagamuamu ku keka pakanan mu ku, kaniting kalutu a malutu; uling bina kung mapagal: uli na niti meaus ing keang laguiu Edom. 	

Genesis <lbl>25:31</lbl> 	At i Jacob sinabi na, Pisali mu pa kanaku ing kekang pangapangane. 

Genesis <lbl>25:32</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Esau, Oini, mamamate na ku: at nanung pakinabang ing arapat na kanaku ning pangapangane? 	

Genesis <lbl>25:33</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob, Isumpa mu pa kaku; at ya sinampa na kea: at pisali na kang Jacob ing keang pangapangane. 

Genesis <lbl>25:34</lbl> 	At i Jacob dininan ne i Esau tinape at lutung gule; at ya mengan ya at mininum, at tinalakad ya, at meko ya; mankanian nang guewang alang ulagang Esau ing keang pangapangane. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:1</lbl> 	At mika danup king labuad, subali king minunang danup king kayaldawan nang Abraham. At mine ya i Isaac kang Abimelek a ari ra ding Filisteos, king Gerar. 

Genesis <lbl>26:2</lbl> 	At pepakit ya kea i GUINU, at sinabi na, E ka mame Egipto; manuknangan ka king labuad a sabian ku keka: 	

Genesis <lbl>26:3</lbl> 	Manuknangan ka king labuad a iti, at aku mantabe ku keka, at panuanan daka; uling keka, at karing dai mu, ibie ku ngan ing labuad a iti, at tibayan ku ing sumpang simpa ku kang Abraham a ibpa mu; 	

Genesis <lbl>26:4</lbl> 	At parakalan ku ing bini mu anti mo ding batuin king banua, at ibie ku king kekang bini ing anggang labuad a iti; at mipanuanan la king kekang bini ding anggang bansa king labuad; 

Genesis <lbl>26:5</lbl> 	Uli ning i Abraham pemintuan na ing siwala ku, at tiparan na ing bilin ku, ding kakung utus, ding kakung tuntunan, at ding kakung kautusan. 

Genesis <lbl>26:6</lbl> 	At menuknangan i Isaac king Gerar: 

Genesis <lbl>26:7</lbl> 	At ding tau king karinan a ita kitnan de tungkul king keang asawa; at ya sinabi na, Kapatad ke: uling mitakutan yang sabian na, Asawa ke; magkang, ngana, patayan daku ding tau keti king uli nang Rebeca; uling malagu yang lalawan. 

Genesis <lbl>26:8</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang mabang panaun karin ya, i Abimelek a ari ra ding Filisteos tinando ya king metung a awang, at ikit na, at, oini, i Isaac makialung ya kang Rebeca a asawa na. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:9</lbl> 	At inaus neng Abimelek i Isaac, at sinabi na, Oini, tune king ya asawa me: at baket sinabi mu, Kapatad ke? At i Isaac sinabi na kea, uling sinabi ku iti, Magkang mate ku king uli na. 

Genesis <lbl>26:10</lbl> 	At i Abimelek sinabi na, Nanu iting depatan mu kekami? bigsu namu ing ninuman king balayan mekasiping ya sa king kekang asawa, at king uli niti depatan mu sang mikasala kami. 

Genesis <lbl>26:11</lbl> 	At i Abimelek penabilin na king mabilug a balayan, sinabi na, Ing tagkil king taung ini o king keang asawa tune king paten ya. 

Genesis <lbl>26:12</lbl> 	At i Isaac sinalbag ya king gabun a ita, at minupul ya king banuang ita tiadinalan balang metung: at pepanuanan neng GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>26:13</lbl> 	At ing lalaki mibandi ya, at meragul neng meragul angga king meguing mayupaya ya: 	

Genesis <lbl>26:14</lbl> 	At mika atin yang kawan a tupa, at kawan a baka, at dakal a katubale: at keririan de ding Filisteos. 

Genesis <lbl>26:15</lbl> 	Ngeni ding anggang talaga a kikul da ding ipus nang Abraham a ibpa na king kapanaunan na, timbunan dala ding Filisteos, at kitmuan dong gabun. 

Genesis <lbl>26:16</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Abimelek kang Isaac, Kawani ka kekami; uling mayupaya kang maiguit kekami. 

Genesis <lbl>26:17</lbl> 	At i Isaac meko ya karin, at menalakad yang kubu king libis ning Gerar, at menuknangan ya karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:18</lbl> 	At kilkul nong pepasibayung Isaac ding talagang danum, a mekulkul king kapanaunan nang Abraham a keang ibpa; uling timbunan dala ding Filisteos pangamate nang Abraham: at pemalaguiuwan nala agpang king laguiung binili nang ibpa na. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:19</lbl> 	At ding ipus nang Isaac kinulkul la king libis, at ikit de karin ing metung a talaga a sisibul na ing keang danum. 

Genesis <lbl>26:20</lbl> 	At ding pastul nang Gerar mekitua la karing pastul nang Isaac, at sasabian da, Kekami ing danum: at ing inaus na ing laguiu ning talaga Esek uling pipate re. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:21</lbl> 	At kinulkul lang aliwang talaga, at anti mu naman mitua la dikil king uli na; at ing inaus da king keang laguiu Sitna. 

Genesis <lbl>26:22</lbl> 	At meko ya karin, at kinulkul yang aliwang talaga; at ita e re pituan: at ing inaus na king keang laguiu Rehobot; at sinabi na, Uling ngeni i GUINU guewa nakatang karinan, at magpakarakal tamu king gabun. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:23</lbl> 	At ibat karin minta la king Beer-Seba.

Genesis <lbl>26:24</lbl> 	At pepakit ya kea i GUINU king kabengian mu ring ita, at ngana, Aku ing Dios nang Abraham a ibpa mu: e ka tatakut, uling aku at i ku keka, at panuanan daka, at parakalan ku ing kekang bini king uli nang Abraham a talasuyu ku. 

Genesis <lbl>26:25</lbl> 	At mitalakad ya karin metung a altar, at minaus ya king laguiu nang GUINU, at telakad ne karin ing keang kubu: at kinulkul la karin ding ipus nang Isaac metung a talaga. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:26</lbl> 	Kanita i Abimelek mine ya kea a ibat Gerar, at i Ahusat a kakaluguran na, at i Ficol a capitan king keang ejercito. 

Genesis <lbl>26:27</lbl> 	At sinabi na karelang Isaac, Baket mine ko keti kaku, ikong masama kanaku, at mitabi kaku karin kekayu? 	

Genesis <lbl>26:28</lbl> 	At ila sinabi ra, ikit ming masalese king i GUINU makayantabe keka: at sinabi mi, Malyari na sa ngeni ing misumpanan tamu, ikami at ika, at gawa keng tipan keka, 

Genesis <lbl>26:29</lbl> 	Bang e mu ke daptananan marawak, a anti mo ikami e raka ninuan, at anti mo ing bukud ming depatan keka ing mayap, at pepalakuan dakang payapa: ika ngeni ing pepanuanan nang GUINU. 

Genesis <lbl>26:30</lbl> 	At pigtawan nala, at mengan la at mininum. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:31</lbl> 	At pesibangun la king galingaldo, at misumpanan la ing metung at metung: at ila pepalakuan nong Isaac, at ila kinawani la keang payapa. 	

Genesis <lbl>26:32</lbl> 	At milyari king aldo mu ring ita, a dinatang la ding ipus nang Isaac, at belitanan de dikil king talaga a kilkul da, at sinabi ra kea, Menakit keng danum. 

Genesis <lbl>26:33</lbl> 	At inaus neng Seba: inya ing laguiu na ning ciudad Beer-Seba angga king aldo ngeni. 

Genesis <lbl>26:34</lbl> 	At kanitang i Esau apat neng pulung banua tua pengasawa ne i Judit a anak nang Beeri a Heteo, at i Basemat a anak nang Elon a Heteo: 

Genesis <lbl>26:35</lbl> 	At meguing kalungkutan la king kaisipan di Isaac ilang Rebeca. 

Genesis <lbl>27:1</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang matua ne i Isaac, at mepula no ding keang mata, nung inya e ne manakit, inaus ne i Esau a anak nang pangane, at sinabi na kea, Anak ku; at ya sinabi na kea, Ati ku keni. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:2</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Oini, ngeni, aku matua na ku, e ku balu ing aldo na ning kamatayan ku. 

Genesis <lbl>27:3</lbl> 	Uli na nin ngeni kuanan mula, ipagamuamu ku keka, ding sandata mu, ing kekang pibibilianan paslu, at ing kekang bai, at lual ka king marangle, at irakap mukung usa; 

Genesis <lbl>27:4</lbl> 	At ipaglutu mukung maniaman a pamangan, anti king buri ku, at idala mu kaku, bang mangan ku; at panuanan naka ning kaladua ku bayu ku mate. 

Genesis <lbl>27:5</lbl> 	At i Rebeca dimdam na inyang misabi la i Isaac ilang Esau a anak na. At mine ya i Esau king marangle bayang mangasung usa, at idala na. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:6</lbl> 	At i Rebeca selita na kang Jacob a anak na, ngana, Oini, aku dimdam ku kang ibpa mu a sasabian na kang Esau a kapatad mu, sinabi na, 

Genesis <lbl>27:7</lbl> 	Pagdala mukung usa, at ilutu meng maniaman, bakung mangan, at panuanan daka king arapan nang GUINU bayu ku mate. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:8</lbl> 	Ngeni pin, anak ku, pamintuan mu ing siwala ku agpang king yutus ku keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:9</lbl> 	Ume ka ngeni king kawan, at idala mo kaku ding aduang mayap a biserung kambing; at ilutu kong maniaman a pamangan kang ibpa mu, nung makananu ing buri na: 	

Genesis <lbl>27:10</lbl> 	At ika dalan mula kang ibpa mu, bayang mangan, ba nakang panuanan bayu ya mate.

Genesis <lbl>27:11</lbl> 	At i Jacob sinabi na kang Rebeca a indu na, Oini, i Esau a kapatad ku tau yang bulbulan, at aku malinatnat ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:12</lbl> 	Nung sakali salatan na kung ibpa ku, at balamu maguing mapamirait ku kaya; at ing kamtan ku sumpa, at e kanuanan. 

Genesis <lbl>27:13</lbl> 	At i indu na sinabi na kea, Anak ku, kanaku mitumpak ing sumpa keka; pamintuan mu mu ing siwala ku, at ume ka idala mo kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:14</lbl> 	At meko ya, at kinanua, at ya dela nala kang indu na: at i indu na linutu nong maniaman, nung makananu ing buri nang ibpa na. 

Genesis <lbl>27:15</lbl> 	At kinanua ya i Rebeca king imalan nang masanting Esau a anak nang pangane, a atiu kea karin bale, at pepasulud na kang Jacob a anak nang bungsu; 

Genesis <lbl>27:16</lbl> 	At ing balat ding biserung kambing timpak na karing keang gamat, at king malinatnat nang batal: 

Genesis <lbl>27:17</lbl> 	At binie na king gamat nang Jacob a anak na ing lutung maniaman a sidia na, at ing tinape. 

Genesis <lbl>27:18</lbl> 	At ya mine ya kang ibpa na, at sinabi na, Ibpa ku: at ya mekibat ya, Ati ku keni: ninu ika, anak ku? 	

Genesis <lbl>27:19</lbl> 	At i Jacob sinabi na kang ibpa na, Aku i Esau a kekang pangane; depatan ku nung makananu ing sinabi mu kaku: mibangun ka, ipagamuamu ku keka, lukluk ka at mangan ka king kakung usa, banakung panuanan ning kaladua mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:20</lbl> 	At i Isaac sinabi na king keang anak, Makananu kang mekakit binang malagawa, anak ku? At sinabi na, Uling i GUINUNG kekang Dios pigkaluban nakung mayap a kalma. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:21</lbl> 	At i Isaac sinabi na kang Jacob, Lumapit ka, ipagamuamu ku keka, at salatan daka, anak ku, nung tune ika ing anak kung Esau o aliwa. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:22</lbl> 	At linapit ya i Jacob kang ibpa nang i Isaac; at ya selat ne, at sinabi na, Ing siwala mu siwala nang Jacob, dapot ding gamat gamat nong Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:23</lbl> 	At e ne akilala, uling ding gamat na bulbulan la, a anti mo ding gamat nang Esau a kapatad na: inya pepanuanan ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:24</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Ika ing tune kung anak a i Esau? At ya sinabi na, Aku pin. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:25</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Ilapit meng malapit kaku, at mangan ku king usa na ning anak ku, banakang panuanan ning kaladua ku. At ya linapit neng malapit kea, at mengan ya: at pigdala naya namang alak, at minum ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:26</lbl> 	At sinabi na keang Isaac a ibpa na, Lumapit ka ngeni, at uman muku, anak ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:27</lbl> 	At linapit ya, at inuma ne: at abau na ing bau na ning keang imalan, at pepanuanan ne, at sinabi na, Oini, ing bau na ning kakung anak Anti mo ing bau na ning marangle a pepanuanan nang GUINU: 	

Genesis <lbl>27:28</lbl> 	At ing Dios dinan naka king ambun ning banua, At king taba ning labuad, At binang dakal a trigu at bayung alak:

Genesis <lbl>27:29</lbl> 	Suyuan daka ding balayan, At pasiduku la keka ding bansa: Maguing guinu raka ding kekang kapatad, At duku la keka ding anak na ning kekang indu: Ding misumpa keka misumpa la, At minuan la ding panuan keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:30</lbl> 	At milyari, panga ibat na ning pamipanuan nang Isaac kang Jacob, at kalakolako na pamung Jacob king arapan nang Isaac a ibpa na, i Esau a kapatad na dinatang ya ibat ya king pangasuan. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:31</lbl> 	At miglutu ya namang maniaman a pamangan, at dela na kang ibpa na; at sinabi na kang ibpa na, Mibangun ya i ibpa ku, at mangan ya king usa na ning keang anak, banakung panuanan ning kaladua mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:32</lbl> 	At i Isaac a ibpa na sinabi na kea, Ninu ika? At ya sinabi na, Aku ing anak mu, ing pangane mu, a i Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:33</lbl> 	At guinalgal yang bina i Isaac, at sinabi na, Ninu pin itang dinakap usa, at dela ne kaku, at pengan ke ngan bayu ka dinatang, at pepanuanan ke? wa, at maguing nuan ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:34</lbl> 	Inyang damdaman nang Esau ing amanu nang ibpa na, kinulisak yang binang masikan at kapaitpaitan a dalung at sinabi na kang ibpa na, aguiang aku, panuanan muku naman, Oh ibpa ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:35</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Mine ya keti ing kekang kapatad king pamamilatan na ning pirait, at kinua na ing kekang kanuanan. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:36</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, E wari mayap ing pangayaus nang Jacob? A inayawan na nakung mekaladua: kingua na ing kakung pangapangane; at, oini, ngeni kinua na ing kakung kanuanan. At sinabi na, E ka wari misimpan kanuanan tungkul kanako? 	

Genesis <lbl>27:37</lbl> 	At i Isaac mekibat ya at sinabi na kang Esau, Oini, aku binili keng guinu mu, at binie kong ipus kea ding anggang keang kapatad; at ing trigu at ing bayung alak binie ku kea: at keka nanu pa ing arapat ku, anak ku? 	

Genesis <lbl>27:38</lbl> 	At i Esau sinabi na kang ibpa na, Ala ka wari nung e mu metung a kanuanan, ibpa ko? aguiang aku, panuanan muku, Oh ibpa ku. At kinulisak ya i Esau, at kiniak ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:39</lbl> 	At i Isaac a ibpa na mekibat ya, at sinabi na kea, Oini, ing maguing tuknangan mu ing taba ning labuad, At ing ambun ning banua manibat babo; 	

Genesis <lbl>27:40</lbl> 	At king kekang talibung mie ka, at king kekang kapatad sumuyu ka; At malyari, panga metimawa ka, Pagpagan me ing keang paud king kekang tundun. 

Genesis <lbl>27:41</lbl> 	At akamuan neng Esau i Jacob king uli na ning kanuanan a pepanuan na kea ning keang ibpa: at sinabi nang Esau king keang pusu, Lalapit na ing aldo a pamagpaldas kang ibpa ku; at aku patayan ke i Jacob a kapatad ku. 

Genesis <lbl>27:42</lbl> 	At ing amanu nang Esau a keang pangane misalita kang Rebeca; at mitubud ya bang maus kang Jacob a keang bungsu, at kea sinabi na, Oini, ing kekang kapatad a i Esau, matutula ya tungkul keka, pagimbutan na ing, apate naka. 	

Genesis <lbl>27:43</lbl> 	Ngeni pin, anak ku, pamintuan mu ing siwala ku; at talakad ka, at tumakas ka a ume ka kang Laban a kapatad ku karin Haran; 

Genesis <lbl>27:44</lbl> 	At manuknangan ka karin kea mapilan aldo, angga king mipayapa ing mua na ning kapatad mu; 	

Genesis <lbl>27:45</lbl> 	Angga king mayaplak ing mua na keka ning kekang kapatad, at akalinguan na ing depatan mu kea: at kanita pituburan daka, at paulian daka keti a manibat karin: baket pagsalbatan dakong adua king metung a aldo? 

Genesis <lbl>27:46</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Rebeca kang Isaac, Mainip na ku king kakung bie king uli ra ding anak nang babaing Het: nung i Jacob makiasawa ya karing anak nang Het, anti mo deti, karing anak na ning labuad a iti, nanu pang kabaldugan na ning kanakung bie? 

Genesis <lbl>28:1</lbl> 	At i Isaac inaus ne i Jacob, at pepanuanan ne, at penabilinan ne, at sinabi na kea, E ka makiasawa karing anak dang babai ding Canaan. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:2</lbl> 	Talakad ka, ume ka king Padan-aram, king bale nang Betuel ibpa nang indu mu; at makiasawa ka karin karing anak nang Laban a kapatad nang indu mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:3</lbl> 	At ing Dios a Mayupaya king sabla panuanan naka, at papamungan naka, at parakalan daka, bang maguing kapamisanan daka ding balayan; 

Genesis <lbl>28:4</lbl> 	At miabie keka ing pamipanuan kang Abraham, keka, ampon king kekang bini a kayantabe mu; bamung manan ing gabun a kekang panuknanganan, a binie na ning Dios kang Abraham. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:5</lbl> 	At pepalakuan na neng Isaac i Jacob: at mine ya king Padan-aram kang Laban, a anak nang Betuel a tau Siria, a kapatad nang Rebeca, a indu nang Jacob ilang Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:6</lbl> 	Ngeni anti ning ikit na ping Esau a pepanuanan neng Isaac i Jacob at pepalakuan na ne a mine king Padan-aram, bayang makiasawa karin; at kanitang panuanan ne penabilin na kea, a sinabi na, E ka makiasawa karing anak nang Canaan: 

Genesis <lbl>28:7</lbl> 	At king memintu ya i Jacob kang ibpa na at kang indu na, at mine ya king Padan-aram: 	

Genesis <lbl>28:8</lbl> 	At ikit nang Esau king e la makaibie tula ding anak nang Canaan kang Isaac a ibpa na; 	

Genesis <lbl>28:9</lbl> 	At mine ya i Esau kang Ismael, at mekiasawa ya kang Mahalat a anak nang Ismael, a anak nang Abraham, a kapatad nang babaing Nabayot, makabukud pa karing asawa nang at i na kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:10</lbl> 	At meko ya i Jacob ibat king Beer-Seba, at mine ya nangan Haran. 

Genesis <lbl>28:11</lbl> 	At dinatang ya king metung a karinan, at menatili ya karin kebukas, uling ing aldo limbug ne; at kinanua yang metung karing batu ketang karinan a ita, at binili ne king lalam ning keang buntuk, at migkera ya king karinan a ita bang matudtud. 

Genesis <lbl>28:12</lbl> 	At meninap ya; at, oini, ing metung a eran a ing keang pun atiu king labuad, at ing sepu makasakdal ya banua; at, oreni, ding angeles na ning Dios manik at tipa la karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:13</lbl> 	At oini, i GUINU makatalakad ya babo na niti, at sinabi na, Aku i GUINU, ing Dios nang Abraham a ibpa mu, at ing Dios nang Isaac: ing gabun a pagkeran mu, ibie ku keka, at king kekang bini. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:14</lbl> 	At ing kekang bini maguing anti lang alikabuk ning labuad, at mikalat ka king albugan, at king aslagan, at king paralaya at king mauli: at keka at king kekang bini mipanuanan la ding anggang sapni king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:15</lbl> 	At, oini, aku mantabe ku keka, at ingatan daka nuka man ume, at papibalikan daka king labuad a iti; uling e raka lakuan anggang e ku arapat ing sinabi ku keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:16</lbl> 	At miguising ya i Jacob king keang pamanudtud, at sinabi na, Tune king i GUINU atiu king karinan a iti, at e ku balu. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:17</lbl> 	At mitakutan ya, at sinabi na, Makapangilabut a karinan iti! iti e aliwa nung e bale ne ning Dios, at pasbul ning banua. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:18</lbl> 	At i Jacob mibangun yang maranun king abak, at kingua ne ing batu a binili na king lalam ning keang buntuk, at telakad neng pekaasias, at tigtugan neng laru babo na. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:19</lbl> 	At ing inaus nang laguiu king karinan a ita Bet-el, dapot ing laguiu na ning ciudad a ita king minuna Luz. 	

Genesis <lbl>28:20</lbl> 	At i Jacob migpanata ya, sinabi na, Nung mantabe ya kanaku ing Dios, at ingatan naku king dalan a iti a kakung lalakaran, at dinan nakung tinape a apangan, at imalan a isulud, 	

Genesis <lbl>28:21</lbl> 	Bakung makapibalik payapa king bale nang ibpa ku, a i GUINU ya ing maguing Dios ku, 	

Genesis <lbl>28:22</lbl> 	Kanita ing batung iti, a telakad ku a peka-asias, maguing bale ne ning Dios: at king anggang ibie mu kaku ing kapulu tune ibie ku a makatungkul keka. 

Genesis <lbl>29:1</lbl> 	At belaus nang Jacob ing keang lakad, at dinatang ya king gabun ding anak ning aslagan. 

Genesis <lbl>29:2</lbl> 	At linawe ya, at, oini, ing metung a talaga king marangle, at, oreni, ding atlung kawan a tupa makakera la siping na; uling king talagang ita karin do painuman ding kawan a tupa: at maragul ya ing batu king babo na ning asbuk na ning talaga. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:3</lbl> 	At karin la mititipun ding anggang kawan a tupa: at tutulang de ing batung makatakap king asbuk ning talaga, at painuman dala ding tupa, at susubli reng pasibayu ing batu king asbuk ning talaga king sadia nang bili. 

Genesis <lbl>29:4</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob karela, Kakung kapatad, nu ko tau? At ila sinabi ra, Tau ke Haran. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:5</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na karela, Balu ye i Laban a anak nang Nacor? At ila sinabi ra, Balu miya. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:6</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na karela, Mayap ya bile? At ila sinabi ra, Mayap ya: at, oini, i Raquel a keang anak a babai daratang yang abe no ding tupa. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:7</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Oini, matas ya pa ing aldo, ni e pa oras ing tipunan la ding animales: painuman yo ding tupa, at ume kayu at pakanan yula. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:8</lbl> 	At ila sinabi ra, E mi arapat, nung e la pa mitipun ding anggang kawan, at itulang ya ing batu king asbuk ning talaga; kanita painuman mila ding tupa. 

Genesis <lbl>29:9</lbl> 	Makipagsalita ya pa karela, kanitang dinatang ya i Raquel a kayabe no ding tupa nang ibpa na; uling ya ing mimingat karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:10</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang akit neng Jacob i Raquel a anak nang Laban a kapatad ning keang indu, at ding tupa nang Laban a kapatad nang indu na, linapit ya i Jacob, at tinulang ne ing batu king asbuk ning talaga, at pepainum na ing kawan nang Laban a kapatad nang indu na. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:11</lbl> 	At i Jacob inuma ne i Raquel, at sikan na ing keang siwala, at kiniak ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:12</lbl> 	At i Jacob sinabi na kang Raquel king ya kapatad neng ibpa na, at anak neng Rebeca: at ya milai ya at pemalita na kang ibpa na. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:13</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang abalu nang Laban ing balita nang Jacob a anak ning keang kapatad a babai, milai yang selubungan ne, at kinaul ne, at inuma ne, at dela ne king keang bale. At selita na ngan kang Laban ing anggang bague a iti. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:14</lbl> 	At sinabi na keang Laban, Tune king butul daka at laman daka. At menuknangan ya keang pabulan. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:15</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Laban kang Jacob, Anti ning kapatad daka, malyaring sumuyu ka kanakung alang bayad? sabian mu kanaku, nung nanu ing maguing upa mu? 	

Genesis <lbl>29:16</lbl> 	At i Laban atin yang aduang anak a babai: ing laguiu na ning kaka Lea, at ing laguiu na ning wali Raquel. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:17</lbl> 	At ding mata nang Lea mapundat la; dapot i Raquel malagu ya at malagu ya anyu. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:18</lbl> 	At i Jacob apalsintan ne i Raquel; at sinabi na, Suyuan dakang pitung banua dikil kang Rachel a anak mung bungsu. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:19</lbl> 	At i Laban sinabi na, Mayap ing ibie ke keka, king kanitang ibie ke king aliwang lalaki: manuknangan ka kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:20 </lbl>	Sinuyu ya i Jacob pitung banua dikil kang Raquel; at anti mong ditak mung aldo kea, uli ning sinta na kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:21</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob kang Laban, Ibie me kaku ing kakung asawa, uling metupad na ing aldo ku bakung sumiping kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:22</lbl> 	Kanita i Laban tinipun nala ding anggang tau king karinan a ita, at migtau ya. 

Genesis <lbl>29:23</lbl> 	At milyari pangabengi, kinua ne i Lea a keang anak, at dela ne kea; at siniping ya kea. 

Genesis <lbl>29:24</lbl> 	At i Laban binie ne i Zilpa a ipus nang babai kang Lea a keang anak bang maguing ipus nang babai. 

Genesis <lbl>29:25</lbl> 	At milyari pangayabak, king oini, ya i Lea: at sinabi na kang Laban, Nanu iting depatan mu kaku? E raka wari siyuwan tungkul kang Raquel? baket pin pirait muku? 

Genesis <lbl>29:26</lbl> 	At i Laban sinabi na, E ra daraptan ing makanian keting kekeng karinan, a ibie re ing wali bayu ing kaka. 

Genesis <lbl>29:27</lbl> 	Pupusan mu keting metung ing keang paruminggu, at ibie miya naman keka ing metung king uli na ning suyung pasibayu a daptan mu kanakung pitung banua. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:28</lbl> 	At makanian ing depatan nang Jacob, at pinupus na ing keang paruminggu: at binie ne kea i Raquel a anak na a meguing asawa na. 

Genesis <lbl>29:29</lbl> 	At binie neng Laban kang Raquel a anak na a maguing ipus na ing ipus nang babai i Bilha. 

Genesis <lbl>29:30</lbl> 	At siniping ya naman kang Raquel, at liguran naya naman i Raquel a maiguit kang Lea, at sinuyu ya kea pitu pang banua. 

Genesis <lbl>29:31</lbl> 	At ikit nang GUINU king i Lea pikasaman ne, at biklat ne ing keang palanakan, dapot i Raquel baug ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:32</lbl> 	At kinagli ya i Lea, at menganak yang metung a lalaki, at pemalaguiuwan neng Ruben, uling sinabi na, Uling lingusan nang GUINU ing kakung kasakitan; uling ngeni pakamalan naku ning kakung asawa. 

Genesis <lbl>29:33</lbl> 	At kinagli yang pepasibayu, at menganak yang metung a lalaki, at sinabi na, Uling dimdam nang GUINU king pikakasaman ku, uli na nita binie naya naman kaku iting anak a lalaki: at pemalaguiuwan neng Simeon. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:34</lbl> 	At kinagli yang pepasibayu, at menganak yang metung a lalaki; at sinabi na, Ngeni makiabe ne kaku ing asawa ku, uling mika anak ku keang atlung lalaki: inya pemalaguiuwan neng Levi. 	

Genesis <lbl>29:35</lbl> 	At kinagli yang pepasibayu, at menganak yang metung a lalaki: at sinabi na, Ngeni kaku yang purian i GUINU: inya pemalaguiuwan neng Juda; at e ne menganak. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:1</lbl> 	At inyang akit nang Raquel a e ne apapanganakan Jacob, i Raquel meriria ya king keang kapatad; at sinabi na kang Jacob, Dinan mukung anak, o nung ali mate ku. 

Genesis <lbl>30:2</lbl> 	At milablab ing mua nang Jacob salang kang Raquel: at sinabi na, Aku wari ing atiu king bili ning Dios, a migkait keka king bunga na ning kekang atian? 

Genesis <lbl>30:3</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Oini, ing ipus kung babai a i Bilha, sumiping ka kea; bayang manganak karing babo ra ding kakung tud, at mirinan ku namang anak king uli na.

Genesis <lbl>30:6</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Raquel, Inatulan naku ning Dios, at pekiramdaman na naman ing siwala ku, at dininan nakung metung a anak a lalaki, uli na niti pemalaguiuwan neng Dan.

Genesis <lbl>30:13</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Lea, Katula ko! uling ausan dakung matula ding anak a babai: at pemalaguiuwan neng Aser. 

Genesis <lbl>30:14</lbl> 	At meko ya i Ruben king panaun na ning pamamalut trigo, at mekatuklas yang mandragoras king marangle, at dela na kang indu na a i Lea. Kanita sinabi nang Raquel kang Lea, Pagamuamu ku keka, dinan muku, king mandragoras na ning kekang anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:15</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Malati pa waring bague ing kinua me ing kakung asawa? at buri mu mu namang kuanan ing mandragoras na ning kakung anak? At sinabi nang Raquel, Matudtud ya pin ngening benging iti a kayabe mu a kalibe na ning mandragoras na ning anak mu. 

Genesis <lbl>30:16</lbl> 	At inyang i Jacob minuli yang ibat king marangle pangagatpanapun, at selubungan neng Lea, at sinabi na, Kaku ka dapat sumiping; uling king katutuan inupajan daka king mandragoras na ning kakung anak. At siniping ya kea king benging ita. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:17</lbl> 	At pekiramdaman ne ning Dios i Lea, at kinagli ya, at penganak ne ing kalima nang anak a lalaki kang Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:18</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Lea, Binie ne kanaku ning Dios ing kanakung kaupajan, uling binie ke ing kakung ipus a babai king kakung asawa: at pemalaguiuwan neng Isacar. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:19 </lbl>	At kinagli yang pepasibayu i Lea, at penganak ne ing keang kanam a anak a lalaki kang Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:20</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Lea, Dininan naku ning Dios metung a mayap a pagkalub; ngeni makiabe ya kanaku ing asawa ku, uling mika anak kung anam a lalaki kea: at pemalaguiuwan neng Zabulon. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:21</lbl> 	At kaibat menganak yang metung a babai, a pemalaguiuwan neng Dina.

Genesis <lbl>30:25</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang apanganak neng Raquel i Jose, a i Jacob sinabi na kang Laban, Palakuan muku, bakung ume king kakung sariling karinan, at king kakung labuad.

Genesis <lbl>30:26 </lbl>	Ibie mo kaku ding kakung asawa at ding kakung anak, uling king uli ra deti aku sinuyu ku keka, at paburean mukung mako: uling balu mu ing suyung depatan ku keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:27</lbl> 	At sinabi na keang Laban, Nung ngeni makakit kung kalam karing kekang mata, manaya ka: uling kakung akilala a pepanuanan na kung GUINU king uli mu.

Genesis <lbl>30:29</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na kea, Pangabaluan mu nung makananu kung sinuyu keka, at nung makananu lang merakal ding kekang animales king uli ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:30</lbl> 	Uling ditak la mu ding atiu keka inyang bayu kung datang, at merakal lang bina; at i GUINU pepanuanan naka nu ku man munta: at ngeni kapilan naku man misadia king kakung sariling bale? 	

Genesis <lbl>30:31</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na, Nanung ibie ku keka? at mekibat ya i Jacob, E muku dirinan nanuman: nung iti daptan mu dikil kaku, pastulan kong pasibayu ding kekang kawan at ingatan. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:32</lbl> 	Balikan kula ding anggang kawan mu king aldo ngeni a kaku lang ikawani kareti ding batikbatikan at ating dusing, at ing balang matuling karing tupa, at ating dungis at batikbatikan karing kambing: at ilang kakung maguing kaupajan. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:33</lbl> 	Makanian nakung pakibatan ning kakung katuliran king paintungul, panga mine ka keti dikil king kakung upa a atiu king arapan mu: ing balang alang batik at alang dungis karing kambing, at matuling karing tupa, a, nung mayakit ya kanaku, abilang mong penako. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:34</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Laban, Oini, imbut ku ing mapalyari nung makananu ing sinabi mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:35</lbl> 	At kewani no king aldo mu ring ita ding lalaking kambing a maki batik at maki dungis, at ding anggang babaing kambing a maki batik at maki dungis, ing balang maki ating ditak a maputi, at ding anggang matuling karing tupa; at binie no king gamat da ding keang anak; 	

Genesis <lbl>30:36</lbl> 	At ya miglakad yang atlung aldo pilatan ning keang sarili at i Jacob: at pepakan nong Jacob ding mitagan karing kawan nang Laban.

Genesis <lbl>30:38</lbl> 	At binili na ing sangang bikbakanan na karing bangbang king arapan da ding kawan karing pinuman a ayan da ding kawan ngening miminum la; at kinagli la inyang ume la karin bang minum. 

Genesis <lbl>30:39</lbl> 	At kinagli la ding kawan king arapan da ding sanga, at menganak la ding kawan a maki gulis, maki batik, at maki dungis. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:40</lbl> 	At kewani nong Jacob ding biserung tupa, at yarap na ing kawan king nangan a maki batik at ding anggang matuling king kawan nang Laban: at binili nong makakawani ding keang kawan, at e no binili karing kawan nang Laban. 	

Genesis <lbl>30:41</lbl> 	At milyari, a king kapilan man kumagli ing masikan karing kawan, binili nang Jacob ing sanga karing bangbang king arapan da ding mata ra ding kawan, banong papakaglian king libutad da ding sanga;

Genesis <lbl>30:43</lbl> 	At ing lalaki dinakal yang bina, at mika atin yang maragul a kawan, at ipus a babai at ipus a lalaki, at camello at karing asno. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:1</lbl> 	At dimdam na ing amanu ra ding anak nang Laban, a sasabian da, Kinua nong Jacob ding anggang kang ibpa tamu; at karetang kang ibpa tamu karin na kimtan ing mabilug a kaligayan a iti. 

Genesis <lbl>31:2</lbl> 	At pegumasdan nang Jacob ing lupa nang Laban, at, oini, alayu kaya ing anti mo ing sadia. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:3</lbl> 	At sinabi nang GUINU kang Jacob, Mibalik ka king labuad da ding kekang mangatua, at karing kekang kamaganakan; at aku mantabe ku keka;

Genesis <lbl>31:5</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela, Akakit ku ing aske na ning kekong ibpa, king e na makatungkul kakung anti mo ing sadia; dapot ing Dios na ning kakung ibpa atiu kanaku.

Genesis <lbl>31:7</lbl> 	At pirait naku ning kekong ibpa, at binayu nang makatapulung ukdu ing kanakung upa; dapot e ne pepaintulutan ning Dios a daptanan nakung marawak. 

Genesis <lbl>31:8</lbl> 	Nung sinabi nang makanian, Ding maki batik ilang maguing upa mu; kanita manganak la ding anggang kawan maki batik: at nung sinabi nang makanian, Ding anggang maki gulis ilang maguing upa mu; kanita ding anggang kawan manganak lang maki gulis. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:9</lbl> 	Makanian nong leko ning Dios ding animales na ning kekong ibpa, at binie no kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:10</lbl> 	At milyari a king panaun a kakagli ing kawan, tinas ko ding kakung mata, at ikit ku king panaguimpan, at, oini, ding kambing a lalaki a luluksu king kawan pawa lang maki gulis, maki batik, at maki dungis. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:11</lbl> 	At sinabi na kanaku ning angel ning Dios king panaguimpan, Jacob: at sinabi ku, Ati ku keni. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:12</lbl> 	At keang sinabi, Ilawe mo ngeni ding kekang mata, at lawan mo: ding anggang kambing a lalaki a luluksu king kawan maki gulis la, maki batik la at maki dungis: uling kanakung ikit ing anggang daraptan na kekang Laban. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:13</lbl> 	Aku ing Dios king Bet-el, nung nu me linian ing asias nung nu ka gumawang panata kanaku: ngeni talakad ka, mako ka king labuad a iti, at mibalik king gabun a kekang tibuan. 

Genesis <lbl>31:14</lbl> 	At mekibat la i Raquel at i Lea at kea sinabi ra, Atin ke pa kayang makatagan a dake o mana king bale na ning kekeng ibpa? 

Genesis <lbl>31:15</lbl> 	E na ke wari gagawan aliwang balayan? uling pisali na kami, at kea lang lubus liklak ding kekeng kualta. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:16</lbl> 	Uling ing mabilug a pibandian a leko na ning Dios king kekeng ibpa, kekami ita at karing kekeng anak: ngeni pin, daptan mu ing anggang sinabi na ning Dios keka. 

Genesis <lbl>31:17</lbl> 	Kanita tinalakad ya i Jacob, at pepasakian nala ding keang anak at ding keang asawa karing camello; 	

Genesis <lbl>31:18</lbl> 	At dela na la ding anggang keang animales, at ing keang mabilug a pibandian a tinipun, ding animales a keang apakinabang, a keang atipun king Padan-aram, balang ume kang Isaac a keang ibpa king labuad na ning Canaan. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:19</lbl> 	Ngeni i Laban meko ya banong ururan ding keang tupa: at penako nong Raquel ding terafim a atiu king keang ibpa.

Genesis <lbl>31:21</lbl> 	Inya tinakas ya at ing anggang kayatinan na; at mibangun ya, at dinalakit ya king Ilug, at minarap ya nangan king bunduk ning Galaad. 

Genesis <lbl>31:22</lbl> 	At mibalita kang Laban king katlung aldo king tinakas ya i Jacob.

Genesis <lbl>31:24</lbl> 	At mine ya ing Dios kang Laban a tau Siria king paninap king benging ita, at sinabi na kea, Ingatan mu a e ka maniabi kang Jacob king mayap o marawak man. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:25</lbl> 	At mine ya i Laban abe nang Jacob. Ngeni telakad nong Jacob ding keang kubu king bunduk: at i Laban a kayabe ra ding keang kapatad menuknangan la namang king bunduk na ning Galaad. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:26</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Laban kang Jacob, Nanung depatan mu, a tekasan mukung lijim, at dela mo ding kakung anak a babai a anti mong a bijag ning talibung? 

Genesis <lbl>31:27</lbl> 	Baket linijim mu ing kekang panakas, at tekasan muku, at e mu pepabalu kanaku, barakang pepalakuan king saya at maki dalit, at maki tambul at maki alpa; 	

Genesis <lbl>31:28</lbl> 	At e mu pepaintulut man a muma ku karing anak kung lalaki at babai? ngeni kamangmangan ing depatan mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:29</lbl> 	Ing upaya atiu king gamat ku bang daptananan dakong marawak: dapot ing Dios ding mangatua yu sinabi na kanaku nabengi, ngana, Ingatan mung e ka maniabi kang Jacob mayap o marawak man. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:30</lbl> 	At ngeni, king bistat birian mung meko ka, uling pagimbutan meng dasnan ing bale na ning kekang ibpa, makanian man baket penako mo ding kakung dioses? 	

Genesis <lbl>31:31</lbl> 	At i Jacob mekibat ya at sinabi na kang Laban, Uling tatakut ku: uling sinabi ku, Magkang ilako mong sapilitan kaku ding kekang anak a babai. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:32</lbl> 	Inya nung kaninu mo akit ding kekang dioses, e ya mie: king arapan da ding kekatang kapatad, kekang siasatan nung nanung keka a atiu kanaku, at dalan mu. Uling e na balung Jacob a i Raquel ya ing menako. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:33</lbl> 	At linub ya i Laban king kubu nang Jacob, at king kubu nang Lea, at king kubu ra ding aduang ipus a babai; dapot e no ikit. At linual ya king kubu nang Lea, at linub ya king kubu nang Raquel. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:34</lbl> 	Ngeni kingua nong Raquel ding teraf, at binili nala king sia na ning camello at liklukan nala. At selugan neng Laban ing mabilug a kubu, dapot e no ikit. 

Genesis <lbl>31:35</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na kang ibpa na, E ya mimumua ing guinu ku king aku e ku makatalakad king arapan mu; uling atin ku king kaugalian da ding babai. At ya penintun nala, dapot e no ikit ding teraf. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:36</lbl> 	At i Jacob mimua ya, at mekitua ya kang Laban: at mekibat ya i Jacob at sinabi na kang Laban, Nanu ing kakung pamanalangsang? Nanu ing kakung kasalanan bang tukian mukung maki mua? 	

Genesis <lbl>31:37</lbl> 	Selugan mu na pin ing anggang kasangkapan ku, nanu ing ikit mu karing kasangkapan na ning kekang pibalebale? Ibili mu kening arapan da ding kakung kapatad at kapatad mu, bang atulan dakatang adua. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:38</lbl> 	Deting aduangpulung banuang pekiabe ku keka; ding kekang babaing tupa at ding kekang babaing kambing e la mewala ding karelang anak, at ding tupang lalaki ding kekang kawan e ko pengan. 

Genesis <lbl>31:39</lbl> 	Ding pinlapak da ding ganid e ko dela keka; aku ing mibabatang kababatingan; yaduan mo king gamat ku, maguing ding mepanako king aldo o mepanako king bengi. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:40 </lbl>	Makanian ing keralanan ku; king aldo tatampusan naku ning pali, at ning dimla king bengi; at ing tundu tatakas karing kakung mata.

Genesis <lbl>31:41</lbl> 	Deting aduangpulung banuang pamanuknangan ku king kekang bale; siywan dakang labingapat a banua dikil karing adua mung anak a babai, at anam a banua dikil karing kekang kawan: at binayu mu ing kakung upa a makatapulung ukdu. 

Genesis <lbl>31:42</lbl> 	Nung e ya minantabe kanaku ing Dios da ding kakung mangatua, ing Dios nang Abraham, at ing Takut nang Isaac, alang salang palakuan mukung alang darala. Ikit na ning Dios ing kakung pamagkasakit at ing kapagalan da ding kakung gamat, inya sebianan naka nabengi. 

Genesis <lbl>31:43</lbl> 	At mekibat ya i Laban at sinabi na kang Jacob, Ding anak a babaing deti kanaku lang anak, at deting anak, anak kula, at ding kawan, kawan kula, at ing anggang akakit mu kanaku ngan: at nanung arapat ku ngeni karing anak kung babai, o karing karelang anak a penganak da? 	

Genesis <lbl>31:44 </lbl>	At ngeni ume ka keni, gawa katang metung a tipan, aku at ika; a maguing pamipatutu kanaku at keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:45</lbl> 	At kinanua ya i Jacob metung a batu, at telakad neng maguing asias. 	And Jacob took a stone, and set it up for a pillar.
Genesis <lbl>31:46</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob karing keang kapatad, Tumipun kong batu; at kinanua lang batu, at guewa rong metung a buntun: at ila pesipangan la karin king makalapit king buntun. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:47</lbl> 	At pamalaguiuwan neng Laban Jegar-sahaduta: dapot pemalaguiuwan neng Jacob Galeed. 

Genesis <lbl>31:48</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Laban, Ing buntun a iti saksi ya kanaku at keka ngening aldo iti. Inya pin mipalaguiuwan yang Galeed.

Genesis <lbl>31:49 </lbl>	At i Mizpa, uling sinabi na, I GUINU bantian naka at aku, king pamikandayu tamu. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:50</lbl> 	Nung pasakitan mo ding kakung anak a babai, at nung kuma kang asawa bukud karing kakung anak, alang lalaking abe ta; lawan mu, ing Dios saksi ya kanaku at keka. 

Genesis <lbl>31:51</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Laban kang Jacob, Oini ing buntun, at oini ing asias, a binili ku king libutad tamu. 

Genesis <lbl>31:52</lbl> 	Maguing saksi ya ing buntun a iti, at saksi ya ing asias a iti, a e ke lagpusan ing buntun a iti keka, at e me lalagpusan ing buntun a iti at ing asias a iti, king ikapajamak mi. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:53</lbl> 	Ing Dios nang Abraham, at ing Dios nang Nacor, ing Dios ding ibpa ra, yang matul kekata. At i Jacob sinumpa ya alangalang king takut na king keang ibpa a i Isaac. 

Genesis <lbl>31:54</lbl> 	At dinaun yang ain i Jacob king bunduk, at inaus no ding keang kapatad balang pasipangan tinape: at ila pesipangan la ping tinape, at ila menatili lang kabukas king bunduk. 	

Genesis <lbl>31:55</lbl> 	At mibangun yang maranun king kayabakan i Laban, at inuma no ding keang anak a lalaki at babai, at pepanuanan nala: at meko ya at minuli i Laban king keang karinan. 

Genesis <lbl>32:1</lbl> 	At i Jacob belaus na ing keang lakad, at selubungan de ding angeles na ning Dios. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:2</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob inyang akit nala, Oreti ding ejercito na ning Dios: at inaus na ing karinan a ita Mahanaim. 

Genesis <lbl>32:3 </lbl>	At i Jacob pepabal no ding tubud king makauna kea king kapatad nang Esau king gabun na ning Seir, marangle na ning Edom. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:4</lbl> 	At inutus nala, sinabi na, Makanian ing sabian yu king guinu kung i Esau: Anti kanini ing sabi na ning kekang talasuyu a i Jacob, Menuknangan ku kang Laban, at menatili karin angga ngeni. 

Genesis <lbl>32:5</lbl> 	At atin kung vaca, at asno, at tupa, at ipus a lalaki at ipus a babai: at mitubud ku bang pabalu king guinu ku, bakung manakit kalam karing kekang mata. 

Genesis <lbl>32:6</lbl> 	At ding tubud mibalik la kang Jacob, ngara, Dinatang kami king kekang kapatad a i Esau, at ya naman sasagana ya keka, at apat lang dalan katau ding abe na. 	

Genesis<lbl> 32:7</lbl> 	Kanita i Jacob mirinan yang maragul a takut, at melungkut ya: at keang pirake ing balayan a kayabe na at ding kawan, at ding vaca, at ding camello karing aduang tapuk; 	

Genesis<lbl> 32:8</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Nung datang ya i Esau king metung a tapuk, at keang sugatan, kanita ing metung a tapuk a mitagan mitakas ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:9</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob, Oh Dios nang ibpa kung Abraham, at Dios nang ibpa kung Isaac, Oh GUINU a miniabi kanaku, Mibalik ka king kekang labuad, at karing kekang kamaganakan, at daptananan dakang mayap: 	

Genesis <lbl>32:10</lbl> 	E ku karampatan king malating dili king anggang kapakaluluan, at king anggang katutuan, a kekang pepakit king kekang talasuyu; uling kagum ning kakung tukud, delakitan ke ing Jordan a iti: at ngeni meguing adua kung tapuk. 	

Genesis<lbl> 32:11</lbl> 	Iligtas muku, ipagamuamu ku keka, king gamat na ning kakung kapatad, king gamat nang Esau: uling aku tatakut ku kea, magkang datang ya at sugatan naku, ing indu ampon ding keang anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:12</lbl> 	At ika ing sinabing, Tune king ika daptananan dakang mayap at gawan ko ding kekang bini anti mong balas ning dayatmalat, a e la mabilang king uli ning keraklan da. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:13</lbl> 	At migsantung ya karin king benging ita, at kinanua ya ketang atin kea a ipagkalub na kang Esau a keang kapatad: 

Genesis <lbl>32:14</lbl> 	Aduang dalan a kambing a babai at aduangpulung kambing a lalaki, aduang dalan a tupang babai at aduangpulung tupang lalaki. 

Genesis <lbl>32:15 </lbl>	Atlungpulung camellong menganak ampon ding karelang biseru, apatapulung vaca at apulung turu, aduangpulung asna at apulung biseru ra reti. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:16</lbl> 	At binie no king gamat da ding keang ipus, makabukud balang kawan, at sinabi na karing keang alipan, Lumabas kayu a makauna kaku at dinan yung pilatan ing balang kawan. 

Genesis <lbl>32:17</lbl> 	At inutus na king mumuna, sinabi na, Nung ing kapatad kung i Esau asaganan naka, at kutna naka, a sabian na, Kaninu ka? at nuka ume? at kaninu la deting mumuna keka? 

Genesis <lbl>32:18</lbl> 	Kanita sabian mu, king talasuyu nong Jacob; metung la ping pagkalub a mipadala king kakung guinung i Esau: at, oini, ya atiu naman king tauli mi. 

Genesis <lbl>32:19</lbl> 	Inutus na naman king kadua, at king katlu, at karing anggang tutuki karing kawan, a sinabi na, King anti kaniting kaparalanan karin kayu makisabi kang Esau, pamanakit yu kea;
