Genesis <lbl>32:20</lbl> 	At sabian yu, Makabukud kaniti, oini, ing kekang talasuyu a i Jacob atiu king gugulatan mi. Uling keang sinabi, Aplakan ku ing keang mua king pamamilatan na ning pagkalub a atiu king mumuna kaku, at kaibat akit ku ing keang lupa; nung sakaling tanggapan naku. 

Genesis <lbl>32:21</lbl> 	Makanian ing pangauna ra kea ding pagkalub: at migsantung ya king benging ita a kayabe ning tapuk.

Genesis <lbl>32:22</lbl> 	At mibangun ya king benging ita, at tiki no ding keang aduang asawa, at ding keang aduang ipus a babai, at ding keang labingmetung a anak, at kea lang delakit king dalakitan ning Jabbok. 

Genesis <lbl>32:23</lbl> 	At kinua nala, at pepadala nala lipat ning batis, at pepadala na itang atiu kea. 

Genesis <lbl>32:24</lbl> 	At melakuan yang magdilidili i Jacob; at karin mekipantuk ya ing metung a lalaki kea angga king sasala. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:25 </lbl>	At inyang akit na king e ya maniambut kea, inapis ne ing pikalukaluan na ning keang puad, at ing pikalukaluan nang Jacob mipasiknangan ya kabang makipantuk ya kea. 

Genesis <lbl>32:26</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Ibili muku, uling sasala na. At sinabi na, E raka ibili anggang e muku panuanan. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:27</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Nanu ing laguiu mu? At sinabi na, Jacob. 	And he said unto him, 

Genesis <lbl>32:28 </lbl>	At sinabi na, E na mayaus pang Jacob ing kekang laguiu, nung e Israel: uling mekipagkal ka king Dios at karing tau, at miniambut ka. 	

Genesis <lbl>32:29</lbl> 	At kitnan neng Jacob, at sinabi na, pagamuamu ku keka, a sabian mu kaku, ing kekang laguiu. At keang sinabi, Baket kukutang mu ing kakung laguiu? At pepanuanan ne karin. 

Genesis <lbl>32:30</lbl> 	At pemalaguiuwan neng Jacob ing karinan a ita Peniel: uling sinabi na, ikit ke ing Dios lupa at lupa, at miligtas ing kakung bie. 

Genesis <lbl>32:31</lbl> 	At inaslagan ne ning aldo kanitang dadalan ya king Penuel, at mapipile ya king keang puad. 

Genesis<lbl> 32:32</lbl>	Inya e la mamangan ding anak na ning Israel king litid ning balakang a atiu king pikalukaluan ning puad, angga king aldo ngeni: uling inapis ne ning taung ita ing pikalukaluan ning puad nang Jacob king litid ning balakang. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:1</lbl> 	At tinas nong Jacob ding keang mata, at linawe ya, at, oini, daratang ya i Esau, at ding apat a dalan a tau a kayabe na. Kanita pirake nala ding anak kang Lea at kang Raquel, at karing aduang ipus a babai. 

Genesis<lbl> 33:2</lbl> 	At binili no ding ipus a kayabe ra ding karelang anak a pekamumuna, at i Lea a kayabe ra ding keang anak king kadua, at i Raquel at i Jose a pekakatlu. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:3</lbl> 	At ya linagpus ya a makauna karela, at dinuku ya king gabun makatapitung ukdu, angga king milapit ya king keang kapatad. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:4</lbl> 	At milai ya i Esau a seganan ne at kinaul ne, at kinaul ne king batal, at inuma ne: at kiniak la. 

Genesis <lbl>33:5</lbl> 	At tinas nong Esau ding mata na, at ikit no ding babai at ding anak; at sinabi na, Ninu deting kayabe mu? At ya mekibat ya, Ding anak a malam nang pigkalub ning Dios king kekang talasuyu. 

Genesis <lbl>33:6</lbl> 	Kanita pesilapit la ding ipus a babai, ila at ding karelang anak, at pesipamugue la. 

Genesis <lbl>33:7</lbl> 	At linapit ya naman i Lea at ding keang anak, at pesipamugue la: at kaibat pesilapit la i Jose at i Raquel, at pesipamugue la. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:8</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Nanu ing buri mung sabian kaniting mabilug a tapuk a atagpuan ku? At sinabi na, Bang makakit kung kalam king panlalawe na ning kakung guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:9</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Esau, Atin kung labis-labis, kapatad ku; bandian mu ing keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:10</lbl> 	At sinabi na keang Jacob, Ali, aku pagamuamu ku keka, nung ngeni menakit kung kalam karing kekang mata, tanggapan mu pin king kakung gamat ing kakung pagkalub; king uli ning panakit ku king kekang lupa, anti mo ing metung a menakit king lupa na ning Dios, at ika metula ka kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:11</lbl> 	Kuanan mu, ipagamuamu ku keka, ing kakung pagkalub a darala ku keka; uling ing Dios meguing malam ya kaku, at uling atin kung labislabis. At pinilit na kea, at tinggap na. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:12</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Tana lumakad tamu, at tara na, at aku muna ku keka. 

Genesis <lbl>33:13</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na kea, Ing guinu ku balu na king ding anak maina la, at ding kawan at ding baka pasusu la: at nung pamalaguanan la king misan mung aldo, mangamate la ding anggang kawan. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:14</lbl> 	Dumalan ya ngeni ing guinu ku, ipagamuamu ku keka, king arapan na ning keang talasuyu: at kaku yang patnubayan pakakale, agpang king lakbang da ding animales a atiu king mumuna kanaku at king lakbang da ding anak, angga king miras ku king kakung guinu king Seir. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:15</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Esau, Ipaintulut mung lakuan ko keka ding mapilan a tau ku. At sinabi na, Nanan la pa deti? ipaintulut mung manakit kung kalam karing mata na ning guinu ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:16</lbl> 	Makanian ing pamibalik nang Esau king aldo muring ita king keang pamaglakbe king Seir. 

Genesis <lbl>33:17</lbl> 	At i Jacob miglakbe ya king Succoth, at mitalakad yang bale na at guewa nong dalundung ding keang animales: inya pemalaguiuwan na ing karinan a ita Succoth. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:18</lbl> 	At dinatang yang payapa i Jacob king ciudad ning Sichem, a atiu king labuad na ning Canaan, king keang pamibalik king Padan-aram; at menuknangan ya king tulid ning ciudad. 	

Genesis <lbl>33:19</lbl> 	At seli na ing metung a dake na ning gabun, a pitalakaran nang kubu, king gamat da ding anak nang Hamor, a ibpa nang Sichem, dinalan a kapising salapi. 

Genesis <lbl>33:20</lbl> 	At mitalakad ya karin metung a altar, at inaus neng El Elohe-Israel. 

Genesis <lbl>34:1</lbl> 	At i Dina a anak nang Lea, a penganak ne iti kang Jacob, linual ya banong lawan ding anak nang babai ning labuad a ita. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:2</lbl> 	At ikit neng Sichem, a anak nang Hamor a Heveo, a principe king labuad a ita, at kinua ne, at siniping ya kea, at sinira ne puri. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:3</lbl> 	At pekisanib ne ing keang kaladua kang Dina a anak nang Jacob, at pepakamalan ne ing dalaga, at mekisabi yang kalugudlugud king dalaga. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:4</lbl> 	At i Sichem miniabi ya kang ibpa nang i Hamor, a sinabi na, Kuanan me ing dalagang iti a maguing asawa ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:5</lbl> 	Ngeni dimdam na ping Jacob king ya inumis ne ing keang anak a i Dina; at ding keang anak atilu kayabe ra ding animales king marangle: at migtajimik ya i Jacob angga king dinatang la. 

Genesis <lbl>34:6</lbl> 	At liwalan neng Hamor a ibpa nang Sichem i Jacob bayang makisabi kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:7</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Jacob pesidatang lang ibat king marangle inyang iti damdaman da: at melungkut la ding lalaki, at milablab ing karelang mua, uling dinapat yang kamulangan king Israel a sipingan ne ing anak nang Jacob; kabagayan a e dapat malyari. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:8</lbl> 	At mekisabi ya i Hamor karela, ngana, Ing kaladua nang Sichem a kakung anak pagnasan ne ing kekang anak a babai: ipakisabi ku kekayu, a ipagkalub ye kea a maguing asawa ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:9</lbl> 	At mamakiasawa ko kekami; ibie yo kekami ding kekong anak a babai, at kuanan yula ding anak ming babai. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:10</lbl> 	At manuknangan kong kayabe mi: at ing labuad maguing atiu king arapan yu; manuknangan kayu at mangalakal kayu, at mika atin kong pibandian kean. 

Genesis <lbl>34:11</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Sichem kang ibpa nang Dina at karing kapatad nang lalaki, Itulut yung makakit kung kalam karing kekong mata, at ing sabian yu kanaku ibie ku. 

Genesis <lbl>34:12</lbl> 	Aduan yu kanaku ing alang bilang a duru at pagkalub, at kakung ibie agpang king sabian yu kanaku: dapot ipagkalub ya mu kaku ing dalaga a maguing asawa. 

Genesis <lbl>34:13</lbl> 	At pesipakibat la ding anak nang Jacob kang Sichem at kang Hamor a keang ibpa king kapamiraitnan, at sinabi ra, uling inumis ne i Dina a karelang kapatad, 	

Genesis <lbl>34:14</lbl> 	At sinabi ra karela, E mi arapat iti, a ibie miya ing kekeng kapatad king metung a e tuli; uling ita kasiran puri kekami. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:15</lbl> 	Bukud mung kaniting kaparalanan karin mi atulut kekayu: nung ipaintulut yung maguing anti ko kekami, a tulian la ding anggang lalaki kekayu; 	

Genesis <lbl>34:16</lbl> 	Kanita, ibie mila kekayu ding anak ming babai, at kuanan mila ding kekong anak a babai, at manuknangan kaming kayabe yu, at itamu maguing metung tamu mung balayan. 

Genesis <lbl>34:17</lbl> 	Dapot nung e yu ke pakiramdaman, a ikayu mangatuli kayu, dalan mila pin ding kekeng anak a babai, at mako kami.

Genesis <lbl>34:18</lbl> 	At ing kerelang amanu mekapatula kang Hamor, at kang Sichem a anak nang Hamor. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:19</lbl> 	At e na liniban ning kayanakan ing pamayapat king bague, uling atin ang tula king anak nang babaing Jacob: at ya migalangan maiguit karing atiu king mabilug nang bale ibpa na. 

Genesis <lbl>34:20</lbl> 	At i Hamor at i Sichem a keang anak mine la king pasbul ning karelang ciudad, at karelang selita karing tau king karelang ciudad, ngara, 

Genesis <lbl>34:21</lbl> 	Ding taung deti payapa la kekatamu; uli nita tulutan lang manuknangan keting labuad, at pasipangalakal; uling, oini, ing labuad ganap ya degulan tungkul karela; kuanan tala ding karelang anak a babai a maguing asawa tamu at ibie tala karela ding kekatang anak a babai. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:22</lbl> 	Bukud mung king anti kaniting kaparalanan a itulut ding lalaki ing manuknangan a kayabe tamu, bang maguing metung mung balayan, nung tulian ya ing balang lalaki kekatamu, a anti mo ila tuli la. 

Genesis <lbl>34:23</lbl> 	E la wari maguing kekatamu ding karelang baka at ing karelang pibandian at ding sabla rang animales? subali mu nung kekatalang paintulutan, at manuknangan lang kayabe tamu. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:24</lbl> 	At pekiramdam de i Hamor at i Sichem a keang anak ding anggang lulual king pasbul ning keang ciudad, at ing balang lalaki metuli ya, ding sablang lulual king pasbulan ning karelang ciudad. 

Genesis <lbl>34:25</lbl> 	At milyari king katlung aldo, kanitang panamdaman da ing maragul a sakit, ding adua karing anak nang Jacob, i Simeon at i Levi, a kapatad nang Dina, balang metung karela kinanua yang talibung, at lijim lang linub king ciudad, at pete rala ding anggang lalaki. 

Genesis <lbl>34:26</lbl> 	At pete re i Hamor at i Sichem a keang anak king taram ning talibung, at kinua re i Dina king bale nang Sichem, at pesilako la. 

Genesis <lbl>34:27</lbl> 	Mine la karin ding anak nang Jacob karing mete, at simsam de ing ciudad, uling inumis de ing kapatad dang babai. 

Genesis <lbl>34:28</lbl> 	Kinua ro ding karelang kawan at ding karelang baka at ding karelang asno, at detang atiu king ciudad at detang atiu king marangle; 	

Genesis <lbl>34:29</lbl> 	At ing sablang pibandian da, at ding sabla rang anak at ding karelang asawa, dela rong bijag at guewa rong dakap, ing anggang atiu king karelang bale. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:30</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob kang Simeon at kang Levi, Guiluan yuku, guewa yu kung makasumami karing manuknangan keting labuad, karing Cananeos at karing Perezeos: at, akung ditak ma king bilang, pipamisanan daku at sugatan; at lipulan daku, aku at ing kakung bale. 	

Genesis <lbl>34:31</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Gawan ne waring anti mong metung a patutut ing kekeng kapatad? 	

Genesis <lbl>35:1</lbl> 	At sinabi ning Dios kang Jacob, Talakad ka, sumaka ka king Bet-el, at tuknang ka karin: at gawa ka karin metung a altar king Dios, a pepakit keka kanitang tatakas ka ibat king arapan na ning kekang kapatad a i Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:2</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi nang Jacob king keang katubale, at karing sabla nang kayabe, Ikawani yula ding dioses da ding aliwa a atiu king libutad yu, at magpakalinis kayu, at alilan yu ing kekong imalan: 

Genesis <lbl>35:3</lbl> 	At talakad tamu, at sampa tamu king Bet-el; at karin gawa kung altar king Dios, a mekibat kaku king aldo na ning kakung kalungkutan, at minantabe kanaku king dalan king kakung lekaran. 

Genesis<lbl> 35:4</lbl> 	At binie ro kang Jacob ding anggang aliwang dioses a atiu king gamat da, at ding tingga a atiu karing karelang balugbug; at selikut nong Jacob king lalam na ning dutung a encina a makalapit king Sichem. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:5</lbl> 	At ila miglakbe la: at ing metung a maragul a sindak mibili king ciudad a makapatulug karela, at e ro tegal ding anak nang Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:6</lbl> 	Inya mine ya i Jacob king Luz, a atiu king labuad ning Canaan (a ya ing Bet-el), ya at ing mabilug a balayan a kayabe na. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:7</lbl> 	At mitalakad ya karin metung a altar, at pemalaguiuwan na ing karinan El-bet-el; uling ing Dios pepatilip ya kea karin, kanitang tatakas ya ibat king arapan na ning keang kapatad. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:8</lbl> 	At mete ya i Debora, a talaingat nang anak Rebeca, at mikutkut ya king makababa ning Bet-el king lalam ning encina: a ing laguiu na inaus dang Allonbacuth. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:9</lbl> 	At ing Dios pepatilip yang pasibayu kang Jacob, kanitang menibatan ya king Padan-aram, at ya pepanuanan ne. 

Genesis <lbl>35:10</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning Dios, Ing laguiu mu Jacob: Ing laguiu mu e na mayaus Jacob, nung e Israel ing maguing laguiu mu: at inaus na ing keang laguiu Israel. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:11</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning Dios, Aku ing Dios a Mayupaya king Sabla: ika mamunga ka at magpakarakal; at metung a bansa at kapisanan ding bansa ing manibatan keka, at ding ari lual la king kekang balakang. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:12</lbl> 	At ing labuad a binie ku kang Abraham at kang Isaac, keka ku ibie, at king kekang bini pangaibat mu ibie ku ing labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:13</lbl> 	At ing Dios pepaitas ya menibat king karinan a nung nu ne pekisabian. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:14</lbl> 	At i Jacob mitalakad yang metung a asias king karinan a nung nu ne pekisabian, metung a asias a batu: at bilusan neng metung a ain a inuman, at tigtugan neng laru. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:15 </lbl>	At pemalaguiuwan neng Jacob Bet-el ing karinan a nung nu ne pekisabian ning Dios. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:16 </lbl>	At linakad la menibat king Bet-el; at marayu pa bayu la datang king Efrata: at miramdam yang bina i Raquel king pamanganak, at migkasakit yang tutu. 

Genesis <lbl>35:17</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang miraramdam yang bina, sinabi na kea ning ilut, E ka tatakut; uling ngeni mika atin kang aliwang anak a lalaki. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:18</lbl> 	At milyari, kabang matatakmus ya inawa (uling mete ya pin), pemalaguiuwan neng Ben-oni: dapot pemalaguiuwan ne ning keang ibpa Benjamin. 

Genesis <lbl>35:19</lbl> 	At mete ya i Raquel, at kitkut de king dalan a tuturu king Efrata (a ya ing Bethlehem). 	

Genesis <lbl>35:20</lbl> 	At mitalakad ya i Jacob metung a asias king babo na ning keang kutkutan: a ya ing asias na ning kutkutan nang Raquel, angga king aldo ngeni. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:21</lbl> 	At linakad ya i Israel, at telakad ne ing keang kubu king nangan na pa karin ning batiawan na ning Eder. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:22 </lbl>	At milyari, kabang i Israel manuknangan ya king labuad a ita, i Ruben mine ya at siniping ya kang Bilha a babai na ning keang ibpa: at abalitan nang Israel. Ngeni labi la ping adua ding anak nang lalaking Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>35:23</lbl> 	Ding anak nang Lea: i Ruben, ya ing pangane nang Jacob, at i Simeon, at i Levi, at i Juda, at i Isacar, at i Zabulon; 

Genesis <lbl>35:24 </lbl>	Ding anak nang Raquel: i Jose at i Benjamin; 

Genesis <lbl>35:25</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Bilha, a ipus nang Raquel: i Dan at i Neftali; 

Genesis <lbl>35:26</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Zilpa, a ipus nang Lea: i Gad at i Aser, deti ilang anak nang Jacob, a penganak da kea king Padan-aram. 

Genesis <lbl>35:27</lbl> 	At mine ya i Jacob kang Isaac a keang ibpa king Mamre, king Kiriat-arba (a iti ing Hebron), nung nu la menuknangan i Abraham at i Isaac. 

Genesis <lbl>35:28</lbl> 	At ding aldo nang Isaac dinalan la at walungpulung banua. 

Genesis <lbl>35:29 </lbl>	At mepatad ya inawa i Isaac at mete ya, at miagum ya king keang balayan, matua ya at ganap ya karing aldo: at kitkut de ding keang anak a i Esau at i Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:1</lbl> 	Ngeni deti pin ilang dai nang Esau (a ya ing Edom). 

Genesis <lbl>36:2</lbl> 	At i Esau mekiasawa ya karing anak nang Canaan: kang Ada a anak nang babaing Elon a Heteo, at kang Aholibama a anak nang babaing Ana, a anak nang babaing Zibeon a Heveo, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:3</lbl> 	At kang Basemat a anak nang Ismael a kapatad nang Nabayot. 

Genesis <lbl>36:4</lbl> 	At penganak neng Ada i Elifaz kang Esau; at penganak neng Basemat i Rewel; 

Genesis <lbl>36:5</lbl> 	At penganak neng Aholibama i Jeus, at i Jalam at i Core: deti ilang anak nang lalaking Esau, a penganak da kea king labuad na ning Canaan. 

Genesis <lbl>36:6</lbl> 	At dela nong Esau ding keang asawa, at ding keang anak a lalaki, at babai, at ding anggang kaladua king keang bale, at ding keang animales, at ding anggang keang kawan, at ing sablang atiu kea, a keang tinipun king labuad na ning Canaan; at mine ya king aliwang labuad a makarayu kang Jacob a keang kapatad. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:7</lbl> 	Uling ing karelang kayatinan tutung mipakaragul at e la malyaring manuknangan miabe; at ing labuad a piglakben da e no aguiu uling dakal lang tutu ding karelang animales. 

Genesis<lbl> 36:8</lbl> 	At tinuknang ya i Esau king bunduk na ning Seir, i Esau ya ing Edom. 

Genesis <lbl>36:9</lbl> 	At deti ilang dai nang Esau a ibpa ra ding Edomita king bunduk ning Seir: 	

Genesis <lbl>36:10</lbl> 	Oreti ding laguiu ra ding anak nang Esau: I Elifaz a anak nang Ada a asawa nang Esau, i Rewel a anak nang Basemat a asawa nang Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:11 </lbl>	At ding anak nang Elifaz, ila pin i Teman, i Omar, i Zefo, at i Gatam, at i Kenaz. 

Genesis <lbl>36:12</lbl> 	At i Timna babai neng Elifaz a anak nang Esau; at ayanak ne i Amalek kang Elifaz: deti ilang anak nang lalaking Ada, a asawa nang Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:13</lbl> 	At oreti ding anak nang lalaking Rewel: i Nahat, at i Zera, i Zama, at i Miza: deti ilang anak nang Basemat, a asawa nang Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:14 </lbl>	At deti ilang anak nang Aholibama a anak nang babaing Ana, a anak nang babaing Zibeon, a asawa nang Esau: at ding ayanak na kang Esau i Jeus, at i Jalam, at i Core. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:15</lbl> 	Deti ilang pekabuntuk karing anak nang Esau: ding anak nang Elifaz a pangane nang Esau: ing pekabuntuk a i Teman, ing pekabuntuk a i Omar, ing pekabuntuk a i Zefo, ing pekabuntuk a i Kenaz, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:16</lbl> 	Ing pekabuntuk a i Core, ing pekabuntuk a i Gatam, ing pekabuntuk i Amalek: deti ila ding pekabuntuk a menibatan kang Elifaz king labuad ning Edom: deti ilang anak nang lalaking Ada. 

Genesis <lbl>36:17</lbl> 	At deti ila ding anak nang lalaking Rewel, a anak nang lalaking Esau: ing pekabuntuk a i Nahat, ing pekabuntuk a i Zera, ing pekabuntuk a i Miza: deti ilang pekabuntuk a menibatan kang Rewel king labuad na ning Edom; deti ilang anak nang lalaking Basemat, a asawa nang Esau. 

Genesis <lbl>36:18</lbl> 	At deti ilang anak nang lalaking Aholibama, a asawa nang Esau: ing pekabuntuk a i Jeus, ing pekabuntuk a i Jalam, ing pekabuntuk a i Core: deti ilang pekabuntuk a menibatan kang Aholibama a anak nang babaing Ana, a asawa nang Esau. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:19</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang lalaking Esau, at deti ding karelang pekabuntuk: a ya ing Edom. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:20</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang lalaking Seir a Horeo, a manuknangan king labuad: i Lotan at i Sobal at i Zibeon at i Ana, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:21</lbl> 	At i Dizon at i Ezer at i Dizan: deti ilang pekabuntuk a menibatan karing Horeos, ding anak nang Seir king gabun na ning Edom. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:22</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Lotan ila i Hori at i Heman; at ing kapatad nang babaing Lotan ya pin i Timna. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:23</lbl> 	At deti ila ding anak nang Sobal: i Alban at i Manahat at i Ebal, i Sefo at i Onam.

Genesis <lbl>36:24</lbl> 	At deti ila ding anak nang Zibeon: i Aya at i Ana; iti ya i Ana a mekakit mapaling sibul king ilang, inyang pakanan no ding asno nang Zibeon a keang ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:25</lbl> 	At deti ila ding anak nang Ana: i Dizon at i Aholibama a anak nang babaing Ana. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:26</lbl> 	At deti ila ding anak nang Dizon: i Hendam at i Hesban at i Itran at i Cheran. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:27</lbl> 	Deti ding anak nang Ezer: i Bilhan at i Zaavan at i Acan. 

Genesis <lbl>36:28</lbl> 	Deti ding anak nang Dizan: i Hus at i Aran. 

Genesis <lbl>36:29</lbl> 	Deti ilang pekabuntuk a menibatan karin Horeos: ing pekabuntuk a i Lotan, ing pekabuntuk a i Zobal, ing pekabuntuk a i Zibeon, ing pekabuntuk a i Ana, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:30</lbl> 	Ing pekabuntuk a i Dizon, ing pekabuntuk a i Ezer, ing pekabuntuk a i Dizan: deti ilang pekabuntuk a menibatan karing Horeos, agpang karing karelang pekabuntuk king labuad na ning Seir. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:31</lbl> 	At deti ila ding ari a sinakup king labuad ning Edom, bayu ya migari ing ninumang ari karing anak na ning Israel. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:32</lbl> 	At i Bela a anak nang lalaking Beor migari ya king Edom; at ing laguiu na ning keang ciudad Dinaba. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:33</lbl> 	At mete ya i Bela, at migari yang kalili na i Jobab a anak nang Zera, a tau Bozra. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:34</lbl> 	At mete ya i Jobab, at migari yang kalili na i Husam king labuad da ding Temaneos. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:35</lbl> 	At mete ya i Husam, at migari yang kalili na i Hadad a anak nang Bedad, a ya naman ing sinugat kang Midian king marangle nang Moab: at ing laguiu na ning keang ciudad Avit. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:36</lbl> 	At mete ya i Adad, at migari yang kalili na i Samla a tau Mazreca. 

Genesis <lbl>36:37</lbl> 	At mete ya i Samla, at migari yang kalili na i Saul a tau Rehabot a lele Ilug. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:38 </lbl>	At mete ya i Saul, at migari yang kalili na i Baal-hanan a anak nang Acbor. 	

Genesis <lbl>36:39</lbl> 	At mete ya i Baal-hanan a anak nang Acbor, at migari yang kalili na i Hadar: at ing laguiu na ning keang ciudad Pau; at ing laguiu na ning keang asawa Mehetabel, a anak nang Matred, a anak nang babaing Mezahab. 

Genesis <lbl>36:40</lbl> 	At deti ding laguiu ra ding pekabuntuk a menibatan kang Esau, agpang karing karelang sapni, agpang karing karelang karinan, at king uli ding kerelang laguiu: ing pekabuntuk a i Timna, ing pekabuntuk a i Elva, ing pekabuntuk a i Jetet, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:41</lbl> 	Ing pekabuntuk a i Aholibama, ing pekabuntuk a i Ela, ing pekabuntuk a i Pinon, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:42</lbl> 	Ing pekabuntuk a i Kenaz, ing pekabuntuk a i Teman, ing pekabuntuk a i Mibzar, 	

Genesis <lbl>36:43</lbl> 	Ing pekabuntuk a i Magdiel, ing pekabuntuk a i Iram: Deti ilang pekabuntuk king Edom, agpang karing karelang tuknangan king labuad a karelang bandi. Iti ya pin i Esau a ibpa ra ding Idumeos. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:1</lbl> 	At menuknangan ya i Jacob king labuad a nung nuya menaliwang balayan i ibpa na, king labuad na ning Canaan. 

Genesis <lbl>37:2</lbl> 	Deti ilang dai nang Jacob. I Jose atin neng labingpitung banua, migpastul yang kawan a kayabe ra ding keang kapatad; at ya anak yang kayabeabe ra ding anak nang Bilha, at ding anak nang Zilpa, a asawa na ning keang ibpa: at migdala yang balita i Jose tungkul king dewakan da king karelang ibpa. 

Genesis <lbl>37:3</lbl> 	Ngeni pakamalan neng Israel i Jose a maiguit karing sabla nang anak, uling ya ing anak na king keang ketuan: at ya guewa neng metung a tunica a maki sari-saring kule. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:4</lbl> 	At ikit de ding keang kapatad king ya pakamalan ne ning keang ibpa a maiguit karing anggang kapatad na; at ya kasaman de, at e malyaring pakisabian deng payapa. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:5</lbl> 	At meninap ya i Jose metung a paninap, at selita ne karing keang kapatad: at lalu re pang akasaman. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:6</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela, Pakiramdaman yu, ipagamuamu ku kekayu, iting paninap a apaninap ku: 	

Genesis <lbl>37:7</lbl> 	Uling oini, manali tamu king aptas ning trigo king marangle, at, oini, tinalakad ing kakung aptas, at, makatalakad matulid; at, oini, ing kekong aptas dinatang makapatulug, at gagalang king kakung aptas. 

Genesis <lbl>37:8</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea ding keang kapatad, Magari ka waring tune kekame? o papanginu ka waring tune kekame? At lalu re pang kesaman king uli na ning keang paninap, at ding keang amanu. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:9</lbl> 	At meninap ya pang aliwang paninap, at selita ne karing keang kapatad, at sinabi na, Oini, aku meninap kung aliwang paninap pa; at, oini, king ing aldo at ing bulan at ding labingmetung a batuin guinalang la kanaku. 

Genesis <lbl>37:10</lbl> 	At selita ne king keang ibpa, at karing keang kapatad; at sebianan neng ibpa na, at sinabi na kea, Nanung paninap iting apaninap mu? Tune waring ume ku at i indu mu at ding kekang kapatad at ikami duku ke king gabun king arap mo? 

Genesis <lbl>37:11</lbl> 	At ding keang kapatad mariria la kea; dapot sinimpan nang ibpa ra king keang pamiisip iting salita. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:12</lbl> 	At mine la ding keang kapatad bang magpastul karing kawan ning karelang ibpa king Sichem. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:13</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Israel kang Jose, E la wari magpastul karing kawan ding kapatad mu king Sichem? Ume ka keni, at utusan daka karela. At mekibat ya kea, Ati ku keni. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:14</lbl> 	At ya sinabi na kea, Ume ka ngeni, lawan mu nung mayap la ding kapatad mu, at nung mayap la ding kawan; at dalan mu kaku ing balita. Makanian neng inutusan a ibat king libis ning Hebron, at mine ya king Sichem. 

Genesis <lbl>37:15</lbl> 	At ikit ne ning metung a tau, at, oini, galagala ya king marangle: at kitnan ne ning taung ita, ngana, Nanung panintunan mu? 	

Genesis <lbl>37:16</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Panintunan ko ding kakung kapatad: ipagamuamu ku keka, sabian mo kaku, nung nuro papastulan ding kawan. 

Genesis <lbl>37:17</lbl> 	At sinabi ning tau, Meko no keti; uling dimdam kung karelang sinabi, Tana ume ta king Dotan. Kanita i Jose tikian nala ding keang kapatad, at ikit no king Dotan. 

Genesis <lbl>37:18</lbl> 	At karela yang abatiawan king marayu, at bayu ya milapit karela, minala lang salang kea bareng paten. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:19</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning metung at metung, Oini, daratang ya ing mapaninap. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:20</lbl> 	Ume ko pin keni ngeni, patayan taya, at iyugse taya king metung karing talaga, at sabian tamu, Metung yang ganid a marawak ing linaklak kea: at akit tamu nung nanung mapalyari karing keang paninap. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:21</lbl> 	At dimdam nang Ruben, at linigtas ne king karelang gamat, a sinabi na, E taya papatayan. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:22</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Ruben karela, E tamu mibububung daya; iyugse ye king talagang iti a atiu king ilang, dapot e ye bubuatanan gamat: bang aligtas ne king karelang gamat, bayang makapibalik kang ibpa na. 

Genesis <lbl>37:23</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang datang ya i Jose karing keang kapatad, linubas da ing imalan nang Jose, ing tunica nang susulud a ating miyayaliwang kule; 	

Genesis <lbl>37:24</lbl> 	At karela yang telanan, at inugse re king talaga: at ing talaga malangi ya, ala yang danum.

Genesis <lbl>37:25</lbl> 	At pesilukluk lang mengan tinape: at tinas do ding karelang mata at linawe la, at, oreni, ing metung a tapuk a Ismaelitas ibat la Galaad, at ding karelang camello magdala lang pabanglu at balsamo, at mira, a darala ra Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:26</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Juda karing keang kapatad, Nanung apakinabang tamu nung paten taya ing kekatang kapatad at ilijim ing keang daya? 

Genesis <lbl>37:27</lbl> 	Ume ko keni, at kekatayang pisali karing Ismaelitas, at e taya bubuatanan gamat: uling kapatad taya, laman taya. At ding keang kapatad mekiramdam la kea. 

Genesis <lbl>37:28</lbl> 	At lalabas la ding Madianitas, a mangalakal; at karela yang sinaka i Jose king talaga, at pisali re i Jose karing Ismaelitas aduangpulu kapising pilak. At dela re i Jose karin Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:29</lbl> 	At mibalik ya i Ruben king talaga; at, oini, i Jose alayu king talaga; at guinabak na ing keang imalan. 

Genesis <lbl>37:30</lbl> 	At mibalik ya karing keang kapatad, at sinabi na, Alayu ing anak; at aku, nuku ume? 

Genesis <lbl>37:31</lbl> 	At kinua ra ing tunica nang Jose, at mekamate lang metung a lalaking kambing, at karelang tilbug ing imalan king daya; 	

Genesis <lbl>37:32</lbl> 	At karelang peparala ing tunicang maki sarisaring kule, at dela ra kang ibpa ra, at sinabi ra, Ikit miya iti: kilalanan me ngeni nung ya ing tunica na ning kekang anak o aliwa. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:33</lbl> 	At akilala ne, at sinabi na, Ing tunica na pin ning kakung anak, metung yang ganid a marawak ing linaklak kea; i Jose alang salang mengapirapirasu ya. 

Genesis <lbl>37:34</lbl> 	At guinabak nang Jacob ing keang imalan, at keang dininan king magaspang a imalan ing keang balakang, at menangis yang makabang aldo dikil king keang anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:35</lbl> 	At pesitalakad la ding anggang anak nang lalaki at babai bareng pamatulan; dapot sikuil na ing pangapatulan na, at sinabi na, Uling kuldas kung tatangis king kakung anak angga king kutkutan. At tengisan ne ning keang ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>37:36</lbl> 	At pisali re ding Madianitas karin Egipto kang Potifar, metung a oficial nang Faraon, capitan de ding bante. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:1</lbl> 	At milyari king panaun a ita, a kinawani ya i Juda karing keang kapatad, at mibalik ya king metung a Adulamita a ing laguiu na Hira. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:2</lbl> 	At ikit ne karing Juda ing anak nang babai ning metung a Cananeo a ing keang laguiu Sua; at kinua ne, at mekiabe ya kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:3</lbl> 	At kinagli ya, at menganak yang metung a lalaki; at pemalaguiuwan neng Er. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:4</lbl> 	At kinagli yang pepasibayu, at menganak yang metung a lalaki; at pemalaguiuwan neng Onan, 	

Genesis <lbl>38:5</lbl> 	At pasibayu yang menganak metung a lalaki, at pemalaguiuwan neng Sela: at ya atiu king Kizib, kanitang penganak ne. 

Genesis <lbl>38:6</lbl> 	At i Juda kinanua yang maguing asawa na ning keang pangane a i Er, a ing keang laguiu Tamar. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:7</lbl> 	At i Er, a pangane nang Juda, meguing marawak ya king panimanman nang GUINU; at pete neng GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:8</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Juda kang Onan, Makiabe ka king asawa na ning kekang kapatad a lalaki, at daptan mu ing katungkulan na ning kapatad mu king pangaasawa na kea, at italakad mu ing bini ning kapatad mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:9</lbl> 	At balu nang Onan a e maguing kea ing bini; at milyari, inyang sisiping ya king asawa na ning keang kapatad, at yugse na king gabun, magkang dinan neng bini ing keang kapatad. 

Genesis <lbl>38:10</lbl> 	At ing kabagayan a depatan na marawak king panlalawe nang GUINU: at pete naya naman. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:11</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi nang Juda kang Tamar a keang manuyang a babai, Manatili kang mebalung babai king bale na ning kekang ibpa, angga king dagul ya i Sela a kanakung anak a lalaki; uling sinabi na, Magkang mate ya naman, anti mo ding keang kapatad. At mine ya i Tamar at menuknangan ya king bale na ning keang ibpa. 	

Genesis<lbl> 38:12</lbl> 	At dinalan ing makabang aldo, mete ya ing anak nang Sua, a asawa nang Juda; at mipatulan ya i Juda, at minta ya karing manurud tupa Timnas, ya at ing keang kaluguran a i Hira a Adulamita.

Genesis<lbl> 38:13</lbl> 	At belita ra kang Tamar, a sinabi ra, Oini, ing kekang katiwangan a lalaki minta ya king Timnas bang manurud karing keang tupa. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:14</lbl> 	At miglukas yang imalan a pangabalu, at migtakap ya king keang bungbung, at binalut na ing sarili na, at linuknuk ya king pasbul na ning Enaim, a atiu king dalan ning Timnas; uling ikit na king i Sela maragul ne, at e ya miabie kea a maguing asawa na. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:15</lbl> 	Inyang akit neng Juda, inisip nang patutut ya; uling migtakap yang lupa. 	When Judah saw her, he thought her to be an harlot; because she had covered her face.
Genesis <lbl>38:16</lbl> 	At linapit ya kea king lele na ning dalan, at sinabi na, Lumapit ka ipagamuamu ku keka, king aku pasipingan muku keka: uling e ne balu king ya ing keang manuyang a babai. 

Genesis <lbl>38:17</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Paralan dakang metung a anak kambing a ibat king kawan. At keang sinabi, Dinan mukung sangla, king ipadala muya? 

Genesis <lbl>38:18</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Nanung sangla a ibie ku keka? At sinabi na, Ing kekang panatak at ing kekang babat, at ing tukud a darala mu king gamat. At binie no kea, at siniping ya kea, at kinagli ya king uli na. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:19</lbl> 	At mibangun ya, at meko ya, at leko ne ing keang bungbung, at sinulud na ing imalan nang pangabalu. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:20</lbl> 	At pepadala neng Juda ing anak ning kambing king pamamilatan na ning gamat na ning keang kakaluguran a Adulamita, bang tanggapan no ding sangla king gamat na ning babai: dapot e ne ikit. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:21 </lbl>	Kanita kitang ne karing tau king karinan a ita, a sinabi na, Nuya karin ing patutut a atiu king lele ning dalan ning Enaim? At karelang sinabi, Alang ninumang patutut keti. 

Genesis <lbl>38:22</lbl> 	At mibalik ya kang Juda, at sinabi na, E ke ikit; at makanian mu naman ding tau king karinan a ita sinabi ra, E mika atin keting patutut. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:23</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Juda, Pabustan yang bandian ne, magkang dumine tamu: oini, kaku yang pepadala ing anak ning kambing a iti, at e me ikit. 	

Genesis<lbl> 38:24</lbl> 	At milyari inyang milabas ing ating atlung bulan, a apamalita ra kang Juda, a sinabi ra, Ing kekang manuyang a i Tamar makipangalugud ya; at makakayaliwa kaniti, oini, mabuktut ya king pamakipangalugud. At sinabi nang Juda, Ilual ye, bayang dulukan. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:25 </lbl>	Kanitang ilual de, mitubud ya king keang katiwangan a lalaki, a sinabi na, King lalaking maki bandi kareni, mebuktut ku: at sinabi na, Pagamuamu ku keka, king kilalanan mula, nung kaninu la deni, ing panatak, at ing babat, at ing tukud. 

Genesis <lbl>38:26 </lbl>	At akilala nong Juda, at sinabi na, ya banal ya pa kanaku, uling e ke binie kea i Selang anak ku. At e ku ne pasibayung akilala pa. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:27</lbl> 	At milyari king keang pamirandam, oreni, kambal la ding atiu king keang atian. 

Genesis <lbl>38:28</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang mirandam ya, liwal ne ning metung ing keang gamat: at telanan ne ning ilut at telian ne king gamat king metung a sinulad a malutu, sinabi na, Ini ing minunang linual. 	

Genesis <lbl>38:29</lbl> 	At milyari, pangaurung na ning keang gamat, king, oini, ing keang kapatad linual ya: at keang sinabi, Baket magpiglas ka? uli na nita pemalaguiuwan neng Fares, 	

Genesis <lbl>38:30</lbl> 	At kaibat linual ya ing keang kapatad, a iti ing maki sinulad a malutu king gamat, at inaus nang Zera ing keang laguiu. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:1</lbl> 	At dela re i Jose karin Egipto; at seli neng Potifar a oficial nang Faraon, a capitan ding bante, a lalaki yang tau Egipto, seli ne king gamat da ding Ismaelitas, a migdala kea karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:2</lbl> 	At i GUINU atiu kang Jose, at meguing lalaki yang mapalad; at ya atiu king bale na ning keang guinu a tau Egipto. 

Genesis <lbl>39:3</lbl> 	At ikit na ning keang guinu king i GUINU atiu kea, at ing anggang daraptan na panuanan nang GUINU king keang gamat. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:4</lbl> 	At mekakit yang kalam i Jose king keang panlalawe, at ya talapanibala ne: at guewa neng talasiasat king keang bale, at ing sablang kayatinan na penibala na king keang gamat. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:5</lbl> 	At milyari manibat king panaun a guewa neng talasiasat king keang bale, at king sablang kayatinan na, pepanuanan neng GUINU ing bale na ning tau Egipto king uli nang Jose; at ing pamipanuan nang GUINU atiu king anggang kayatinan na, king bale at king marangle. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:6 </lbl>	At keang penibala ing sablang atiu kea king gamat nang Jose; at e ya makialam king nanumang bague a kayatinan na, nung e mu king tinape a keang kakanan. At i Jose masanting ya, at piluluguran. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:7</lbl> 	At milyari pangayari na ning bague a iti, king ing asawa na ning keang guinu dinangat no ding mata na kang Jose; at sinabi na, Sipingan muku. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:8</lbl> 	Dapot tinanggui ya, at sinabi na king asawa na ning keang guinu, Oini, ing kakung guinu e ya makialam kanaku tungkul king atiu keti bale, at ing sablang kayatinan na penibala na king kakung gamat: 

Genesis <lbl>39:9</lbl> 	Ya e ya maragul king bale iti a maiguit kanaku; ni ya ala yang pigkait kanaku nanumang bague nung e mu ika, uling asawa naka: Makananu ku ping daptan iting maragul a dewakan, at mikasala salang king Dios? 

Genesis <lbl>39:10</lbl> 	At milyari, kabang ya makisabi ya kang Jose aldo-aldo, at e ya mekiramdam kea, a sipingan ne o makiabe ya kea. 

Genesis <lbl>39:11</lbl> 	At milyari king panaun a iti, a linub ya king bale banang daptan ing keang dapat; at karin alalu ding tau king kilub ning bale. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:12</lbl> 	At telanan ne imalan, ngana, Sipingan muku: at likuan na ing keang imalan king gamat na, at tinakas ya, at linual ya. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:13 </lbl>	At milyari, pamanakit nang likuan na ing keang imalan king gamat na, at tinakas ya lual. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:14 </lbl>	Minaus yang tau king keang bale, at karela sinabi na, Ikit yu na, pigdala nakatamung metung a Hebreo banakatang biruan: linapit ya kaku banakung sipingan, at aku kinulisak kung masikan. 

Genesis <lbl>39:15</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang damdaman nakung sikan ku ing siwala ku at kinulisak, likuan na ing keang imalan king siping ku, at tinakas yang linual. 	

Genesis<lbl> 39:16 </lbl>	At binili na ing imalan king keang siping angga king dinatang ya ing keang guinu king keang bale. 

Genesis <lbl>39:17</lbl> 	At selese na kea agpang king pangasabing iti, a ngana, Linapit ya kanaku ing ipus a Hebreo, a dela mu keti kekatamu, banakung biruan: 

Genesis <lbl>39:18</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang sikan ku ing kanakung siwala ku at kukulisak ku, likuan na ing imalan na king siping ku, at tinakas ya lual. 

Genesis <lbl>39:19</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang damdaman na ning keang guinu ing amanu ning keang asawa, a sinabi na kea, ngana, Makanian a pangaparalan ing depat na kaku ning kekang ipus; milablab ing keang mua. 

Genesis <lbl>39:20</lbl> 	At dela ne ning keang guinu i Jose, at binili ne king sukulan, karinan a pikukulungan da ding makasukul ning ari: at karin ya king sukulan. 

Genesis <lbl>39:21 </lbl>	Dapot i GUINU atiu kang Jose, at pepakit na kea ing ganaka, at dininan neng kalam king panlalawe na ning katiwala king sukulan. 

Genesis <lbl>39:22</lbl> 	At pepanibala na ning katiwala king sukulan king gamat nang Jose ding anggang makasukul a atiu king sukulan: at ing anggang daraptan da karin, ya ing darapat. 	

Genesis <lbl>39:23</lbl> 	E na lalawan ning katiwala ning sukulan ing nanumang bague a atiu king keang gamat, uling i GUINU kayantabe ne; at ing keang daraptan, panuanan nang GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:1</lbl> 	At milyari pangaibat na ning bague a iti, king ing katiwala na ning ari king Egipto at ing keang mangawang tinape mikasala la salang king karelang guinu a ari king Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:2</lbl> 	At mikasbu ya i Faraon laban karing adua nang talapanibala, laban king pekapun da ding katiwala, at king pekapun da ding mangawang tinape. 

Genesis <lbl>40:3</lbl> 	At sinukul no king sukulan, king bale na ning capitan ding bante, king sukulan, a kesukulan nang Jose. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:4</lbl> 	At binie no ning capitan ding bante kang Jose, at ya ing memajala karela: at menuknangan lang ditak a panaun king sukulan. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:5</lbl> 	At ila parapara lang meninap, ing balang katau king keang paninap, king misan a bengi, ing balang katau agpang king kasalesean na ning keang paninap, ing katiwala at ing mangawang tinape ning ari Egipto, mung ninu ding makasukul king sukulan. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:6</lbl> 	At i Jose pintalan nala panga abak, at ikit nala, at, oreni, malungkut la. 

Genesis <lbl>40:7</lbl> 	At kitnan nala ding talapanibala nang Faraon a kayabe na king sukulan king bale na ning keang guinu, a sinabi na, Baket malungkut kong akakit ku ngening aldo iti? 	

Genesis <lbl>40:8</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea, Meninap kaming metung a paninap, at ala ninumang makapalino. At sinabi na karelang Jose, E wari king Dios ing pamipalino? Ipagamuamu ku kekayu, a salesean yu kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:9</lbl> 	At ing pekapun ding katiwala selese na kang Jose ing keang paninap, at sinabi na kea, King kakung paninap, oini, ing kapun a wake king arapan ku; 	

Genesis <lbl>40:10</lbl> 	At king pun na ning wake ating atlung sanga: at deti anti lang mamuku, at lalsut la ding sampaga na; at ding sapunggul na pesipamunga lang uvas a malulut: 	

Genesis <lbl>40:11</lbl> 	At ing copa nang Faraon atiu king kakung gamat; at kinanua ku karing uvas, at pisla kula king copa nang Faraon, at binie ke ing copa king gamat nang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:12</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose kea, oini ing kalinawan na nita: ding atlung sanga atlu lang aldo;

Genesis <lbl>40:13</lbl> 	King lub ning atlung aldo italakad neng Faraon ing kekang buntuk, at isubli naka king kekang katungkulan: at ibie me ing copa nang Faraon king keang gamat, anti mo ing sadia mung daraptan kanitang katiwala naka. 

Genesis <lbl>40:14</lbl> 	Dapot ganakan muku panga mipakayap na ka, at pagamuamu ku keka, at pakitanan mukung mayap a lub, at saglawayan muku kang Faraon, at ilako muku king bale a iti: 	

Genesis <lbl>40:15</lbl> 	Uling tune a aku penako raku king labuad da ding Hebreos: at keti naman ala kung daraptan nanuman bang ibili raku king sukulan. 

Genesis <lbl>40:16</lbl> 	Inyang akit na ning pekapun da ding magtitinape king mayap a pangapalino, sinabi na kang Jose, Aku meninap ku naman, at, oini, atlung salikap a tinape maputi atilu king babo na ning buntuk ku: 	

Genesis <lbl>40:17</lbl> 	At king kabababawan ning salikap ating sarisaring pamangan a linutu ding mangawang tinape dikil kang Faraon; at pengan da ding ayup ing king salikap a atiu king babo kung buntuk. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:18</lbl> 	At i Jose mekibat ya at sinabi na, Oini ing kalinawan na nita: Ding atlung salikap atlu lang aldo; 	

Genesis <lbl>40:19</lbl> 	King lub ning atlung aldo italakad neng Faraon ing kekang buntuk, bang ilako keka, at ibitin naka king metung a pun ning dutung; at kanan da ding ayup ing kekang laman. 

Genesis <lbl>40:20</lbl> 	At milyari inyang katlung aldo, ya ing aldo a kebaitan nang Faraon, guinawa yang metung a pamagtau karing anggang ipus na: at telakad ne king libutad ding keang ipus ing buntuk na ning pekabuntuk da ding katiwala, at ing buntuk na ning pekapun ding mangawang tinape. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:21</lbl> 	At sibli ne ing pekabuntuk da ding katiwala king keang pangakatiwala; at pasibayu binie ne ing copa king gamat nang Faraon: 

Genesis <lbl>40:22</lbl> 	Dapot ing pekabuntuk da ding magtitinape binitin ne: anti mo ing pepalino na karelang Jose. 	

Genesis <lbl>40:23</lbl> 	Makanian man e ne aganaka i Jose ning pekabuntuk ding katiwala, nung e akalinguan ne. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:1</lbl> 	At milyari king kapupusan na ning aduang banuang ganap, i Faraon meninap ya: at, oini, makatalakad ya king lele ning ilug. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:2</lbl> 	At, oreni, sinaka la king ilug ding pitung vaca, masanting la anyu at mataba laman; at mamangan la king katalaiban. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:3</lbl> 	At, oreni, ding aliwang pitung vaca sinaka la king ilug king gugulutan da, maitsura ing karelang anyu at payat ing karelang laman, at tinuknang la king siping da ding minunang vaca king lele ning ilug. 

Genesis <lbl>41:4</lbl> 	At ding vacang maitsura anyu at payat a laman liklak dala ding pitung vacang masanting a anyu at mataba. Kanita miguising ya i Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:5</lbl> 	At ya metudtud ya at meninap yang kaduang ukdu: at, oreni, ding pitung pinusu a mangataba at mangayap, a linsut king metung muring tangke. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:6</lbl> 	At, oreni, ding pitung pinusu a payat at papaspas na ning angin king aslagan, pesitubu lang makatuki karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:7</lbl> 	At ding pitung pinusung payat pengan dala ding pitung pinusung mataba at mitmu. At miguising ya i Faraon, at, oini, metung mung paninap. 

Genesis <lbl>41:8</lbl> 	At milyari king kamamaranunan ing keang espiritu melingasngas ya; at mitubud ya at pepayaus nala ding anggang magos king Egipto, at ding anggang biasa karin: at selese nang Faraon karela ing keang paninap; dapot alang makapalino kang Faraon. 

Genesis <lbl>41:9</lbl> 	Kanita miniabi ya ing pekabuntuk ding katiwala kang Faraon, a sinabi na, Aganaka ku king aldo iti ing kanakung kasalanan: 	

Genesis <lbl>41:10</lbl> 	Mikasbu ya i Faraon tungkul karing keang ipus, at pepasukul daku king bale na ning capitan ding bante, aku at ing pekabuntuk da ding mangawang tinape: 	

Genesis <lbl>41:11</lbl> 	At meninap kami king paninap king misan a bengi, aku at ya; meninap keng adua agpang king kalinawan ning kekeng paninap. 

Genesis <lbl>41:12</lbl> 	At atiu karin kayabe mi ing metung a kayanakan, metung yang Hebreo, ipus ne ning capitan ding bante; at ya ing kekeng selitanan, at ya pepalino na kekami ing kekeng paninap; at pepalino na king balang metung agpang king keang apaninap. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:13</lbl> 	At milyari, nung makananu ing binie nang kalinawan kekami makanian ing mepalyari; aku pepabalikan daku king kakung katungkulan, at ya pepabitin de. 

Genesis <lbl>41:14</lbl> 	Kanita i Faraon mitubud ya at pepayaus ne i Jose, at liwal deng mirarapal king sukulan: at menurud ya at mibablas, at mine ya kang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:15</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon kang Jose, Meninap kung metung a paninap, at alang makapalino: at dimdam ku ing sabi tungkul keka a pamanamdam mu king metung a paninap a pepalino mu. 

Genesis <lbl>41:16</lbl> 	At mekibat ya i Jose kang Faraon, a sinabi na, Ala kanaku: ing Dios ya ing munie pakibat a kapayapan kang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:17</lbl> 	At selita nang Faraon kang Jose, King kakung paninap, oini, makatalakad ku king siping ning ilug:

Genesis <lbl>41:18</lbl> 	At, oini, sinaka la king ilug ding pitung vaca, a mangataba laman at mangasanting a anyu; at mamangan la king katalaiban: 

Genesis <lbl>41:19</lbl> 	At, oreni, ding aliwang pitung vaca a sasaka king gugulutan da, payat la at mipakaitsura ing anyu ra at payat la laman, kapilan man e ku mekakit king mabilug nang labuad ning Egipto a kalupa ra deta king dewakan: 

Genesis <lbl>41:20</lbl> 	At pengan do ding pitung vacang payat at maitsura ding pitung vacang mumuna a mangataba: 

Genesis <lbl>41:21</lbl> 	At inyang apangan dala, malyaring matalastas ing pangapangan da; dapot ing karelang anyu maitsura murin anti mo ing sadia. Kanita miguising ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:22</lbl> 	At ikit ku naman king paninap ku, at, oreni, ding pitung pinusu linsut la king metung muring tangke, mangataba la at mangayap: 

Genesis <lbl>41:23</lbl> 	At, oreni, ding pitung pinusu, malangi, payat, at papaspas no ning angin king aslagan, tinubu lang katuki ra deti: 

Genesis <lbl>41:24</lbl> 	At ding pitung pinusung payat pengan do ding pitung pinusung mayap: at kakung selese karing magos; at alang makapabalu kanaku kaniti. 

Genesis <lbl>41:25</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose kang Faraon, Ing paninap nang Faraon metung mu: nung nanu ing ume nang daptan na ning Dios pepabalu na kang Faraon. 

Genesis <lbl>41:26</lbl> 	Ding pitung vacang mangasanting pitu lang banua; at ding pitung pinusung mayap pitu lang banua: ing paninap metung mu. 

Genesis <lbl>41:27</lbl> 	At ding pitung vacang payat at maitsura a sasakang tutuki king gugulutan da deti pitu lang banua, at anti murin ding pitung pinusung alang laman a papaspas na ning angin king aslagan; maguing pitung banuang danup. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:28</lbl> 	Iti ing bague a sinabi ku kang Faraon: nung nanu ing ume nang daptan na ning Dios pepakilala na kang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:29</lbl> 	Oini, datang ing pitung banuang maragul a kabsi king mabilug nang labuad ning Egipto: 	

Genesis <lbl>41:30</lbl> 	At karin salisi, panga-ibat na nita ing pitung banuang danup; at ing mabilug a kabsi makalinguan king gabun na ning Egipto; at ing danup lipulan na ing labuad; 

Genesis <lbl>41:31</lbl> 	At ing kabsi e na mabalu king labuad king sangkan uli ning danup a tuki; uling binang tutung maragul. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:32</lbl> 	At tungkul king panga-adua ning paninap kang Faraon, uling iting bague telaga na ning Dios, at parapat nang malagawa ning Dios. 

Genesis <lbl>41:33</lbl> 	Ngeni pin manintun ya i Faraon metung a taung maisip at biasa, at ibili ne king labuad na ning Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:34</lbl> 	Ipaintulut nasang daptan na iting Faraon, at malal yang talapanibala king labuad, at kuanan na ing kalimang dake ning labuad na ning Egipto king lub ning pitung banuang kabsi. 

Genesis <lbl>41:35</lbl> 	At karelang tipunan ing anggang pamangan kaniting mangayap a banuang daratang, at mikamalig king trigo king kayupayan na ning gamat nang Faraon a maguing pamangan da ding ciudades, at isimpan da. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:36</lbl> 	At ing pamangan a mikamalig dikil king labuad king pitung banuang danup, a mapalyari king gabun na ning Egipto; bang ing labuad e mate king danup. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:37</lbl> 	At ing kabagayan meyapan nang Faraon karing keang mata, at karing mata ra ding anggang keang ipus. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:38</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon karing keang ipus, Makakit ta pa wari a aliwang anti ini, taung pakasautan na ning Espiritu ning Dios? 	

Genesis <lbl>41:39</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon kang Jose, Anti na ning pepabalu na keka ning Dios ing sablang bague a iti, alang maisip o biasa mang anti ika: 

Genesis <lbl>41:40</lbl> 	Ika ing magpun king kakung bale, at agpang king kekang amanu makanian mung pamajalan ing balayan ku: king luklukan mung ari karin ku mu bukud maguing matas keka. 

Genesis <lbl>41:41</lbl> 	At sinabi na pang Faraon kang Jose, Oini, aku binili raka king mabilug a labuad ning Egipto. 

Genesis <lbl>41:42</lbl> 	Kanita i Faraon leko ne ing singsing na king keang gamat, at binili ne king gamat nang Jose, at pepasuluran ne king imalan a lienzong masinsin, at pepasulud ne king keang batal ing metung a talikalang guintu. 

Genesis <lbl>41:43</lbl> 	At pepasakayan ne king kadua nang carro a atiu kea; at kukulait da king keang arapan, Isiklaud la ding tud: at inalal deng pekapun king mabilug nang labuad ning Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:44</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon kang Jose, Aku i Faraon, at nung ala ka e ne itas ning tau ing keang gamat o ing keang bitis king mabilug a labuad ning Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:45</lbl> 	At pemalaguiuwan neng Faraon i Jose Zapenat-panea; at binie neng asawa na i Asenat, a anak nang Potifar a sacerdote king On. At linual ya i Jose king labuad na ning Egipto. 

Genesis <lbl>41:46</lbl> 	At i Jose atlu neng pulung banua tua kanitang tinalakad ya king arapan nang Faraon a ari Egipto. At meko ya i Jose king arapan nang Faraon, at libutan na ing mabilug nang labuad ning Egipto. 

Genesis <lbl>41:47</lbl> 	At memunga ing gabun king lub ning pitung banua ning kabsi. 

Genesis <lbl>41:48</lbl> 	At tinipun na ing anggang pamangan king lub ning pitung banua a atiu king gabun na ning Egipto, at sininup na ing pamangan karing ciudad: ing pamangan king marangle, a makapatulug king balang ciudad, at sininup na king bala muring ciudad a ita. 

Genesis <lbl>41:49</lbl> 	At i Jose mikamalig yang trigo a anti mong balas king dayatmalat, mipakarakal, angga king e na mabilang; uling alang bilang. 

Genesis <lbl>41:50</lbl> 	At bayu dinatang ing banuang danup penganak no kang Jose ding aduang lalaki, a ayanak na kang Asenat, a anak nang Potifar, a sacerdote king On. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:51</lbl> 	At pemalaguiuwan neng Jose ing pangane Manases: Uling, sinabi na, Pepakalinguan na kanaku ning Dios ing sabla kung kapagalan at ing mabilug nang bale ning kakung ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:52</lbl> 	At ing pemalaguiu na king kadua Efraim: Uling aku pepalabung naku ning Dios king gabun ning kakung kasakitan.

Genesis <lbl>41:53</lbl> 	At ing pitung banuang kabsi, a atiu king Egipto mepupus na. 

Genesis <lbl>41:54 </lbl>	At ing pitung banuang danup migmulang dinatang, agpang king sinabi nang Jose: at mika danup king mabilug a labuad; dapot king mabilug nang labuad ning Egipto ating tinape. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:55</lbl> 	At kanitang ing mabilug nang labuad ning Egipto meranup, dinalung ing balayan kang Faraon tungkul king tinape: at sinabi nang Faraon karing anggang tau Egipto, Ume ko kang Jose; ing sabian na kekayu, ya ing kekong daptan. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:56</lbl> 	At ing danup atiu king babo na ning mabilug a labuad: at biklat nong Jose ding sablang kamalig, at misali ya karing tau Egipto; uling miraragdag ing danup king labuad ning Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>41:57</lbl> 	At ding anggang balen mine la Egipto kang Jose balang manyaling trigo, uling miraragdag ing danup king mabilug a labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:1</lbl> 	Ngeni ikit nang Jacob king ating trigo king Egipto, at sinabi nang Jacob karing keang anak, Baket milalawayan kayu ing metung at metung? 

Genesis <lbl>42:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Oini, kanakung dimdam king ating trigo karin Egipto: ume ko karin; at sali ko karin a maguing kekatamu; batang mie, at e tamu mate. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:3</lbl> 	At ding apulu nang kapatad Jose mine lang sinaling trigu karin Egipto.

Genesis <lbl>42:4</lbl> 	Dapot i Benjamin, a kapatad nang Jose, e ne tinubud Jacob a kayabe ra ding keang kapatad; uling ngana, Magkang sakaling ating malyari keang nanumang kapanganiayan.

Genesis <lbl>42:5</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Israel mine la karin a sinaling kayabe ra ding anggang mame karin: uling mikakadanup king labuad na ning Canaan. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:6</lbl> 	At i Jose ya ing gobernador king labuad; ya ing misasali karin sablang balayan king labuad. At dinatang la ding kapatad nang Jose, at memagsakab la king arapan na a ding karelang lupa makasubsub la king labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>42:7</lbl> 	At ikit nong Jose ding keang kapatad, at kea lang akilala, dapot migkanuaring aliwa ya karela, at ya pekisabian no king guilas; at sinabi na karela, Nuko menibatan? At ila sinabi ra, King labuad na ning Canaan bang saling pamangan. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:8</lbl> 	At akilala nong Jose ding keang kapatad, dapot ya e re balu. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:9</lbl> 	At aganaka nang Jose ing paninap a keang apaninap tungkul karela, at karela sinabi na, Tiktik kayu; bang lawan yu ing kalubasan na ning labuad inya mine ko keti. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:10</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea, Ali, guinu ku, nung e ding kekang talasuyu mine la keti balang saling pamangan. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:11</lbl> 	Ike ngan anak nakami mu ning metung mung lalaki; ikami tau keng tapat, ding kekang talasuyu e la tiktik. 

Genesis <lbl>42:12</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela, Ali, nung e bang lawan yu ing kalubasan ning labuad inya mine ko keti. 

Genesis <lbl>42:13</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Ikeng talasuyu mu labi keng aduang lalaking mikakapatad, anak nakami ning metung mung lalaki king gabun na ning Canaan; at, oini, ing bungsu atiu kang ibpa mi ngeni, at ing metung ala na yu. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:14</lbl> 	At sinabi na karelang Jose, Yan ing sinabi ku kekayu, ngana, Tiktik kayu: 	

Genesis <lbl>42:15</lbl> 	Kaniti rako asubuk: alangalang king bie nang Faraon e ko mako keti, nung e ya ume keti ing kekong kapatad a bungsu. 

Genesis <lbl>42:16</lbl> 	Itubud ye ing metung kekayu, at idala ne keti ing kekong kapatad, at ikayu masukul kayu, bang masubuk ing kekong amanu, nung katutuan kekayu: o nung ali alangalang king bie nang Faraon tiktik kayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:17</lbl> 	At kea la ngang binili a miabeabe king sukulan atlung aldo. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:18</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose karela king katlung aldo, Daptan yu iti, at mie kayu; uling tatakut ku king Dios: 

Genesis <lbl>42:19</lbl> 	Nung tau kong tapat malakuan ya ing metung kekayung mikakapatad a makasukul king bale a pisukulan kekayu; dapot ume kayu, dalan yu ing trigo dikil king danup karing kekong katubale:

Genesis <lbl>42:20</lbl> 	At dalan ye kaku ing kekong kapatad a bungsu; kaniti makilala ing kekong amanu, at e ko mangamate. At karelang depatan a makanian. 

Genesis <lbl>42:21</lbl> 	At misabisabi la ing metung at metung, Katutuan king mikasala tamu a laban king kekatang kapatad, uling ikit tamu ing kalungkutan na ning keang kaladua, kanitang magamuamu ya kekatamu, at e taya pekiramdaman; inya daratang kekatamu ing kalungkutan a iti. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:22</lbl> 	At i Ruben mekibat ya karela, ngana, E ku wari sinabi kekayu, ngaku, E ko mikakasala salang king anak; at e yu pakiramdaman? inya naman, oiti, ing keang daya mandalum. 	

Genesis<lbl> 42:23</lbl> 	At e ra balu king ila atalastas nong Jose; uling ating talapanalese karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:24</lbl> 	At ya kinawani ya karela, at kiniak ya; at ya mibalik ya karela, at pekisabian nala, at kinua ne karela i Simeon, at telian ne king arapan da ding karelang mata. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:25</lbl> 	Kanita inutus nang Jose king katmuan dala ding karelang bayung king trigo, at ibalik ko ding salapi ning balang metung karing karelang bayung, at dinan dong pamangan king dalan: at depatan da karelang makanian. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:26</lbl> 	At pepapusanan dong trigo ding karelang asno, at meko la a ibat karin. 

Genesis <lbl>42:27</lbl> 	At pamamuklat ning metung karela king keang bayung baneng dinan pamangan ing keang asno king pipanlayunanan, ikit no ding keang salapi; at oreni, atilu king labi na ning bayung. 

Genesis <lbl>42:28</lbl> 	At sinabi na karing keang kapatad, Ding salapi ku misubli la; at, oreni, atilu king kakung bayung: at kinutug ing karelang pusu, at milalawayan la a gagalgal, ngara, Nanu iting depatan na ning Dios kekatamu? 	

Genesis <lbl>42:29</lbl> 	At dinatang la kang Jacob a karelang ibpa king labuad na ning Canaan, at selita ra kea ing anggang milyari karela, a sinabi ra, 

Genesis <lbl>42:30</lbl> 	Ing lalaki, a guinu king labuad a ita, pekisabian nakaming maguilas, at binilang nang anti keng tiktik king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:31</lbl> 	At sinabi mi kea, Ikami tau keng tapat; e ke tiktik:

Genesis <lbl>42:32</lbl> 	Ikami labi keng aduang lalaking mikakapatad, a anak ning kekeng ibpa: ing metung ala na yu, at ing bungsu atiu king kekeng ibpa ngeni king labuad na ning Canaan. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:33</lbl> 	At sinabi na kekami ning lalaki, a guinu king labuad, Kaniti ku akilala king ikayu tau kong tapat: milakuan ko kanakung metung karing kekong kapatad, at pasipagdala kong trigo tungkul king danup karing kekong katubale, at mako kayu;

Genesis <lbl>42:34</lbl> 	At dalan ye keti kanaku ing kekong kapatad a bungsu: nung makanian akilala ku king e ko tiktik, nung e ikayu tau kong tapat: kaniti isubli ke kekayu ing kekong kapatad, at maglakbe kayu king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:35 </lbl>	At milyari inyang ilako ra ing laman na ning karelang bayung, king, oini, balang metung makabili la ding salapi rang makabalut karing karelang bayung: at inyang ila at ing karelang ibpa akit dala ding karelang salaping makabalut, mengatakutan la. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:36</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela ning karelang ibpa a i Jacob, Leko yu no kanaku ding kakung anak: i Jose ala na yu, at i Simeon ala na yu, at ilako ye pa i Benjamin: ing sablang bague a iti salang kanaku. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:37</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Ruben king keang ibpa, ngana, Ipapate mula ding adua kung anak, nung warit ya e ke dalan keka: Ibie me king kakung gamat, at ya kaku yang ibalik keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>42:38</lbl> 	At sinabi na, E ya mako ing kanakung anak a kayabe yu: uling ing keang kapatad mete ne, at ya na mu ing mitagan: nung malyari kea ing nanumang kapanganyayan king dalan ning kekong ayan, kanita idala yu pin ing kakung uban king kutkutan a ating lungkut. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:1</lbl> 	At ing danup maragul king labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>43:2</lbl> 	At milyari, pangaguisan na ning trigong dele ra a ibat Egipto, a sinabi na karela ning karelang ibpa, Mibalik kayu, sali kong ditak a pamangan tungkul kekatamu. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:3</lbl> 	At i Juda miniabi ya kea, ngana, Ing lalaki miniabi yang masaklo kekami, ngana, E ye akit ing kakung lupa, subali nung ituki ye ing kekong kapatad. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:4</lbl> 	Nung patukian ye kekami ing kekeng kapatad, ume kami at isali rakang pamangan: 

Genesis <lbl>43:5</lbl> 	Dapot nung e me patuki, e ke ume; uling sinabi na kekami ning lalaking ita, E ye pakikitan ing kakung lupa, subali nung ituki ye ing kekong kapatad. 

Genesis <lbl>43:6</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Israel, Baket diptananan yukung marawak, a kekong sinabi king lalaki king atin ko pang aliwang kapatad? 	

Genesis <lbl>43:7</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Kitnan nakami ning lalaki king lubus a pamaniasat dikil kekami, at dikil karing kekeng kamaganakan, ngana, Mabie ya pa wari ing kekong ibpa? atin ko pang aliwang kapatad? at sinabi mi kea agpang king anti kaniting pangasalese: e mi kamalayan a sabian nang, Ituki ye keti ing kekong kapatad? 	

Genesis <lbl>43:8</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Juda kang Israel a keang ibpa, Patukian me kanaku ing anak, at pasitalakad kami at ume; batang mie, at e mate, ikami, at ika, at makanian mu naman ding kekeng mangalating anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:9</lbl> 	Aku ing makibat kea; king kanakung gamat karin me panintunan: nung e ke ibalik keka, at ibili king arapan mu, kanita pusanan ku ing kasalanan keka angga king kapilan pa man: 

Genesis <lbl>43:10</lbl> 	Uling nung e tamu migluat, mekapibalik na keng makaladua. 

Genesis <lbl>43:11</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela ning karelang ibpa a i Israel, Nung makanian ngeni, daptan yu iti: magdala kayu karing piling bunga niting labuad, at magdala kayung pagkalub king lalaki, ditak a balsamo, at ditak a pulut, pabanglu, at mirra, pili, at almendras; 	

Genesis <lbl>43:12</lbl> 	At magdala kayung makaladuang ukdu karakal a salapi king kekong gamat; at ding salaping misubli king asbuk da ding kekong bayung dalan yong pasibayu king kekong gamat; mekad pamagkamali mu: 	

Genesis <lbl>43:13</lbl> 	Ituki yuya naman ing kekong kapatad, at talakad kayu, at mibalik king lalaki: 	

Genesis <lbl>43:14</lbl> 	At pagkaluban nako ning Dios a Mayupaya king Sabla king kapakaluluan king arap na ning lalaking ita, baneng isubli kekayu ing metung yung kapatad at i Benjamin. At nung mawala la ding anak ku, mawala ku. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:15 </lbl>	At dela ra ding lalaki ing pagkalub, at makataduang ukdu karakal a salapi ing dela ra king karelang gamat, at i Benjamin; at pesi talakad la, at mine la Egipto, at minarap la kang Jose. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:16</lbl> 	At inyang ikit neng Jose i Benjamin a kayabe ra, sinabi na king katiwala king keang bale, Dalan mo deang lalaki king bale, at makamate ka, at magsadia ka; uling ding lalaki maugtu lang kasulu ku king ugtung aldo tapat. 

Genesis<lbl> 43:17</lbl> 	At depatan na ning lalaki ing agpang king inutus nang Jose; at dela nala ning lalaki king bale nang Jose. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:18</lbl> 	At ding lalaki mengatakutan la, uling dela no king bale nang Jose; at sinabi ra, Tungkul karing salapi a misubli karing kekatang bayung king minuna inya dela rakatamu keti; banang salesean kekatamu, at nakatamu, at gawan nakatang anti mong alipan, ampon ding kekatang asno. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:19</lbl> 	At pesilapit la king katiwala king bale nang Jose, at pekisabian de king pasbul ning bale, 	

Genesis <lbl>43:20</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Oh, guinu ku, katutuan king minuna a sinaling pamangan: 	

Genesis<lbl> 43:21 </lbl>	At milyari, inyang datang kami king paglayunanan, a biklat mila ding kekeng bayung, at, oini, atilu ding salapi ning balang metung king asbuk na ning bayung na, ding salapi mi king tune a timbang: at dela milang pasibayu karing kekeng gamat. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:22</lbl> 	At migdala keng aliwang salapi karing kekeng gamat bang isali ming pamangan: e mi balu nung ninung mibili karing salapi mi karing kekeng bayung. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:23</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Kapayapaan kekayu, a ko tatakut: ing Dios yu, at ing Dios na ning kekong ibpa, dininan nakong pibandian karing kekong bayung: tinggap kula ding kekong salapi. At liwal de i Simeon karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:24</lbl> 	At dela no ning lalaki ding lalaki king bale nang Jose, at dininan nong danum, at menuas lang bitis: at dininan dong pamangan ding karelang asno. 

Genesis<lbl> 43:25</lbl> 	At sidia ra ing pagkalub tungkul king pamaniatang nang Jose king kaugtuan aldo a tapat: uling karelang dimdam king karin la mangan tinape. 

Genesis <lbl>43:26</lbl> 	At inyang datang ya i Jose king bale, dela ro kea king bale ding pagkalub a atiu king karelang gamat, at migsakab la king labuad king arapan na. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:27</lbl> 	At kitnan nala tungkul king karelang bili, at sinabi na, Mayap ya ing kekong ibpa, ing matua a kekong sasabian? Mabie ya pa? 

Genesis <lbl>43:28</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Mayap ya ing kekang talasuyu a kekeng ibpa, mabie ya pa. At diku ro ding buntuc da, at guinalang. 

Genesis<lbl> 43:29</lbl> 	At linawe no ding keang mata, at ikit ne i Bejamin a kapatad na, a anak na ning keang indu, at sinabi na, Ini ya ing kekong kapatad a bungsu, a sinabi yu kanako? At sinabi na, Panuanan naka ning Dios, anak ku. 

Genesis <lbl>43:30</lbl> 	At mirarapal ya i Jose; uling milalablab ing keang lub tungkul king keang kapatad: at menintun yang karinan a apikiakan na, at linub ya king keang silid, at kiniak ya karin. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:31</lbl> 	At menimu ya, at linual; at mengawat yang lub, at sinabi na, Iyapag yu ing pamangan. 	

Genesis <lbl>43:32</lbl> 	At minapag lang makakawani dikil kea, at dikil karing tau Egipto, a mengan a kayabe na, makabukud la: uling ding tau Egipto e la makapangan a kasulu ro ding Hebreos; uling kasumasumami iti karing tau Egipto. 

Genesis <lbl>43:33</lbl> 	At ila pesilukluk la king arapan na, ing pangane tungkul king keang pangapangane, at ing bungsu tungkul king keang pangabungsu: at ding lalaki migmulala la ing metung at metung. 

Genesis <lbl>43:34</lbl> 	At ila dimput no king arapan na king ulam dikil karela; dapot ing pamangan nang Benjamin maiguit makatalimang ukdu king dake na ning ninuman karela. At mininum la, at mekikatula la kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:1</lbl> 	At inutus na king katiwala na ning keang bale, ngana, Katmuan mula king pamangan ding bayung da ding lalaki, nung nu anti ing karelang adala, at ibili mula ding salapi king asbuk na ning bayung na ning balang metung karela. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:2</lbl> 	At ibili me ing kakung copa, ing copang pilak, king asbuk na ning bayung ning bungsu, at ding salapi ning keang trigo. At depatan na ing makaagpang king amanu nang Jose. 

Genesis <lbl>44:3</lbl> 	At kabukasan inyang sasala na, pepalakuan na nala ding lalaki, ila at ding karelang asno. 

Genesis <lbl>44:4</lbl> 	At inyang milual no king ciudad, at e la pa makarayu, sinabi nang Jose king keang katiwala, Mibangun ka, tagalan mula ding lalaki; at pangadisan mula, sabian mu karela, Baket inablas yu ing dewakan king kayapan? 	

Genesis<lbl> 44:5</lbl> 	E wari iti ing pinuman na ning kakung guino, at tune ya ing keang panula? Ikayu dinapat kong marawak king depatan yung yan. 	

Genesis<lbl> 44:6</lbl> 	At kea lang disan, at sinabi na karela ing amanung iti. 

Genesis <lbl>44:7</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea, Baket sasabian na ning guinu ku ing amanung anti iti? Marayu a daptan da ding kekang alipan ing anti kaniang bague. 

Genesis <lbl>44:8</lbl> 	Oreni, ding salapi, a ikit mi king asbuk ding kekeng bayung dela milang pasibayu keka ibat king labuad na ning Canaan: makananu keng manako king bale na ning kekang guinu king pilak o guintu? 	

Genesis <lbl>44:9</lbl> 	Itang kayakitanan karing kekang talasuyu, mate ya, at ike naman maguing alipan nakami ning kekeng guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:10</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Malyari pin ing agpang king kekong amanu: itang kayakitanan maguing alipan ke; at ikayu mayala kong kasalanan. 

Genesis <lbl>44:11</lbl> 	Kanita mirarapal ya, at kildas ne king gabun ning balang metung karela ing karelang bayung, at biklat ne ning balang lalaki ing keang bayung. 

Genesis <lbl>44:12 </lbl>	At keang penintun, at pigmulan na king pangane, at teuli na king bungsu: at ikit ne ing copa king bayung nang Benjamin. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:13</lbl> 	Kanita pinlaput da ing karelang imalan, at sekian ne ning balang metung ing keang asno, at mibalik la king ciudad. 

Genesis <lbl>44:14</lbl> 	At i Juda at ding keang kapatad mine la king bale nang Jose; at ya atiu pa karin: at ila migsakab la king gabun king arapan na. 	

Genesis<lbl> 44:15 </lbl>	At sinabi na karelang Jose, Nanung dapat ing kekong depatan? E yu wari balu king ing metung a tau a anti aku tune a makapanula ya? 

Genesis <lbl>44:16</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Juda, Nanu ing sabian mi king kakung guinu? nanu ing salesean mi? o makananu keng patutu? Ikit ning Dios ing dewakan da ding kekang talasuyu: oini, ikami alipan nake ning kekeng guinu, ikami, anti naman ing keakitanan king copa. 

Genesis <lbl>44:17</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Marayu a dapat ku king makanian: ing taung keakitanan king copa, ya ing maguing kakung alipan; dapot dikil kekayu, ume kong payapa king kekong ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:18</lbl> 	Kanita linapit ya i Juda kea, at sinabi na, Oh, guinu ku, tulutan me ing kekang talasuyu, pagamuamu ku keka, a miniabi ya metung a amanu king daramdaman na ning kanakung guinu, at e sa mikaluku ing keang lub salang king kekang talasuyu; uling ika anti ka mo i Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:19</lbl> 	Kitnan no ning guinu ku ding keang talasuyu, ngana, Atin kong ibpa o metung a kapatad? 

Genesis <lbl>44:20 </lbl>	At sinabi mi king kekeng guinu, Ikami atin keng ibpa, metung yang matua, at metung a anak king keang ketuan, metung yang bungsu; at ing keang kapatad mete ya, at ya mu ing akalakuanan na ning keang indu; at kaluguran ne ning keang ibpa. 

Genesis <lbl>44:21</lbl> 	At sinabi mu karing kekang talasuyu, Dalan ye keti kanaku, bakong alawe ding kakung mata kea. 

Genesis <lbl>44:22</lbl> 	At sinabi mi king kekang guinu, E ne alakuan ning anak ing keang ibpa: uling nung lakuan ne ing keang ibpa, i ibpa na mate ya. 

Genesis <lbl>44:23</lbl> 	At sinabi mu karing kekang talasuyu, E yu ne pakikitan ing kakung lupa, subali nung ituki ye keti ing kekong kapatad a bungsu. 

Genesis <lbl>44:24</lbl> 	At milyari inyang datang kami king kekang talasuyu a kakung ibpa, ke kaming selita ing amanu na ning kakung guinu. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:25</lbl> 	At sinabi ning kekeng ibpa, Mibalik kayu, sali kayu tungkul kekatamu ditak a pamangan. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:26</lbl> 	At sinabi mi, E ke milako: nung ing kekeng bungsung kapatad kayabe miya mako kami: uling e mi e pakikitan ing lupa na ning lalaking ita subali nung ing kapatad ming bungsu kayabe miya. 

Genesis <lbl>44:27</lbl> 	At sinabi na kekami ning kekang talasuyu a kekeng ibpa, Pangabaluan yu king ing kakung asawa mikaanak ya kanaku a aduang lalaki:

Genesis <lbl>44:28</lbl> 	At ing metung meko ya kanaku, at sinabi ku, tune king mengapirasu ya; at e ku ne ikit ibat kanita: 	

Genesis <lbl>44:29</lbl> 	At nung kekayu ya pang kuanan kanaku ing metung a iti, at ating malyaring kapanganiayan kea, kekayung ikuldas ing kakung uban king Kutkutan king kalungkutan. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:30</lbl> 	Ngeni pin nung datang ku king kekang talasuyu a kakung ibpa, at ing anak e miya kayabe; uling ing keang bie makatali king bie na ning anak a yan; 	

Genesis <lbl>44:31</lbl> 	Malyari pin, nung keang akit a ing anak e miya kayabe, mate ya: at ikuldas da ding kekang talasuyu ing uban na ning kekang talasuyu a kekeng ibpa a ating kalungkutan king Kutkutan. 	

Genesis <lbl>44:32</lbl> 	Uling ing kekang talasuyu ya ing mengaku king anak king kakung ibpa, ngana, Nung e ke dalan keka, kanita pusanan ku pin ing kasalanan king kakung ibpa king kapilan pa man. 

Genesis <lbl>44:33</lbl> 	Ngeni pin, ipaintulut mu king ing kekang talasuyu, pagamuamu ku keka, malakuan ya a kalibe ning anak a peka alipan king kakung guinu; at kekang ipaintulut king ing anak sampa yang kayabe ra ding keang kapatad.

Genesis <lbl>44:34</lbl> 	Uling makananu kung ume king kanakung ibpa, nung ing anak e ke kayabe? magkang akit ku pa ing dewakan amiras king kakung ibpa. 

Genesis <lbl>45:1</lbl> 	Kanita i Jose e ya mekapangawat king arapan ding sabla a makatalakad king siping na, at guinulisak ya, Palakuan yula ding anggang tau king arapan ku. At alang taung tinalakad king siping na, kabang i Jose pekilala ya karing keang kapatad. 

Genesis <lbl>45:2</lbl> 	At ya kiniak yang masikan: at dimdam da ding tau Egipto, at dimdam na ning bale nang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:3</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose karing keang kapatad, aku i Jose; mabie ya mu ing kakung ibpa? At ding kapatad na e la makapakibat kea; uling magugulu la king keang arap. 

Genesis <lbl>45:4</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose karing keang kapatad, Lumapit kayu kanaku, pagamuamu ku kekayu. At linapit la. At sinabi na, Aku i Jose a kekong kapatad, a kekong pisali king Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:5</lbl> 	At ngeni e ko magsalbat, o mimua mu man king kekong sarili, king pisali yuku keti: uling pepabal naku ning Dios king arapan yu bang magligtas king bie. 

Genesis <lbl>45:6</lbl> 	Uling atin nang aduang banua ing danup king labuad: at atin pang limang banua, a e mika ating pamanasik, ni pamamupul man. 

Genesis <lbl>45:7</lbl> 	At pepabal naku ning Dios king kekong arapan barakong iligtas at mitagan pa keti king labuad, at iligtas dakong mabie king pamamilatan na ning maragul a pamanligtas. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:8</lbl> 	Inya ngeni aliwa pin ikayu ing pepabal kanaku keti, nung e ing Dios: at ya guewa nakung ibpa kang Faraon, at guinu king mabilug nang bale, at talapanibala ning mabilug a labuad ning Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:9</lbl> 	Mamirapal kayu, at ume ko king kakung ibpa, at sabian yu kea, Makanian ing sabi na ning kekang anak a i Jose, Guewa na kung guinu ning Dios king mabilug a Egipto: ume ka keni kaku, e ka magluat; 	

Genesis <lbl>45:10</lbl> 	At ika manuknangan ka king gabun ning Gosen, at milapit ka kaku, ika at ding kekang anak, at ding anak da ding kekang anak, at ding kekang kawan, at ding kekang vaca at ing mabilug mung kayatinan: 	

Genesis <lbl></lbl>45:11 	At karin pakanan daka; uling atin pang limang banuang danup; magkang makalulu ka, ika, at ing kekang katubale, at ing mabilug mung kayatinan. 

Genesis <lbl>45:12</lbl> 	At, oini, ding kekang mata akit da, at ding mata na ning kakung kapatad a i Benjamin, king ing kakung asbuk ya ing maniabi kekayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:13</lbl> 	At isalita yu kang ibpa ku ing anggang kaligayan ku keti king Egipto, at ing anggang ikit yu; at mamirapal kayu at ikuldas ye keti ing kakung ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:14</lbl> 	At kinaul ne king batal ing keang kapatad a i Benjamin, at kiniak ya; at i Benjamin kiniak ya king babo na ning keang batal. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:15</lbl> 	At ya inuma nala ding anggang kapatad na, at kiniakan nala: at pangaibat nita ding kapatad na mekipagsalita la kea. 

Genesis <lbl>45:16</lbl> 	At ing kasalesayan a ita meramdam king bale nang Faraon, ngara. Dinatang la ding kapatad nang Jose: at meyapan nang Faraon, at ding keang ipus. 

Genesis <lbl>45:17</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon kang Jose, Sabian mu karing kekang kapatad, Iti daptan yu: papamusanan yula ding kekong animales, at ume kayu, muli ko king labuad na ning Canaan: 	

Genesis <lbl>45:18</lbl> 	At dalan ye ing kekong ibpa at ding kekong katubale, at ume ko keti kaku: at ibie ka kekayu ing pekamayap king labuad ning Egipto, at kanan yu ing taba ning gabun. 

Genesis <lbl>45:19</lbl> 	Ngeni miutus kekayu, iti daptan yu: kuma kayu karing karitun king labuad na ning Egipto tungkul karing kekong anak, at karing kekong asawa, at idala ye ing kekong ibpa, at ume ko keti. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:20</lbl> 	Makanian mu naman e yu gaganakan ing kekong pibandian; uling ing anggang mayap king gabun na ning Egipto kekayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:21</lbl> 	At depatan dang makanian ding anak nang Israel: at i Jose dininan nong karitun, agpang king utus nang Faraon, at dininan nong apangan da king dalan. 

Genesis<lbl> 45:22</lbl> 	Ila ngan dininan nong piblasan; dapot i Benjamin dininan neng atlung dalan a kapising pilak at lima kapiblas a imalan. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:23</lbl> 	At kang ibpa na peparala yang anti kanining kayayusan: apulung asnong maki pupusanan mangayap a bague ning Egipto, at apulung asnong babai a maki pusan a trigo at tinape at pamangan ning keang ibpa king dalan. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:24</lbl> 	Makanian nong pepalakuan ding keang kapatad, at meko la: at sinabi na karela, Lawan yu king e ko sa mababaldug king dalan. 

Genesis <lbl>45:25</lbl> 	At sinampa lang ibat Egipto, at mine la king labuad na ning Canaan, kang Jacob a karelang ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>45:26</lbl> 	At selita ra kea, ngara, I Jose mabie ya pa, at pun ya king mabilug a labuad ning Egipto. At ing keang pusu mengalambut ya, uling e no paniwalan. 

Genesis <lbl>45:27</lbl> 	At selita ra kea ing sablang amanu nang Jose, a sinabi na karela: at inyang ikit nala ding karitun a peparala nang Jose bang pipagdalan da kea, ing espiritu nang Jacob a karelang ibpa mika diwa yang pasibayu: 

Genesis <lbl>45:28</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Israel, Makaguiu na; i Jose a kakung anak mabie ya pa: aku ume ku at pakikitan ke bayu ku mate. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:1</lbl> 	At i Israel miglakbe ya, pati na ing sablang atiu kea, at mine ya Beer-Seba, at dinaun yang ain king Dios na ning ibpa na a i Isaac. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:2</lbl> 	At pekisabian ne ning Dios i Israel king malikmata king bengi, at sinabi na, Jacob, Jacob. At ngana, Ati ku keni. 

Genesis <lbl>46:3</lbl> 	At sinabi na, aku ing Dios, ing Dios na ning kekang ibpa: e ka tatakut kuldas king Egipto; uling karin gawan dakang metung a maragul a bansa: 	

Genesis <lbl>46:4</lbl> 	Aku kuldas kung kayabe mu Egipto; at tune a isampa rakang pasibayu: at itumpak nong Jose ding kekang gamat karing keang mata. 

Genesis <lbl>46:5</lbl> 	At mibangun ya i Jacob ibat king Beer-Seba: at dela re ding anak nang Israel i Jacob a karelang ibpa, at ding karelang anak, at ding karelang asawa, karing karitun a peparala nang Faraon bang pinagdalan da kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:6</lbl> 	At dela rala ding karelang animales, at ing karelang pibandian, a tinipun da king labuad na ning Canaan, at mine la Egipto, i Jacob, at ing mabilug nang bini a kayabe na: 	

Genesis <lbl>46:7</lbl> 	Ding keang anak a lalaki, at ding anak dang lalaki ding anak nang lalaki kayabe nala, ding keang anak a babai, at ding anak dang babai ding anak nang lalaki, at ing keang mabilug a bini dela nang kayabe na Egipto. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:8</lbl> 	At oreti ding laguiu ra ding anak nang Israel, a mine Egipto, i Jacob at ding keang anak: i Ruben, a anak nang pangane Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:9</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Ruben: i Hanoc, at i Paliu, at i Hezron, at i Carmi. 

Genesis <lbl>46:10</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Simeon: i Jemuel, at i Jamin, at i Ohad, at i Jaquin, at i Zohar, at i Shaul a anak na ning metung a babaing Cananea. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:11</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Levi: i Gerson, i Cohat, at i Merari. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:12</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Juda: i Er, at i Onan, at i Sela, at i Perez, at i Zera; dapot i Er at i Onan mete la king labuad na ning Canaan. At ding anak nang Perez; i Hezron at i Hamul.
