Genesis <lbl>46:13</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Isacar: i Tola, at i Puva, at i Job, at i Simron. 

Genesis <lbl>46:14</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Zabulon: i Sered, at i Elon, at i Jahleel. 

Genesis <lbl>46:15</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang Lea, a penganak na kang Jacob king Padan-aram, ampon ing keang anak a babaing i Dina: ding anggang kaladua ra ding keang anak a lalaki at babai atlu lang pulu at atlu. 

Genesis <lbl>46:16</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Gad: i Zifion at i Hagui, i Suni, at i Hezbon, i Eri at i Arodi, at i Areli. 

Genesis <lbl>46:17</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Aser: i Imna, at i Isva, at i Isvi, at i Beria, at i Sera a karelang kapatad a babai: at ding anak nang Beria: i Heber, at i Malquiel. 	

Genesis<lbl> 46:18</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang Zilpa, a ya ing binie nang Laban kang Lea a keang anak a babai; at deti panganak no kang Jacob, labi lang anam a kaladua. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:19</lbl> 	Ding anak nang Raquel a asawa nang Jacob: i Jose at i Benjamin. 

Genesis <lbl>46:20</lbl> 	At kang Jose king labuad na ning Egipto, mibait la ri Manases at i Efraim, nung ninu i Asenat, a anak nang babaing Potifera, a sacerdote king On ayanak no kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:21</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Benjamin: i Bela, at i Bequer, at i Asbel, i Guera at Naaman, i Ehi, at i Ros, i Mupim, at i Hupim at i Ard. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:22</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang Raquel, a penganak na kang Jacob: ding sablang kaladua labi lang apat. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:23</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Dan: i Husim. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:24</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Neftali; i Jahzeel, at i Guni, at i Jezer, at i Silem. 

Genesis <lbl>46:25</lbl> 	Deti ilang anak nang Bilha, a binie nang Laban kang Raquel a keang anak, at deti ilang penganak na kang Jacob: ding anggang kaladua pitu la. 

Genesis <lbl>46:26</lbl> 	Ding anggang kaladua a tinuki kang Jacob karin Egipto, a linual king keang balakang, makabukud la pa ding asawa ra ding anak nang Jacob, ding sabla anam lang pulu at anam a kaladua; 	

Genesis <lbl>46:27</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Jose a penganak da kea king Egipto, adua lang kaladua: ding anggang kaladua king bale nang Jacob, a linub Egipto, pitu lang pulu. 

Genesis <lbl>46:28</lbl> 	At tinubud ne i Juda kang Jose a mumuna kea, bang turu king dalan king mumuna kea a tumuru king Gozen; at ila mine la king labuad ning Gozen. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:29</lbl> 	At pepasadia neng Jose ing keang carru, at sinampa yang selubungan ne i Israel a keang Ibpa, karin king Gozen; at inarap na ing sarili na kea, at kinaul ya king keang batal, at kiniak yang maluat king keang batal. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:30</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Israel kang Jose, Ngeni itulut mung mate na ku, yarin king ikit ku ne ing kekang lupa, king ika mabie ka pa. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:31</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose karing keang kapatad, at karing katubale na ning keang ibpa, Sampa ku, at salesean ku kang Faraon, at sabian ku kea, Ding kakung kapatad, at bale na ning kakung ibpa, a atiu king labuad na ning Canaan, mine la keti kanaku; 	

Genesis <lbl>46:32 </lbl>	At ding lalaki pastul la, uling ila meguing talapanibala lang animal; at dela ro ding karelang kawan, at ding karelang vaca at ing sabla rang kayatinan. 	

Genesis <lbl>46:33</lbl> 	At malyari, nung ausan nakong Faraon, at sabian na, Nanu ing kekong kapanintunan? 

Genesis <lbl>46:34</lbl> 	Sabian yu, Ding kekang talasuyu talapanibala lang kawan manibat pa king anak la angga ngeni, ikami at ding mangatua mi: bakong manuknangan king labuad ning Gozen; uling balang pastul makasumami ya karing tau Egipto.

Genesis <lbl>47:1</lbl> 	Kanita mine ya i Jose at selese na kang Faraon, at sinabi na, Ing kakung ibpa at ding kakung kapatad, at ding karelang kawan, at ding karelang vaca, at ing sablang atiu karela, dinatang lang menibat king labuad ning Canaan; at, oreni, atilu king labuad ning Gozen. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:2</lbl> 	At karing kayabe ra ding keang kapatad kinanua yang limang lalaki, at inarap no kang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:3</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon, karing keang kapatad, Nanu ing kekong kapanintuan? At sinabi ra kang Faraon, Ding kekang pastul pastul la, ikami ngan, anti naman ding mangatua mi. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:4</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kang Faraon, Mine ke keti bang manaliwang balen; uling ala lang apangan ding kawan da ding kekang talasuyu; uling ing danup maragul king labuad na ning Canaan; ngeni pin, pagamuamu mi keka, paintulutan mu la ding kekang talasuyu a manuknangan la king labuad na ning Gozen. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:5</lbl> 	At miniabi ya i Faraon kang Jose, ngana, Ing kekang ibpa at ding kekang kapatad mine la keti keka; 	

Genesis <lbl>47:6</lbl> 	Ing labuad na ning Egipto atiu king arapan mu; king pekamayap king labuad papanuknanganan me ing kekang ibpa at ding kekang kapatad; king labuad ning Gozen papanuknanganan mula; at nung atin kang akikilalang mayaguiung lalaki karela, papagpekapunan mula karing kakung animal. 

Genesis <lbl>47:7</lbl> 	At dela nong Jose i Jacob a keang ibpa, at likluk ne king arap nang Faraon: at pepanuanan neng Jacob i Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:8</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon kang Jacob, Pilan la ding aldo ra ding banua mu king kekang bie? 	

Genesis <lbl>47:9</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob kang Faraon, Ding aldo ra ding banua na ning pamanaliwa kung labuad dinalan at atlungpulung banua: ditak at mangarawak ing meguing aldo ra ding banua na ning kanakung bie, at e la miras karing aldo ra ding banua na ning bie ra ding kakung mangatua karing aldo na ning karelang pamanaliwang labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>47:10</lbl> 	At pepanuanan neng Jacob i Faraon, at meko ya king arap nang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:11</lbl> 	At binili nong Jose ing keang ibpa at ding keang kapatad, at dininan nong pibandian king labuad na ning Egipto, king pekamayap king labuad, king labuad na ning Rameses, anti mo ing inutus nang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:12</lbl> 	At pakanan neng Jose i ibpa na, at ding keang kapatad, at ing mabilug a katubale na ning keang ibpa, king tinape, agpang karing karelang katubale. 

Genesis <lbl>47:13</lbl> 	At alang tinape king mabilug a labuad; uling ing danup tutung makatakut, nanu pata in labuad na ning Egipto at ing labuad na ning Canaan mengalambut king uli ning danup. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:14</lbl> 	At tinipun nong Jose ding anggang salapi a penakitan king labuad na ning Egipto, at king labuad na ning Canaan, uling ning trigong seli ra: at linub nong Jose ding kualta king bale nang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:15</lbl> 	At kanitang megugul nala ding salapi king anggang labuad na ning Egipto, at king labuad na ning Canaan, ding anggang tau Egipto mine la kang Jose, at ngara, Dinan mukeng tinape: uling baket mangamate kami king kekang arapan? uling ding kekeng salapi meguisan la. 

Genesis <lbl>47:16</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose, Ibie yo ding kekong animal; at dinan dakayu king uli ra ding kekong animal, nung meguisan no ding salapi. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:17</lbl> 	At dela rala ding karelang animal kang Jose; at dininan nong tinape Jose a pekalibe karing kabayu, at karing kawan, at karing vaca, at karing asno: at pepakan nalang tinape king banuang ita a kalibe ra ding anggang animal da.

Genesis <lbl>47:18</lbl> 	At kanitang mepupus ing banuang ita, mine la kea king kaduang banua, at sinabi ra kea, E mi ilijim king kekeng guinu, nung makananung ding kekeng salapi meguisan la; at ding kawan ding animal ati na lu king kekeng guinu; ala nang mitagan king lalawan na ning kakung guinu, nung e ding kekeng katawan at ing kekeng gabun: 

Genesis <lbl>47:19</lbl> 	Baket mangamate kami king arapan da ding kekang mata, ikami at ing kekeng gabun? saliwan mu kami at ing kekeng gabun paipus kang Faraon: at dinan mukeng bini, bakeng mie, at eke mangamete, at ing gabun bang e masira. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:20</lbl> 	Makanian nang seling Jose ing mabilug a labuad na ning Egipto dikil kang Faraon; uling pisali na ning balang metung karing tau Egipto ing keang marangle, uling ing danup tutung makatakut karela: at ing labuad meguing kang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:21</lbl> 	At tungkul king balayan, inalis nala karing ciudad manibat king metung a kawakasan ning angganan ning Egipto angga king kasumangid a angganan. 

Genesis <lbl>47:22</lbl> 	Ing gabun damu ding sacerdotes yang e na asali: uling ding sacerdotes atin lang dake kang Faraon, at karelang kakanan ing karelang dake a babie na karelang Faraon; inya e ra pisali ing karelang gabun. 

Genesis <lbl>47:23</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi nang Jose king balayan Oini, seli rakayu king aldo a iti at ing kekong gabun dikil kang Faraon: oini, ing gawan yung bini, at sarulan yu ing gabun. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:24</lbl> 	At milyari king pamibangan, ibie yu ing kalimang dake kang Faraon, at ing apat a dake kekayu, dikil king bini na ning gabun, at king kekong pamangan, at karing kekong katubale, at pekapamangan da ding mangalati yung anak. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:25</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Kekang linigtas ing kekeng bie: itulut mung manakit keng kalam karing mata na ning kekeng guinu, at ikami maguing ipus nakeng Faraon. 

Genesis <lbl>47:26</lbl> 	At guewa nang tuntunan Jose ing gabun ning Egipto angga king aldo ngeni, king mike kang Faraon ing kalimang dake; subali mu ing gabun da ding sacerdotes a e mibie kang Faraon. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:27</lbl> 	At i Israel tinuknang ya king labuad na ning Egipto, king gabun ning Gozen; at ila mika atin lan pibandian karin, at tutung mapamunga at binang merakal. 

Genesis <lbl>47:28</lbl> 	At i Jacob menuknangan ya king labuad na ning Egipto labingpitung banua: inya ding meguing aldo nang Jacob, ding banua na ning keang bie, dinalan at apatapulu at pitung banua. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:29</lbl> 	At ing panaun lalapit king kamatayan nang Israel: at kea yang inaus ing anak nang i Jose, at sinabi na kea, Nung ngeni menakit kung kalam karing kekang mata, ipagamuamu ku keka, ibili me ing kekang gamat king lalam ning kakung puad, daptan mu kaku ing ganaka at katutuan: ipagamuamu ku keka a e mu ku kutkutkut keti Egipto. 

Genesis <lbl>47:30</lbl> 	Dapot pamanudtud ku a kayabe ra ding kakung mangatua, dalan muku manibat Egipto, at ikutkut muku king karelang kutkutan. At sinabi na, Daptan ku anti mo ing sinabi mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>47:31</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Sumpa ka kanaku: at sinumpa ya kea. At diku nang Israel ing sarili king kabuntukan naning keang pagkeran. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:1</lbl> 	At milyari pangaibat na ning bague iti, sinabi na ning metung kang Jose, Oini, ing kekang ibpa masakit ya: at tiki nala ding keang aduang anak i Manases at i Efraim. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:2</lbl> 	At ing metung sinabi na kang Jacob, at ngana, Oini, ayan naka ning anak mung Jose: at i Israel mibangun ya at linuknuk ya king pagkeran. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:3</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jacob kang Jose, Ing Dios a Mayupaya king Sabla pepakit ya kanaku king Luz king labuad na ning Canaan, at pepanuanan naku, 	

Genesis <lbl>48:4</lbl> 	At sinabi na kanaku, Oini, papamungan daka, at parakalan daka, at gawan dakang metung a kapamisanan da ding balayan, at kanakung ibie ing labuad a iti king kekang bini pangamate mu, a pekabandi kapilan man. 

Genesis <lbl>48:5</lbl> 	At ngeni ding kekang aduang anak a lalaki, a mibait king gabun ning Egipto bayu ku mine keti keka king Egipto, kaku la; i Efraim at i Manases, aguiang i Ruben at i Simeon maguing kaku la. 	

Genesis<lbl> 48:6</lbl> 	At ding kekang anak, a maguing anak mu kaibat da deti, maguing keka la; ila mayaus la king laguiu ra ding karelang kapatad a karelang mana. 

Genesis <lbl>48:7</lbl> 	At tungkul kanaku kanitang dinatang ku, a ibat Paddan, i Raquel mete ya kanaku king dalan king labuad na ning Canaan, a marayu pang ditak bayu ka datang king Efrata: at kitkut ke karin king dalan na ning Efrata (a ya murin ing Bethlehem) 

Genesis <lbl>48:8</lbl> 	At ikit nong Israel ding anak nang Jose, at sinabi na, Ninu deti? 	

Genesis <lbl>48:9</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose kang ibpa na, Anak kula, ilang binie na kanaku ning Dios keti. At sinabi na, Pagamuamu ku keka, king dalan mula, keni kaku, at panuanan kula. 

Genesis <lbl>48:10</lbl> 	Ngeni ding mata na ping Israel mapula la king uli ning ketuan, nanupata e ne makakit. At kea lang linapit kea; at inuma nala, at kinaul nala. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:11</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Israel kang Jose, E ku inisip a akit ke ing lupa mu: at oini, pepakit ne kanaku ning Dios pati na ding kekang bini. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:12</lbl> 	At kingua nong Jose king pilatan da ding keang tud; at ya dinuku ya at migsakab king labuad. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:13</lbl> 	At i Jose kinua nong parapara, i Efraim king keang wanan a gamat king nangan nang kailing Israel, at i Manases king kaili nang gamat king nangan nang wanan Israel, at linapit no kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:14</lbl> 	At inatyat neng Israel ing keang wanan a gamat, at timpak ne king buntuk nang Efraim, a ya ing wali, at ing keang kailing gamat king buntuk nang Manases, at patnubayan nong talaga ding keang gamat; uling i Manases ya ing pangane. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:15</lbl> 	At pepanuanan ne i Jose, at sinabi na, Ing Dios a king keang arapan linakad la ding mangatua ku a i Abraham at i Isaac, ing Dios a minie pamangan kanaku king mabilug kung bie angga king aldo ngeni, 	

Genesis <lbl>48:16</lbl> 	Ing angel a minatbus kanaku king anggang dewakan, panuanan nala ding anak; at itulut mung ausan dala king kakung laguiu, at king laguiu ra ding kakung mangatua a i Abraham at i Isaac; at dakal lang bina king libutad ning labuad. 

Genesis <lbl>48:17</lbl> 	At inyang akit nang Jose a timpak neng ibpa na ing wanan nang gamat king buntuk nang Efraim, e na meapan: at tinas ne ing gamat nang ibpa na, baneng ilipat king buntuk nang Manases manibat king buntuk nang Efraim. 

Genesis <lbl>48:18</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose kang ibpa na, E makanian, ibpa ku, uling ini ing pangane; itumpak me ing kekang wanan a gamat king keang buntuk. 

Genesis <lbl>48:19</lbl> 	At tinanggui ya i ibpa na, at sinabi na, Balu ku, kanakung anak, balu ku; ya man maguing metung yang balayan, at ya man maguing maragul ya: makanian man ing keang kapatad a wali maguing lalu yang maragul a maiguit kea, at ing keang bini maguing karaklan de ding bansa. 

Genesis <lbl>48:20</lbl> 	At pepanuanan nala king aldo a ita, ngana, King uli mu panuan ya i Israel, ngana, Gawan naka ning Dios anti mo i Efraim at anti mo i Manases: at binili ne i Efraim king mumuna nang Manases. 	

Genesis <lbl>48:21</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Israel kang Jose, Oini, aku mamamate ku: dapot ing Dios mantabe ya kekayu, at dalan nakong pasibayu king labuad da ding kekong mangatua. 	

Genesis<lbl> 48:22</lbl> 	Bukud kaniti dininan dakang metung a dake maiguit karing kekang kapatad, a kinua ku king kakung talibung at bai king gamat da ding Amoreo. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:1</lbl> 	At inaus nong Jacob ding keang anak, at sinabi na: Mitipun kayu, bang sabian ku kekayu ing mapalyari kekayu king tauling aldo. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:2</lbl> 	Mitipun kayu, at makiramdam, ikayu nang anak nang Jacob; At pakiramdaman ye i Israel a kekong ibpa. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:3</lbl> 	Ruben, ika ing kakung pangane, ing kakung kayupayan, at mula na ning kakung sikanan; Ing ulaga naning kamalan, at ing ulaga na ning kayupayan. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:4</lbl> 	Bubukal anti mong danum, e ka mika ating ulaga; Uling mine ka king pagkeran na ning kekang ibpa; Kanita dinatan me pin: sinampa ka king kakung pagkeran. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:5</lbl> 	I Simeon at i Levi mikapatad la; sandata lang pamigla ding karelang talibung. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:6</lbl> 	Oh kaladua ko, e ka lulub king karelang pulung; King karelang katipunan, kanakung kaligayan, e ka makiagum; Uling king mua ra mekamate lang tau, At king karelang kusang kaburian kinutud lang puad vaca. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:7</lbl> 	Misumpa ing karelang mua, uling mabangis At ing karelang pamikapali, uling mabagsik; Kaku lang pirakayan kang Jacob, At mikalat la king Israel. 

Genesis <lbl>49:8</lbl> 	Juda, purian daka ding kekang kapatad: Ding kekang gamat atilu king batal da ding kekang salang; Ding anak na ning kekang ibpa daku la king arapan mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:9</lbl> 	I Juda metung yang anak ning leon; Manibat king dakap, anak ku, talakad ka: Dinuku ya, miglugmuk yang anti mong leon, At anti ning metung yang leon a babai; ninung guinising kea? 	

Genesis <lbl>49:10</lbl> 	Ing cetro e ya kawani kang Juda, O ing tukud na man ning pengapekapun king pilatan da ding keang bitis, Angga king ing Siloe datang ya; At kea ing kapamintuan da ding balayan.

Genesis <lbl>49:11</lbl> 	At itali ne ing keang pollino king pun na ning wake, At ing biseru na ning asnang babai king pun na ning wake a pili; Pipian na ing susulud na king alak, 

Genesis <lbl>49:12</lbl> 	Ding keang mata lumutu la king alak, At ding keang ipan muti la king gatas. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:13</lbl> 	I Zabulon manuknangan ya king dungan na ning dayatmalat; At ya maguing dungan de ding daung; At ing keang angganan maguing angga king Sidon. 

Genesis <lbl>49:14</lbl> 	I Isacar metung yang masikan a asno, A maglugmuk ya king libutad da ding tupa: 

Genesis <lbl>49:15</lbl> 	At ikit na ing karinan pipainawan king ita mayap, At ing gabun king binang makayama; At diku ne ing keang pago bang mamusan, At meguing ipus ne ning talapaniapat. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:16 </lbl>	I Dan matul ya king keang balayan, Anti mong metung karing dai nang Israel. 

Genesis <lbl>49:17</lbl> 	I Dan maguing ubingan ya king dalan, At kamamalu king daklat, At kekeat king sakung da ding kabayu, Bang ing kea makasake mabaldug ya king gugulatan. 

Genesis <lbl>49:18</lbl> 	Kakung penaya ing kekang pamagligtas, Oh GUINU. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:19</lbl> 	I Gad, tagalan ne ning metung a tapuk; Dapot ya ing tagal karela. 

Genesis <lbl>49:20</lbl> 	Kang Aser ing tinape na maguing mataba ya, At ya midaun yang maniaman tungkul king panga-ari. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:21</lbl> 	I Neftali metung yang usang babaing makabulus: Babie yang mangasanting a amanu. 

Genesis <lbl>49:22</lbl> 	I Jose sanga yang mabunga, Sanga yang mabunga a atiu king siping ning bukal; Ding keang sanga gagapang la king babo kuta. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:23</lbl> 	Ding mamana melungkut la kea, At pinana re, at ligaligan de: 	

Genesis <lbl>49:24</lbl> 	Dapot ing keang bai manuknangan ya king sikanan, At ding takde ra ding keang gamat meguing masikan la, King pamamilatan da ding gamat na ning Mayupayang nang Jacob (A manibat karin ing pastul, ing batu ning Israel), 	

Genesis <lbl>49:25</lbl> 	King pamamilatan na ning Dios na ning kekang ibpa, a ya ing sumaup keka, At king pamamilatan na ning Mayupaya king Sabla ya ing panuan keka, King kanuanan na ning banua karin babo, Kanuanan ning kalalaman a makabili king mababa. Kanuanan da ding salu, at ding atian. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:26</lbl> 	Ing kanuanan ning kekang ibpa miniguit king kanuanan da ding kakung kanunuanan Angga king wakas da ding bundukbundukan a alang angga: Mibili la king buntuk nang Jose, At king bunbunan na ning keang buntuk a makakawani karing keang kapatad. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:27</lbl> 	I Benjamin metung yang lobo a manamsam: King kayabakan laklakan ne ing dakap, at pangagatpanapun pirakayan na ing mesamsam. 

Genesis <lbl>49:28</lbl> 	Ding sablang deti labi lang aduang dai nang Israel: at iti ya ing selese nang ibpa ra karela at pepanuanan nala; balang metung pepanuanan ne agpang king kenag kanuanan. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:29</lbl> 	At penabilin na karela at sinabi na karela, Aku miagum ku king kakung balayan: ikutkut yuku a kayabe ra ding kakung ibpa king lukib a atiu king marangle nang Efron a Heteo, 	

Genesis <lbl>49:30</lbl> 	King lukib a atiu king marangle nang Macpela, a atiu king tulid ning Mamre, king labuad na ning Canaan, a seli nang Abraham a kayabe na ning marangle kang Efron a Heteo a pekapibandian a kutkutan. 	

Genesis <lbl>49:31</lbl> 	Karin de kitkut i Abraham at i Sarang keang asawa; karin de kitkut i Isaac at i Rebecang keang asawa; at karin de kitkut i Lea

Genesis <lbl>49:32</lbl> 	Ing marangle at ing lukib a atiu karin, a mesali karing anak nang Het. 

Genesis <lbl>49:33</lbl> 	At inyang meari neng mekapanabilin i Jacob karing keang anak, tinipun no ding keang bitis king pagkeran, at mepatad ya inawa, at miagum ya king keang balayan. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:1</lbl> 	At migsucub ya i Jose king lupa na ning keang ibpa, at kaniak ya king babo na, at inuma ne. 

Genesis <lbl>50:2</lbl> 	At inutus nang Jose karing keang ipus a manulu a balsamuan de ing keang ibpa: at binalsamuan de ding manulu i Israel. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:3</lbl> 	At apatapulung aldo ing inari ra kea; uling makanian a inari ra ing aldo a pamagbalsamu ra: at kiniakan de ding tau Egipto pitungpulung aldo. 	

Genesis<lbl> 50:4</lbl> 	At inyang ing aldo na ning pamangiak kea milabas na, miniabi ya i Jose king bale nang Faraon, ngana, Nung ngeni menakit kung kalam karing kekang mata, sabian mu, king daramdaman nang Faraon, pagamuamu ku keka, sabian mu, 

Genesis <lbl>50:5</lbl> 	Pepasumpa nakung ibpa ku, ngana, Oini, mamamate ku: king kutkutan a kanakung kilkul a makatungkul kaku king labuad na ning Canaan, karin muku ikutkut. Ngeni pin paintulutan yukung mako, pagamuamu ku kekayu, at ikutkut ke ing kakung ibpa, at mibalik kung pasibayu. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:6</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Faraon, Mako ka, at ikutkut me ing kekang ibpa, agpang king pepasumpa na keka. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:7</lbl> 	At meko ya i Jose baneng ikutkut i ibpa na; at kayabe nong meko ding anggang ipus nang Faraon, ding mangatua king keang bale, at ding anggang mangatua king labuad na ning Egipto, 	

Genesis <lbl>50:8</lbl> 	At ing mabilug a bale nang Jose, at ding keang kapatad, at ing bale na ning keang ibpa: ding karela mung anak, at ding karelang kawan, at ding karelang vaca, ilang karelang likuan king labuad ning Gozen. 

Genesis <lbl>50:9</lbl> 	At karin mine lang abe ra ding carro, at ding sasake kabayu: at binang maragul a tapuk. 

Genesis <lbl>50:10</lbl> 	At dinatang la king pidadaran nang Atad, a atiu pa nangan na karin ning Jordan, at karin la menagulele masikan at kapaitpaitan a tagulele: at guinawa yang pamagpaldas king keang ibpa pitung aldo. 

Genesis <lbl>50:11</lbl> 	At inyang ding manuknangan king labuad, ding Cananeos, ikit da ing pamagpaldas king pidadaran nang Atad, sinabi ra, Iti metung a kalunuslunus a pamagpaldas ding tau Egipto, inya ing pemalaguiu ra kaniti Abel-mizraim, a nangan na karin ning Jordan. 

Genesis <lbl>50:12</lbl> 	At depatan da kea ding keang anak ing agpang king inutus na karela: 

Genesis <lbl>50:13 </lbl>	Uling dela re ding keang anak king labuad na ning Canaan, at kitkut de king lukib na ning marangle ning Macpela, a seli nang Abraham pati ing marangle, a pekapibandian a kutkutan, kang Efron, a Heteo king tulid ning Mamre.

Genesis <lbl>50:14</lbl> 	At mibalik ya i Jose king Egipto, ya, at ding keang kapatad, at ding anggang mine a kayabe nang mikutkut king keang ibpa, pangayari neng kitkut i ibpa na. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:15</lbl> 	At inyang akit da ding kapatad nang Jose king ing karelang ibpa mete ya, sinabi ra, Mekad i Jose akasaman nakatamu, at ablasan nang lubus kekatamu ing anggang dewakan a depatan ta kea. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:16</lbl> 	At i peparala lang balita kang Jose, ngana, Inutus nang ibpa mu bayu ya mete, ngana, 	

Genesis <lbl>50:17</lbl> 	Sabian yung makanian kang Jose, Patawad, pagamuamu ku keka ngeni, ing pamanalangsang da ding kekang kapatad, at ing karelang kadewakan. At ngeni, ipagamuamu mi keka, ipatawad mu ing pamanalangsang da ding talasuyu na ning Dios ning kekang ibpa. At i Jose kiniak ya inyang maniabi la kea. 

Genesis <lbl>50:18</lbl> 	At mine la naman kea ding keang kapatad at migsakab la king arapan na ning keang lupa; at sinabi ra, Oini, ikami ding talasuyu mu. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:19</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose karela, E ko tatakut: uling atiku king pangabilian na ning Dios? 	

Genesis <lbl>50:20</lbl> 	At tungkul king kekayu, ibibilang yung dewakan salang kanaku; dapot ibibilang nang kayapan ning Dios, bang mapalyari, ing anti mo iti king aldo ngeni, a miligtas la bie ding dakal a tau. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:21</lbl> 	Inya pin e ko tatakut: pakanan dakayu, at ding kekong anak. At pematulan nala, at miniabi ya karela king kasampatan a lub. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:22</lbl> 	At i Jose menuknangan ya Egipto, ya, at ing bale na ning keang ibpa: at i Jose mebie yang dinalan at apulung banua. 

Genesis <lbl>50:23</lbl> 	At ikit nong Jose ding anak nang Efraim angga king katlung dai: ding anak na namang Makir a anak nang Manases penganak la naman karing tud nang Jose. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:24</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Jose karing keang kapatad, Mate ku: dapot tune a dalawan nako ning Dios, idala nakayu manibat king labuad a iti angga king labuad a pengaku na kang Abraham, kang Isaac, at kang Jacob. 	

Genesis <lbl>50:25</lbl> 	At sinumpa ya i Jose karing anak nang Israel, ngana, Tune a dalawan na ko ning Dios, at idala yula ding kanakung butul manibat keti. 

Genesis <lbl>50:26</lbl> 	Makanian ing pangamate nang Jose, a dinalan ya at apulung banua tua; at binalsamuan de, at binili re king metung a kabaung karin Egipto. 	

Title:Deuteronomy


<b>Deuteronomio Deuteronomy</b>

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:1</lbl>	Deti ila ding amanu a sinabi nang Moises king mabilug a Israel king nangan na karin ning Jordan king ilang, king Araba king tulid ning Suf, king pilatan ning Paran, at Tofel, at Laban, at Hazerot, at Di-zahab.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:2</lbl>	Labingmetung a aldo a paglakben manibat king Horeb king dalan ning bunduk ning Seir angga king Cades-barnea.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:3</lbl>	At milyari kanitang kapat apulung banua, king kalabing metung a bulan, king mumuna nang aldo ning bulan, a miniabi ya i Moises karing anak na ning Israel, agpang king anggang binie na kea a utus nang GUINU karela;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:4</lbl>	Kaibat neng sigatan i Sehon a ari ra ding Amoreos, a manuknangan king Hesbon, at i Og a ari king Basan, a manuknangan king Astarot, king Edrei.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:5</lbl>	King nangan na karin ning Jordan, king labuad na ning Moab, pigmulan nang Moises a selese ing kautusan a iti, ngana,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:6</lbl>	I GUINU a kekatang Dios a miniabi kekatamu king Horeb, ngana, Ikayu tinuknang na kong maluat king bunduk a iti:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:7</lbl>	Mibalik kayu, at maglakbe kayu, at ume kayu king karinan a bunduk-bundukan ding Amoreos, at karing anggang karinan a makalapit karin, king Araba, king labuad a bunduk-bundukan, at king kababan, at king Mauli, at king bebe na ning dayatmalat, ing labuad da ding Cananeos, at ing Libano, angga king maragul a ilug, ing ilug ning Eufrartes.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:8</lbl>	Oini, kanakung binili ing labuad king arapan yu: lungub kayu at bandian yu ing labaud a simpa nang GUINU karing kekong mangatua, kang Abraham, kang Isaac, at kang Jacob, a binie na karela at karing karelang bini kaibat da.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:9</lbl>	At aku miniabi ku kekayu king panaun a ita, ngaku, E rako adalang magdilidili ku:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:10</lbl>	Peparakal nakong GUINU a kekong Dios, at oini, anti kayu, king aldo a iti, ding batuin king banua king karakal.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:11</lbl>	I GUINU, a Dios da ding kekong mangatua, gawan nakong makalilibung ukdu karakal a maiguit kekayu ngeni, at panuanan nakayu, anti mo ing pengaku na kekayu!	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:12</lbl>	Makananung idala kung dilidili ing kekong pangabala, at ing kekong pusan, at ing kekong piamanuan?

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:13</lbl>	Kuma kayu karing lalaking biasa, at maki pamanalastas, at pikabaluan, agpang karing kekong dai, at ila gawan kong pekabuntuk kekayu.	Take you wise men, and understanding, and known among your tribes, and I will make them rulers over you.
Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:14</lbl>	At mekibat ko kaku, at sinabi yu, Ing bague a kekang sinabi mayap kekami baming daptan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:15</lbl>	Inya kinua kula ding pekabuntuk da ding kekong dai, lalaking biasa, at pikabaluan, at guewa kong pekabuntuk kekayu, capitan do ding libulibu, at capitan do ding dina-dinalan, at capitan do ding tialima-limang pulu, at capitan do ding tiapulu-pulu, at pekapun la, agpang karing kekong dai.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:16</lbl>	At penabilinan kula ding kekong ukum kanitang panaun a ita, sinabi ku, Pakiramdaman yu ing pisasabian libutad da ding kekong kapatad, at atulan ye king matulid ing metung a lalaki at ing keang kapatad, at ing tau king aliwang labuad a kayabe na.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:17</lbl>	E ko kikilalang pangatau king pamanatul; pakiramdaman ye ing malati anti mo ing maragul; e ko mitatakutan king lupa na ning tau; uling ing pamantul king Dios: at ing pisasabian a binang masakit kekayu, idala yu kanaku, at pakiramdaman ku.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:18</lbl>	At inutus ku kekayu kanitang panaun a ita ing sablang bague a kekong sukat daptan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:19</lbl>	At miglakad tamung menibat king Horeb, at biltangan tamu itang anggang maragul at makapangilabut a ilang a kekong ikit, king dalan a tumuru king karinan a bunduk-bundukan ding Amoreos, anti mo ing inutus na kekatamung GUINU a kekatang Dios; at dinatang tamu king Cades-barnea.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:20</lbl>	At sinabi ku kekayu, Disnan yu ing karinan a bunduk-bundukan ding Amoreos, a binie na kekatamung GUINU a kekatang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:21</lbl>	Oini, binili nang GUINU a kekong Dios ing labuad king arapan yu: ukiatan yu, bandian yu, anti mo ing sinabi na kekong GUINU a Dios da ding kekong mangatua; e ko tatakut, ni mangalambut man.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:22</lbl>	At linapit ko kanaku balang metung kekayu, at sinabi na, Mitubud tang lalaki king mumuna kekatamu, barang siasatan ing labuad dikil kekatamu, at magdala lang amanung pasibayu kekatamu king dalan a dapat tang sampan, at karing ciudad a kekatang dasnan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:23</lbl>	At ing bague pepatulan nakung mayap; at aku kinanua kung labingaduang lalaki kekayu, metung a lalaki king balang metung a dai:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:24</lbl>	At mibalik la at sinampa la king bunduk-bundukan a karinan, at dinatang la king libis ning Escol, at tiniktikan da.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:25</lbl>	At kinanua la karing karelang gamat karing bunga na ning labuad, at dela rala kekatamu, at migdala lang pasibayung amanu kekatamu, at ngara, Mayap a labuad ing binie na kekatamung GUINU a kekatang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:26</lbl>	Makanian man e ko minukiat, nung e sinalangsang kayu laban king utus nang GUINU a kekong Dios:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:27</lbl>	At milmura kayu kilub ding kekong kubu, at sinabi yu, Uling akamuan nakatamung GUINU, liwal nakatamu king labuad na ning Egipto, bang ibie nakatamu king gamat da ding Amoreos, ba rakatang lipulan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:28</lbl>	Nu tamu sampa? Pepalungkut do ding kekatang pusu ding kapatad tamu, ngara, Ding tau mangaragul la at mangatas kekatamu; ding ciudad mangaragul la at makakuta lang angga banua; at bukud kaniti ikit mila ding anak da ding Anakim karin.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:29</lbl>	Kanita sinabi ku kekayu, E ko mangilabut, ni tumakut man karela.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:30</lbl>	I GUINU a kekong Dios a manimuna kekayu, makipamuk ya dikil kekayu, agpang king sablang depatan na kekayu karin Egipto king arapan da ding kekong mata,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:31</lbl>	At king ilang, nung nu yu ikit nung makananung dela nakong GUINU a kekong Dios, anti mo ing pamibabata na ning metung a lalaki king keang anak a lalaki, karing anggang dalan a inayan yu, angga king dinatang kayu king karinan a iti.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:32</lbl>	Makanian man king anti kaniting bague e ye peniwalan i GUINU a kekong Dios,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:33</lbl>	A menimuna kekayu king dalan, bang ipanintun nakayung karinan a pitalakaran yu karing kekong kubu, king api panga bengi, bang ituru na kekayu nung nu karing dalan a dumalan kayu, at king lulam panga aldo.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:34</lbl>	At dimdam nang GUINU ing siwala na ning kekong amanu, at mikapali ya, at sinumpa ya, ngana,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:35</lbl>	Tune a e na akit ning metung man karing taung deti niting marawak a dai ing mayap a labaud, a simpa kung ibie karing kekong mangatua,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:36</lbl>	Subali kang Caleb a anak nang Jefune; ya ing manakit; at kea ku ibie ing labaud a keang dilpak, at karing keang anak, uling ya lubus yang tinuki kang GUINU.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:37</lbl>	I GUINU man mimua ya kanaku, king uli yu, ngana, Ika man e ka milub karin:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:38</lbl>	I Josue a anak nang Nun, a makatalakad king arapan mu, lungub ya karin: pasiknangan me lub; uling keang ipamana king Israel.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:39</lbl>	Bukud kaniti ding kekong mangalating anak, a sinabi yung maguing bijag, at ding kekong anak, a king aldo a iti ala pang pangabaluan king mayap o marawak, ila lungub la karin, at karela ibie ku iti, at karelang bandian.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:40</lbl>	Dapot dikil kekayu, mibalik kayu, at maglakbe ko king ilang king dalan a tumuru king Dayatmalat a Malutu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:41</lbl>	Kanita mekibat kayu at sinabi yu kanaku, Mikasala kami salang kang GUINU, sampa kami at makipamuk, agpang king anggang inutus na kekaming GUINU a kekeng Dios. At pesipagtakas kayu balang metung king keang takas a pakipamuk, at migmalawa kong sinampa king bunduk-bundukan a karinan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:42</lbl>	At i GUINU sinabi na kanaku, Sabian mu karela, E ko sasampa, ni makipamuk man; uling ala ku kekayu; a magkang masugat kayu king arapan da ding kekong kasalang.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:43</lbl>	Inya miniabi ku kekayu, at e yu pekiramdaman; nung e sinalangsang kayu king kautusan nang GUINU, at migpalalu kayu, at minukiat ko king bunduk-bundukan a karinan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:44</lbl>	At ding Amoreos, a manuknangan kanitang bunduk-bundukan a karinan, pesilual lang salang kekayu, at tegal dakayu, anti mo ing depatan da ding panilan, at simbut dakayu king Seir, angga man king Horma.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:45</lbl>	At mibalik kayu at menangis king arapan nang GUINU; dapot e na pekiramdaman GUINU ing kekong siwala, ni tiningid man kekayu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>1:46</lbl>	Inya tinuknang kong dakal a aldo king Cades, agpang king aldo a penuknangan yu karin.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:1</lbl>	Kanita mibalik tamu, at miglakbe tamu king ilang king dalan a tumuru king Dayatmalat a Malutu, anti mo ing sinabi nang GUINU kanaku; at liniguid tamu king bunduk ning Seir dakal a aldo.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:2</lbl>	At i GUINU miniabi ya kanaku, ngana,	And the LORD spake unto me, saying,
Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:3</lbl>	Liguiran ye ing bunduk a iti a makabang panaun: magbalik kayu king nangan paralaya.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:4</lbl>	At yutus mu king balayan, ngamu, Dumalan kayu king angganan ding kekong kapatad a anak nang Esau, a manuknangan king Seir; at ila tumakut la kekayu. Mingat ko ping mayap karing kekong sarili king uli na niti:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:5</lbl>	E ko makitua karela; uling e ku ibie kekayu ing karelang labuad, ali, aguiang ing daralpakan na mu ning talampakan na ning metung a bitis; uling kanakung binie ing bunduk ning Seir kang Esau a pekabandi na.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:6</lbl>	Sali kong pamangan karela king pamamilatan na ning salapi, bakong mangan; at sali kayu namang danum karela king pamamilatan na ning salapi, bakong minum.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:7</lbl>	Uling pepanuanan nakong GUINU a kekong Dios king sablang dapat da ding kekong gamat; keang abalu ing kekong pamaglakbe keti king maliwalas a ilang: kareting apatapulung banua minantabe ya kekayu i GUINU a kekong Dios; e ko kekulangan nanumang bague.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>2:8</lbl>	Inya dinalan tamu karing kekatang kapatad a anak nang Esau, a manuknangan king Seir, manibat king dalan na ning Araba manibat king Elat at manibat king Eziongeber. At mibalik tamu at dinalan ta king ilang ning Moab.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:9</lbl>	Mingat kayu mu king kekong sarili, at ingatan ye ing kekong kaladua king lubus a pamaningat, magkang kekayu lang kalinguan ding bague a ikit yu karing kekong mata, at magkang kawani la king kekong pusu king anggang aldo na ning kekong bie; dapot pabalu yula karing kekong anak at karing anak da ding kekong anak;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:10</lbl>	King aldo a tinalakad ko king arapan nang GUINU a kekong Dios king Horeb, kanitang sabian na kanakung GUINU, Tipunan mu kanaku ing balayan, at iparamdam ku karela ing kanakung amanu, balang magaral tumakut kanaku king sablang aldo a mabibie la king babo ning labuad, at bang aturu ra karing karelang anak.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:11</lbl>	At linapit kayu at tinalakad king lalam ning bunduk; at ing bunduk milalablab ya king api angga king kapitna na ning banua, kagum ning karalumduman, lulam, at makapal a dalumdum.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:12</lbl>	At i GUINU miniabi ya kekayu a ibat king libutad ning api: dimdam yu ing siwala na ning amanu, dapot ala kong ikit a anyu; bukud mung dimdam yu ing siwala.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:22</lbl>	Dapot kailangan kung mate king labuad a iti, e ku dapat dalakit king Jordan; dapot ikayu dalakit kayu, at kekayung bandian ing labuad a mayap a ita.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:23</lbl>	Mingat ko pin karing kekong sarili, a magkang akalinguan yu ing tipan nang GUINU a kekong Dios, a guewa na kekayu, at gawa kong larawan a initsuran king kalupa na ning nanumang bague a binawal na kekayung GUINU a kekong Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:24</lbl>	Uling i GUINU a kekong Dios metung yang aping manampus, mapangalalu ya ping Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:26</lbl>	Kaku yang ausan ing banua at ing labuad bang magsaksi la salang kekayu king aldo a iti, bang malipul kong agad a alang sala king labuad a kekong ayan king kangatba ning Jordan bang bandian; e yo apakaban karin ding kekong aldo, nung e lubus a malipul kayu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:27</lbl>	At ikalat nakong GUINU karing balayan, at kataganan kayung ditak king bilang king libutad da ding bansa, a nung nu nako idalang GUINU.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:28</lbl>	At karin sumuyu kayu karing dioses, gawa ra ding gamat da ding tau, dutung at batu, a e manakit, ni makaramdam, ni makapangan, ni makabau.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:29</lbl>	Dapot manibat karin panintunan ye i GUINU a kekong Dios, at malyari yeng akit, ngening panintunan ye king kekong mabilug a pusu at mabilug a kaladua.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:30</lbl>	Ngening ati ko king kagutgutan, at ing anggang bague a iti datang kekayu, karing tauling aldo mibalik kayu kang GUINU a kekong Dios, at pakiramdaman yu ing keang siwala:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:31</lbl>	Uling i GUINU a kekong Dios mapamakalulu yang Dios; e nako paburen, ni e nako lipulan, ni e na kalinguan ing keang tipan karing mangatua yu a simpa na karela.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:32</lbl>	Uling ikutang yu ngeni karing aldo a milabas, a minuna kekayu, manibat king aldo a lelangan ne ning Dios ing tau king babo na ning labuad, at manibat king metung a angganan na ning banua angga king kasumangid, nung mika ating nanu mang bague a anti mo ing maragul a bague a iti, o meramdam kaya ing anti kanite?

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:33</lbl>	Dimdam na kaya kapilan man ning insamang balayan ing siwala na ning Dios a miniabi karela king libutad ning api, a anti mo ing dimdam yu, at mebie la?	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:34</lbl>	O ing Dios wari migmunikala ya bang ume at kuma dikil kea metung a bansa, ibat king libutad na ning aliwang bansa, king pamamilatan na ning subuk, karing tanda, at karing makapagmulala, at king pamipamuk, at king mayupayang gamat, at king makayatyat a takde, at king maragul a makapangilabot, agpang karing anggang depatan nang GUINU a kekong Dios dikil kekayu karin Egipto king arapan da ding kekong mata?	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:35</lbl>	Kekayu mipakit iti, bayung abalu king i GUINU ya ing Dios; ala nang aliwa subali kea.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:36</lbl>	Manibat banua peparamdam na kekayu ing keang siwala, ba nakong ituru: at king babo na ning labuad pepakit na kekayu ing keang maragul a api; at dimdam yu ing keang amanu king libutad na ning api.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:37</lbl>	At uli ning liguran nala ding kekong mangatua, inya pinili nala ding karelang bini king tauli ra, at kinua nakayu king Egipto king keang pamakiarap, king maragul nang kayupayan;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:38</lbl>	Banong palakuan king arap yu ding bansa a lalung mangaragul at lalung mangayupaya kesa kekayu, banakong paluban, banang ibie kekayu ing karelang labuad a pekamana, anti mo king aldo ngeni.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:39</lbl>	Talastasan yu pin king aldo iti, at ibili yu king kekong pusu, king i GUINU ya ing Dios king babo na ning banua at king lalam ning labuad; ala nang aliwa.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:40</lbl>	At ingatan yula ding keang tuntunan, at ding keang utus, a inutus ku kekayu king aldo a iti, bang ume yang mayap kayabe yu, at karing kekong anak king tauli yu, at bayong apakaba ding kekong aldo king babo na ning labuad, a binie na kekong GUINU a kekong Dios king kapilan man.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:41</lbl>	Kanita i Moises mikawani yang atlung ciudad king lipat ning Jordan nangan king aslagan ning aldo;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:42</lbl>	Bang ing taung mekamate a mekapate king e na seria king kalupa nang tau, at e ne kamuan king panaun a milabas, tumakas ya karin; at king pamanakas na king metung kareting ciudad malyari yang mie:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:43</lbl>	A milalaguiuwan, Bezer king ilang, king labuad a kapatagan, dikil karing Reubenitas; at ing Ramot king Gilead, dikil karing Gaditas; at ing Golan king Basan, dikil karing Manasitas.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:44</lbl>	At iti ya ing kautusan a binili nang Moises king arapan da ding anak na ning Israel:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:45</lbl>	Deti ila ding patutu, at ding tuntunan, at ding utus, a sinabi nang Moises karing anak na ning Israel, inyang lual lang manibat king Egipto,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:46</lbl>	King nangan na karin ning Jordan, king libis a tulid na ning Betpeor, king labuad nang Sihon a ari ding Amoreos, a menuknangan king Hesbon, a nung ninu ding sinugat da di Moises ila ding anak na ning Israel, inyang lual lang menibatan Egipto.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:47</lbl>	At kinua ra ing keang labuad a pekabandi, at ing labuad nang Og a ari king Basan, ding adua rang ari ding Amoreos, a atiu king lipat ning Jordan nangan king aslagan ning aldo;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:48</lbl>	Manibat king Aroer, a atiu king wakas na ning libis ning Arnon, angga pin king bunduk ning Sion (iti ya ing Hermon),	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>4:49</lbl>	At ing mabilug a Araba king lipat ning Jordan nangan aslagan, angga pin king dayatmalat na ning Araba, king lalam da ding baidbid ning Pisga.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:1</lbl>	At i Moises inaus na ing mabilug a Israel, at sinabi na karela, Makiramdam ka, Oh Israel, karing tuntunan at utus a sabian ku karing kekang balugbug king aldo iti, bang abalu mula, at tuparan mong daptan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:2</lbl>	I GUINU a kekatang Dios guinawa yang tipan kekatamu king Horeb.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:3</lbl>	I GUINU e ne guewa ing tipan a iti karing kekatang mangatua, nung e kekatamu, kekatamu pin, a nung ninu pin itamung sablang mabie ngeni keti.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:4</lbl>	I GUINU miniabi ya kekayung lupa at lupa king bunduk manibat king libutad na ning api

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:5</lbl>	(Tinalakad ku king pilatan nang GUINU at kekayu king panaun a ita, bang ipakit ku kekayu ing amanu nang GUINU: uling mitakutan kayu king uli na ning api, at e ko minukiat king bunduk), ngana,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:6</lbl>	Aku i GUINU a kekang Dios, a milual keka king labuad na ning Egipto, king bale na ning pangayalipan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:7</lbl>	E ka mikaka dioses a aliwa king arapan ku.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:8</lbl>	E ka gagawa dikil keka a metung a larawan a dinukit, ni kalupa na ning nanumang bague a atiu king babo banua, o king atiu lalam na ning labuad, o king atiu king danum king lalam na ning labuad:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:9</lbl>	E ka duruku karela, ni susuyu karela; uling aku, i GUINU, a kekang Dios, Dios kung mapangalalu, a daralawan ku ing dewakan da ding mangatua karing anak, at king katlu at king kapat a dai ra ding misasakuil kanaku;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:10</lbl>	At papakit kung kapakaluluan karing libu-libung lulugud kanaku at tutupad karing kakung utus.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:11</lbl>	E me gagamitan ing laguiu nang GUINU a kekang Dios kekang Dios king alang kabaldugan: uling i GUINU e ne payalan kasalanan ing gumamit alang kabaldugan king laguiu na.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:12</lbl>	Ipangiling me ing aldo ning sabbath, bang aingat meng banal, anti mo ing inutus na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:13</lbl>	Anam a aldo dapat ka, at daptan mu ing anggang kekang dapat;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:14</lbl>	Dapot ing kapitung aldo metung yang sabbath kang GUINU a kekang Dios: kaniti e ka darapat nanumang dapat, ika, ni ing anak mung lalaki, ni ing anak mung babai, ni ing ipus mung lalaki, ni ing ipus mung babai, ni ing kekang vaca, ni ing kekang asno, ni ing isanuman karing kekang animal, ni ing aliwang balen a atiu kilub mung pasbulan; bang ing ipus mung lalaki at ing ipus mung babai mipainawa lang anti mo ika.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:15</lbl>	At ganakan mu king meguing alipan ka king labuad na ning Egipto, at i GUINU a kekang Dios liwal naka manibat karin king pamamilatan na ning metung a masikanan a gamat at king pamamilatan na ning metung a makayatyat a takde: king uli na nita i GUINU a kekang Dios inutus na keka king ipangiling me ing aldo na ning sabbath.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:16</lbl>	Igalang me i ibpa mu at i indu mu, anti mo ing inutus na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios; bang ding kekang aldo kumaba la, at bang iti ikakayap mu, king labuad a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:17</lbl>	E ka makamate.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:18</lbl>	Ni darapat mang pamakipaliwas.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:19</lbl>	Ni manako man.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:20</lbl>	Ni sasaksi man king e katutuan laban king kalupa mung tau.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:21</lbl>	Ni angkaminan man ing asawa na ning kalupa mung tau; ni pagimbutan man ing bale na ning kalupa mung tau, ing keang marangle man, o ing ipus na mang lalaki, o ing ipus na mang babai, ing keang vaca man, o ing keang asno man, o ing nanumang bague a bandi ning kalupa mung tau.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:22</lbl>	Deting amanu sinabi nong GUINU king kekong mabilug a kapulungan king bunduk manibat king libutad na ning api, ning lulam, at ning makapal a dalumdum, king masikan a siwala: at ala neng digdag pa.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:23</lbl>	At milyari, inyang dimdam yu ing siwala manibat king libutad na ning dalumdum, kabang ing bunduk milalablab ya king api, king linapit ko kanaku, ding angga pin pekabuntuk da ding kekong dai, at ding kekong makatua;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:24</lbl>	At sinabi yu, Oini, i GUINU a kekatang Dios pepakit na kekami ing keang ligaya, at ing keang degulan, at dimdam mi ing keang siwala manibat king libutad na ning api: ikit mi king aldo iti king ing Dios makipagsalita ya king tau, at mabie ya.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:25</lbl>	Ngeni pin baket mate kami? uling iting maragul a api tampusan nakami: nung damdaman ming pasibayu pa ing siwala nang GUINU a kekatang Dios, kanita mate kami.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:26</lbl>	Uling ninu karing sablang laman, a dinamdam king siwala na ning Dios a mabie a maniabi manibat king libutad na ning api, anti mo ikami, at mebie ya?

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:27</lbl>	Lumapit ka, at pakiramdaman mu ing anggang sabian nang GUINU a kekatang Dios: at sabian mu kekami ing anggang sabian na kekang GUINUNG kekatang Dios: at pakiramdaman mi, at daptan mi.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:28</lbl>	At i GUINU dimdam na ing siwala ding kekong amanu, inyang maniabi ko kanaku; at sinabi na kanakung GUINU, Dimdam ku ing siwala ra ding amanu ning balayan a iti, a sinabi ra keka: miniabi lang mayap king sablang sinabi ra.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:29</lbl>	Oh mananu sang maki ating metung a pusung anti iti karela, bang tumakut la kanaku, at tuparan dong parati ding sabla kung utus, bang mipakayap la, at ding karelang anak king kapilan pa man!

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:30</lbl>	Ume ka sabian mu karela. Mibalik ko karing kekong kubu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:31</lbl>	Dapot tungkul keka, talakad ka keni king kanakung siping, at sabian ku keka ing mabilug a utus, at ding tuntunan, at ding kautusan, a ituru mu karela, bang daptan dala king labuad a ibie ku karela bang bandian da.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:32</lbl>	Keko ping tuparan daptan ing anti mo ing inutus nang GUINUNG kekong Dios kekayu: e ko liliku king wanan o king kaili.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>5:33</lbl>	Lumakad kayu king lubus a pamanlakad a inutus na kekayung GUINU a kekong Dios, bang mie kayu, at bang maguing ikakayap yu, at bang apakaban yula ding kekong aldo king labuad a kekong bandian.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:1</lbl>	Ngeni iti ya ing utus, ding tuntunan, at ding kautusan, a inutus nang papaturu kekayung GUINUNG kekong Dios, bang daptan yula king labuad a kekayung ayan bang bandian yu;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:2</lbl>	Bang tumakut kayu kang GUINU a kekong Dios, a tupad karing sabla nang tuntunan, at keang utus, a yutus ku kekayu, kekayu at king kekong anak, king sablang aldo na ning kekong bie; at bang ding kekong bie; at bang ding kekong aldo kumaba la.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:3</lbl>	Pakiramdaman mu pin, Oh Israel, at tuparan mung daptan; bang kekang ikakayap, at bang dakal kang bina, anti mo ing pengaku nang GUINU, a Dios da ding kekang mangatua, keka, king metung a labuad a agusan na ning gatas at pulut.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:4</lbl>	Pakiramdaman mu, Oh Israel: i GUINU a kekatang Dios metung yang GUINU:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:5</lbl>	At luguran me i GUINU a kekang Dios king mabilug mung pusu, at king mabilug mung kaladua, at king mabilug mung sikanan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:6</lbl>	At ding amanung deti, a yutus ku keka king aldo iti, magbili la king kekang pusu;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:7</lbl>	At keka lang ituru king kasipagan karing kekang anak, at isalita mo karela ngening makalukluk ka king kekang bale, at ngening lalakad ka king dalan, at ngening makakera ka, at ngening mibangun ka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:8</lbl>	At itali mulang pekatanda king kekang gamat, at maguing pekaaptas lang pamuti karing pilatan da ding kekang mata.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:9</lbl>	At isulat mula king babo nang asias pasbul ning kekang bale, at king babo ra ding kekang pasbulan dalan.	And thou shalt write them upon the posts of thy house, and on thy gates.
Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:10</lbl>	At malyari, ngening ilub nakang GUINU a kekang Dios king labuad a simpa na karing kekang mangatua, kang Abraham, kang Isaac, at kang Jacob, bang ibie na keka, ding mangaragul at mangayap a ciudad, a e mu telakad,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:11</lbl>	At bale a mitmu king anggang mangayap a bague, a e mu kitmuan, at talagang batu a mekulkul, a e mu kilkul, uvasan at dutung a oliva, a e mu tenam, at kanan mula at mipakabsian ka;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:12</lbl>	Kanita mingat ka a magkang kalinguan me i GUINU, a milual keka manibat king labuad na ning Egipto, manibat king bale na ning pangayalipan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:13</lbl>	Pitakutan me i GUINUNG kekang Dios; at ya ing kekang suyuwan, at sumpa ka king uli ning keang laguiu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:14</lbl>	E ka tutuki karing aliwang dioses, karing dioses da ding balayan a makapatulug keka;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:15</lbl>	Uling i GUINUNG kekang Dios a atiu libutad mu metung yang mapangalalung Dios; a magkang ing mua nang GUINUNG kekang Dios milablab laban keka, at lipulan naka ibat king lupa na ning labuad.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:16</lbl>	E me tutuksuan i GUINU a kekang Dios, anti mo inyang tuksuan me king Masa.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:17</lbl>	Ingatan mu king kasipagan ing utus nang GUINUNG kekang Dios, at ding keang patutu, at ding keang tuntunan, a inutus na keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:18</lbl>	At daptan mu itang matulid at mayap king panimanman nang GUINU; bang maguing ikakayap mu, at bamung aluban at abandi ing mayap a labuad a simpa nang GUINU karing kekang mangatua,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:19</lbl>	Bang itabi nala ding anggang kekang kasalang king kekang arapan, anti mo ing sinabi nang GUINU.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:20</lbl>	Ngening kutnan daka ding kekang anak king panaun a daratang, ngara, Nanu ing kabaldugan da ding patutu, at ding tuntunan, at ding kautusan, a inutus nang GUINUNG kekatang Dios keka?

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:21</lbl>	Kanita sabian mu king kekang anak, Meguing alipan nakeng Faraon king Egipto: at i GUINU linual nakami a manibatan king Egipto king pamamilatan na ning metung a masikanan a gamat;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:22</lbl>	At i GUINU pepakit yang tanda at makapagmulala, mangaragul at panlasak, king Egipto, kang Faraon, at king mabilug nang bale, king lalawan da ding kekeng mata;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:23</lbl>	At liwal nakeng manibat karin, ba nakeng alub, ba nang ibie kekami ing labuad a simpa na karing kekeng mangatua.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:24</lbl>	At i GUINU inutus na kekami king daptan mila ding anggang tuntunan a deti, bang tumakut kang GUINUNG kekatang Dios, king kekatang ikakayap kapilan man, bang aingat nakatang mabie, anti mo ing king aldo ngeni.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>6:25</lbl>	At maguing katuliran kekatamu, nung tuparan tamu ing mabilug a utus a iti king arapan nang GUINU a kekatang Dios, anti mo ing inutus na kekatamu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:1</lbl>	Ngening i GUINU a kekang Dios dalan naka king labuad a kekang ayan bang abandi, at itabi nala ding dakal a bansa king arapan mu, ing Heteo, at ing Gergeseo, at ing Amoreo, at ing Cananeo, at ing Perezeo, at ing Heveo, at ing Jebuseo, pitung bansa a mangaragul at masikanan a maiguit keka;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:2</lbl>	At ngening i GUINU a kekang Dios ibie no king arapan mu, at sugatan mula; kanita lipulan mong lubus a lubus: e ka makitipanan karela, ni papakit pakalulu karela;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:3</lbl>	Ni darapat mang pamakiasawa karela; ing kekang anak a babai e me babie king keang anak a lalaki, ni ing keang anak mang babai e me kakuanan dikil king anak mung lalaki.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:4</lbl>	Uling ikawani ne ing anak mung lalaki king pamanuki kanaku, bang sunuyu la karing aliwang dioses: king anti kanita milablab ing mua nang GUINU laban keka, at lipulan nakang agad.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:5</lbl>	Dapot makanian kang makiutus karela: lasakan mula ding karelang altares, at pamimirasuan mong mangalati ding karelang asias, at panabualan mula ding karelang Asera, at dulukan mula king api ding larawan dang dinukit.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:6</lbl>	Uling metung kang banal a balayan kang GUINUNG kekang Dios: i GUINUNG kekang Dios pinili nakang maguing metung a balayan a sarili nang pibandian, lapo karing sablang balayan a atiu king babo na ning lupa na ning labuad.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:7</lbl>	I GUINU e na binili ing lugud na keka, ni pinili naka, uli ning maiguit ka king bilang kesa king kaisanumang balayan; uling ika ing ditak dili karing anggang balayan:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:8</lbl>	Nung e uling kaluguran nakang talagang GUINU, at uling talagang tuparan na ing sumpa a keang simpa karing kekang mangatua, liwal nakang GUINU kambe ning metung a masikanan a gamat, at inatbus naka king bale ning pangayalipan, manibat king gamat nang Faraon a ari Egipto.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:9</lbl>	Talastasan mu pin king i GUINU a kekang Dios, ya ing Dios, ing tapat a Dios, a mimingat king tipan at kapakaluluan karetang lulugud kea at tutupad karing utus na angga king metung a libung dai,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:10</lbl>	At ablasan nala king karelang lupa detang mua kea, bang lipulan nala: e ya makupad kanitang mimumua kea, ablasan ne king keang lupa.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:11</lbl>	Tuparan mu pin ing utus, at ding tuntunan, at ding kautusan, a yutus ku keka king aldo a iti, bang daptan mula.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:12</lbl>	At malyari, uling mekiramdam ka kareting tuntunan, at iningat at tiparan mula, king i GUINU a kekang Dios tuparan na keka ing tipan at ing kapakaluluan a simpa na karing kekang mangatua:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:13</lbl>	At luguran naka, at panuanan naka, at parakalan naka; panuanan nia naman ing bunga na ning kekang katawan at ing bunga na ning kekang gabun, ing kekang binutil at ing kekang bayung alak at ing kekang laru, ing miragdag da ding kekang animal at ing biseru ra ding kekang kawan, king labuad a simpa na karing kekang mangatua bang ibie na keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:14</lbl>	Mipanuanan kang maiguit karing anggang balayan: alang maguing baug a lalaki o babai king libutad mu, o karing kekang animal.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:15</lbl>	At i GUINU ilako na keka ing anggang sakit; at ala karing mangarawak nang sakit ning Egipto, a kekang balu, a ibili na keka, nung e ibili nala karing anggang mimumua keka.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:16</lbl>	At lipulan mo ding anggang balayan a i GUINUNG kekang Dios ibie na keka; ing kekang mata e no lunusan: ni e mo susuyuwan ding karelang dioses; uling ita metung a silu keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:17</lbl>	Nung sabian mu king kekang pusu, Ding bansang deti maiguit la kanaku; makananu kong kamkaman?

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:18</lbl>	E ka tatakut karela: ganakan mung mayap ing depatan nang GUINU a kekang Dios kang Faraon, at king mabilug a Egipto;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:19</lbl>	Ding mangaragul a subuk a ikit da ding kekang mata, at ding tanda, at ding makapagmulala, at ing masikanan a gamat, at ing masikanan a gamat, at ing makayatyat a takde, a king karelang pamamilatan linual nakang GUINUNG kekang Dios: makanian ing daptan nang GUINUNG kekang Dios karing anggang balayan a kekang katakutan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:20</lbl>	Maiguit kaniti i GUINU a kekang Dios itubud no ding putakti karela, angga king ding makatagan, at isalikut da ing sarili ra, mangamate la king kekang arapan.	
Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:21</lbl>	E ka masasdan karela; uling i GUINUNG kekang Dios atiu king libutad mu, metung a maragul a Dios at makapangilabut.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:22</lbl>	At i GUINU a kekang Dios itabi nala ding bansang deta king arapan mu king ditak-ditak: e mo alipul king misan, magkang ding animal king marangle dakal la keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:23</lbl>	Dapot i GUINU a kekang Dios ibie no king arapan mu, at gutgutan nala king maragul a kagutgutan, angga king malipul la.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:24</lbl>	At ibie nala ding karelang ari king kekang gamat, at patdan mu ing karelang laguiu king lalam na ning banua: alang taung makatalakad king arapan mu, angga king alipul mula.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>7:25</lbl>	Ding larawan dang dinukit ding karelang dioses dulukan mo king api: e mu angkaminan ing pilak o ing guintu a atiu karela, ni kakuanan man dikil keka, magkang masilu ka kaniti; uling iti metung a makasumami kang GUINU a kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>11:21</lbl>	Bang ding kekong aldo dakal la, at ding aldo ra ding kekong anak, king labuad a simpa nang GUINU karing kekong mangatua bang ibie karela, anti mo ding kayaldawan da ding banua king babo na ning labuad.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>11:23</lbl>	Kanita i GUINU itabi no ding anggang bansa a deti manibat king kekong arapan, at kamkam kong bansa a mangaragul at masikanan a maiguit kekayu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>12:5</lbl>	Dapot king karinan a pilinan nang GUINUNG kekong Dios karing anggang kekong dai, bang ibili ne karin ing keang laguiu, king keang tuknangan pin karing ye panintunan, at karin ko datang;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>12:6</lbl>	At karin yo dalan ding kekong ain a durulukan, at ding kekong daun, at ding kekong sikapulu, at ing ain a tinas ning kekong gamat, at ding kekong panata, at ding kekong ain a kusa, at ding pangane ra ding kawan yung vaca at kawan yung tupa:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>12:11	</lbl>At malyari king king karinan a pilinan nang GUINUNG kekong Dios, bang papanuknanganan ne karin ing keang laguiu, karin yu dalan ing anggang yuyutus ku kekayu: ding kekong ain a durulukan, at ding kekong daun, ding kekong sikapulu, at ing ain a tinas ning kekong gamat. at ding anggang pili yung panata a penata yu kang GUINU.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>12:12</lbl>	At tumula kayu king arapan nang GUINUNG kekong Dios, ikayu, at ding kekong anak a lalaki, at ding kekong anak a babai, at ding kekong ipus a lalaki, at ding kekong ipus a babai, at ing Levita a manuknangan kilub ding kekong pasbulan, uli ning ala yang dake ni mana a kayabe yu.
