Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>14:29	</lbl>At ing Levita, anti ning ala yang dake ni mana man a kayabe yu, at ing makipanuknangan, at ing ulilang tata, at ing babaing mebalu, a atiu kilub ding kekong pasbulan, datang la, at mangan la at kumabsi la; bang i GUINU a kekong Dios panuanan nakayu king sablang dapat ning kekong gamat a kekong daraptan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:1</lbl>	King wakas na ning balang pitung banua dapat kong pamamatawad.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:10</lbl>	Dinan ye ping alang sala, at ing kekong pusu e ya lulungkut ngening babie ko kea; uling king uli na niti i GUINUNG kekong Dios panuanan nakayu king sablang kekong dapat, at king sablang atalan na ning kekong gamat.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:2</lbl>	At oini ing kaparalanan king pamamatawad: ing balang pikautangan ipatawad na itang pepautang na king kalupa nang tau; e na na isingil iti king kalupa nang tau at king keang kapatad; uling ing pamamatawad nang GUINU mipasiag na.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:3</lbl>	King metung a manaliwang balen asingil yu iti: dapot ing nanumang kayatinan yu a atiu king kekong kapatad ipatawad na ning kekong gamat.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:4</lbl>	Makanian man e mika ating maluka kekayu (uling i GUINU tune nakong panuanan king labuad a ibie nang GUINUNG kekong Dios kekayu a pekamana bayung bandian),	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:5</lbl>	Nung maingat yu mung pakiramdaman ing siwala nang GUINU a kekong Dios, bang tuparan yung daptan ing mabilug a utus a iti a yuyutus ku kekayu king aldo iti.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:6</lbl>	Uling i GUINU a kekong Dios panuanan nakayu, anti mo ing pengaku na kekayu: at pautang kayu karing dakal a bansa, dapot e ko manutang; at sumakup kong dakal a bansa, dapot e la sumakup kekayu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:7</lbl>	Nung ating kong kayabe metung a taung maluka, a metung ya karing kekong kapatad, kilub ning kaisanuman karing kekong pasbulan king kekong labuad i GUINU a kekong Dios ibie na kekayu, e ye pasiasan ing kekong pusu, ni isara man ing kekong gamat king kekong malukang kapatad;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:8</lbl>	Nung e alang pangakablang busnian ye ing kekong gamat kea, at tune yeng pautangan ganap dikil king keang kailangan ketang buri na.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:9</lbl>	Mingat kayu a e sa mikaka ating jamak a pamiisip king kekong pusu, ngayu, Ing kapitung banua, ing banua na ning pamamatawad, malapit na; at ding kekong mata maguing marawak la laban king maluka yung kapatad, at e ye dinan; at dalung ya kang GUINU laban kekayu, at maguing kasalanan yu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:11	</lbl>Uling e milako maluka ing labuad king kapilan pa man: uli nita yutus ku kekayu, ngaku, Ibuklat yeng alang sala ing kekong gamat king kekong kapatad, king kekong magkailangan, at king kekong maluka, king kekong labuad.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:12</lbl>	Nung ing kekong kapatad, a Hebreong lalaki, o Hebreang babai, pisali re kekayu, at sumuyu ya kekayung anam a banua; kanita king kapitung banua palakuan yu neng timawa.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:13</lbl>	At nung palakuan yu neng timawa kekayu, e ye palakuan alang daralan:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:14	</lbl>Malam yeng papagbakalan king kekong kawan a tupa, at king kekong pidadaran, at king kekong pipapaslan alak; anti mo ing pamipanuan nang GUINU kekayu munie ko kea.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:15</lbl>	At ganakan yu king meguing metung kong alipan king labuad na ning Egipto, at i GUINU a kekong Dios inatbus nakayu: inya yuyutus ku kekayu ing bague a iti ngeni.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:16</lbl>	At malyari, nung sabian na kekayu, E ku mako kekayu: uling kaluguran nakayu at ing kekong bale, uling mikasundu kayu;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:17</lbl>	Kanita kuma kong metung a pamusbus at ibusbus ye king keang balugbug king pasbul, at ya maguing ipus ye king kapilan pa man. At makanian mu naman king kekong ipus a babai ing kekong daptan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:18	</lbl>E sa mabayat king kekong lub ngening palakuan yeng timawa; uling aduang ukdu iguit king kaupajan ning makikiupa ing sinuyu na kekayu king anam a banua: at i GUINUNG kekong Dios panuanan nakayu king sablang kekong daraptan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:19</lbl>	Ding sablang pangane a lalaki a ipanganak da ding kawan mung vaca at ding kekang kawan a tupa italaga mula kang GUINU a kekang Dios: e me paniapat ing pangane na ning kawan mung vaca, ni ururan ing pangane ning kekang kawan a tupa.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:20	</lbl>Kanan me king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios banua banua king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU, ika at ing kekang katubale.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:21</lbl>	At nung atin yang nanumang kapintasan, anti mo nung pile ya o bulag, nanumang marawak kapintasan, e me daraun iti kang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:22	</lbl>Kanan me kilub ding kekang pasbulan: ing e malinis at ing malinis mangan lang para-para, anti mo ing malating usa, at anti mo ing maragul a usa.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>15:23</lbl>	Bukud mung e mu kakanan ing daya na niti; ibulus mu king labuad anti mong danum.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:1</lbl>	Keka yang pagmasusian ing bulan na ning Abib, at pangilinan me ing pascua kang GUINU a kekang Dios; uling king bulan ning Abib i GUINU a kekang Dios linual nakang manibat Egipto king bengi.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:2</lbl>	At idaun me ing pascua kang GUINU a kekang Dios, king kawan a tupa at king kawan a vaca, king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU, ba nang papanuknangan karin ing keang laguiu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:3</lbl>	E ka mamangan tinape a maki levadura a kayabe na niti; pitung aldo a kanan mu ing tinape alang levadura, ing tinape pin king kasakitan; uling meko ka king labuad na ning Egipto king pamagmalagua: ba mung aganaka ing aldo a pamanlako mu king labuad na ning Egipto karing sablang aldo na ning kekang bie.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:4</lbl>	At pitung aldo a alang mayayakit a levadura keka king anggang kekang angganan; ni king nanuman king laman, king kekang idaun king mumunang aldo king gatpanapun, alang mitatagan king kabukas angga king abak.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:5</lbl>	E me adaun ing pascua king kilub na ning isanuman karing pasbulan mu, a babie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:6</lbl>	Nung e king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, ba nang papanuknanganan karin ing keang laguiu, karin me idaun ing pascua king gatpanapun, king pangalbug ning aldo, king panaun a pamanlako mu Egipto.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:7</lbl>	At inangnang me at kanan king karinan a pilinan nang GUINUNG kekang Dios: at ika mibalik ka pangaabak, at ume ka karing kekang kubu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:8</lbl>	Anam a aldo a mangan kang tinape alang levadura; at king kapitung aldo maguing metung yang masusing pamipulung kang GUINU a kekang Dios; e ka darapat nanumang dapat kanita.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:9</lbl>	Pitung paruminggu ing bilangan mu keka: manibat king pamagmula a ibili ya ing lait king makatalakad a binutil magmula kang milang pitung paruminggu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:10	</lbl>At ipangiling me ing pista ra ding paruminggu kang GUINUNG kekang Dios a kagum ning buis ning metung a daun a kusa king kekang gamat, a ibie mu, agpang king pamipanaun na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:11</lbl>	At ika magsaya ka king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, ika, at ing kekang anak a lalaki, at ing kekang anak a babai, at ing kekang ipus a lalaki, at ing kekang ipus a babai, at ing Levita a atiu king kilub ding kekang pasbulan, at ing aliwang balen, at ing ulilang tata, at ing babaing mebalu, a atiu king libutad mu, king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, ba neng papanuknanganan karin ing keang laguiu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:12</lbl>	At ganakan mu king ika meguing alipan ka king Egipto: at tuparan mo at daptan ding tuntunan a deti.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:13</lbl>	Pagmasusian mu ing pista ra ding tabernaculos pitung aldo, pangaibat mung abangan ing kekang pupul a ibat king kekang pidadaran at king kekang pipapaslan alak:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:14</lbl>	At tumula ka king kekang pista, ika, at ing kekang anak a lalaki, at ing kekang anak a babai, at ing kekang ipus a lalaki, at ing kekang ipus a babai, at ing Levita, at ing aliwang balen, at ing ulilang tata, at ing babing mebalu, a atiu king kilub ding kekang pasbulan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:15	</lbl>Pitung aldo a pagmasusian mu ing metung a pista kang GUINU a kekang Dios king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU; uling panuanan nakang GUINU a kekang Dios king sablang kekang bunga, at king sablang dapat da ding kekang gamat, at ika lubus kang tumula.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:16</lbl>	Makatatlu king pabanua a ding kekang lalaki pasidurup la king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios king karinan a keang pilinan: king pista na ning tinape a alang levadura, at king pista ra ding paruminggu, at king pista ra ding tabernaculos, at e la dudurup king arapan nang GUINU a ala lang daralan:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:17	</lbl>Balang lalaki munie ya king keang kaguiuwan, agpang king kanuanan nang binie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:18</lbl>	Malal ka keka ukum at pekapun kilub ding anggang pasbulan mu, a babie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, agpang karing kekang dai; at atulan da ing balayan king matulid a pamanatul.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:19</lbl>	E mu lilisian ing matulid; e ka kikilalang pamialiwa karing tau; ni e ka kakuang susup; uling ing susup bubulagan no ding mata ra ding mata ra ding blasa, at lilisia na ing amanu ra ding matulid.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:20	</lbl>Tukian mu ing lubus a matulid, bakang mie, at manan mu ing labuad a babie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:21</lbl>	E ka mitatalakad Asera king nanumang dutung king siping ning altar nang GUINUNG kekang Dios, a gawan mung makatungkul keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>16:22</lbl>	Ni e ka mitatalakad asias a makatungkul keka; a pikakasaman nang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:1</lbl>	E ka mamain vaca kang GIUNU a kekang Dios, o metung a tupa, a maki kapintasan, o ing nanumang bague marawak; uling ita metung a makasumami kang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:2</lbl>	Nung ating mayakit king libutad mu, king kilub na ning isanuman karing kekang pasbulan a babie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, a lalaki o babai, a darapat king dewakan king panlalawe nang GUINU a kekang Dios, king pamanalangsang king keang pangaku,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:3</lbl>	At minie ya at sinuyu ya karing aliwang dioses, at sinamba ya karela, o king aldo, o king bulan, o king nanuman king ejercitu ning banua, a e ku inutus,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:4</lbl>	At nung selita ra keka, at kekang abalitan; kanita keka ping usisan a maingat; at, oini nung tutu, at ing bague katunayan, king ing anti kanitang makasumami merapat king Israel,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:5</lbl>	Kanita ilual me pin ing lalaki o babaing ita, a dinapat kaniting bague a marawak, karing pasbulan mu, ing lalaki pin o ing babai; at keka lang pukulan batu ba lang mangamate.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:6</lbl>	King asbuk da ding aduang saksi, o atlung saksi, mate ya ing miatulan patayan; king asbuk ning metung a saksi e ya patayan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:7</lbl>	Ing gamat da ding saksi yang munang dumpa kea ba yang patayan, at kaibat ing gamat na ning mabilug a balayan. Makanian mung ilako ing dewakan king libutad mu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:8</lbl>	Nung mika ating binang masakit a bague keka king pamanatul, king daya at daya, king piamanuan at piamanuan, at king palupalu at palupalu, a bague a pamipagkamua king kilub ding kekang pasbulan; kanita talakad ka, at sampa king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU a kekang Dios;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:9</lbl>	At ume ka karing sacerdotes a Levitas, at king ukum a salukuyan karing aldo deta; at ikutang mu; at ipakit da keka ing atul ning kayatulan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:10	</lbl>At daptan mu agpang king atul a ipakit da keka manibat king karinan a ita a pilinan nang GUINU; at kekang pamintuan daptan ing agpang king sablang ituru ra keka:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:11</lbl>	Agpang king kautusan a ituru ra keka, at agpang king kayatulan a sabian da keka, daptan mu; e ka liliku, aguiang king wanan o king kaili, king atul a ipakit da keka,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:12</lbl>	At ing tau a darapat kapalaluan, king e pamakiramdam king sacerdote a tatalakad bang manibala karin king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, o king ukum, ing tau ping ita mate ya: at ilako mu ing dewakan king Israel.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:13</lbl>	At makiramdam, at tumakut ing mabilug a balayan, at e ne dapat kapalaluan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:14	</lbl>Pamaniatang mu king labaud a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, at bandian mu iti, at manuknanganan ka karin, at kekang sabian, Aku mibili kung metung a ari a mamajala kanaku, anti mo ding anggang bansa a atiung makapatulug kaku;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:15	</lbl>Ika tune meng ibiling ari a mamajala keka, itang pilinan nang GUINU a kekang Dios: metung ya karing kekang kapatad ing ibili mung ari a mamajala keka; e me abili a mamajala keka ing metung a aliwang balen, a e mu kapatad.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:16</lbl>	E ya mu parakal dikil kea karing kabayu, ni pabalikan naman ing balayan karing Egipto, a bayang makaparakal kabayu; nung makananung sinabi na kekang GUINU, E mu na babalikan manibat ngeni ing dalan a ita.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:17</lbl>	Ni e ya parakal asawa na, bang ing keang pusu e malili: ni parakal mang pilak at guintu king keang sarili.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:18	</lbl>At mapalyari, nung lukluk ya king luklukan na ning keang kayarian, king gawa ya keang metung a likas king kautusan a iti king metung a libru, kanitang atiu king arapan da ding sacerdotes a Levitas;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:19	</lbl>At manatili ya kea, at kea yang basan aldoaldo kabang bie na; ba yang magaral a tumakut kang GUINU a keang Dios, bang pamintuan nang daptan ing anggang amanu na ning kautusan a iti at ding tuntunan a deti;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>17:20	</lbl>Bang ing keang pusu e ya magmatas karing keang kapatad, at bang e ya lisia king utus, aguiang king wanan, o king kaili: king bang kea lang apakaba ding keang aldo king keang kayarian, ya at ding keang anak, king libutad na ning Israel.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:1</lbl>	Ding sacerdotes a Levitas, ing mabilug a dai na ping Levi, e la mika dake ni mana man king Israel; mangan la karing ain kang GUINU a merapat king api, at king keang mana.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:2</lbl>	At ila e la mika mana a kayabe ra ding karelang kapatad: i GUINU ya ing mana ra, anti mo ing sinabi na karela.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:3</lbl>	At iti ya ing maguing karing sacerdotes a kuanan da king balayan manibat karing mamain metung a daun a vaca ya man o tupa, king ibie ra king sacerdote ing pago, at ding aduang pisngi at ing dungus.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:4</lbl>	Ing mumuna nang bunga ning kekang binutil, ning kekang alak a bayu, at ning kekang laru, at ing mumunang inurud mung balat karing kekang tupa, ibie mu kea.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:5</lbl>	Uling pinili neng GUINU a kekang Dios karing anggang dai mu, bayang talakad a manibala king laguiu nang GUINU, ya at ding keang anak kapilan man.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:6</lbl>	At nung ing metung a Levita mako ya king kaisanuman karing kekang pasbulan king mabilug a Israel, a keang peniliwan balayan, at ume ya karin king mabilug nang kapagnasan ning keang kaladua king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:7</lbl>	Kanita manibala ya king laguiu nang GUINU a keang Dios, anti mo ing daraptan da ding anggang kapatad na a Levitas, a tatalakad karin king arapan nang GUINU.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:8</lbl>	Mika atin lang mikakametung a dake a kanan, subali king manibatan karing abli king mana king keang ibpa.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:9</lbl>	Pamanlub mu king labuad a ibie kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, e ka magaral darapat king agpang king makasumami ding bansang deta.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:10</lbl>	E mayayakit keka ing ninumang paralan ne king api ing keang anak a lalaki o ing keang anak a babai, metung a mamamanula, metung a darapat king pamaganitu, o metung a encantador, o metung a maganting-anting,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:11	</lbl>O metung a manaliguat, o metung a mangutang king metung a espiritung marinat, o metung a magkukulam, o metung a mangutang karing mete.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:12</lbl>	Uling ninumang darapat karing anti kareting bague makasumami ya kang GUINU: at king uli ding makasumaming deti i GUINU a kekang Dios itatabi no king arapan mu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:13</lbl>Maguing sakdal ka kang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:14</lbl>	Uling ding bansang deti, a kekang kamkaman, makiramdam la karetang darapat king pamaganitu, at karing darapat king pamaganitu, at karing mamamanula; dapot tungkul keka, e na apibatang GUINU a kekang Dios a daptan mung makanian.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:15</lbl>	Ipalto ne kekang GUINU a kekang Dios ing metung a manula king libutad mu, karing kekang kapatad, a anti mo kanaku; kea kayu makiramdam;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:16	</lbl>Makaagpang king sablang pignasan mu kang GUINU a kekang Dios karing king Horeb king aldo na ning pamipamisan, ngamu, E mu paramdam pasibayu kaku ing siwala nang GUINU a kakung Dios, ni e mu na papakit pa iting maragul a api, ba kung a mate.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:17</lbl>	At sinabi nang GUINU kanaku, Sinabi rang mayap ing karelang selese.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:18</lbl>	Kaku yang italakad karela ing metung a manula manibat king libutad da ding karelang kapatad, a anti mo ika; at ibili ku ing kakung amanu king asbuk na, at salesean na karela ing anggang yutus ku kea.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:19</lbl>	At mapalyari, king ninumang e makiramdam karing kakung amanu a salesean na king kanakung laguiu, kakung usisan kea.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:20	</lbl>Dapot ing manula, a manalese king metung a amanu a maki kapalaluan king kakung laguiu, a iti e ku inutus pasabi kea, o maniabi ya king laguiu ra ding aliwang dioses, ing kabud manulang ita mate ya.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:21	</lbl>At nung sabian mu king kekang pusu, Makananu ming abalu ing amanung e na sinabing GUINU?	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>18:22</lbl>	Ngening ing metung a manula manalese ya king laguiu nang GUINU, nung ing bague e salisi ni mapalyari man, oita ing bague a e na selese GUINU: ing manula sinabi na king pamagpalalu, e me pitatakutan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:1</lbl>	Nung ikawani nong GUINU a kekang Dios ding bansa, a ing labuad da ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, at keka lang alilan, at manuknangan ka karing karelang ciudad, at karing karelang bale;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:2</lbl>	Mikawani kang atlung ciudad king libutad na ning kekang labuad, a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios ba mung bandian.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:3</lbl>	Isadia me keka ing dalan, at pirakayan mu ing angganan na ning kekang labuad, a pamana na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, king atlung dake, bang ing balang mekamate tau makatakas ya karin.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:4</lbl>	At oini ing bague na ning mekamate tau, a tumakas karin at mie ya; ninumang mekapate king keang kalupang tau king e na sasarian, at e ne kemuan king panaun a milabasan;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:5</lbl>	Anti mo ngening ing metung a tau ume ya king kakewan a kayabe ne ing lupa nang tau ba lang kubutud dutung, at ing gamat na mitabagkus ya king metung nang asiwas king palakul king pamangutud na king dutung, at mibalukas ya ing pataram king palda, at dimpa ya king lupa nang tau, nanupata iti mate ya; iti tumakas ya king metung karing ciudad a deti at mie ya:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:6</lbl>	Magkang tagalan ne ning manablas king daya ing mekapate tau, kabang ing keang pusu milalablab ya, at dasnan ne, uling ing dalan makaba ya, at sugatan neng mabayat; a e ya man karampatan king kamatayan, pauli ning e ne kemuan king panaun a milabsan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:7</lbl>	Inya yuyutus ku keka, sasabian ku, Mikawani kang atlung ciudad dikil keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:8</lbl>	At nung paragulan na ing kekang angganan GUINUNG kekang Dios, anti mo ing simpa na karing kekang mangatua, at ibie na keka ing mabilug a labuad a pengaku nang ibie karing kekang mangatua;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:9</lbl>	Nung pamintuan mung daptan ing mabilug a utus a iti, a yuyutus ku keka king aldo a iti, a luguran me I GUINU a kekang Dios, at lumakad ka ka kapilan man karing keang dalan; kanita dagdag ka pang atlung ciudad dikil keka, subali kareting atlu:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:10</lbl>	Bang e mibubu ing dayang alang kasalanan king libutad ning kekang labuad, a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios a pekamana, at uli niti mitumpak keka ing daya.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:11</lbl>	Dapot nung ninumang lalaki pikasaman ne ing kalupa nang tau, at abatan ne, at talakad yang salang kea, at sugatan neng mabayat, nanupata mate ya, at tumakas ya king metung karing ciudad a deti;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:12</lbl>	Kanita ding makatua pin king keang ciudad mitubud la at kuanan de karin, at ibie re king gamat na ning talapanablas daya, ba yang mate.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:13</lbl>	Ing kekang mata e ne lunusan, nung e ilako mu king Israel ing dayang alang kasalanan, ba yang ume mayap keka.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:14	</lbl>E me yayalis ing tanda nang gabun ning lupa mung tau, a binili ra kanita pang panaun a minuna, king kekang mana a kekang manan, king labuad a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios bamung bandian.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:15</lbl>	Ing metung a saksi e ya makatalakad salang king metung a lalaki dikil king nanumang dewakan, o dikil king nanumang kasalanan, king nanumang kasalanan a keang pikasalanan: king asbuk da ding aduang saksi, o king asbuk da ding atlung saksi, ing metung a piamanuan mipatibayan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:16</lbl>	Nung ing metung a malaram a saksi talakad yang salang king kaninumang tau bayang magsaksi salang kea king metung a marawak a dapat,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:17</lbl>	Nung makanian ding adua kataung deta, a mika pisasabian talakad la king arapan nang GUINU, king arapan da ding sacerdotes at ding ukum a salukuyan karing aldo a deta;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:18	</lbl>At siasatan dang mayap ding ukum: at, oini, nung ing saksi metung yang saksing malaram, at sinaksi yang kalaraman salang king kapatad na;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:19	</lbl>Kanita daptan mu pin kea, anti mo ing inisip nang daptan king keang kapatad; nung makanian alako mu ing dewakan king libutad mu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:20</lbl>	At ding mitagan damdaman da, at tumakut la, at e no magkamit pa king anti kanitang dewakan king libutad mu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>19:21</lbl>	At ding kekang mata e la lumunus; ing bie milako tungkul king bie, mata libe mata, ipan libe ipan, gamat libe gamat, bitis libe bitis.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:1</lbl>	Ngening lulual kang makipamuk laban karing kekang kasalang, at manakit kang kabayu, at carro, at metung a balayan a maiguit keka, e ka tatakut karela; uling i GUINU a kekang Dios mamantabe ya keka, a ya ing milual keka ibat king labuad na ning Egipto.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:2</lbl>	At mapalyari, pangalapit yu king pamipamuk, a ing sacerdote lumapit ya at maniabi ya king balayan,	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:3</lbl>	At sabian na karela, Pakiramdaman mu, Oh Israel, lumapit kayu king aldo a iti king pamipamuk laban karing kekong kasalang: e ye paburen masisindak ing kekong pusu; e ko tatakut, ni gagalgal man, ni maguing mataloti man tungkul karela;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:4</lbl>	Uling i GUINU a kekong Dios ya ing mame a kaya be yu, bang makipamuk tungkul kekayu laban karing kekong kasalang, ba nakong iligtas.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:5</lbl>	At ding pekapun maniabi la king balayan, a sabian da, Ninung tau ing mitalakad metung a bayung bale, at e ne telaga? Pabustan yang mako at mibalik ya king keang bale, magkang mate ya king pamipamuk, at aliwa yang tau ing mitalaga kaniti.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:6</lbl>	At ninung tau ing ating tenam a metung a uvasan, at e ne guinamit ing bunga na niti? pabustan yang mako at mibalik ya king keang bale, magkang mate ya king pamipamuk, at aliwa yang tau ing gumamit king bunga na niti.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:7</lbl>	At ninung lalaki ing pepakasal king metung a babai, at e ne kinua? pabustan yang mako at mibalik ya king keang bale, magkang mate ya king pamipamuk, at aliwa yang tau ing kuma king keang asawa.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:8</lbl>	At maniabi la pa ding pun king balayan, at karelang sabian, Ninung lalaki ing mataloti at maina lub? pabustan yang mako at mibalik king keang bale, magkang ing pusu ra ding keang kapatad malaso ya anti mo ing keang pusu.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:9</lbl>	At malyari, nung ding pekapun meari nong mekapaniabi king balayan, a malal lang capitan karing ejercitos king makauna king balayan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:10	</lbl>Ngening lumapit ka king metung a ciudad bang makipamuk laban kaniti, kanita ipasiag mu pin kaniti ing kapayapan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:11</lbl>	At malyari, nung pakibatan naka king kapayapan, at busnianan naka, kanita mapalyari pin, king ing mabilug a balayan a mayakit king kilub na maguing sakup mu, at sumuyu keka.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:14	</lbl>Dapot ding babai, at ding mangalating anak, at ding animal, at ing anggang atiu king ciudad, pati na pin ing mabilug a mesamsam karin, kuanan mung pekasamsam tungkul keka; at kanan mu ing mesamsam karing kekang kasalang, a binie na kekang GIUNU a kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:15</lbl>	Makanian ing kekang daptan karing anggang ciudad a tutung marayu keka, a e la karing ciudad ding bansang deti.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:16	</lbl>Dapot karing ciudad da ding balayan a deti, a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios a pekamana, e ka mitatagan a maki bie karing nanumang bague a mangisnawa;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:17</lbl>	Nung e lipulan mong lubus: ing Heteo, at ing Amoreo, ing Cananeo, at ing Perezeo, ing Heveo, at ing Jebuseo; anti mo ing inutus na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:18</lbl>	Ba rakong e iturung dapat king makaagpang karing sabla rang makasumami, a daraptan da karing karelang dioses; nanupata mikasala kayu laban kang GUINU a kekong Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>20:19</lbl>	Ngening kukubkuban yeng makabang panaun ing metung a ciudad, king pamakipamuk yu laban kea bang akua ye, e yo sisiran ding dutung a makatanam karin king pamamilatan na ning palakul a ipalakul yu karela; uling malyaring kanan yula at e yo kukuturan; uling ing dutung king marangle wari tau ya, a kailangan ya pang kubkuban yo?

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:5</lbl>	At ding sacerdotes a anak nang Levi lumapit la; uling ila ing pinili nang GUINU a kekang Dios bang manibala dikil kea, at panuan king laguiu nang GUINU; at agpang king karelang amanu mayari ing balang piamanuan at balang pamipate.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:6</lbl>	At ding anggang makatua king ciudad a ita, a makalapit king taung pete, manuas lang gamat babo ning dumalagang vaca a pikli ra batal king libis;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:14</lbl>	At malyari, nung ala kang tula kea, kanita paburen me ping mako nung nukarin ing buri na; dapot e me pisasali king salapi, e me pakiutusan anti mong metung a alipan, uling keka yang inumis.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:15	</lbl>Nung ing metung a lalaki atin yang aduang asawa, ing metung kaluguran ne, at ing metung pikakasaman, ne at deti parapara lang mikaanak kea, ing luluguran na at ing pikakasaman na; at nung ing maguing pangane a lalaki king pikakasaman ya;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:16	</lbl>Kanita malyari, king aldo a pamana na karing keang anak ing keang bandi, king e ne agawang pangane ing anak na king kaluguran na a makauna king anak ning pikakasaman na, a ya ing pangane;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:17	</lbl>Nung e kea yang patunayan ing pangane, ing anak na ning pikakasaman na, a dinan neng aduang dake karakal king sablang kayatinan na; uling ya ing mula na ning keang sikanan; ing katuliran na ning pangapangane kea.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:18</lbl>	Nung ing metung a tau mika atin yang anak a lalaki a masias a lub at mapanlaban, a e ya mamintu king siwala na ning keang ibpa, o king siwala na ning keang indu, at, king bistat parusan de, e ya makiramdam karela;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:19</lbl>	Kanita talanan ne pin ning keang ibpa at ning keang indu, at dalan de karing makatua king keang ciudad, at king pasbulan ning keang karinan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>21:21</lbl>	At pamukulan deng batu ding anggang lalaki king keang ciudad bayang mate: makanian mung ilako ing dewakan king libutad mu; at damdaman na ning mabilug a Israel, at tumakut.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>22:2</lbl>	At nung ing kekang kapatad e ya malapit keka, o nung e me balu, kanita yuli me pin king kekang bale, at atiu keka angga king ing kapatad mu panintunan ne, at isubli me kea.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>22:5</lbl>	Ing metung a babai e na susulud ing makatungkul king metung a lalaki, ni ing metung a lalaki man e ya misusulud imalan babai; uling ninumang darapat king bague a iti makasumami ya kang GUINU a kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>22:7</lbl>	King makananumang bague ibulus me ing gaindu, dapot ding malutub akua mulang maguing keka; bakang maguing mayap, at bang apakaban mo ding kekang aldo.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>22:8</lbl>	Nung maitatalakad kang metung a bayung bale, kanita gawa kang metung a kulung dikil king kekang bubungan, bakang e magdalang daya king babo ning kekang bale, nung ing ninumang tau mabaldug ya manibat kaniti.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>22:9</lbl>	E me tatamnan ing kekang uvasan karing aduang itsurang bini; magkang ing anggang bunga masira ya, ing bini a kekang tenam, at ing bunga na ning uvasan.

At iladlad da ing imalan king arapan da ding makatua ning ciudad.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:3</lbl>	E ya milub ing metung a Ammonita o metung a Moabita king kapulungan nang GUINU; angga man pin king kapulung dai alang kapaintulutan karing kananayunan da a milub king kapulungan nang GUINU king kapilan man;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:4</lbl>	Uling e rako seganan tinape at danum king dalan, kanitang lual kong ibat Egipto, at uling inupajan de laban keka i balaam a anak nang Beor manibat king Petor ning Mesopotamia banakang isumpa.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:5</lbl>	Makanian man e ne pekiramdaman GUINUNG kekang Dios i balaam; nung e guewa nang kanuanan GUINU a kekang Dios ing sumpa na keka, uling kaluguran nakang GUINUNG kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:8</lbl>	Ding anak a king katlung dai a penganak karela milub la king kapulungan nang GUINU.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:10</lbl>	Nung atin ka king ninumang tau, a e malinis tungkul king nanumang ararapat na king bengi, kanita lual ya ping malakue king parang, e lulub king parang:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:11</lbl>	Dapot mapalyari, pangagatpanapun, mandilu ya king danum; at pangalbug na ning aldo, lungub ya king parang.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:12	</lbl>Ika mika atin ka namang metung a karinan king lual ning parang, a kekang pilualan:	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:13</lbl>	At ika mika atin ka namang metung a pala a kayabe ra ding kekang sandata at malyari, ngening ika ume kang gulut king malakue, kulkul ka karin, at mibalik ka at takpan mu ing linual a ibat keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:14	</lbl>Uling i GUINU a kekang Dios lalakad ya king libutad na ning kekang parang, banakang iligtas, at ibie no ding kasalang mu king arapan mu; inya pin ing kekang parang maguing banal sa, bayang e manakit nanumang marinat a bague keka, at mako yang gumulut keka.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:15	</lbl>E me babie king keang panginuan ing metung a ipus a tinakas ibat king keang panginuan a mine ya keka;	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:16</lbl>	Ya tuknang yang kayabe mu, king libutad mu, king karinan a keang pilinan king kilub na ning metung karing pasbulan mung dalan, a keang mayapan dili: e me alipitan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:17</lbl>	E ka mikaka ating babaing salaula karing anak nang babai ning Israel, ni mikaka atin mang sodomita karing anak nang lalaki ning Israel.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:18	</lbl>E mu daralan ing upa ning metung a patutut, o ding upa ning metung a asu, king bale nang GUINU a kekang Dios dikil king nanumang panata: uling ding adua ping deti makasumami la kang GUINU a kekang Dios.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:19</lbl>	E ka paparam a maki patubu king kekang kapatad; patubu ning salapi patubu ding kakanan, patubu ning nanumang bague a paparam a patubuan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:20</lbl>	King metung a manaliwang balen makaparam kang patubuan; dapot king kekang kapatad e ka paparam a patubuan, banakang panuanan GUINU a kekang Dios king sablang atalan mu king kekang gamat, king labuad a luban mu bamung bandian.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:21	</lbl>Ngening manata kang metung a panata kang GUINU a kekang Dios, e ka makupad king pamamayad: uling alang salang usisan nang GUINU a kekang Dios keka; at maguing kasalanan keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:22</lbl>	Dapot nung ika mingat kang manata, e maguing kasalanan keka.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:23	</lbl>Ing lual karing kekang labi kekang tuparan at daptan; agpang king penata mu kang GUINU a kekang Dios, metung a kusang ain, a pengaku mu king kekang asbuk.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:24	</lbl>Ngening lungub ka king uvasan na ning lupa mung tau, kanita makapangan ka karing uvas king kaburian mu angga king kumabsi ka; dapot e ka milululan aguiang nanu king kekang lulanan.	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>23:25</lbl>	Ngening lungub ka king makatalakad nang binutil ning lupa mung tau, kanita ayagtal muking kekang gamat ing tinalague; dapot e me kikimut ing lait king makatalakad nang binutil ning lupa mung tau.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:1</lbl> 	Ngening ing metung a lalaki kinanua yang asawa na, at kesal ne, kanita malyari pin, nung king babai e ya menakit malyari pin, uling menakit yang makarine a bague kea, king sumulat yang metung a pitandanan king pamikawani, at ibie ne king keang gamat, at palakuan ne king keang bale. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:2</lbl> 	at pangalako na king bale na, malyari yang ume a maguing asawa na ning aliwang lalaki. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:3</lbl> 	At nung akasaman ne ning tauli nang asawa, at isulat neng metung a pitandanan king pamikawani, at ibie ne king keang gamat, at palakuan ne king keang bale; o nung mate ya ing tauli nang asawa, a kinanua kea baneng maguing asawa; 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:4</lbl> 	Ing keang minunang asawa, a mitabi kea, e na ne akuang pasibayu a maguing asawa na, kaibat na ning keang pangamusingan; uling ita makasumami king arapan nang GUINU: at e mu gagawan palpikasala ing labuad a binie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios a pekamana. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:5</lbl> 	Ngening ing metung a lalaki bayu yang kasal, e ya lulual a kayabe king ejercito, ni papanibalan man king nanumang kapanintunan: maguing timawa ya king pibale-bale king lub ning pabanua, at pasayan ne ing keang asawa a keang kinua. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:6</lbl> 	E ne kakuanan sangla ning ninumang tau ing panlalam ning guilingan o ing pamabo man; uling anti ne mong kinuang pekasangla ing bie na ning tau. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:7</lbl> 	Nung ing metung a tau mayakit yang panakawan ne ing ninuman karing keang kapatad karing anak na ning Israel, at pakiutusan neng anting metung a alipan, o pisali ne; kanita ing mapanako a ita mate ya: makanian mung ilako ing dewakan king libutan mu. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:8</lbl> 	Maningat ka king sakit a lepra, bamung banten maingat, at daptan mu ing agpang king anggang ituru ra keka ding sacerdoteng Levitas: nung makananu ing inutus ku karela, makanian mung pamintuan daptan. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:9</lbl> 	Ganakan mu ing depatan nang GUINU a kekang Dios kang Miriam, king dalan inyang lulual kong ibat Egipto. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:10</lbl> 	Ngening paparam ka king lupa mung tau king nanumang bague a dinam, e ka lulub king keang bale bang kuma king keang sangla. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:11</lbl> 	Talakad ka lual, at ing lalaki a kekang peparaman ilual na ing sangla keka. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:12</lbl> 	At nung iti kalulu ya e ka matudtud king sangla na keka; 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:13</lbl> 	Alang salang isubli me kea ing sangla pangalbug ning aldo, bayang matudtud king keang imalan, at panuanan naka: at maguing katuliran keka king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:14</lbl> 	E me alipitan ing metung a ipus a makiupa a maluka at mangailangan, aguiang karing kekang kapatad, o karing manaliwang labuad a atiu king kekang labuad king kilub ding kekang pasbulan dalan: 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:15</lbl> 	King keang aldo ibie mu kea ing keang upa, ni e ya kayayalbugan mang aldo (uling pakakalulu ya, at yang patakaran na ning keang pusu); magkang dalung ya kang GUINU salang keka, at maguing kasalanan mu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:16</lbl> 	E la patayan ding ibpa king uli ra ding anak na, ni patayan man ding anak king uli ra ding mangatua ra: ing balang katau patayan ya king uli na ning kasalanan nang sarili. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:17</lbl> 	E mu liliku ing matulid a mangaintulid king tau king aliwang labuad, o king ulilang tata, ni e mu mu naman kakuanan sangla ing imalan na ning babaing mebalu; 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:18</lbl> 	Dapot kekang ganakan king ika meguing alipan ka karin Egipto, at inatbus nakang GUINU a kekang Dios a menibatan karin: inya yutus ku keka a daptan mu ing bague a iti. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:19</lbl> 	Ngening palutan mu ing kekang pupul king kekang marangle, at mekakalinguan kang metung a kaptas king marangle, e mu ne babalikan kakuanan: mike ne king tau king aliwang balayan, king ulilang tata, at king mebalung babai; banakang panuanan GUINU a kekang Dios king sablang dapat da ding kekang gamat. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:20</lbl> 	Ngening keka yang papaspasan ing kekang kapun a olivo, e mu no babalikan pasibayu ding sanga: mike na mu king tau king aliwang balayan, king ulilang tata, at king babaing mebalu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:21</lbl> 	Ngening mamagtal ka karing uvas king kekang uvasan, e mu nanapnapan ing king guilutan mu: mike king tau king aliwang balen, king ulilang tata, at king babaing mebalu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>24:22</lbl> 	At ganakan mu king meguing alipan ka king labuad na ning Egipto: inya yutus ku keka a daptan mu ing bague a iti. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:1</lbl> 	Nung mika atin lang pamisalangsangan ding lalaki, at magsakdal la king piukuman, at ding ukum atulan dala; kanita ya ping pamatuliran da ing maki katuliran, at parusan de ing marawak.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:2</lbl> 	At malyari, nung ing marawak a tau karampatan yang batbatan, king pasakban ne ning ukum, at mabatbat ya king keang arapan, agpang king keang dewakan, makabilang. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:3</lbl> 	Apatapulung batbat ing ibie na kea, e na palapsuan; magkang, nung palapsuan na, at batbatan neng maiguit kaniti a dakal a batbat, ing keka ping kapatad kanita maguing balamu mura ya keka. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:4</lbl> 	E me dirinan busal ing vaca nung dadara yang binutil. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:5</lbl> 	Nung ding mikapatad manuknangan lang miabe, at nung ing metung karela mate ya, at ala yang anak, ing asawa na ning mete e ya makiasawa king lual king metung a aliwang labuad: ing kapatad na ning keang asawa sumiping ya kea, at kuanan neng maguing keang asawa, at tuparan na kea ing katungkulan na ning pangakapatad na kea ning keang asawa. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:6</lbl> 	At malyari, king ing pangane a keang ipanganak mialili ya king laguiu na ning kapatad nang mete, bang ing keang laguiu e mapda king Israel. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:7</lbl> 	At nung e ne buring kuanan ning lalaki ing asawa na ning keang kapatad, kanita ing asawa na pin ning keang kapatad sampa ya king pasbulan dalan karing makatua, at sabian na, Ing kapatad na ning kakung asawa tatanggiu yang italakad na king Israel ing laguiu na ning keang kapatad; e na buring tuparan kanaku ing katungkulan na ning keang kapatad king pangaasawa. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:8</lbl> 	Kanita ausan de ding makatua king keang ciudad, at pakisabian de: at nung talakad ya, at sabian na, E ke buring kuanan;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:9</lbl> 	Kanita ing asawa na ning kapatad na ume ya kea king arapan da ding makatua, at ilukas ne ing sapin na king keang bitis, at luran ne king lupa; at makibat ya at sabian na, Makanian ing marapat king lalaki a e bisang mitalakad king bale na ning keang kapatad.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:10</lbl> 	At ing laguiu na mayaus king Israel, Ing bale na ning likas a sapin. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:11</lbl> 	Ngening ding aduang lalaki mipapate la ing metung at metung, at ing asawa na ning metung linapit ya baneng iligtas ing keang asawa king gamat na ning susugat kea, at guinong ne ing keang gamat, at telanan no ding kasangkapan nang lijim; 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:12</lbl> 	Kanita pututan me pin ing keang gamat, ing kekang mata e la lumunus.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:13</lbl> 	E ka mikaka atin king kekang bulsa a timbangan a e mititimbang, metung a maragul at metung a malati. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:14</lbl> 	E ka mikaka atin king kekang bale takalan a e misusukad, metung a maragul at metung a malati. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:15</lbl> 	Mika atin kang metung a tapat at katutuan a timbangan; mika atin kang metung a tapat at katutuan a takalan: bang ding kekang aldo kumaba la king babo na ning labuad a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:16</lbl> 	Uling detang anggang darapat king anti kaniting bague, detang anggang darapat pin a e katuliran, makasumami la kang GUINU a kekang Dios. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:17</lbl> 	Ganakan mu ing depatan na kekang Amalek king dalan inyang lulual ka Egipto; 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:18</lbl> 	Nung makananu nakang selubungan king dalan, at sigatan no ding tauling dili keka, detang anggang maina a atiu king tauli mu, kanitang mangalambut na ka at tikal; at e ya tinakut king Dios. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>25:19</lbl> 	Uli niti malyari pin, ngening i GUINU a kekang Dios dininan nakang kapainawan karing sabla mung kasalang king makapatulug, king labuad a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios a pekamana bamung bandian, bang apatda mu ing kapigaganakan kang Amalek king lalam ning banua; e mu kakalinguan. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:1</lbl> 	At malyari, pangalub mu king labuad a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios a pekamana, at kekang bandian iti, at kekang panuknanganan iti, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:2</lbl> 	King kuanan mu ing mumuna king sablang bunga na ning gabun, a kekang ilub manibat king kekang labuad a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios; at ilulan mu king buslu, at ume ka king karinan a pilinan nang GUINU kekang Dios, banang papanuknanganan ing keang laguiu karin. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:3</lbl> 	At ume ka king sacerdoteng salukuyan karing aldo a deta, at sabian mu kea, Kakung papasiag king aldo ngeni kang GUINU a kekang Dios, king aku linub ku king labuad a simpa nang GIUNU karing kekeng mangatua banang ibie kekami. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:4</lbl> 	At kuanan ne ning sacerdote ing buslu king kekang gamat, at ibili ne king arapan ning altar nang GUINU a kekang Dios. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:5</lbl> 	At ika makibat ka, at sabian mu king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, Metung yang tau Siria a malapit nang mate ing kanakung ibpa; at kinuldas ya karin Egipto, at menaliwang balen karin, a ditak mu king bilang; at karin meguing metung yang bansa, maragul, masikanan, at dakal.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:6</lbl> 	At pekiutusan dakeng marawak ding tau Egipto, at pepasakitan dakami, at timpak da kekami ing masakit a pangaalipan:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:7</lbl> 	At dinalung kami kang GIUNU, ing Dios da ding kekeng mangatua, at pekiramdaman nang GUINU ing kekeng siwala, at ikit na ing kekeng kasakitan, at ing kekeng daraptan, at ing kekeng pangaalipit; 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:8</lbl> 	At liwal nakaming GUINU karin Egipto kambe ning metung a gamat a masikanan, at kambe ning makayatyat a takde, at kambe ning maragul makapangilabut, at kambe ding tanda, at kambe ding makapagmulala;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:9</lbl> 	At dela nakami king karinan a iti, at binie na kekami ing labuad a iti, metung a labuad a agusan na ning gatas at pulut. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:10</lbl> 	At ngeni, oini, dela ku ing mumunang bunga na ning gabun, a ika, Oh GUINU, binie mu kaku. At ibili mu king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, at samba ka king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios: 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:11</lbl> 	At tumula ka king anggang mayap a ibie na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios, at king kekang bale, ika, at ing Levita, at ing tau king aliwang balen king libutad mu.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:12</lbl> 	Nung ayari mu na ing pamagsikapulu king sablang sikapulu ning kekang alabis a pupul king katlung banua, a ya ing banua na ning pamagsikapulu, kanita ibie mu pin king Levita, king tau king aliwang balen, king ulilang tata, at king babaing mebalu, balang mangan king kilub ding kekang pasbulan dalan, at kumabsi la. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:13</lbl> 	At sabian mu king arapan nang GUINU a kekang Dios, Kanaku lang leko ding pepapagbanalan a bague king kakung bale, at binie kula naman king Levita, at king tau king aliwang labuad, king ulilang tata, at king babaing mebalu, agpang king anggang utus mu a inutus mu kanaku: e ku sinalangsang kaisanuman karing kekang utus, ni e ko kelinguan man: 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:14</lbl> 	E ku mengan kaniti king kakung pamagpaldas, ni e ku minugse man kaniti, bistat marinat, ni e ku naman minie kaniti dikil king mete: mekiramdam ku king siwala nang GUINU a kakung Dios; depatan ku ing agpang kanitang sablang inutus mu kanaku. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:15</lbl> 	Lumawe ka lalam a manibatan king kekang banal a tuknangan, manibat banua, at panuanan me ing kekang balayan a Israel, at ing gabun a binie mu kekami, anti mo ing simpa mu karing kekeng mangatua, a metung a labuad a agusan na ning gatas at pulut. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:16</lbl> 	King aldo a iti yuyutus na kekang GUINU a kekang Dios a tuparan mula deting tuntunan at kautusan: keka la ping tuparan at daptan king mabilug mung pusu, at king mabilug mung kaladua. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:17</lbl> 	Keka yang pisiag king aldo a iti i GUINU a ya ing kekang Dios, at king ika lumakad ka karing keang dalan, at tuparan mula ding keang tuntunan, at ding keang utus, at ding keang kautusan, at pekiramdaman mu ing keang siwala: 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:18</lbl> 	At papasiag nakang GUINU king aldo a iti a maguing metung kang balayan a keang sariling bandi, anti mo ing pengaku na keka, at king bamong tuparan ding anggang utus na. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>26:19</lbl> 	At banakang itas babo ra ding anggang bansa a keang guewa, king kapurian, at king laguiu, at king puri; at bang ika maguing metung kang banal a balayan kang GUINU a kekang Dios, anti mo ing sinabi na. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:1</lbl> 	At i Moises at ding makatua na ning Israel inutus da ing balayan, sinabi ra, Tuparan yu ing anggang utus a yutus ku kekayu king aldo a iti. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:2</lbl> 	At malyari king aldo a dalakitan ye ing Jordan a mame ko king labuad a ibie na kekayung GUINU a kekong Dios, a misalansan kong kekayu mangaragul a batu, at palitadan yong palitada: 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:3</lbl> 	At isulat yo kareti ding anggang amanu na niting kautusan, nung midalakit na kayu; bayung aluban ing labuad a babie na kekayung GUINU a kekong Dios, a metung a labuad a agusan na ning gatas at pulut, anti mo ing pengaku nang GUINU, a Dios da ding mangatua yu, kekayu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:4</lbl> 	At malyari, pangadalakit yu king Jordan, king isalansan yo ding batung deti, a yutus ku kekayu king aldo a iti, king bunduk ning Ebal, at palitadan yong palitada. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:5</lbl> 	At karin mitalakad kong metung a altar kang GUINU a kekong Dios, metung a altar karing batu: e ko mibubuat kareti a kasangkapan a bakal. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:6</lbl> 	Italakad ye ing altar nang GUINU a kekong Dios karing batu a e melabra; at miain ko king babo na ain a durulukan kang GUINU a kekong Dios. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:7</lbl> 	At midaun kong ain tungkul king kapayapan, at mangan kayu karin; at magsaya kayu king arapan nang GUINU a kekong Dios. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:8</lbl> 	At kekong isulat a masala karing batung deta ing anggang amanu na ning kautusan a iti. 

Moises at ding sacerdoteng Levitas miniabi la king mabilug a Israel, a sinabi ra, Magtajimik ka, at pakiramdaman mu, Oh Israel: King aldo ngeni meguing balayan nakang GUINU a kekang Dios. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:10</lbl> 	Keka ping pamintuan ing siwala nang GUINU a kekang Dios, at daptan mula ding keang utus at ding keang tuntunan, yuyutus ku keka king aldo a iti. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:11</lbl> 	At penabilinan nang Moises ing balayan king aldo mu ring ita, a sinabi na, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:12</lbl> 	Deti talakad la king babo ning bunduk ning Gerizim barang panuanan ing balayan, ngening adalakitan yu ne ing Jordan: i Simeon, at i Levi, at i Juda, at i Isacar, at i Jose, at i Benjamin. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:13</lbl> 	At deti talakad la king babo na ning bunduk ning Ebal dikil king sumpa: i Reuben, i Gad, at i Aser, at i Zabulon, i Dan, at i Naftali.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:14</lbl> 	At ding Levitas makibat la, at maniabi la king masikan a siwala karing sablang lalaki king Israel, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:15 </lbl>	Misumpa ya ing lalaking gawang metung a larawan a dinukit o bibu, metung a makasumami kang GUINU, ing dapat da ding gamat na ning mamangawa, at tatalakad de king lijim. At ing mabilug a balayan makibat at sabian na, Yanasa. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:16</lbl> 	Misumpa ya itang lapastangan king keang ibpa o king keang indu. At ing mabilug a balayan sabian na, Yanasa. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:17</lbl> 	Misumpa ya itang mialis king tanda ning gabun na ning keang kalupang tau. At ing mabilug a balayan sabian na, Yanasa.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:18</lbl> 	Misumpa ya itang milili king dalan king bulag. At ing mabilug a balayan sabian na, Yanasa. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:19</lbl> 	Misumpa ya itang miliku king katuliran na ning tau king aliwang balayan, ning ulilang tata, at ning babaing mebalu. At ing mabilug a balayan sabian na, Yanasa. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:20</lbl> 	Misumpa ya itang sumiping king asawa nang ibpa na, uling linislis ne ing balabal nang ibpa na. At ing mabilug a balayan sabian na, Yanasa. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>27:21</lbl> 	Misumpa ya itang mekipangatawan king kaisanumang animal. At ing mabilug a balayan sabian na, Yanasa.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:36</lbl> 	Uling atulan nang GUINU ing keang balayan, At sumisi yang dili na uli ding keang talasuyu; Pamanakit nang ing karelang kayupayan mewala, At ala nang makatagan, a makatakap o melakuan king karagulan. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:37</lbl> 	At sabian na, Nu la karin ding karelang dioses, Ing roca a nung nula migsantung; 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:38</lbl> 	A mengan king taba ra ding karelang daun, At mininum king alak ning karelang ain a inuman? Pabustan mong mibangun at saupan daka, Pabustan mung ila ding kekang manlualu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:39</lbl> 	Lawan mu ngeni king aku, aku pin, aku ya, At alang dios a kayabe ku: Makamate ku, at bibie ku; Susugat ku, at pakayap ku; At alang malyaring miligtas king gamat ku.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:40</lbl> 	Uling tatas ke ing kanakung gamat banua, At sasabian ku, Anti ning aku mabie ku king kapilan pa man, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:41</lbl> 	Nung kaku yang itais ing makintab kung talibung, At ing kakung gamat talanan na ing kayatulan; Ibie ku ing kakung pamanablas karing kakung kaskal, At ablasanan kula detang mimua kanaku. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:42</lbl> 	Palasingan ko king daya ding kanakung uyung, At ing talibung ku manlaklak yang laman; King daya ra ding pete sandata at karing bijag, Manibat king buntuk da ding talataid na ning kasalang. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:43</lbl> 	Pasipagsaya kayu, Oh ikong bansa, a kagum ning keang balayan: Uling yablas na ing daya ra ding keang talasuyu, At munie yang kablasan karing karelang kaskal, At dapat yang pamamatawad dikil king keang labuad, dikil king keang balayan. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:44</lbl> 	At i Moises mine ya at selese no ding anggang amanu na ning dalit a iti king daramdaman na ning balayan, ya, at i Oseas a anak nang Nun. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:45</lbl> 	At pinupus nong selese Moises ding anggang amanung deti king mabilug a Israel; 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy<lbl> 32:46</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela, Ibili ye ing kekong pusu karing anggang amanu a patutuan ku kekayu king aldo a iti, a yutus yu karing kekong anak barang tuntunan daptan, ding anggang amanu na pin ning kautusan a iti. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:47</lbl> 	Uling iti e alang kabaldugan a bague dikil kekayu; uling iti kekong bie, at uling king bague a iti pakaban yo ding kekong aldo king labuad, a kekong dalakitan king sumangid ning Jordan bayung bandian.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:48</lbl> 	At i GUINU miniabi ya kang Moises king aldo mu ring ita, sinabi na, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:49</lbl> 	Sampa ka king bunduk nang iti ning Abarim, a taglus angga king bunduk ning Nebo, a atiu king labuad na ning Moab, a atiu king tulid ning Jerico; at oini ing labuad na ning Canaan, a ibie ku karing anak na ning Israel a pekabandi;

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:50 </lbl>	At mate ka king bunduk a kekang sampan, at miagum ka king kekang balayan, anti mo i Aaron a kapatad mu a mete king bunduk na ning Hor, at miagum ya king keang balayan:

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:51</lbl> 	Uling sinalangsang kayu kanaku king libutad da ding anak na ning Israel king danum ning Meriba ning Cades, king ilang ning Zin; uling e yuku benalan king libutad da ding anak na ning Israel.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>32:52</lbl> 	Uling akit mu ing labuad king arapan mu; dapot karin e ka milub king labuad a ibie ku karing anak na ning Israel.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:1</lbl> 	At iti ing kanuanan a pepanuan nang Moises a lalaki ning Dios karing anak na ning Israel bayu ing keang kamatayan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na, I GUINU menibatan ya king Sinai, At mibangun yang menibatan king Seir a tumuru karela; Sinlag ya menibat king bunduk ning Paran, At menibatan ya karing apulu rang libu ding banal: King wanan nang gamat atiu ing metung a mabagsik a kautusan dikil karela. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:3</lbl> 	Wa, kea yang kaluguran ing balayan; Ding sabla nang banal ati lu king kekang gamat; At linukluk la karing kekang bitis; Ing balang metung tanggap ya karing kekang amanu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:4</lbl> 	I Moises minutus ya kekatamu a metung a kautusan, Metung yang mana dikil king kapulungan nang Jacob.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:5</lbl> 	At meguing ari ya king Jesurun, Inyang ding pekabuntuk na ning balayan mitipun la, Ding anggang dai ning Israel a makapamisan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:6</lbl> 	Mie ya i Reuben, at e mate; Ni e la naman diritak ding keang tau.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:7</lbl> 	At iti ing kanuanan kang Juda: at ngana, Makiramdam ka, GUINU, king siwala nang Juda, At ilub me king keang balayan. Karing keang gamat mekiaskal ya dikil king sarili na; At maguing metung kang saup salang karing keang kaskal.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:8</lbl> 	At kang Levi ngana, Ing kekang Tumim at ing kekang Urim ati lu karing kekang banal, A kekang sibukan king Masa, A nung kenu mekitua ka king danum ning Meriba; 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:9</lbl> 	A nung ninu ing miniabi king keang ibpa, at king keang indu, e ke ikit; Ni e no man pepakilala ding keang kapatad, Ni balu man ding kabud sariling anak na: Uling karelang pemintuan ing kekang amanu, At tiparan da ing kekang tipan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:10</lbl> 	Ituru ro kang Jacob ding kekang tuntunan, At king Israel ing kekang kautusan; Mibili lang labun king kekang arapan, At mabilug a ain a durulukan king babo ning kekang altar.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:11</lbl> 	Panuanan mu, GUINU, ing keang kayatinan, At tanggapan mu ing dapat ding gamat na: Sugatan mo king balakang detang mibabangun laban kea, At detang mimumua kea, bang e no mibangun miuman.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:12</lbl> 	Kang Benjamin ngana, Ing kaluguran nang GUINU manuknangan yang alang panganib siping na; Ya takpan ne king kekaban ning aldo, At manuknangan ya king pilatan ding keang pago.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:13</lbl> 	At kang Jose ngana, Pepanuanan na sang GUINU ing keang labuad, Dikil karing mal nang bague ning banua, dikil king ambun, At dikil king kalalaman a makabili lalam, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:14 </lbl>	At dikil karing mal a bague ding bunga ning aldo, At dikil karing mal a bague ning panubu ding bulan, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy<lbl> 33:15</lbl> 	At dikil karing pekamasanting a bague ding mangatuang bunduk, At dikil karing mal a bague ding alang anggang bunduk-bundukan, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:16 </lbl>	At dikil karing mal a bague ning labuad at ing anggang atiu kea, At ing mayap nang pilubluban ning manuknangan king mababang dutung. Pabustan yung dumpa ing kanuanan king buntuk nang Jose, At king bunbunan na ning keang buntuk nitang mikawani karing keang kapatad. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:17</lbl> 	Ing pangane ning keang kawan a vaca, dangalan ing kea; At ding sagu na sagu no ning maliap a toro: Uli ra deti idapulpul no ding balayan ila ngan, angga man pin ing wakas ning labuad: At ila ding apulu nang libu ning Efraim, At ila ding libu-libu nang Manases. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:18 </lbl>	At kang Zabulon ngana, Magsaya ka, Zabulon, king kekang pamaglual; At, Isacar, karing kekang kubu. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:19</lbl> 	Ausan do ding balayan king bunduk; Karin la main daun ning katuliran: Uling karelang aldukan ing kabsi ra ding dayatmalat, At ding makasalikut nang pibandian ning balas. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:20</lbl> 	At kang Gad ngana, Nuan ya itang paragul kang Gad; Manuknangan yang anti mong metung a leona, At pamirasuan ne ing takde, wa, ing bunbunan na ning buntuk. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:21</lbl> 	At telaga na kea ing mumunang dake dikil king sarili na, Uling karin ing dake na ning talapamie kautusan makatagan; At dinatang yang kayabe ra ding pekabuntuk ning balayan; Pepatupad na ing katuliran nang GUINU, At ding keang tuntunan king Israel. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:22</lbl> 	At kang Dan ngana, I Dan metung yang anak ning leon, A luluksung ibat king Basan. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:23 </lbl>	At kang Naftali ngana, Oh Naftali, a mabsi king kalam, At mitmu king kanuanan nang GUINU, Bandian mu ing albugan at ing mauli.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:24</lbl> 	At kang Aser ngana, Mipanuanan yang anak i Aser; Pabustan yang matanggap ya karing keang kapatad, At pabustan yang italbug ne ing keang bitis king laru. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:25 </lbl>	Ding kekang sandallas maguing bakal la at tangsu; At agpang karing aldo mu, makanian ing kekang sikanan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:26</lbl> 	Ala nang anti mo king Dios, Oh Jesurun, A sasake karing babo ding banua a pekasaup mu, At king keang karangal-dangalan king babo ra ding katasan. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:27</lbl> 	Ing alang anggang Dios ya ing kekang tuknangan, At king lalam ila ding alang anggang takde. At tutulak ne ing kasalang ibat king kekang arapan, At ngana, Sintangan mula. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:28</lbl> 	At ing Israel manuknangan yang alang panganib, Ing bukud na mung bukal Jacob, King metung a labuad ding binutil at bayung alak; Wa, ding keang banua papatak da ing ambun. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>33:29</lbl> 	Kasaya mo, Oh Israel: Ninu ing anti ika, a metung a balayan a linigtas nang GUINU, Ing kalasag ning kekang saup, At ing talibung ning kekang karangal-dangalan! At ding kekang kasalang isuku ra ing sarili ra keka; At tuklu ka king babo ra ding karelang mangatas a karinan.

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:1</lbl> 	At i Moises minukiat yang ibat karing kapatagan ning Moab king bunduk ning Nebo, angga king taluktuk ning Pisga, a atiu king tulid ning Jerico. At pepakit nang GUINU kea ing mabilug a labuad ning Gilead, angga king Dan, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:2</lbl> 	At ing mabilug a Naftali, at ing labuad ning Efraim at ning Manases, at ing mabilug a labuad na ning Juda angga king nangan nang gugulutan ning dayatmalat,

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:3</lbl> 	At ing Mauli, at ing Kapatagan ning libis ning Jerico, a ciudad da ding dutung a palma, angga king Zoar. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:4</lbl> 	At sinabi nang GUINU kea, Iti ing labuad a simpa ku kang Abraham, kang Isaac, at kang Jacob, a sinabi na, Ibie ku king kekang bini: kanakung pepaintulut keka a akit da ding kekang mata, dapot e ka dalakit a lungub karin. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:5</lbl> 	Inya i Moises a talasuyu nang GUINU mete ya karin king labuad na ning Moab, agpang king amanu nang GUINU. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:6</lbl> 	At kitkut ne king libis king labuad ning Moab a atiu king tulid na ning Betpeor: dapot ninumang lalaki alang makibalu king kutkutan na angga king aldo iti. 	

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:7</lbl> 	At i Moises dinalan ya at aduangpulung banua tua inyang mate ya: ing keang mata e ya melabug, ni ing talaga nang sikanan e kinulang. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:8</lbl> 	At kiniakan de ding anak na ning Israel i Moises karing kapatagan na ning Moab atlungpulung aldo: makanian meari ing aldo a pamanangis da king pamagpaldas kang Moises. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:9</lbl> 	At i Josue a anak nang Nun, mitmu yang espiritu ning kabiasnan; uling timpak nong Moises ding keang gamat kea: at pekiramdaman de ding anak na ning Israel, at depatan da ing anti mo ing inutus nang GUINU kang Moises. 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:10</lbl> 	At ala pang tinalakad a metung a manula king Israel a anti mo i Moises, a mekakilala kang GUINU lupa at lupa, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:11 </lbl>	Karing anggang tanda at makapagmulala, a pepabal nang GUINU kea a keang daptan king labuad na ning Egipto, kang Faraon, at karing anggang ipus na, at king mabilug nang labuad, 

Deuteronomio Deuteronomy <lbl>34:12</lbl> 	At king mabilug a mayupayang gamat, at king anggang maragul a makapangilabut, a depatan nang Moises king lalawan na ning mabilug a Israel. 


Title:Judges

<b>Ding Ukum Judges</b>

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:14</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang lungub ya kea ing babai, king inaguiag ne a maniawad ya kang ibpa na metung a marangle: at kinuldas ya king keang asno; at sinabi nang Caleb kea, Nanung buri mu? 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:15</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Dinan mukung metung a kanuanan; anti ning binili muku king labuad ning Mauli, dinan muku naman karing sibul ning danum. At i Caleb binie no kea ding sibul babo at ding sibul lalam. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:16</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Kineo, a bayo nang lalaking Moises, sinampa lang kayabe ra ding anak nang Juda manibat king ciudad da ding dutung a palma angga king ilang ning Juda a atiu king mauli na ning Arad; at mine la at menuknangan lang kayabe ning balayan. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:17</lbl> 	At i Juda mine ya a kayabe Simeon a kapatad na, at sigatan do ding Cananeos a manuknangan king Sefat, at lesakan deng lubus. At Horma ing inaus dang laguiu king ciudad a ita. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:18</lbl> 	Anti mu rin i Juda kinua na ing Gaza pati na ding keang angganan, at ing Ascelon pati na ding keang angganan, at ing Ecron pati na ding keang angganan, 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:19</lbl> 	At minantabe ya i Guinu kang Juda; at tinabi no ding manuknangan king karinan a bunduk-bundukan; uling e no atabi ding manuknangan king libis, uling atin lang carrong bakal. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:20</lbl> 	At binie ra kang Caleb ing Hebron, anti mo ing sinabi nang Moises: at tinabi no karin ding atlu nang anak Anak. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:21</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Benjamin e ro tinabi ding Jebuseos a menuknangan king Jerusalem; nung e manuknangan la ding Jebuseos a kayabe ra ding anak nang Benjamin king Jerusalem angga king aldo iti. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:22</lbl> 	At ing bale nang Jose, ila sinampa la naman salang king Bet-el; at minantabe ya i Guinu karela. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:23</lbl> 	At ing bale nang Jose mitubud ya barang tiktikan ing Bet-el. (Ngeni ing laguiu na ning ciudad kanitang minuna Luz). 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:24</lbl> 	At ikit de ding bante ing metung a lalaki a lulual ya king ciudad, at sinabi ra kea, Ipakit me kekami, pagamuamu mi keka, ing piluluban king ciudad, at makiabiayan keng maganaka keka. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:25</lbl> 	At tiru ne karela ing piluluban king ciudad; at sigatan de ing ciudad king taram na ning talibung; dapot pepalakuan de ing lalaki pati na ing mabilug nang sapni. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:26</lbl> 	At ing lalaki mine ya king labuad da ding Heteos, at telakad ne ing metung a ciudad, at pemalaguiuwan neng Luz, a iti ya ing laguiu na angga king aldo iti. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:27</lbl> 	At e no tinabing Manases ding manuknangan king Bet-sean at ding keang balen, ni ing Taanac man at ding keang balen, ni ding manuknangan man king Dor at ding keang balen, ni ding manuknangan king Ibleam at ding keang balen, ni ding manuknangan man Megido at ding keang balen; nung e ding Cananeos ilang makapanuknangan king labuad a ita. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:28</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang ing Israel mesikan ya, binili ro ding Cananeos king pamaniapat, at e no lubus palakuan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:29</lbl> 	At i Efraim man e no tinabi ding Cananeos a menuknangan king Gezer; nung e menuknangan la ding Cananeos king libutad da king Gezer. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:30</lbl> 	I Zabulon e no tinabi ding manuknangan king Kitron, ni ding manuknangan man king Nahalol; nung e ding Cananeos menuknangan la king libutad da, at meguing makasakup la king pamaniapat. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:31</lbl> 	I Aser e no tinabi ding manuknangan king Acco, ni ding manuknangan man king Sidon, ni ding king Ahlab, ni ding king Aczib ni ding king Helba, ni ding king Afic, ni ding king Rehob; 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:32</lbl> 	Dapot ding Aseritas menuknangan la king libutad da ding Cananeos, ding manuknangan king labuad; uling e ro tinabi. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:33</lbl> 	I Naftali e no tinabi ding manuknangan king Bet-semes, ni ding manuknangan king Bet-anat; nung e menuknangan ya king libutad da ing Cananeos, ding manuknangan king labuad: makanian man ding manuknangan king Bet-semes at king Bet-anat, meguing mesakup la king pamaniapat. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:34</lbl> 	At ding Amoreos pinilit do ding anak nang Dan a pepapuntan king karinan a bunduk-bundukan; uling e ro pepaintulutan kuldas king libis; 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:35</lbl> 	Dapot ding Amoreos makapanuknangan la king bunduk ning Heres, king Aijalon, at king Saalbim: makanian man miniambut ya ing gamat na ning bale nang Jose nanupata mesakup la king pamaniapat. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>1:36</lbl> 	At ing angganan da ding Amoreos manibat king ukiatan na ning Acrabim, manibat ya king batu, at paitas. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:1</lbl> 	At ing angel nang Guinu sinampa ya king Boquim manibat king Gilgal. At sinabi na, pepasampan dakayu a menibat Egipto, at dela rako king labuad a simpa ku karing kekong mangatua; at sinabi ku, E ku labagan kapilan man ing tipan ku kekayu: 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:2</lbl> 	At ikayu e ko gawang tipan karing manuknangan king labuad a iti; lasakan yula ding karelang altares. Dapot e ko mekiramdam king kanakung siwala: baket depatan yu iti? 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:3</lbl> 	Inya aku man sinabi ku, E ko itabi manibat king arapan yu: nung e maguing anti lang suksuk karing kekong katalindikingan, at ding karelang dioses maguing metung lang silu kekayu. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:4</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang ing angel nang Guinu asabi no deting amanu karing anggang anak na ning Israel, king ing balayan sikan na ing keang siwala at kiniak. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:5</lbl> 	At inaus dang Boquim ing laguiu ning karinan a ita; at dinaun la karin kang GUINU. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:6</lbl> 	Ngeni kanitang i Josue apalakuan na na ing balayan, ding anak na ning Israel mine la balang metung king karelang mana barang bandian ing labuad. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:7</lbl> 	At ing balayan sinuyu kang GUINU karing sablang aldo nang Josue, at karing sablang aldo ra ding makatuang mitagan a mebie kayabe nang Josue, a menakit king anggang mangaragul a dapat a depatan nang GUINU dikil king Israel. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:8</lbl> 	At i Josue a anak nang Nun, a talasuyu nang Guinu, mete ya, king tuang dinalan at apulung banua. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:9</lbl> 	At kitkut de king angganan na ning keang sariling mana king Timnat-heres, king karinan a bunduk-bundukan na ning Efraim, king paralaya na ning bunduk ning Gaas. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:10</lbl> 	At anti naman ing sablang daing ita miagum la karing karelang mangatua: at tinalakad la ding aliwang dai kaibat da, a e re balu i GUINU, ni ing dapat man a depatan na dikil king Israel. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:11</lbl> 	At ding anak na ning Israel dinapat lang marawak king panlalawe nang GUINU, at sinuyu la karing Baalim; 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:12</lbl> 	At pepaimburisan de I GUINU, ing Dios da ding karelang mangatua, a kinanua karela king labuad na ning Egipto, at tinuki la karing aliwang dioses, karing dioses da ding balayan a makapatulug karela, at dinuku la king arapan da: at pemungkasian de king mua i GUINU. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:13 </lbl>	At pepaimburisan de i GUINU, at sinuyu la kang baal at kang as-tarot. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:14</lbl> 	At ing mua nang GUINU milablab salang king Israel, at binie nala king gamat da ding manlub a minlub karela; at pisali nala king gamat da ding karelang kasalang king makapatulug, nanupata e no mitalakad maluat king arapan da ding karelang kasalang. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:15</lbl> 	Nu la man mine, ing gamat nang GUINU makalaban ya karela king pangarawak, anti mo ing sinabi nang GUINU, at anti mo ing simpa nang GUINU karela: at megutgut lang bina. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:16</lbl> 	At mitalakad yang ukum i GUINU, a migligtas karela king gamat da ding minlub karela. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:17</lbl> 	At makanian man e la mekiramdam karing karelang ukum; uling memialung lang patutut karing aliwang dioses, at dinuku la karela: pepailili lang malagua king dalan a lekaran da ding karelang mangatua, king pamamintu karing utus nang GUINU; dapot ila e ra depatan ing makanian. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:18</lbl> 	At inyang italakad nong ukum GUINU, kanita i GUINU mamantabe ya king ukum, at linigtas nala king gamat da ding karelang kasalang king sablang aldo na ding ukum: uling sinisi ya i Guinu king uli ning karelang dalung king uli ra ding menalipit karela at ding mengulu karela. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:19</lbl> 	Dapot milyari, pangamate na ning ukum, king mibalik la, at lalu la pang merawak a maiguit karing karelang mangatua, king pamanuki karing aliwang dioses barong suyuwan, at balang duku karela; e la tinuknang karing karelang dapat, ni king karelang paralan a kesiasan lub. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:20</lbl> 	At ing mua nang Guinu milablab salang king Israel; at ngana, Anti ning ing bansang iti lepastangan na ing tipan ku a inutus ku karing karelang mangatua, at e ra pekiramdaman ing siwala ku; 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:21</lbl> 	Aku man manibat ngeni e ku no itabi king arapan da ding bansa a likuan nang Josue kanitang mate ya; 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:22</lbl> 	Bang king pamamilatan da asubuk ku ing Israel, nung tuntunan da ing dalan nang GUINU bang lumakad la kaniti, anti mo ing pamamintu ra ding karelang mangatua kaniti, o ali. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>2:23</lbl> 	Inya likuan nong GUINU ding bansang deta, a e no tinabing marapal; ni binie man king gamat nang Josue. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:1</lbl> 	Ngeni oreti ila ding bansa a likuan nang GUINU, banang asubuk ing Israel king pamamilatan da, nung pilan at pilan la pin ding king Israel a e mekabalu karing anggang pamakipamuk ning Canaan; 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:2</lbl> 	Baramung abalu ding dai ra ding anak na ning Israel, banong ituru king pamakipamuk, ita mu mang e makibalu kaniti king minuna: 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:3</lbl> 	Ila pin, ding limang GUINU ra ding Filisteos, at ding anggang Cananeos, at ding Sidonios, at ding Heveos a manuknangan king bunduk na ning Libano, manibat king bunduk na ning baal-hermon angga king piluluban na ning Hamat. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:4</lbl> 	At mitagan la, bang masubuk ing Israel king pamamilatan da, bang mabalu nung pakiramdaman do ding utus nang GUINU, a inutus na karing karelang mangatua king pamamilatan nang Moises. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:5</lbl> 	At ding anak na ning Israel menuknangan la king libutad da ding Cananeos, ding Heteos, at ding Amoreos, at ding Perezeos, at ding Heveos, at ding Jebuseos: 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:6</lbl> 	At kinua rala ding anak dang babai barong maguing asawa, at ding anak dang babai binie ro karing anak dang lalaki, at sinuyu la karing karelang dioses. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:7</lbl> 	At ding anak na ning Israel depatan da ing marawak king panimanman nang GUINU, at kelinguan de i GUINU a karelang Dios, at sinuyu la karing baalim at karing Asherot. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:8</lbl> 	Inya pin milablab ing mua nang GUINU salang king Israel, at pisali nala king gamat nang Cusan-risataim a ari king Mesopotamia: at sinuyu la ding anak na ning Israel kang Cusan-risataim walung banua. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:9</lbl> 	At inyang ding anak na ning Israel dinalung la kang GUINU, i GUINU mitalakad yang metung a mangabus karing anak na ning Israel, a ya ing migligtas karela, ya pin i Otniel a anak nang Kenaz, a wali nang Caleb. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:10</lbl> 	At ing Espiritu nang GUINU dinatang ya kea, at inatulan na ing Israel; at linual ya king pamakipamuk, at i GUINU binie ne king gamat na i Cusanrisataim a ari Mesopotamia: at ing gamat na miniambut ya salang kang Cusanrisataim. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:11</lbl> 	At mika ating kapainawan ing labuad apatapulung banua. At mete ya i Otniel a anak nang Kenaz. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:12</lbl> 	At depatan dang pasibayu ding anak na ning Israel ing marawak king panimanman nang GUINU: at i GUINU pepasiknangan ne i Eglon a ari king Moab salang king Israel, uling depatan da ing marawak king panimanman nang GUINU. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:13</lbl> 	At tinipun nala kea ding anak nang Ammon at Amalec; at mine ya at sigatan na ing Israel, at bindian da ing ciudad da ding dutung a palma. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:14</lbl> 	At ding anak na ning Israel sinuyu la kang Eglon a ari king Moab, labingwalung banua. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:15</lbl> 	Dapot inyang ding anak na ning Israel dinalung la kang GUINU, i GUINU mitalakad yang metung a mangabus karela, i Ehud a anak nang Gera, a Benjamita, lalaki yang kinaili. At ding anak na ning Israel peparala lang buis king pamamilatan na kang Eglon a ari king Moab. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:16</lbl> 	At i Ehud guinawa yang kea metung a punyal a ating adua taram, atin yang metung a siku king kaba; at tekas ne king lalam na ning keang imalan, nangan king puad nang wanan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:17</lbl> 	At inain na ing buis kang Eglon a ari king Moab: ngeni i Eglon metung yang lalaking binang mataba. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:18</lbl> 	At pangaibat na nang ayain ing buis, pepalakuan na ing balayan a migdala king buis. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:19</lbl> 	Dapot ya mibalik ya manibat king kabatuan a atiu king siping ning Gilgal, at sinabi na, Atin kung metung a daralan a balita a lijim keka, Oh ari. At sinabi na, Magtajimik ka. At meko la ding anggang atiu makatalakad king siping na. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:20</lbl> 	At i Ehud mine ya kea; at makalukluk ya a magsasarili king marimlang silid a matas. At sinabi nang Ehud, Atin kung daralan a balita keka a ibat king Dios. At tinalakad ya king keang luklukan. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:21</lbl> 	At liwal neng Ehud ing gamat nang kaili, at begut ne ing punyal a ibat king keang puad a wanan, at siksak ne king keang katawan: 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:22</lbl> 	At ing kapitna na man linub a makatuki king taram; at misara ing taba king taram, uling e ne begut ing punyal king katawan na; at linsut ya king gulut. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:23</lbl> 	Kanita linual ya i Ehud king piluluban, at kebat no ding pasbul king matas a silid kea, at sinusi nala. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>3:24</lbl> 	Ngeni inyang mako ne, ding ipus na dinatang la; at ikit da, at, oini, ding pasbul ning matas a silid makasusi la; at sinabi ra, Katutuan king tatakpan nala ding keang bitis king keang silid a matas.
