Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:1</lbl> 	At kinuldas ya i Samson king Timna, at menakit yang metung a babai king Timna karing anak dang babai ding Filisteos. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:2</lbl> 	At sinampa ya, at sinabi na kang ibpa na at kang indu na, at sinabi na, Menakit kung metung a babai king Timna karing anak da ding Filisteos: ngeni pin kuanan ye a maguing asawa ku.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:3</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi nang tata na at indu na kea, Ala na waring babai karing anak da ding kekang kapatad, o king mabilug kung balayan, a mame kang makiasawa karing e tuling Filisteos? At sinabi nang Samson king keang ibpa, Kuanan me iti dikil kaku; uli ning makatula yang bina kanaku. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:4</lbl> 	Dapot i ibpa na at i indu na e ra balu king kaburian nang GUINO; uling ya manintun yang paralan salang karing Filisteos. Ngeni king panaun a ita ding Filisteos atin lang pamaniakup king Israel. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:5</lbl> 	Kanita kinuldas ya i Samson, at i ibpa na at i indu na, king Timna, at mine ya king uvasan ning Timna: at, oini, ing metung a biserung leon mamius yang salang kea. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:6</lbl> 	At ing Espiritu nang Guinu masikanan yang dinatang kea, at sigmit ne a anti mo ing pamaniagmit na king metung a biserung kambing; at ya ala ya nanuman king keang gamat: dapot e na sinabi kang ibpa na at kang indu na nung nanu ing keang depatan. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:7</lbl> 	At kinuldas ya, at mekisabi ya king babai; at ya mekapatula yang bina kang Samson. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:8</lbl>	At pangalabas na ning ditak a panaun mibalik ya baneng kuanan; at sinalangi ya king dalan bang lawan ne ing bangke ning leon: at, oini, ating metung a kawan a pukiutan kilub ning katawan ning leon, at pulut. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:9</lbl> 	At dela ne karing gamat na, at sinulung ya, a kakanan na kabang mame ya; at dinatang ya kang ibpa na at indu na, at dininan nala, at pengan da: dapot e na sinabi karela a kinua na ing pulut king katawan ning leon.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:10</lbl> 	At kinuldas ya i ibpa na king babai: at i Samson guinawa yang metung a pista karin; uling makanian ing kaugalian dang daraptan ding kayanakan a lalaki.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:11</lbl> 	At milyari, pamanakit da kea, king migdala lang atlungpulung kayabe a maguing kayantabe na.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:12</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson karela, Pabustan yung ibulus ke kakayu ing metung a bugtung: nung asalese ye kanaku king lub na niting pitung aldo ning pista, at kekayu yang turan, nung makanian dinan dakong atlungpulung barung lienzo at atlungpulu kapiblas a imalan:

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:13</lbl> 	Dapot nung e ye asalese kanaku, nung makanian ikayung munie kanaku atlungpulung barung lienzo at atlungpulu kapiblas a imalan. At sinabi ra kea, Ibulus me ing kekang bugtung, bamiyang damdaman. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:14</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela, King maglaklak linual ing pamangan, At king masikan linual ing yumu. At e re adinan kasalesean ing bugtung king atlung aldo. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:15</lbl> 	At milyari king kapitung aldo, king sinabi ra king asawa nang Samson, Piraitnan me ing kekang asawa, baneng salesayan kekami ing bugtung, nung ali ikami dulukan daka at ing bale na ning kekang ibpa king api: inagkat yuke wari bang papagkasakitan? E makanian? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:16</lbl> 	At kiniak ya ing asawa nang Samson king arapan na, at sinabi na, Tune king kasaman muku, at e muku kaluguran: mibulus kang metung a bugtung karing anak na ning kakung balayan, at e me selese kanaku. At sinabi na kea, Oini, e ke selese kang ibpa ku ni kang indu ku man, at salesean ke keka? 	And 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:17</lbl> 	At kiniak ya king arapan na king pitung aldo, angga king meari ing karelang pista: at milyari king kapitung aldo, king selese ne kea, uling pinilit neng bina; at selese ne ing bugtung king arapan da ding anak na ning keang balayan.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:18</lbl> 	At sinabi re kea ding lalaki king ciudad king kapitung aldo bayu ya limbug ing aldo, Nanu kaya ing maguing mayumu pa kesa king pulut? At nanu kaya ing maguing masikan pa kesa king metung a leon? At sinabi na karela, Nung e ye piniarul ing kakung dumalaga, E ye sana asalese ing kanakung bugtung. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:19</lbl> 	At ing Espiritu nang GUINO masikanan yang dinatang kea, at kinuldas ya king Asquelon, at sinugat yang atlungpulung lalaki karela, at kinua na ing mesamsam karela, at binie na ing piblasan karing mekasalese king bugtung. At ing keang mua milablab, at menik ya king bale nang ibpa na. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>14:20</lbl> 	Dapot ing asawa nang Samson miabie ya king keang kayabe, a ya ing inapus nang anti nang kakaluguran.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:1</lbl> 	Dapot mepalyari pangalabas na ning ditak a panaun, king panaun na ning pamamupul trigu, king dinalo ya i Samson a magdala yang metung a biserung kambing king keang asawa; at sinabi na, Luban ke ing asawa ku king kilub ning silid. Dapot e ne pepaluban ning keang ibpa. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning keang ibpa, Tune a tune inisip ku king lubus meng pikasaman; inya binie ke king kekang kayabe: e wari ing keang waling babai maiguit ya lagu kea? Pagamuamu ku keka, kuanan me, a maguing kalili na. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:3</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson karela, Maguing ala kung kapintasan king panaun a iti karing Filisteos, nung daptananan kong kalikutan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:4</lbl> 	At meko ya i Samson at dinakap yang atlung dalan a zora, at kinanua yang mitsa, at pitaidtaid no ding karelang iki, at dininan nong metung a mitsa king libutad na ning pilatan da ding balang aduang iki. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:5</lbl> 	At inyang asulsulan na no ding mitsa, binulus nala king makatalakad a binutil da ding Filisteos, at silaban da ing pun at ing makatalakad a binutil, at makanian mu naman ding mulajan oliva.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:6</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi ra ding Filisteos, Ninung dinapat kaniti? At karelang sinabi, I Samson, a manuyang ning Timniteo, uling kinua ne ing keang asawa, at binie ne king keang kayabe. At sinampa la ding Filisteos, at dilukan de ing babai at ing keang ibpa. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:7</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson karela, Nung daraptan yu ing anti kaniting bague, alang salang yablas ku kekayu, at kaibat na nita tuknang na ku. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:8</lbl> 	At sigatan nala king balakang at puad a kayagum na ning maragul a pamakamate: at kinuldas ya at menuknangan king puang na ning batu king Etam. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:9</lbl> 	Kanita sinampa la ding Filisteos, at menalakad la king Juda, at kinalat da ing sarili ra king Lehi. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:10</lbl> 	At sinabi ra ding lalaki ning Juda, Baket sinampa kayu salang kekami? At sinabi ra, Bamiyang gapusan i Samson sinampa kami, baming daptan kea ing anti mo ing depatan na kekami.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:11</lbl> 	Kanita ding atlung libung lalaki ning Juda kinuldas la king puang ning batu king Etam, at sinabi ra kang Samson, E mu wari balu king ding Filisteos sasakup la kekatamo? Nanu pin iting depatan mu kekami? At sinabi na karela, Nung makananu ing depatan da kanaku, makanian mu naman ing depatan ku karela. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:12</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea, Kinuldas kami barakang gapusan, barakang ibie king gamat da ding Filisteos. At sinabi nang Samson karela, Sumpa ko kanaku, bang aliwa ikayu ding dumpa kanaku.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:13 </lbl>	At sinabi ra kea, ngara, Ali; nung e gapusan dakang matalik, at ibie raka king karelang gamat: dapot tune e raka patayan. At guinapus deng aduang bayung lubid, at simpa reng ibat king batu. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:14 </lbl>	Inyang datang ya king Lehi, ding Filisteos pesikulio la kabang sasaganan de: at ing Espiritu nang GUINO masikanan yang dinatang kea, at ding lubid a atiu karing keang takde meguing anti lang lienzo a meduluk king api, at ding keang tali mebaldug la manibat karing keang gamat. 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl>15:15</lbl> 	At menakit yang metung a bayung sikang ning metung a asno, at inatyat ne ing keang gamat, at kinua ne, at piniugat ne karing libung lalaki. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:16</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson, King pamamilatan ning sikang na ning metung a asno, mibuntunbuntun la, King pamamilatan na ning sikang na ning metung a asno sinugat kung libung lalaki. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:17</lbl> 	At milyari, inyang mayari neng miniabi, king besibas ne ing sikang king gamat na; at ing karinan a ita meaus Ramat-lehi. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:18</lbl> 	At mika atin yang maragul a kau, at minaus ya kang GUINO, at ngana, Binie mu king gamat na ning kekang talasuyu iting maragul a kaligtasan; at ngeni mate ku wari king uli na ning kau, at manabu ku king gamat da deting e tule? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:19</lbl> 	Dapot biklat ne ning Dios ing metung a kulkul a atiu king Lehi, at linual karin ing danum; at inyang mekainum ne, mibalik pasibayu ing keang diwa, at mesikan ya: inya ing laguiu na nita meaus En-hakkore, a atiu king Lehi, angga king aldo ngeni.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>15:20</lbl> 	At inatulan na ing Israel karing aldo ra ding Filisteos aduangpulung banua. 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 16:1</lbl> 	At i Samson mine ya Gaza, at karin menakit yang metung a patutut, at siniping ya kea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:2</lbl> 	At belita ra karing tau Gaza, ngara, I Samson dinatang ya keti. At kibkuban de, at inabatan de king mabilug a bengi king pasbulan dalan ning ciudad, at tajimik la king kabukas, ngara, Manaya tamu angga king mamunag, kanita patayan taya. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:3</lbl> 	At i Samson makakera ya anggang kapitangan bengi, at mibangun ya inyang kapitangan bengi, at tinalan ya karing takap ning pasbulan dalan ning ciudad, at karing aduang asias, at begut nala, pati na barateja at sabla, at pisanan nala, at dela nong sinampa king taluktuk ning bunduk a atiu king arapan ning Hebron. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:4</lbl> 	At milyari kaibat na niti, king milsinta ya king metung a babai a atiu king libis na ning Sorec, a ing laguiu na Delila. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:5</lbl> 	At simpan de ding guinu ra ding Filisteos, at sinabi ra kea, Siluan me, at lawan mu nung nu makabili ing keang maragul a sikanan, at nung nanung paralan a malyari keng maniaul laban kea, bamiyang agapus bang apasakitan miya: at dinan daka balang metung kekami libu at dinalan a kapising pilak. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:6</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Delila kang Samson, Pagamuamu ku keka, sabian mu kanaku, nung nu makabili ing kekang maragul a sikanan, at nung makananu kang malyaring migapus bang malyaring pasakitan daka. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:7</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson kea, Nung gapusan daku karing pitung saguiwang yantuk a kapilan man e pa melangi, kanita malyaring mina ku, at maguing anti ku mo ing aliwang lalaki.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:8</lbl> 	Kanita ding guinu ra ding Filisteos migdala la kea a pitung saguiwang yantuk a e pa melangi, at guepusan ne kareti.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:9 </lbl>	Ngeni atin yang bante gulung a atiu king silid kilub. At sinabi na kea, Ding Filisteos orian na, Samson. At petad na ing yantuk, anti mo ing pangapatad ning taling sinulad ngening atagkil na ing api. Nanupata e mebalu ing keang sikanan.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:10</lbl> 	At i Delila sinabi na kang Samson, Oini, pirait muku, at piglaraman muku: pagamuamu ku ngeni keka, salesean mu kaku, nung makananu kang migapus.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:11</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Nung talian daku mung bayung lubid a e ra pa guinamit, kanita mina ku, at maguing anti na ku mu ing aliwang lalaki. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:12 </lbl>	Nung inya kinanua ya i Delila bayung lubid, at guepusan ne kaniti, at sinabi na kea, Samson, orian na ding Filisteos. At ding bante gulung atilu king silid kilub. At petad no karing keang takde a anti mong sinulad. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:13</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Delila kang Samson, Angga ngeni pirait muku, at piglaraman muku: sabian mu kanaku nung makananu kang malyaring agapus. At sinabi na kea, Nung ilala mo ding pitung ikat king kanakung buntuk king metung a abalan.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:14</lbl> 	At tinali ne king tulus, at sinabi na kea, Samson, orian na ding Filisteos. At miguising ya king keang pangatudtud, at begut ne ing tulus ning pabakle, at ing abalan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:15</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Makananung asasabi mu, aku kaluguran daka, ngening ing kekang pusu ala yu kanaku? Pirait mu na ku kaniting makatatlung ukdu, at e mu sinabi kanaku nung nu makabili ing kekang maragul a sikanan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:16</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang pinilit na neng pinilit karing keang amanu aldoaldo, at susukilkilan ne, king melingasngas ya ing kaladua na angga king kamatayan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:17</lbl> 	At selese na kea ing keang mabilug a pusu, at sinabi na kea, Alang labasas a dinalan king kanakung buntuk; uling meguing Nazareno ku king Dios manibat pa king bale nang pungul ning kanakung indu: nung masatsat ku, kanita kawani kanaku ing sikanan ku, at mina ku, at maguing anti na ku mu ing ninumang lalaki. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:18 </lbl>	At inyang ikit nang Delila a selese na kea ing mabilug nang pusu, mitubud ya at pepayaus nala ding guinu ra ding Filisteos, ngana, Sampa kayu ngening ngeni, uling selese na kanaku ing mabilug nang pusu. Kanita simpan de ding guinu ra ding Filisteos, at darala ro ding salapi king karelang gamat.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:19</lbl> 	At pepatudtud ne karing keang tud; at minaus yang metung a lalaki, at sitsat nala ding pitung ikat king keang buntuk; at pigmulan neng pepasakitan, at ing keang sikanan meko kea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:20</lbl> 	At sinabi na, Samson, orian na ding Filisteos. At miguising ya king keang pangatudtud, at sinabi na, Lual kung anti mo ing karing aliwang panaun, at ikisig kung timawa ing sarili ku. Dapot e na balu king i GUINO kinawani ya kea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:21</lbl> 	At dekapan de ding Filisteos, at dinukit do ding mata na; at kildas de king Gaza, at guepusan de karing talikalang tangsu; at guiniling ya king sukulan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:22</lbl> 	Makanian man migmulang tinubu ing buak na king buntuk kaibat nang mesatsat.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:23</lbl> 	At ding guinu ra ding Filisteos mitipun lang makapamisan balang main metung a maragul a daun kang dagon a dios da, at bang magsaya la; uling sinabi ra, Binie ne ning kekatang dios king kekatang gamat i Samson a kasalang tamu. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:24</lbl> 	At inyang akit ne ning balayan, pinuri re ing karelang dios; uling sinabi ra, Binie ne ning kekatang dios king kekatang gamat ing kekatang kasalang, at ing manlasak king kekatang labuad, a mekamate karing dakal kekatamu. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:25</lbl> 	At milyari, kanitang matula la ding karelang pusu, king sinabi ra, Ausan ye i Samson, bayang gawang pikatulan kekatamu. At inaus de pin i Samson king sukulan; at guinawa yang pikatulan king arapan da. At binili re king pilatan da ding asias: 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 16:26</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson king anak a tataid king keang gamat, Ipaintulut mung asalat kula ding asias a magdala king bale, bakung magjilig kareti.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:27</lbl> 	Ngeni ing bale mitmu yang lalaki at babai; at atilu karin ding anggang guinu ra ding Filisteos; at king babo ning bubungan ating atlung libung lalaki at babai, a lalbe kabang i Samson gagawa yang pikatulan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:28</lbl> 	At minaus ya i Samson kang GUINO, pagamuamu ku keka, ganakan muku, at pasiknangan muku, pagamuamu ku keka, aguiang misan na mu, Oh Dios, bang king misan mu man makayablas ku karing Filisteos karing adua kung mata. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:29</lbl> 	At i Samson telan nala ding aduang asias a makalibutad a magdala king bale, at migsandal ya kareti, ing metung king gamat nang wanan, at ing metung king gamat nang kaili. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:30</lbl> 	At sinabi nang Samson, Pabustan mukung mate a kayabe ra ding Filisteos. At tinulak nala king mabilug nang sikanan; at ing bale misaldak ya karing guinu, at king mabilug a balayan a atiu karin kilub. Inya ding mete a apate na king keang kamatayan maiguit la karing pete na king keang bie. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>16:31</lbl> 	Kanita kinuldas la ding keang kapatad at ing mabilug a bale nang ibpa na, at kinua re, at simpa re, at kitkut de king pilatan na ning Zora at Estaol king kutkutan nang Manoa a keang ibpa. At inatulan na ing Israel aduangpulung banua. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:1</lbl> 	At ating metung a lalaki king karinan a bunduk-bundukan ning Efraim, a ing laguiu na Mica. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:2</lbl> 	At sinabi na kang indu na, Ding libu at dinalan kapising pilak a meakua keka, a ilang bigsu mu piniumpa, at sinabi mu mu naman karing kakung balugbug, oini, ing pilak atiu kanaku; kinua ku. At sinabi nang indu na, Panuanan neng GUINO ing anak ku. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:3</lbl> 	At sibli nala ding libu at dinalan a kapising pilak kang indu na; at sinabi nang indu na, Kakung italagang tune kang GUINO ing pilak a ibat king gamat ku dikil king kakung anak, balang gawan metung a larawan a dinukit at metung a larawan a bibu: ngeni pin isubli ko keka. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:4</lbl> 	At inyang isubli nala ding salapi kang indu na, kinanua ya i indu na aduang dalan a kapising pilak, at binie no king mamubu, a nung ninu ing guinawa kareta metung a larawan a dinukit at metung a larawan a bibu: at atiu king bale nang Mica. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:5</lbl> 	At ing lalaking Mica mika atin yang metung a bale karing dioses, at guinawa yang metung a efod, at terafim, at telaga ne ing metung karing keang anak a lalaki, a meguing keang sacerdote. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:6</lbl> 	Karing aldo a deta alang ari king Israel: balang katau depatan na ing matulid karing sarili nang mata. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:7</lbl> 	At ating metung a kayanakan a lalaking ibat king Beth-lehem-juda, king sapni nang Juda, metung yang Levita; at menaliwa yang balen karin. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:8</lbl> 	At ing lalaki meko ya king ciudad, king Beth-lehem-juda, bayang makipanuknangan nung nu ya manakit metung a karinan; at miras ya king karinan a bunduk-bundukan ning Efraim king bale nang Mica, king pamaglakbe na. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:9</lbl> 	At sinabi na keang Mica, Nu ka ibat? At sinabi na kea, Metung kung Levita king Beth-lehem-juda, at mame ku bang makipanuknangan ku nung nu ku manakit metung a karinan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:10 </lbl>	At sinabi na keang Mica, Manuknangan kang kayabe ku, at maguing metung kang ibpa kanaku at metung a sacerdote, at aku dinan dakang apulu kapising pilak balang banua, at kasuluran a piblas, at ing kekang pamangan. Uli nita ing Levita linub ya. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:11</lbl> 	At ing Levita pitutulan na ing manuknangan a kayabe na ning lalaki; at ing kayanakan kea anti ya mong metung karing keang anak. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:12 </lbl>	At i Mica telaga ne ing Levita, at meguing sacerdote ne ing kayanakan, at atiu king bale nang Mica. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>17:13</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi nang Mica, Ngeni balu ku na king daptananan nakung mayap GUINO, anti ning atin kung metung a Levita a pekasacerdote ku. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:1</lbl> 	Karing aldo a deta alang ari king Israel: at karing aldo a deta ding dai ra ding Danitas manintun lang metung a mana a apanuknanganan da; uling angga man king aldo a ita e pa mebaldug karela king libutad da ding dai na ning Israel ing karelang mana. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:2</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Dan mitubud lang limang lalaki king karelang sapni manibat king karelang kabilugan a bilang, lalaki lang bantug king tapang, a menibatan Zora, at ibat king Estaol, barang tiktikan ing labuad, at bang siasatan da; at sinabi ra karela, Ume kayu, siasatan yu ing labuad. At ila miras la king karinan a bunduk-bundukan nang Efraim, king bale nang Mica, at migsantung la karin. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:3</lbl> 	Kanitang malapit na la king bale nang Mica, balu ra ing siwala na ning kayanakan a lalaking Levita; at sinalangi la karin, at sinabi ra kea, Ninu ing migdala keka keti? At nanu ing kekang daraptan king karinan a iti? At nanu ing atiu keka keti? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:4</lbl> 	At sinabi na karela, Makanian at makanian ing pamakiutus na kanakung Mica, at inupajan naku, at meguing sacerdote naku.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:5</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea, Mawad kang usuk, pagamuamu mi keka, king Dios, baming abalu nung ing kekeng lakad a ayan mi mipala. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:6</lbl> 	At ing sacerdote sinabi na karela, Ume kong payapa: atiu king arapan nang GUINO ing dalan a kekong ayan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:7</lbl> 	Kanita meko la ding limang lalaki, at miras la king Lais, at ikit da ing balayan a atiu karin, nung makananu lang menuknangan king kapanatagan, a anti mo ding Sidonios, tajimik at panatag; uling ala king labuad, a kukumkum upaya, bang abili ro king kamarinayan king nanumang bague, at marayu la karing Sidonios, at ala lang pamakiutus king kenumang tau. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:8</lbl> 	At dinatang la pin karing kapatad da king Zora at king Estaol: at ding karelang kapatad sinabi ra karela, Nanu ing sasabian yu?

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:9</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Talakad kayu, at sampa tamu a salang karela; uling ikit mi ing labuad, at, oini, binang mayap: a maratun kayo? E ko magmakupad a ume at lungub bang bandian ing labuad. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:10</lbl> 	Pamaglako yu, datang kayu king metung a balayan a panatag, at ing labuad maragul; uling binie ning Dios iti king kekong gamat, metung a karinan a ala nang kulang king kakailanganan a nanumang bague keti sulip.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:11 </lbl>	At meko lang menibatan karin ding king sapni ra ding Danitas, manibat king Zora at manibat king Estaol, anam lang dalan a lalaking makatakas karing sandatang pakipamuk. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:12</lbl> 	At sinampa la, at menalakad la king Kiriat-jearim, king Juda: inya pin inaus da ing karinan a ita Mahane-dan angga king aldo ngeni; oini, atiu king gugulutan na ning Kiriat-jearim.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:13</lbl> 	At dinalan la manibat karin angga king karinan a bunduk-bundukan nang Efraim, at dinatang la king bale nang Mica. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:14</lbl> 	Kanita mekibat la ding limang lalaki a mintang tiniktik king labuad ning Lais, at sinabi ra karing kapatad da, Balu yu king atin karing bale a deti metung a efod, at terafim, at metung a larawan a dinuket, at metung a larawan a bibo? Ngeni pin balakan yu ing sukat yung daptan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:15</lbl> 	At sinalangi la karin, at miras la king bale na ning kayanakan a Levita, king bale na ping Mica, at kitnan de king keang pangabili. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:16</lbl> 	At ding anam a dalan a lalaki a makasandatang pakipamuk, a anak nang Dan, tinalakad la king piluluban ning pasbulan dalan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:17</lbl> 	At ding limang lalaki a mine bang tiktik king labuad sinampa la, at linub la karin, at kinua re ing larawan a dinukit, at ing efod, at ding terafim, at ing larawan a bibu: at ing sacerdote tinalakad ya king lele ning piluluban ning pasbulan dalan a kayabe no ding anam a dalan a lalaki a makasandatang pakipamuk.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:18</lbl> 	At inyang deti linub la king bale nang Mica, at kinua re ing larawan a dinukit, ing efod, at ding terafim, at ing larawan a bibu, ing sacerdote sinabi na karela, Nanu ing daraptan yu? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:19</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea, Tajimik ka, itakap me ing gamat mu king kekang asbuk, at tuki ka kekami, at maguing ibpa ka kekami at metung a sacerdote: mayap kaya keka a maguing sacerdote ka king bale na ning metung mung lalaki, o maguing sacerdote ka king metung a dai at metung a sapni king Israel? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:20</lbl> 	At metula ya ing pusu na ning sacerdote, at kinua ne ing efod, at ding terafim, at ing larawan a dinukit, at mine king libutad ning balayan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:21</lbl> 	Inya mibalik na la at meko, at binili rala king karelang arapan ding anak a mangalati at ding vaca at ing pibandian. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:22</lbl> 	Inyang marayu na la king bale nang Mica, ding lalaking atiu karing bale a makalapit king bale nang Mica mitipun lang makapamisan, at tegal do ding anak nang Dan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:23 </lbl>	At kinulio la karing anak nang Dan. At melikid la, at sinabi ra kang Mica, Nanung makalingasngas keka, a dinatang kang kambe mu ing anti kaniang tapuk?

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:24 </lbl>	At sinabi na, Kinua yo ding kanakung dioses a guewa ku, at ing sacerdote, at meko kayu, a nanu pang kanaku? At makananu ping sabian yu kanaku, Nanung makalingasngas keka? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:25</lbl> 	At sinabi ra kea ding anak nang Dan, E mu na paramdam ing kekang siwala king libutad mi, magkang dalusungan daka ding mua karing tau, at ibating me ing kekang bie, pati na ing bie ra ding kekang katubale. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:26 </lbl>	At belaus da ding anak nang Dan ing karelang lakad: at inyang ikit nang Mica king milalu la kasikan dikil kea, mibalik ya at minuli ya king keang bale.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:27</lbl> 	At kinua re ing guewa nang Mica, at ing sacerdote na, at mine la king Lais, king balayan a tajimik at panatag, at sigatan dala king taram na ning talibung; at dilukan da ing ciudad king api. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:28</lbl> 	At alang magligtas, uling marayu king Sidon, at ala lang pamakiabiayan kaninumang tau; at atiu iti king libis a atiu king siping ning Betrehob. At telakad de ing ciudad, at penuknanganan de. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:29</lbl> 	At ing laguiu ning ciudad inaus deng Dan, agpang king laguiu ning Dan a karelang ibpa, a mibait king Israel: makanian man ing laguiu ning ciudad king minuna Lais.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>18:30</lbl> 	At telakad de dikil king karelang sarili ding anak nang Dan ing larawan a dinukit; at i Jonatan, a anak nang Gersom, a anak nang Moises, ya at ding keang anak ilang sacerdotes king dai ra ding Danitas angga king aldo a pangabijag na ning labuad. 

Ding Ukum Judges 18:31 	Makanian deng telakad karela ing larawan nang dinukit Mica a guewa na, king sablang panaun a atiu ing bale na ning Dios king Silo.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:1</lbl> 	At milyari karing aldo a deta, inyang alang ari king Israel, king ating metung a Levita a manaliwang balen king nangan na karin ning karinan a bunduk-bundukan ning Efraim, a ya kinanua yang metung nang babai king Beth-lehem-juda. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:2</lbl> 	At ing keang babai migkamit yang pamipaliwas salang kea, at likuan ne a mine ya king bale nang ibpa na king Beth-lehem-juda, at karin ya king lub ning apat a bulan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:3</lbl> 	At ing keang asawa mibangun ya, at tinuki ya kea, bayang makisabing maganaka kea, bang ibalik neng miuman, a kayabe ne ing keang ipus, at metung a kaparis a asno: at dela ne king bale nang ibpa na; at inyang ikit ne ning ibpa na ning babai, matula yang seganan ne. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:4</lbl> 	At kinawat ne ning keang katiwangan, a ibpa na ning babai; at menuknangan yang kayabe na atlung aldo: inya mengan la at minum la, at migsantung la karin.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:5</lbl> 	At milyari king kapat a aldo, king mibangun lang maranun king abak, at mibangun ya bang mako: at sinabi na ning ibpa na ning babai king keang manuyang, Pasiknangan me ing kekang pusu king tinape, at kaibat ibalaus mu na ing kekang lakad. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:6</lbl> 	Inya linukluk la, at mengan la, at minum, ilang adua a miabe: at sinabi ning ibpa na ning dalaga king lalaki, Pagamuamu ku keka, magpakasaya ka, a manatiling kabukas, at pasayan me ing kekang pusu. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:7</lbl> 	At ing lalaki mibangun ya bang mako, dapot pinilit ne ning keang katiwangan, at migsantung yang pasibayu karin.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:8</lbl> 	At mibangun yang maranun panga abak king kalimang aldo bayang mako; at sinabi na ning ibpa na ning babai, Pagamuamu ku keka, pasiknangan me ing kekang pusu, at manaya ka angga king kulimlim ya ing aldo; at mengan la, ilang adua. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:9</lbl>	At kanitang ing lalaki tinalakad ya bayang mako, ya, at ing keang babai, at ing keang ipus, sinabi na kea ning katiwangan na, a ibpa na ning babai, Oini, ngeni ing aldo lalapit na king bengi, pagamuamu ku kekayu manaya ko king kabukas: oini, ing aldo lilipas ne, magsantung ko keti, bayang tumula ing kekong pusu; at bukas pagmulan yung maranun ing kekong lakad, banakong muli bale. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:10</lbl> 	Dapot ing lalaki e ne menaya pa king benging ita, dapot tinalakad ya at meko ya, at miras ya king tulid ning Jebus (a ya naman ing Jerusalem): at karin abe nala ding kaparis a asno a makasiya; ing keang babai man kayabe naya. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:11</lbl> 	Kanitang ati na lu king siping ning Jebus, ing aldo linipas ne; at sinabi na ning ipus king keang guinu, Pagamuamu ku keka, ume ka keni, at mibalik tamu kaniting ciudad da ding Jebuseos, at magsantung tamu kaniti. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:12</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea ning guinu na, E ta mibabalik king ciudad ning aliwang balen, a e karing anak na ning Israel; nung e dumalan tamu a malaus king Gilbea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:13 </lbl>	At sinabi na king keang ipus, ume ka keni at lumapit tamu king metung karing karinan a deti; at magsantung ta king Gibea, o king Rama. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:14</lbl> 	Inya dinalan la at melaus king karelang lakad; at kealbugan lang aldo king malapit king Gibea, a bandi nang Benjamin. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:15</lbl> 	At sinalangi la karin, balang lungub at magsantung king Gibea: at linub ya, at linukluk ya king dalan na ning ciudad; uling alang lalaki a pabalaus karela king keang bale balang magsantung karin. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:16</lbl> 	At, oini, mumuli ya ing metung a matua a ibat ya king keang dapat king marangle kanitang sisilim: ngeni ing lalaki tau ya king karinan a bunduk-bundukan nang Efraim, at makipanuknangan ya king Gibea; dapot ding tau king karinan a ita Benjamitas la. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:17 </lbl>	At inatna no ding keang mata, at ikit ne ing lalaking maglakbe king dalan na ning ciudad; at sinabi na ning matuang lalaki, Nu ka ume? At nu ka ibat?

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:18</lbl> 	At sinabi na kea, Daralan kaming menibatan king Beth-lehem-juda a mame king nangan na karin ning karinan a bunduk-bundukan ning Efraim; tau ku karin, at mine ku king Beth-lehem-juda: at mame ku ngeni king bale nang GUINO; at alang taung pabalaus kanaku king bale na.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:19</lbl> 	Makanianman ating are at dikut dikil karing kekeng asno; at atin mu namang tinape at alak dikil kanaku, at king kekang ipus a babai, at dikil king kayanakan a lalaki a kayabe ra ding kekang ipus: alang kakulangan king nanumang bague.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:20</lbl> 	At sinabi na ning matuang lalaki, Kapayapan keka; makanian man paburean mung mitumpak kanaku ing kekang sablang kakailanganan; e ka mu magsantung king dalan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:21</lbl> 	Nung inya dela ne king keang bale, at dininan nong pamangan ding asno; at inos do ding karelang bitis, at mengan la at mininum. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:22</lbl> 	Kabang patulan do ding karelang pusu, oreni, ding lalaki ning ciudad, taung mangababa asal, kibkuban de ing bale king makapatulug, papaluka la king pasbul; at miniabi la king guinu ning bale, ing matuang lalaki, ngara, Ilual me ing lalaki a linub king bale mu, bamiyang abalu. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:23</lbl> 	At ing lalaki, ing guinu ning bale, liwalan nala, at sinabi na karela, Ali, kapatad ku, e ko darapat marawak, pagamuamu ku kekayu; anti ning ing lalaking iti linub ya king kanakung bale, e yu daraptan iting manawang. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:24</lbl> 	Oini, ing anak ku dalaga yang alang bakas, at ing keang babai; ila ilual ko ngeni, at umisan yula, at daptan yu karela ing kekong minamayap: dapot e yu daraptan king lalaking ini ing makanian a kanawangan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:25</lbl> 	Dapot e re pekiramdaman ding lalaki: nung inya telanan ne ning lalaki ing keang babai, at liwal ne karela; at abalu re, at newangan de king lub ning kebukas anggang abak: at inyang mamunag na ing aldo, pepalakuan de. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:26</lbl> 	Kanita dinatang ya ing babai inyang sasala na, at miragsa ya king pasbul ning bale ning lalaki a nung nu ya karin ing keang guinu, angga king mesala.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:27</lbl> 	At mibangun ya ing keang guinu king abak, at biklat no ding pasbul ning bale, at linual ya banang isundu ing keang lakad; at, oini, ing babai a kayang babai miragsa ya king pasbul ning bale, a ding keang gamat atilu king guyabnan eran. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:28</lbl>	At sinabi na kea, Mibangun ka, at tara na; dapot alang makibat: kanita seke ne king asno; at ing lalaki mibangun ya, at mine ya king keang karinan.

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 19:29</lbl> 	At pamaniatang na king keang bale, kinanua yang metung a punyal, at telanan ne ing keang babai, at penagsag ne, butul at butul, king labingaduang dake, at peparala ne karing anggang angganan na ning Israel. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>19:30</lbl> 	At milyari, king ding sablang menakit kaniti sinabi ra, Alang anti kaniting dapat a merapat na ni meakit man manibat king aldo a sinampa la ding anak na ning Israel a menibatan king labuad na ning Egipto angga king aldo a iti: talastasan yu, kuma kong sangguni, at maniabi kayu. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:1</lbl> 	Kanita linual la ngan ding anak na ning Israel, at ing kapamisanan mitipun anti mong metung mung tau, manibat king Dan angga pin king Beer-seba, a kayagum na ing labuad ning Gilead, kang Guinu king Mizpa. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:2</lbl> 	At ding pekapun ning mabilug a balayan, ding anggang dai na pin ning Israel, inarap da ing sarili ra king kapulungan na ning balayan na ning Dios, a apat lang dalan a libung lalaking lalakad a tinalan sandata. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:3</lbl> 	(Ngeni ding anak nang Benjamin dimdam da king sinampa la ding anak na ning Israel king Mizpa). At sinabi ra ding anak na ning Israel, Sabian yu kekami, makananung mepalyari iting marawak a iti? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:4</lbl> 	At ing Levita, ing asawa na ning babaing pete, mekibat ya sinabi na, Mine ku king Gibea atiu king Benjamin, aku at ing kakung babai, bang magsantung karin. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:5</lbl> 	At tinalakad la ding lalaki king Gibea salang kanaku, at kibkuban de ing bale king makapatulug kanaku king bengi; aku pignasan dakung paten, pinilit de ing kakung babai, at mete ya. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:6</lbl> 	At kinua ke ing kanakung babai, at penagsag ke, at peparala ke king mabilug a labuad ning mana na ning Israel; uling migkamit la king kalibian at kanawangan king Israel. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:7</lbl> 	Oini, ikong anak na ning Israel, ikong sabla, ibie yu keti ing kekong minamayapan at usuk. 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 20:8</lbl> 	At ing mabilug a balayan tinalakad anti mong katau mu, ngara, E ne ume ing ninuman kekami king keang kubu, ni muli ya ing ninuman kekami king keang bale. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:9</lbl> 	Dapot ngeni oini ing bague a kekeng daptan king Gibea: sampa kami salang kea king pamamilatan na ning pamipaningalma;

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:10 </lbl>	At kuma kaming apulung lalaki king balang dinalan karing anggang dai na ning Israel, at dinalan king balang libu, at libu karing apulung libu, a magdalang bakal dikil king balayan, barang daptan, pangaras da king Gibea na ning Benjamin, ing agpang king anggang kanawangan a depatan da king Israel. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:11</lbl> 	Inya pin mitipun la ding anggang lalaki ning Israel salang king ciudad, a migpakatibe lang makapamisan anti mong katau mu.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:12</lbl> 	At mitubud la ding dai na ning Israel king mabilug a dai nang Benjamin, a sinabi ra, Nanung dewakan iti a mepalyari king libutad yu? 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 20:13 </lbl>	Ngeni pin ibie yula ding lalaki, ding taung mababa asal, a atiu king Gibea, bamilang patayan, at milako ing dewakan king Israel. Dapot e na pekiramdaman Benjamin ing siwala ra ding keang kapatad a anak na ning Israel. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:14</lbl> 	At mitipun lang makapamisan ding anak nang Benjamin karing ciudad a tumuru king Gibea, balang lual makilaban salang karing anak na ning Israel. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:15</lbl> 	At ding anak nang Benjamin mebilang la king aldo a ita karing ciudad adua lang pulu at anam a libung lalaki a tatalan talibung, makabukud pa karing manuknangan king Gibea, a mika bilang pitung dalan a piling lalaki. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:16</lbl> 	Kayabe na ning mabilug a balayan a iti atin lang pitung dalan a piling lalaki a kinaili; balang metung makabasibas yang batu king honda a tumud ya aguiang king metung mung sukad buak, at e sumala.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:17</lbl> 	At ding lalaki ning Israel, subali pa kang Benjamin, mebilang la ding apat lang dalan a libung lalaki a tatalan talibung: deting sabla lalaki la king pamipamuk.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:18</lbl> 	At tinalakad la ding anak na ning Israel, at sinampa la king Bet-el, at miniawad lang usuk king Dios; at sinabi ra, Ninu ing sampa kekami bang munang makilaban salang karing anak nang Benjamin? At sinabi nang GUINU, I Juda ya ing sampang muna.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:19</lbl> 	At mibangun la ding anak na ning Israel king abak, at menalakad lang salang king Gibea.

Ding Ukum Judges 20:20 	At linual la ding lalaki ning Israel bang makilaban salang kang Benjamin; at ding lalaki ning Israel binili ra ing pamipamuk king ayus laban karela king Gibea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:21</lbl> 	At linual la ding anak nang Benjamin king Gibea, at ding sinintang dang digsa king aldo a ita king gabun adua lang pulu at aduang libung lalaki karing Israelitas. 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 20:22</lbl> 	At ing balayan, ding lalaki ning Israel, pepatapang da ing sarili ra, at migayus lang pasibayu king pamakipamuk king karinan mu ring ita nung nu la migayus king minunang aldo. 	

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 20:23 </lbl>	At sinampa la ding anak na ning Israel at kiniak la king arapan nang GUINU anggang gatpanapun; at kitang da kang GUINU ngara, Lumapit kung pasibayu bakung makilaban salang karing anak nang Benjamin a kakung kapatad? At sinabi nang GUINU, Sampa kang salang kea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:24</lbl> 	At linapit la ding anak na ning Israel salang karing anak nang Benjamin king kaduang aldo. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:25</lbl> 	At i Benjamin linual ya king kaduang aldo king Gibea a salang karela, at asintang nong digsang pasibayu king gabun karing anak na ning Israel ding labingwalung libung lalaki; deting sabla telan de ing talibung. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:26</lbl> 	Kanita ding anggang anak na ning Israel, at ing mabilug a balayan sinampa, at mine king Bet-el, at kiniak, at linukluk karin king arapan nang GUINU, at migkulaciun la king aldo a ita angga king gatpanapun; at minain la karing ain a durulukan at karing ain king kapayapan king arapan nang GUINU. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:27</lbl> 	At kitang da ding anak na ning Israel kang GUINU (uling ing kaban ning tipan nang GUINU atiu karin karing aldo a deta, 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:28</lbl> 	At i Fineas, a anak nang Eliazar, a anak nang Aaron, tinalakad ya king arapan na karing aldo a deta), a sinabi na, Lual kung pasibayu bang makilaban salang karing anak nang Benjamin a kapatad ko, o tuknang ku? At sinabi nang GUINU, Sampa ka; uling bukas ibie ke king kekang gamat. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:29</lbl> 	At ing Israel mibili yang mamabat king makapatulug salang king Gibea. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:30</lbl> 	At sinampa la ding anak na ning Israel salang karing anak nang Benjamin king katlung aldo, at inayus da ing sarili ra salang king Gibea, anti mo ing karing milabas a ukdu. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:31</lbl> 	At linual la ding anak nang Benjamin salang king balayan, at mirayu la king ciudad; at pigmulan dang miniugat mekamate king balayan, anti mo ing karing milabas a ukdu, karing dalan a matas, a ing metung sasampa ya king Betel, at ing metung king Gibea, king marangle, atin lang atlungpulung lalaki ning Israel.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:32</lbl> 	At sinabi ra ding anak nang Benjamin, Mesugat lang miragsa king arapan tamu, anti mo king minuna. Dapot sinabi ra ding anak na ning Israel, Tumakas tamu, at idayu tala manibat king ciudad angga karing matas a dalan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:33</lbl> 	At ding anggang lalaki ning Israel tinalakad la king karelang karinan, at migayus la king baal-tamar; at ding mamabat na ning Israel linual la manibat king karelang karinan, king lual na pin ning Maareh-geba. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:34</lbl> 	At linague la salang king Gibea ding apulung libung piling lalaki king mabilug a Israel, at ing pamilaban makapangablab; dapot e ra balu king ing marawak miraras malapit karela.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:35</lbl> 	At sigatan neng GUINU i Benjamin king arapan na ning Israel; at ding linipul da ding anak na ning Israel king Benjamin king aldo a ita adua lang pulu at limang libu at dinalan a lalaki: deting sabla telan de ing talibung. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:36</lbl> 	Nanupata ikit da ding anak nang Benjamin king mesugat la; uling ding lalaki ning Israel minie lang karinan king Benjamin, uling menalig la karing mamabat a karelang binili salang king Gibea.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:37</lbl> 	At migmalagawa la ding mamabat, a sinagasa la king Gibea; at melaus la ding mamabat, at sigatan da ing mabilug a ciudad king taram na ning talibung. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:38</lbl> 	Ngeni ing pakilalanan dang tanda ding anak na ning Israel at ding mibiling mamabat ya pin, king paukiat lang metung a maragul a lulam ning asuk king ciudad.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:39</lbl> 	At ding anak na ning Israel minurung la king pamipamuk, at ing Benjamin migmula yang miniugat at mekamate karing lalaki ning Israel a ating atlungpulu katau; uling sinabi ra, Tune masugat la king arapan tamu, anti mo ing king minunang pamilaban. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:40</lbl> 	Dapot kanitang ing lulam, migmulang minukiat a ibat king ciudad king metung a asias a asuk, ding Benjamitas melikid la king gugulutan da: at, oini, ing kabilugan ning ciudad minukiat ya banua king asuk. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:41 </lbl>	At mibalik la ding lalaki ning Israel, at ding lalaki ning Benjamin mengagutgut la; uling ikit da king ing dewakan dimpa karela. 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 20:42</lbl> 	Inya pin guinulut la king arapan da ding lalaki ning Israel a melaus la king ilang; dapot tatagalan nong masipit ning pamilaban; at detang linual karing ciudad sinintang do karin king libutad. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:43</lbl> 	Kibkuban dala ding Benjamitas king makapatulug, at tegal dala, at piniamusak dala king karinan dang pipainawan, angga king tulid ning Gibea king nangan a piaslagan ning aldo.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:44</lbl> 	At ding miragsa king Benjamin labi lang walung libung lalaki; deti ngan lalaki lang bantug king tapang. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:45</lbl> 	At mibalik la at tinakas la nangan king ilang angga king batu ning Rimon; at penagal dala karing dalan a matas ding limang libung lalaki; at tegal dong masipit angga king Gidom, at ding asugat da karela adua lang libung lalaki. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:46</lbl> 	Nanupata ding miragsa king aldo a ita kang Benjamin adua lang pulu at limang libung lalaki a tinalan king talibung; deti ngan lalaki lang matapang. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:47</lbl> 	Dapot ding anam a dalan a lalaki mibalik la at tinakas nangan king ilang angga king batu ning Rimon, at migsantung la king batu ning Rimon apat a bulan. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>20:48</lbl> 	At belikan dong pasibayu ding lalaki ning Israel ding anak na ning Benjamin, at sigatan dala king taram na ning talibung, ing mabilug a ciudad, at ding kawan a vaca, at ing anggang ikit da; maiguit kaniti detang anggang ciudad a ikit da silaban dala king api. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:1</lbl> 	Ngeni ding lalaki ning Israel sinumpa la king Mizpa, ngara, Ala ninuman kekami a ibie ne ing anak nang babai kang Benjamin a maguing asawa na. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:2</lbl> 	At ing balayan miras king Bet-el, at linukluk karin anggang gatpanapun king arapan ning Dios, at sikan da ing karelang siwala, at tinangis lang bina. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:3</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Oh GUINU, a Dios ning Israel, baket milyari ngeni iti king Israel, a atin ngeni metung a dai a kulang king Israel? 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:4</lbl> 	At milyari king kabukasan, king ing balayan mibangun maranun, at mitalakad metung a altar karin, at minain ain a durulukan at ain king kapayapan. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:5</lbl> 	At sinabi ra ding anak na ning Israel, Ninu ing atiu ken karing anggang dai na ning Israel a e sinampa king kapulungan kang GUINU? Uling dinapat lang maragul a sumpa tungkul karetang e sinampa kang GUINU king Mizpa, ngana, Alang pangakablang patayan ya. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:6</lbl> 	At pesisisi la ding anak na ning Israel dikil kang Benjamin a karelang kapatad, at sinabi ra, Ating metung a dai a mikawani king Israel king aldo a iti. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:7 </lbl>	Makananu ing kekatang daptan a pamanintun asawa dikil karing melakuan, anti na ning sinumpa tamu kang GUINU a e tala ibie karela a maguing asawa ra ding anak tang babai? 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:8 </lbl>	At sinabi ra, Ninu karing dai ning Israel ing e sinampa kang GUINU king Mizpa? At, oini, alang miras king parang a menibat king Jabes-gilead king kapulungan. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:9</lbl> 	Uling inyang mebilang ing balayan, oini, karin ala metung man karing manuknangan king Jabes-gilead. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:10 </lbl>	At mitubud ing kapamisanan labingaduang libung lalaki karing matapang dili, at inutus na karela, ngana, Ume kayu at sugatan yo ding manuknangan king Jabes-gilead king taram na ning talibung, pati na ding babai at ding anak a mangalati. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:11</lbl> 	At oini ing bague a kekong daptan: sintangan yeng lubus ing balang lalaki, at ing balang babai a sipingan ning lalaki. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:12</lbl> 	At ikit dala karing manuknangan king Jabes-gilead ding apat a dalan a dalagang alang bakas, a e pa kinilalang lalaki king pamakisiping kea; at dela ro king parang king Silo, a atiu king labuad na ning Canaan.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:13</lbl> 	At mitubud ing mabilug a kapamisanan at miniabi la karing anak nang Benjamin a atiu king batu ning Rimon, at pisiag da ing kapayapan karela. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:14</lbl> 	At mibalik ya ing Benjamin king panaun a ita; at binie ro karela ding babai a linigtas dang mabie karing babai ning Jabes-gilead: at makanian man e ro apatulan. 	

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 21:15</lbl> 	At ing balayan sinisi la dikil king Benjamin, uling i GUINU guinawa yang metung a pamikawani karing dai na ning Israel. 	

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:16</lbl> 	Kanita sinabi ra ding makatua ning kapamisanan, Makananu ing kekatang daptan a pamanintun asawa karetang makatagan, anti na ning ding babai melipul la king Benjamin?

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:17</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Karampatan mika ating metung a mana dikil karetang mitakas kang Benjamin, bang ing metung a dai e mapda king Israel. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:18</lbl> 	Makanian man e tala adinan maguing asawa ra karing anak tang babai; uling ding anak na ning Israel sinumpa la, a sinabi ra, Makasumpa ya itang munie metung a asawang babai kang Benjamin. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:19</lbl> 	At sinabi ra, Oini, ating metung a pista kang GUINU banua-banua king Silo, a atiu king paralaya na ning Bet-el, nangan king aslagan ning matas a dalan a sasampa king Siquem manibat king Betel, at king mauli ning Libano. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:20</lbl> 	At inutus do ding anak nang Benjamin, ngara, Ume kayu at mabat ko karing uvasan; 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:21</lbl> 	At lawan yu, at, oini, nung ding anak nang babaing Silo lual la a terak karing terakan, kanita lual kayu karing uvasan, at dakap ya ing balang lalaki kekayu a maguing keang asawa karing anak nang babaing Silo, at ume kayu king labuad na ning Benjamin.

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:22</lbl> 	At mapalyari, nung ding karelang ibpa o ding karelang kapatad datang la barakeng pakiamanuan, king sabian mi karela, Ipagkalub yong binang malam kekami; uling e mila kinuang maguing asawa ing balang metung karela king pamilaban ni e yu no man binie karela; nung ali atin kong kasalanan ngeni. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:23</lbl> 	At depatan dang makanian ding anak nang Benjamin, at kinua rong asawa ra, agpang king karelang bilang, karetang tinerak, ilang dela ra: at mine la at mibalik la king karelang mana, at telakad do ding ciudad, at penuknanganan dala. 

Ding Ukum Judges<lbl> 21:24</lbl> 	At meko la ding anak na ning Israel king panaun a ita a menibatan la karin, balang katau king keang dai at king keang sapni, at meko la a menibatan karin ing balang katau a minuli king keang mana. 

Ding Ukum Judges <lbl>21:25</lbl> 	Karing aldo a deta alang ari king Israel: balang katau depatan na ing mayap king sarili nang mata. 

Title:Prayers
Kapampangan Prayers
<b>The Sign of the Cross</b>
Uli ning tanda ning Santa Cruz, caring masamá quecami, icabus Mu cami, Guinu ming Dios.
Qñg laguiu ning +Ibpa, ampon ning Anac, ampon ning Espiritu Santo. Amen.

<b>The Creed</b>
Sasalpantaya cu qñg Dios, Ibpang mayupayang tutu, linalang qñg banua't yatu.
At cang Jesucristong Anac nang Bugtung a Guinu tamu.
Pengagli Ya qñg upaya ning Banal a Espiritu, mibayit Ya cang Santa Mariang Virgen.
Linasa Ya lalam nang upaya nang Poncio Pilato. Mipacu ya qñg cruz, mete Ya't micutcut.
Tinipa Ya caring mete. Qñg catlung aldo, sinubli yang mebie. Pepaitas Ya banua,
macalucluc uanan ning Dios Ibpang mayupayang tutu. Ibat carin, magbalic Ya naman queti
ban mucum caring mabie ampon mengamate.
Sasalpantaya cu qñg Banal a Espiritu, qñg Santa Iglesia Catolica, qñg pamisamac ding Santos,
qñg pangapatauadda ring casalanan, qñg pangasubli rang mie ring mete, at qñg bie alang angga.
Amen.

<b>The Lord's Prayer</b>
Ibpa mi, a atiu banua. Misamban ya ing lagyu Mu. Datang quecami
ing cayarian Mu. Mipamintuan ing lub Mu, queti sulip anti banua.
Ing cacanan mi qñg aldo-aldo ibie Mu quecami qñg aldo ngeni.
Ampon ipatauad Mo quecami ring sala mi Queca, anti ing pamamatauad
mi caring micasala quecami. E Mu que ipaisaul qñg tucsu, nune icabus
Mu cami caring sablang maroc. Amen.

<b>Angelic Salutation</b> (Hail, Mary!)
Bapu, Maria! Mitmu ca qñg gracia. Ing Guinung Dios atiu queca. Nuan ca caring sablang babayi, at nuan ya pa naman ing bunga ning atian mu, y Jesús.
Santa Maria, Indu ning Dios. Ipanalangin mu queng macasalanan, ngeni, ampon qñg oras ning camatayan mi. Amen.

<b>The Gloria Patri</b>
Ligaya qñg Ibpa, at qñg Anac, at qñg Espiritu Santo. Antimo ing sadia nang ligaya ibat qñg camumulan, ngeni't capilan man, mangga man qñg alang angga. Amen.

<b>The Salve Regina</b>
Bapu Reyna, Indung Mamacalulu, bie ampon yumu, manga panaligan mi,
Bapu Reyna, icang ausan mi, iqueng pepalacuan a anac nang Eva;
icang pangisnawan ming malalam, daralung que manga tatangis queni qñg carinan ning lua.

Ngamu na Reyna, Patulunan mi, balicdan mu cami caring mata mung mapamakalulu,
ampon nung mapupus, pangalako mu queti sulip, paquit me quecami i Jesus,
a bungang masampat ning atian mu.
O malugud ! O mapamacalulu! O Santa Maria Birhen a mayumu!
V:Ipanalangin mu cami, O Santang Indu ning Dios.
R: Ba’queng sucat maquinabang caring pengacu nang Jesucristong Guinu tamu.

<u><b>Religious Writings</b></u>


<b>Salamat Po O’Guinu</b>					<b>Panalangin Para Karing Kapanamdaman</b>

Sanung pusu kaya ing e manangis				Ibpa mi, atiyu banua, mamaus kami ngeni murin
King libutad ning kapagsubukan?				ing makapasubaling paralan.
Makananu kaya nung keng pamanudtud ku			Kapamilatan na ning kekang upaya nung inia melalang kami
Migulantang ku king darabulbul a lahar?				Balang pangisnawa mi, baling abak a makagising kami
Makananu kaya nung aku ing mengayanud			at balang penandit na ning panaun a mabibie kami,
king lahar, mikutkut, at mebuluk?				lalam ngan iti king upaya mu. 
Makananu kaya nung king kagising ku
Ala na kung anak a kakandungan?				Ibpa, nung lelangan mu kami ibat king ala, 
Makananu kaya nung king kabalikid ku				paniwalan ming lalu mu kaming alalang pasibayu.
Ala na kung asawang kayaduangan?				Katmuan mu kami king espiritu mung makapaldan.
Makananu kaya nung king pangalingat ku			Idayu mu ing nanu mang bague a e dapat atiyu kekami.
Ala na ku mu naman pengaring luluguran?
Makananu kaya nung king pamanuli ku				Tanggalan mu ing nanumang babie sakit king katawan.
Ala ne ing bale kung tuknangan?				Ibusni mu la ding nanu mang baradung uyat at
Makananu kaya nung king pamagbalik ku			nanu mang daluyan daya at mie lang pasibayu ding
Ala ne mu naman in balen kung pakamalan?			Sakitan nang parte ning katawan. 
Makananu mung tanggapan ing pagsubuk			Ilako mu ing nanumang makalbag at linisan mu
Ning Indung Kalikasan?					ing nanu mang impeksyun. 
Makananu mung yamyaman ing meging kapalaran?
							Ipaintulut mu ing dumalan king mabilug ming katawan
King dalumdum at dimla ning kabengian				ing pali ning lugud mung makapaldan,
Alus mabating ya ing sarili mung kaisipan			ban milako na ing nanu mang sakit at magobra ya 
Eka sana manangis at gugulisak				ing mabilug ming katawan ayun king pangalalang na.
King sakit at pait niting kapagsubukan.
Eka mu naman sana duduku tanda ning pagsuku			At Ibpa, ibalik mu kami king malusug a kaisipan 
Talakad ka, kapatad ku, ing lahar labanan mu!			at pamikakatawan, ban apagsilbian da ka
Atin kang tapang at sibukan a lininang ning panaun		king balang penandit ning bie mi keti sulip.
Ing lahar yang dalpakan mu, 
Ngeni mu na ipakit ing tetagan mu				Iti aduan mi king kapamilatan nang Kristong Guinu mi. 
Uling ing pago mu ya ing sablayan ning balayan mu		Amen.
Nung nanu mang bage king gabun a mikutkut na
Emu na sana kukulkulan pa.
Sulyap ka babo banua at ing biga sasabian na
King kaibat ning unus ating sibul ning bie a mamagus.
Manalangin kata, kapatad ku, a sana ing Guinu
Saupan nakatang mtitkdo pasibayu.
Aduan ta Kaya na sana ing tula at ligaya
King pusu manatili ya.
Talan ka kanaku, kapatad ku, at igulisak ta
Ing “Salamat Po O’ Guinu”.
   


<u><b>PANALANGIN KING SANTISIMA TRINIDAD</b></u>

Alang-alang pakundangan king Santisima Trinidad.
Dios Ibpa, Dios Anak, at Dios Espiritu Santo, kuldasan mu ke pu at aslagan king banal mung Espiritu at sukuban mu ke king mal mung manto.
Dios Ibpa, pagkaluban mu kaming matibe casalpantayanan.
Dios anak, pagkaluban mu kaming matibe pamikakalugud.
Dios Espiritu Santo, kuldasan mu kami king matibe pamikakalugud.
Dios Espiritu Santo, kuldasan mu kami king banal mung Espiritu at sukuban mu kami king mal mung manto.
Sasalpantay ku king Santisima Trinidad.
Manalig ku king Santisima Trinidad.
Malsinta ku king Santisima Trinidad.
Sisisian ku ing pamikasala ku king Santisima Trinidad.
Pagnasan mi ne man akamit ing santisima Trinidad.


<u><b>Ibpa Mi</b></u>						<u><b>Panalangin</b></u>

Ibpa mi, atyu ka banua, misamban ya ing lagyu mu,		King lagyu ning Dios Ibpa, Dios Anak, at Dios Espiritu Santo,
Dating ing kayarian mu, mipamintuan ing lub mu,			Amen.
Keti sulip, anti banua, mipamintuan ing lub mu.		
Ing kakanan mi king aldo-aldo,				Dios Ibpa, Dios Anak, Dios Espiritu Santo, 
Ibye mu kekami king aldo ngeni.				Sasamban at gagalang ding sablang tao.
Ampo ipatawad mu kekami, ing sala mi keka.			Padre Jesus-Nazareno, sinakup king mabilig yatu
Anti ing pamamtawad mi					King kasalanan ding sablang tao.
Kareng mikasala kekami					Padre Jesus-Nazareno, Dios Espiritu Santo, sulu ding sablang tao
Manga emu ke ipaisawul king tuksu,				Luguran taya ing guinung Dios Ibpang malam,
Nune ikabus king marok.					King luklukan nig katasan, ilang kekatang akasiping,
							Ding aral ning Jesukristo ilang dapat tukian.
<u><b>Bapu Maria</b></u>
							Tapat pusung manalangin, dapat tamung mikakalugud,
Bapu Maria, mipnu king gracia					Ing kamua dapat tamung palabasan.
Ing Guinu atyu keka,					Ing Dios Espiritu Santo, layun na katang luguran. 
Nuan ka karing sablang babai
At nuan ya pa naman ing bunga ning atyan mung I Jesus.		Ing Virgen Santo Rosario yang kang Jesus a Indu na,
							Bapu Maria mipnu king gracia, Ing Dios Ibpa atyu keka,
<u><b>Santa Maria</b></u>				Virgen alang kaparis.
							
Santa Mariang Indu ning Dios,					Virgen alang akapara, pinili ne at liguran ning Dios a mapalsinta
Ipanalangin mu keng makasalanan,				Dios Espiritu Santo, pinili ne y Santa Maria, Y San Joseph,
Ngeni at king oras na ning kamatayan mi,			Ilang tune kayabe.
Amen.							Jesus, Maria, Y Joseph, ilang sulu tamu king panlakad 
							A papunta king Dios Ibpang matas.

<u><b>Panalangin</b></u>				Dapat tamung manalangin, pibandian alang kupas,	
							tipunan tamung ditak-ditak, karing baling pusung maniawad,
Jesus, Jesus, Jesus, Maria Y Joseph,				dapat tamu pin tumipon, pibandian, pibandian a ena asira ning
sagipan yuk e ngan king panganib,				kalawang, king abak maging pangapun, balang penandit dapat 
panganib man pung susun-susun.				tamung manalangin, karing altar ding pibale-bale tamu,
Kekaming tau maliaring datang,				karing bisitas at pisamban, pamaniaus king Dios Ibpa e tamu sa
dumalan mung anti mong angin,				 kakalinguan, ba tamung magkamit king gracia nang mal,
nung ikayu pu Dios ko,					a alang kapupusan.
Ing kekaming ausan


<u><b>Pamagbasbas</b></u>					
							
Ibpa, king kaorasan a iti, ati ke ngan po keti at ibabie mi ing mayap a bengi, at nung malyari pu, ipagkalub yu pu ing kekayung mal a bendisyon, salamat pung alang anti.					
							
O Dios Padre Eterno, king kaorasan pung iti, ati ke ngan po keti at ibabie mi ing mayap a bengi at nung malyari pu, ipagkalub yu na pu kekami, ing mal a bendisyon, salamat pung alang anti.

O Virgen santisima, a kekaming depensora, king kaorasan a iti, ati ke ngan po keti, at ibabie mi ing mayap a bengi at nung malyari pu, ipagkalub yu na pu kekami ing mal a bendisyon, salamat pung alang anti.

O Senior Patriarca San Jose a kekaming abogado, king kaorasan a iti, ati ke ngan po keti at ibabie mi ing mayap a bengi at nung malyari pu, ipagkalub yu nap u kekami ing mal a bendisyon. Salamat pung alang anti.

Ibpa ko, Dios ko at Guinu ko, king kaorasan a iti, ati ke ngan po keti at sisisian ing kakaming pamagkamali, patawaran yu nap u ing kekaming kasalanan pati na ding kasalanan ding kekaming pengari, kapatad, kamag-anak, kaluguran, kakilala, ampon ding kekaming kasalang at ding anggang tau keti king sikluban, kekayu la ngan patawaran Ibpang malam.

Jesus, Jesus, Jesus kung ligaya alang kapupusan, mayumu kung Jesus, Hari ning catasan. Jesus, tanggapan mu la sa ding kaladuami at keka lang sagipan. Jesus ko, Sinta ko, Jesus Maria Y Joseph, Ibpa ko, salamat kekayu, at linigtas yu kami king kakamal-kamalan a benging iti, iligtas yu ke pung pasibayu king kakamal-kamalan a kabukas a alang sakuna at alang karamdaman ding kekaming kaladua at katawan, lunusan yuk e sa at pagkaluban king gracia yung mal kabang mabie kami keting sikluban.

<u><b>Pamanisi</b></u>

Maniklaud kami karing bitis mu Jesus a Guinu ko, ing aduan mi kekayu ing patawad karing sablang kasalanan ku, kekami no man pung sisisian ding sabla ming kasalanan, at layun mi lang tatangisan king mal yung arapan, matibe ing pangaku ku king ena ku mikakaksala king saup ning mal a gracia mu, ania ing aduan ku keka Jesus ko ing pagsilbian daka. Gawan mu kaming maging tapat ing pamagsilbi mi keka, ing kakaming pangarimla, dinan mu pung kalunusan kekami yu pu ituru ing tapat a pamanuyu  dig kaladua mi at pusu, king Dios pagparalampu. Sasamban da kop u Guinu kung Jesukristo, at gagalangan da ka, uling king mal a Hostia atiu ken king kekayung kakamal-kamalan a katawan, akaldua, at panga-Dios.

<u><b>Pamon</b></u>

O pusung makabuklat, tuknangan a binang maslag, mamun na kami o Jesus kong liyag, Bendisyon yu pu ilapat.
O pususng mibabata king krus at pasakit, mamun na kami Jeusu kong kasi. Bendisyon yu pu kekami ipakamit.
O pusung sinugatan ning pamaglilu ku’t pamangaliuan, mamun na kami Jesus kong nuan. Bendisyon yu pu kekami ipabal.
O kasi ko at sinta, amakibandi karing kaladua, maun na ku Jesus ku’t Ibpa. Bendisyon yu pu ibie mu na.

<b> ATLUNG PANALANGIN</b>

<b>BAYU MANGAN</b>

Ibpa, salamat pung dakal,
Kening grasya Mung pepabal,
Keka sanang bendisyun
Ba’rang lubus ikasikan
Ding kaladwa mi’t katawan,
Ngeni at kapilan pa man;
At ibalik Mu sa ‘ng myuman
Kening kekeng piyapan.
Antimurin, ding danupan.
Keka la sanang pakabsyan.Amen.

<b>BAYU MATUDTUD</b>

Ibpa,salamat
King kaku Mu pamaningat,
King patingapung linabas
Ing kalam Mu kakung sa’ng mayap,
King salang kakung arapat
Ibpa Mu pu ing patawad;
At nyuman Mu kung iligtas
King disgrasya nang Satanas.Amen.

<b>KAGISING NENG ABAK</b>

Salamat pu keka,Ibpa,
Mipaynawa kung payapa,
Ngening abak adwan ku sa
Ing mamale Kang mistula
Kening pusu ku at diwa
Ban king marok ku milisya,
At atupad kung mausta
Ing kaburyan Mu at nasa;
Layun ibye Mung matula
Ing kalam Mu’t pamipala.Amen.

Mayo 17,1982


<b>PANALANGIN -2</b>

Nung ing daraptan ku makatud at ustu,
Ing kalam Mu, Ginu, mipagkalub kaku;
At makanyan sanang papanatilyan Mu
Ba’ rang ikatula ring para kung tau.

Dapot nung e ustu at karapat-dapat,
Mipatawaran sa ing mali kung dapat;
Layun ituru Mu nung nanu ing sukat
Ba’tung makatuntun king mayap a aklat.

Ing panandama’ng ning aliwang tau
Panandama’na sa ning pangatau ku;
King kayang kamalayan bulagan Mu na ku
Ba’ ken e misagkul king e pamitonu.

Nung makananu keng tune aluguran
Ya sa ing tumubu kening pilubluban;
E mu king salitang alang kabaldugan
Nune sa king dapat king Kekang kaburyan.

Mabyasa ku sanang tutung mamatawad
Karing mikasalang kanakung kapatad;
Uling nung iti ya ing kakung atupad
Tanggapan ku naman ing Kekang patawad.

Babo na ning sabla, mamale Ka sana
Keing kakung diwa at pusung malsinta;
Ulinhg nung kanaku paratng ati Ka,
Klakwan’ne ning tuksu ing kakung kaladwa!

Mayo 6, 1982




<b>DING DALIT</b>
<b>MUMUNANG LIBRU</b>


 
<b>Ing pamialiwa ning matulid at ning marawak</b>

Nuan ya ing tua a e lalakad king usuk na ning marawak, Ni tatalakad man king dalan da ding Makasalanan, Ni lulukluk man king luklukan da ding mapanlibak:  Dapot ing keang tula atiu king kautusan ng JEHOVA; At king kautusan na mibulebule ya king aldo at bengi. At maguing anti yang metung a dutung a mitanam king siping na ning agus na  ning danum, A mamunga ya king keang kapanaunan, A ing keang bulung e malalanat; At nanuman ing daptan na mipapala.  Ding marawak e la makanian, Nung e anti la mo ing apa a papaid ning angina.  Inya pin ding marawak e la mitalakad king pamanukum, Ni ding makasalanan king kapamisanan da ding matulid.  Uling i JEHOVA balu ne ing dalan na ning matulid; Dapot ing dalan na ning  marawak mawala ya.

<b>Ing pamagari na ning linian nang JEHOVA</b>

Baket  ding bansa magugulu la, At ding balayan mibulebule la king metung a alang kabaldugan a bague?  Ding ari ning labuad pesipagsadia la, At ding pekapun misasangguni lang makapamisan, Salang kang JEHOVA, at salang king keang linian, sasabian da,  Tára pamatdan tala ding karelang gapus, At yugse tála a manibat kekatamu ding karelang lubid.  Ing makalukluk karing banua maili ya: Ing Guinu daptan na ing kalibakan karela.  Kanita maniabi ya karela king mua, At guluan nala king makaluku nang kasbu: Makanianman likluk ke ing kanakung ari King babo ning kanakung banal a bunduk-bundukan ning Zion. Sabian ke ing kautusan: I JEHOVA sinabi na kaku , Ika ing kakung anak; King aldo iti aku penganak daka. Maniawad ka kaku, at ibie ko keka ding bansa a kekang pekamana, At ding kawawakasan a dake na ning labuad a kekang pekabandi. Pakalian mula king tukud a bakal; Yugse mong paglasilasian a anti mo ing metung a lulanan na ning magtatalu. Ngeni pin magpakabiasa kayu, Oh ikong ari: Pausuk kayu, ikong ukun ning labuad. Suyawan yeng maki galgal. Uman ye ing anak a lalaki, a magkang mimua ya, at mangamate kayu king dalan, Uling ing keang mua malablab. Nuan la ding sabla a magsantung kea.

<b>Panalangin king abak king kapanaligan king Dios: metung a dalit nang David, inyang takasan ne I Absalom a anak na</b>

JEHOVA , kasikan dang binang miragdag ding kanakung kasalang! Dakal la ding mibabangun a salang kaku.  Dakal la ding sasabi king kakung kaladua, Alang saup dikl kea king Dios. (Selah)  Dapot ika, Oh JEHOVA, kalasag ka king makapatulug kaku; Kaku kang ligaya, at mitatas king kanakung buntuk.  Kukulisak ku kang JEHOVA king kanakung siwala,  At pakibatan naku manibat king keang banal a bunduk-bundukan.  (Selah)  Migkera ku at metudtud;  Miguising ku; uling alalayan nakung JEHOVA.  E ku mitakutan karing apulu nang libu ning balayan a mibili king sarili ra salang kanaku king makapatulug.  Talakad ka, Oh JEHOVA; iligtas muku, Oh Dios ko: Uling sinugat mula king pisngi ding anggang kasalang ku; Sinira mula ding ipan da ding mangarawak.  Ing kaligtasan bandi nang JEHOVA;  Ing kekang kanuanan magbili sa king kekang balayan. (Selah)

<b>Panalangin king bengi a pamanalig king Dios; king pekapun a masico; karing titigtigan a ating cuerdas; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Pakibatan muku nung mamaus ku, Oh Dios ning kakung katuliran; Binili muku king degulan inyang atiku king kagutgutan:  Pakalulu ka kanaku, at pakiramdaman mu ing kanakung panalangin.  Oh ikayung anak da ding tau, anggang kapilan a ing ligaya ku mibalik king kealan puri?  Anggang kapilan luguran yu ing alang kabaldugan at panintunan yu ing kalaraman?  (Selah)  Dapot kilalanan yu king i JEHOVA kewani neng dikil king keang sarili ing banal:  I JEHOVA makiramdam ya ngening maus ku kea.  Talakad ko king takut, at e ko mikakasala:  Mibulebule kayu king kekong sariling pusu king kekong pagkeran, at magtajimik kayu.  (Selah)  Yain yo ding daun ning katuliran, At ibili yu ing kekong kapanaligan kang JEHOVA.  Dakal la ding sasabi, Ninu ing pakilala kekatamu king nanumang mayap?  JEHOVA, itas mu ing sala na ning kekang lupa kekami.  Binili mu ing tula king kanakung pusu, A maiguit king karela inyang ing binutil da at ing karelang bayung alak miragdagan.  King kapayapan magkera ku at matudtud; Uling ika mung dili, JEHOVA, ing misasantung kaku king kaligtasan.

<b>Panalangin bang ingatan king marawak; king pekapun a musico; karing titigtigan a titiupan; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Pakiramdaman mula ding kakung amanu, Oh JEHOVA,  Pakundangan mu ing kakung pamibulebule, Makiramdam ka king siwala na ning kanakung kulisak, kanakung Ari, at kanakung Dios;  Uling keka ku manalangin.  Oh JEHOVA, king abak pakiramdaman mu ing kanakung siwala;  King abak idurup ku ing kanakung panalangin keka, at maglame ku.  Uling ika e ka metung a Dios a matutula king dewakan:  Ing marawak e ya makipanuknangan keka.  Ing mayabang e ya talakad king kekang lalawan:  Pikakasaman  mula ding anggang talapaniapat king marawak.  Lipulan mula ding maniabi king kalaraman:  Kasusumamian neng JEHOVA ing maung daya at mapamirayang tau.  Dapot dikil kaku, king keraklan na ning kekang kayubuan a lub lungub ku king kekang bale: King takut keka samba ku king kekang banal a templo.  Patnubayan muku, Oh JEHOVA, king kekang katuliran uli ra ding kanakung kasalang;  Tuliran me ing kekang dalan king arapan na ning kakung lupa.  Uling alang katapatan king karelang asbuk;  Ing karelang dake king lub tune karawakan;  Ing karelang akmulan kutkutan yang makabuklat; Maniunu la king karelang dila.  Ibilang mong mikasala, Oh Dios: Pabustan mong miragsa karing karelang sariling usuk; Ibulusuk mula king keraklan na ning karelang pamanalangsang; Uling sinalangsang lang laban keka.  Dapot pabustan mung detang anggang magsantung keka magsaya la,  Pabustan mong kapilan man ikulio ra ing tula, uling ipanlualu mula: Pabustan mula naman detang malugud king kekang laguiu magsaya la keka.  Uling panuanan me ing matulid: Oh JEHOVA, kulungan me king kapanusigan anti mong king metung a kalasag.

<b>Panalangin tungkul king kapakaluluan king panaun ning kaligaligan; king pekapun a musico; karing titigtigan a maki cuerdas a misasadia king octava; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Oh JEHOVA, e muku pangamanuan king kekang mua,  Ni e muku parusan king mapali mung kasbu.  Pakalulu ka kaku, Oh JEHOVA; uling meyayat ku:  Oh JEHOVA, pakayapan muku; uling ding kanakung butul malingasngas la.  Ing kaku mang kaladua malilingasngas yang bina:  At ika, Oh JEHOVA, nu anti kaluat? Mibalik ka, Oh JEHOVA, iligtas me ing kaladua ku:  Iligtas muku alang alang king kayubuan mung lub.  Uling king kamatayan alang pamigaganaka keka;  King Sheol ninung munie pasalamat keka?  Mapagal ku king kanakung ngulangul;  Balang bengi pakawen ke ing kanakung pagkeran; Didiligan ke ing kanakung ulunan king kanakung lua.  Ing kanakung mata mangaslak ya king uli na ning pagsalbat; Matutua ya king uli ra ding anggang kanakung kasalang.  Kawani ko kanaku, ikong anggang talapaniapat marawak; Uling dimdam nang JEHOVA ing siwala na ning kanakung kiak.  Dimdam nang JEHOVA ing kanakung pamanigapu; I JEHOVA tanggapan na ing kanakung panalangin.  Ding anggang kasalang ku mipakarine la at malingasngas lang bina;  Pasibalik la, mipakarine lang bigla.

<b>I JEHOVA penigapuan ya bang panlualu ne ing salmista, salang king marawak; Shiggaion nang David, a keang dalit kang JEHOVA, tungkul karing amanu nang Cus a Benjamita</b>

Oh JEHOVANG kanakung Dios, keka ku magpasantung:  Iligtas muku karing anggang tatagal kanaku, a itimawa muku.  Magkang ing kanakung kaladua pangilayan de a anti ing leon,  Pamimirasuan de, kabang alang ninumang magligtas.  Oh JEHOVANG kakung Dios, nung aku depatan ku iti;  Nun gating dewakan karing kakung gamat;  Nung minablas kung dewakan kanitang atiu king kapayapan kanaku  (Wa, linigtas ke itang king alang nanumang kasangkanan meguing kasalang ke);  Pabustan mung tagalan ne ning kasalang ing kakung kaladua, at dasnan ne;  Wa, pabustan meng dalpakan ne ing kakung bie king labuad,  At ibili na ing kakung ligaya king alikabuk.  (Selah)  Mibangun ka, Oh JEHOVA, king kekang mua;  Itas mu ing kekang sarili salang king kasbu ra ding kakung kasalang,  At miguising ka dikil kaku; inutus mu ing kayatulan,  At pabustan mung ing kapamisanan da ding balayan kulungan dakang makapatulug; At babo ra mibalik ka king katasan.  I JEHOVA darapat yang kayatulan karing balayan: Atulan muku, Oh JEHOVA, agpang king kanakung katuliran, at king kakung katapatan a atiu kanaku.  Oh pabustan mung ing dewakan da ding marawak mapupus, dapot italakad me ing matulid;  Uling ing Dios a matulid susubukan no ding kaisipan at ding pusu.  Ing kalasag ku kambe ne ning Dios.  A mililigtas king matulid a pusu.  Ing Dios metung yang matulid a ukum.  Wa, metung yang Dios a maki mua king baling aldo.  Nung ing metung a tau e ya mibalik, itais ne ing keang talibung; Binatak ne ing keang bai, at sidia naya;  Sidia nala naman dikil kea ding kasangkapan na ning kamatayan;  Igagawa nong mangabagsik a paslu ding keang uyung.  Oini, miraramdam ya king dewakan;  Wa, pengagli na ing piraya, at penganak na ing kalaraman.  Guinawa yang metung a kulkul, at inaun ne,  At menabu ya king paligui a keang guewa.  Ing keang piraya mibalik king babo ning sarili nang buntuk.  At ing keang pamamigla kuldas king keang sariling bunbunan.  Munie kung pasalamat kang JEHOVA agpang king keang katuliran,  At dalit kung kapurian king laguiu nang JEHOVANG Kakataskatasan.

<b>Ing ligaya nang JEHOVA at ing kamalan ning tau; king pekapun a musico; misadia king Gittith; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Oh JEHOVA, a kekeng Guinu, Karangal na nang da ning kekang laguiu king mabilug a labuad, Ikang mibili king ligaya mu babo ding banua!  Manibat king asbuk da ding bingut at ding sususu tinatag mu ing sikanan,  King uli ra ding kekang kasalang at ing mapanablas.  Ngening pibulebulayan kula ding kekang banua, ding dapat da ding kekang tarili,  Ing bulan at ding batuin, a kekang tinatag;  Nanu ya ing tau, a keka yang gaganakan?  At ing anak ning tau, a keka yang daralawan?  Uling guewa meng mababa mung ditak king Dios,  At pitungan me king ligaya at puri.  Guewa men gating pamaniakup karing dapat da ding kekang gamat; Binili no ding sablang bague king lalam da dng keang bitis:  Ding anggang tupa at vaca, Wa, at ding lasip king marangle, Ding ayup karing banua, at ding asan king dayatmalat,  Nanumang daralan karing dalan da ding dayatmalat.  Oh JEHOVA, a kekeng Guinu, Karangal na nang da ning kekang laguiu king mabulig a labuad!

<b>Metung a dalit a kapasalamatan dikil king justicia ning Dios; king pekapun a musico; misadia king Muth-labben; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Munie kung kapasalamatan kang JEHOVA king mabilug kung pusu;  Ipakilala ko ding anggang makapagmulala mung dapat.  Tumula ku at magpakasaya keka;  Dalit kung kapurian king kekang laguiu, Oh Kakataskatasan.  Ngening ding kakung kasalang mibalik la, Mitakid la at malipul king arapan mu.  Uling inalalayan mu ing kanakung katuliran at ing kanakung pisabian;  Makalukluk ka king luklukan a mamatul king katuliran.  Sebianan mula ding bansa, linipul mula ding marawak;  Pitda mu ing karelang laguiu angga king kapilan pa man.  Ding kasalang miras la king metung a kawakasan; magdilidili la angga king kapilan pa man;  At ding ciudad a kekang digsa, Ing kabud pamigaganaka karela mebating.  Dapot i JEHOVA makalukluk yang anting ari king kapilan pa man: Sidia ne ing keang luklukan dikil king kayatulan;  At atulan na ing yatu king katuliran,  Manibala ya king kayatulan karing balayan king karampatan.  I JEHOVA man maguing metung yang matas a batiawan dikil karing mayayalipit, Metung a matas a batiawan king panaun na ning kaligaligan; At ding makibalu king kekang laguiu ibili ra ing pamanalig da keka;  Uling ika, JEHOVA, e mo pepaimburisan ding manintun keka.  Dalit kayung kapurian kang JEHOVA, a manuknangan king Zion: Ibulalag yo king libutad na ning balayan ding keang dapat.  Uling ing darapat king pamanusisa tungkul king daya ganakan nala; E na kakalinguan ing kulisak ning pakakalulu.  Pakalulu ka kaku, Oh JEHOVA; Lawan mu ing kakung kasakitan a pibabatan ku karing mimumua kanaku, Ika a mitatas kanaku manibat karing pasbulan ning kamatayan;  Bakung apakilala ing anggang kekang kapurian.  Karing pasbulan dalan ning anak nang babaing Zion.  Tumula ku king kekang kaligtasan.  Ding bansa limbug la king kulkul a karelang guewa:  King lambat a karelang selikut ing karelang sariling bitis yang merakap.  I JEHOVA pepabalu na ing keang sarili, dinapat yang kayatulan: Ing marawak mesilu ya king dapat da ding keang sariling gamat.  (Higgaaion. Selah)  Ing marawak mibalik ya king Sheol.  Ding anggang bansa pin a mangalinguan king Dios.  Uling ing magkailangan e ya makalinguan kapilan man.  Mibangun ka, Oh JEHOVA; e mu pabustan manyaul ya ing tau;  Pabustan mung miatulan la ding bansa king lalawan mu.  Ibili mula king takut, Oh JEHOVA; Pabustan mung ding bansa abalu ra ing sarili ra king ila tau la mu. (Selah)

<b>Metung a panalangin king pangasaldak da ding marawak</b>
 
Baket makatalakad ka king marayu, Oh JEHOVA?  Baket sasalikut mu ing kekang sarili king panaun na ning kalingasngasan?  King kapagmaragulan na ning marawak ing pakakalulu matatagal yang masipit;  Pabustan mung marakap la karing kalalangan a karelang inukul. Uling ing marawak magmayabang ya king nasa na ning keang pusu, At ing mapanangkamin sasakuil ne, wa, pimumuan ne ih JEHOVA. Ing marawak, king kapagmaragulan na ning keang aske, sasabian na, E ne kaministilan iti. Ding anggang pamiisip na ila pin, Alang Dios. Ding keang lakad  maki kesiasan la king sablang panaun; Ding kekang kayatulan marayu lang labis king keang panlalawe: Tungkul karing anggang kasalang na, magmaragul ya karela. Sasabian na king keang pusu, E ku makimut; Karing sablang dai e ku mibili king kasakitan.  Ing keang asbuk mitmu ya king pamalmura at pamamiraya at pamanalipit:  King lalam na ning keang dila atiu ing kamulangan at dewakan.  Makalukluk ya karing makasalikut a karinan da ding nayun;  Karing lijim a karinan Karin ne papatayan ing alang malit;  Ding keang mata makadangat lang pasuklab salang karing alang akarapat.  Manasdap ya king lijim a anti mong leon king keang lukib;  Mamabang ya baneng dakpan ing pakakalulu;  Darakpan ne ing pakakalulu, ngening akulung ne king keang lambat.  Gugulung ya, duruku ya,  At ding alang akarapat mababaldug la king uri ra ding keang mangasikan.  Sasabian na king keang pusu: Ing Dios akalinguan na, Sasalikut ne ing keang lupa, e na ne akit iti.  Mibangun ka, Oh JEHOVA; Oh Dios, itas me ing kekang gamat:  E me kakalinguan ing pakakalulu.  Baket pimumuan ne nung marawak ing Dios, At sasabian na king keang pusu, E me aduan ite?  Ikit me iti; uling manakit kang kasakitan at pangajuajagui, bamung kuananan ablas king kekang gamat.  Ing alang akarapat payampun na ing sarili na keka; Ika ing meguing talasaup na ning ulilang tata.  Paklian me ing takde na ning marawak; At makatungkul king marawak a tau, panintunan mu ing keang dewakan angga king ala na kanga kit.  I JEHOVA Ari ya king kapilan pa man:  Ding bansa malilipul la king keang labuad.  JEHOVA, dimdam mu ing nasa ra ding mamu lub; Isadia me ing karelang pusu, daptan mung ing balugbug mu ipakiramdam me;  Baneng atulan ing ulirang tata at ing mayayalipit, Bang ing tau a king labuad e ne maguing makapangilabut pa.  

<b>I JEHOVA metung yang santungan at talapanlualu; king pekapun a musico; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Kang JEHOVA karin ku magsantung: Makananung sabian yu king kakung kaladua.  Tumakas kang anti mong metung a ayup king kekang bunduk;  Uling, oini, ding marawak binatak de ing bai, Sasadia re ing karelang uyung king litid, Balang mugnus king busal dalumdum king matulid a pusu; Nung ding pitatalakaran malasak la, Nanung malyari nang daptan ning matulid?  I JEHOVA atiu king keang banal a templo; I JEHOVA ing keang luklukan atiu banua; Ding keang mata lalawe la, ding keang talukab mata magumasid la, karing anak da ding tau.  I JEHOVA susubukan ne ing matulid;  Dapot king marawak at ing lulugud king pamamigla mimumua ya ing keang kaladua.  King marawak pauran yang silu; Api at asufre at milalablab a angin ing maguing dake na ning karelang copa.  Uling I JEHOVA matulid ya; kaluguran na ing katuliran:  Ing matulid atangalan ne ing keang lupa.

<b>Ing Dios a talasaup salang karing taksil; king pekapun a musico; misasadia king octava; metung a dalit nang David</b>

Sumaup ka, JEHOVA; uling ing banal a tau mawawala ya;  Uling ing tapat magkulang ya king libutad da ding anak da ding tau.  Maniabi la e tutu baling metung king kalupa nang tau;  karing labing mapanyunu, at ating adua pusu, maniabi la.  I JEHOVA katuran nala ding anggang labing mapanyunu,  Ing dila a maniabing mangaragul a bague.  Ding miniabi, King pamamilatan na ning kekeng dila manyaul kami; Ding kekaming labi kekami lang sarili: ninu ing panginuan mi? Uli ning pangaalipit ning kalulu, uli ning saingsing na ning magkailangan, Ngeni mibangun ku, nganang JEHOVA; Ibili ke king kaligtasan a keang pagnasan.  Ding amanu nang JEHOVA malinis lang amanu;  A anti la mong pilak a mesubuk king hornu king labuad, A mekatapitu medalise.
